manum ekāgram āsīnam abhigamya maharṣayaḥ 
pratipūjya yathānyāyam idaṃ vacanam abruvan  Mn 
bhagavan sarvavarṇānāṃ yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ 
antaraprabhavānāṃ ca dharmān no vaktum arhasi  Mn 
tvam eko hy asya sarvasya vidhānasya svayaṃbhuvaḥ 
acintyasyāprameyasya kāryatattvārthavit prabho  Mn 
sa taiḥ pṛṣṭas tathā samyag amitaujā mahātmabhiḥ 
pratyuvācārcya tān sarvān maharṣīñ śrūyatām iti  Mn 
āsīd idaṃ tamobhūtam aprajñātam alakṣaṇam 
apratarkyam avijñeyaṃ prasuptam iva sarvataḥ  Mn 
tataḥ svayaṃbhūr bhagavān avyakto vyañjayann idam 
mahābhūtādi vṛttaujāḥ prādur āsīt tamonudaḥ  Mn 
yo 'sāv atīndriyagrāhyaḥ sūkṣmo 'vyaktaḥ sanātanaḥ 
sarvabhūtamayo 'cintyaḥ sa eva svayam udbabhau  Mn 
so 'bhidhyāya śarīrāt svāt sisṛkṣur vividhāḥ prajāḥ 
apa eva sasarjādau tāsu vīryam avāsṛjat  Mn 
tad aṇḍam abhavad dhaimaṃ sahasrāṃśusamaprabham 
tasmiñ jajñe svayaṃ brahmā sarvalokapitāmahaḥ  Mn 
āpo narā iti proktā āpo vai narasūnavaḥ 
tā yad asyāyanaṃ pūrvaṃ tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
yat tat kāraṇam avyaktaṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmakaṃ 
tadvisṛṣṭaḥ sa puruṣo loke brahmeti kīrtyate  Mn 
tasminn aṇḍe sa bhagavān uṣitvā parivatsaram 
svayam evātmano dhyānāt tad aṇḍam akarod dvidhā  Mn 
tābhyāṃ sa śakalābhyāṃ ca divaṃ bhūmiṃ ca nirmame 
madhye vyoma diśaś cāṣṭāv apāṃ sthānaṃ ca śāśvataṃ  Mn 
udbabarhātmanaś caiva manaḥ sadasadātmakam 
manasaś cāpy ahaṃkāram abhimantāram īśvaram  Mn 
mahāntam eva cātmānaṃ sarvāṇi triguṇāni ca 
viṣayāṇāṃ grahītṝṇi śanaiḥ pañcendriyāṇi ca  Mn 
teṣāṃ tv avayavān sūkṣmān ṣaṇṇām apy amitaujasām 
saṃniveśyātmamātrāsu sarvabhūtāni nirmame  Mn 
yan mūrtyavayavāḥ sūkṣmās tānīmāny āśrayanti ṣaṭ 
tasmāc charīram ity āhus tasya mūrtiṃ manīṣiṇaḥ  Mn 
tad āviśanti bhūtāni mahānti saha karmabhiḥ 
manaś cāvayavaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ sarvabhūtakṛd avyayam  Mn 
teṣām idaṃ tu saptānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ mahaujasām 
sūkṣmābhyo mūrtimātrābhyaḥ saṃbhavaty avyayād vyayam  Mn 
ādyādyasya guṇaṃ tv eṣām avāpnoti paraḥ paraḥ 
yo yo yāvatithaś caiṣāṃ sa sa tāvad guṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
sarveṣāṃ tu sa nāmāni karmāṇi ca pṛthak pṛthak 
vedaśabdebhya evādau pṛthak saṃsthāś ca nirmame  Mn 
karmātmanāṃ ca devānāṃ so 'sṛjat prāṇināṃ prabhuḥ 
sādhyānāṃ ca gaṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ yajñaṃ caiva sanātanam  Mn 
agnivāyuravibhyas tu trayaṃ brahma sanātanam 
dudoha yajñasiddhyartham ṛgyajuḥsāmalakṣaṇam  Mn 
kālaṃ kālavibhaktīś ca nakṣatrāṇi grahāṃs tathā 
saritaḥ sāgarāñ śailān samāni viṣamāni ca  Mn 
tapo vācaṃ ratiṃ caiva kāmaṃ ca krodham eva ca 
sṛṣṭiṃ sasarja caivemāṃ sraṣṭum icchann imāḥ prajāḥ  Mn 
karmaṇāṃ ca vivekārthaṃ dharmādharmau vyavecayat 
dvandvair ayojayac cemāḥ sukhaduḥkhādibhiḥ prajāḥ  Mn 
aṇvyo mātrā vināśinyo daśārdhānāṃ tu yāḥ smṛtāḥ 
tābhiḥ sārdham idaṃ sarvaṃ saṃbhavaty anupūrvaśaḥ  Mn 
yaṃ tu karmaṇi yasmin sa nyayuṅkta prathamaṃ prabhuḥ 
sa tad eva svayaṃ bheje sṛjyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ  Mn 
hiṃsrāhiṃsre mṛdukrūre dharmādharmāv ṛtānṛte 
yad yasya so 'dadhāt sarge tat tasya svayam āviśat  Mn 
yathā rtuliṅgāny ṛtavaḥ svayam eva rtuparyaye 
svāni svāny abhipadyante tathā karmāṇi dehinaḥ  Mn 
lokānāṃ tu vivṛddhyarthaṃ mukhabāhūrupādataḥ 
brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyaṃ vaiśyaṃ śūdraṃ ca niravartayat  Mn 
dvidhā kṛtvātmano deham ardhena puruṣo 'bhavat 
ardhena nārī tasyāṃ sa virājam asṛjat prabhuḥ  Mn 
tapas taptvāsṛjad yaṃ tu sa svayaṃ puruṣo virāṭ 
taṃ māṃ vittāsya sarvasya sraṣṭāraṃ dvijasattamāḥ  Mn 
ahaṃ prajāḥ sisṛkṣus tu tapas taptvā suduścaram 
patīn prajānām asṛjaṃ maharṣīn ādito daśa  Mn 
marīcim atryaṅgirasau pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum 
pracetasaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca bhṛguṃ nāradam eva ca  Mn 
ete manūṃs tu saptān yān asṛjan bhūritejasaḥ 
devān devanikāyāṃś ca maharṣīṃś cāmitaujasaḥ  Mn 
yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāṃś ca gandharvāpsaraso 'surān 
nāgān sarpān suparṇāṃś ca pitṝṇāṃś ca pṛthaggaṇam  Mn 
vidyuto 'śanimeghāṃś ca rohitendradhanūṃṣi ca 
ulkānirghātaketūṃś ca jyotīṃṣy uccāvacāni ca  Mn 
kinnarān vānarān matsyān vividhāṃś ca vihaṅgamān 
paśūn mṛgān manuṣyāṃś ca vyālāṃś cobhayatodataḥ  Mn 
kṛmikīṭapataṅgāṃś ca yūkāmakṣikamatkuṇam 
sarvaṃ ca daṃśamaśakaṃ sthāvaraṃ ca pṛthagvidham  Mn 
evam etair idaṃ sarvaṃ manniyogān mahātmabhiḥ 
yathākarma tapoyogāt sṛṣṭaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam  Mn 
yeṣāṃ tu yādṛṣaṃ karma bhūtānām iha kīrtitam 
tat tathā vo 'bhidhāsyāmi kramayogaṃ ca janmani  Mn 
paśavaś ca mṛgāś caiva vyālāś cobhayatodataḥ 
rakṣāṃsi ca piśācāś ca manuṣyāś ca jarāyujāḥ  Mn 
aṇḍājāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ sarpā nakrā matsyāś ca kacchapāḥ 
yāni caivaM prakārāṇi sthalajāny audakāni ca  Mn 
svedajaṃ daṃśamaśakaṃ yūkāmakṣikamatkuṇam 
ūṣmaṇaś copajāyante yac cānyat kiṃ cid īdṛṣam  Mn 
udbhijjāḥ sthāvarāḥ sarve bījakāṇḍaprarohiṇaḥ 
oṣadhyaḥ phalapākāntā bahupuṣpaphalopagāḥ  Mn 
apuṣpāḥ phalavanto ye te vanaspatayaḥ smṛtāḥ 
puṣpiṇaḥ phalinaś caiva vṛkṣās tūbhayataḥ smṛtāḥ  Mn 
gucchagulmaṃ tu vividhaṃ tathaiva tṛṇajātayaḥ 
bījakāṇḍaruhāṇy eva pratānā vallya eva ca  Mn 
tamasā bahurūpeṇa veṣṭitāḥ karmahetunā 
antaḥsaṃjñā bhavanty ete sukhaduḥkhasamanvitāḥ  Mn 
etadantās tu gatayo brahmādyāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ 
ghore 'smin bhūtasaṃsāre nityaṃ satatayāyini  Mn 
evaṃ sarvaṃ sa sṛṣṭvedaṃ māṃ cācintyaparākramaḥ 
ātmany antardadhe bhūyaḥ kālaṃ kālena pīḍayan  Mn 
yadā sa devo jāgarti tad evaṃ ceṣṭate jagat 
yadā svapiti śāntātmā tadā sarvaṃ nimīlati  Mn 
tasmin svapiti tu svasthe karmātmānaḥ śarīriṇaḥ 
svakarmabhyo nivartante manaś ca glānim ṛcchati  Mn 
yugapat tu pralīyante yadā tasmin mahātmani 
tadāyaṃ sarvabhūtātmā sukhaṃ svapiti nirvṛtaḥ  Mn 
tamo 'yaṃ tu samāśritya ciraṃ tiṣṭhati sendriyaḥ 
na ca svaṃ kurute karma tadotkrāmati mūrtitaḥ  Mn 
yadāṇumātriko bhūtvā bījaṃ sthāsnu cariṣṇu ca 
samāviśati saṃsṛṣṭas tadā mūrtiṃ vimuñcati  Mn 
evaṃ sa jāgratsvapnābhyām idaṃ sarvaṃ carācaram 
saṃjīvayati cājasraṃ pramāpayati cāvyayaḥ  Mn 
idaṃ śāstraṃ tu kṛtvāsau mām eva svayam āditaḥ 
vidhivad grāhayām āsa marīcyādīṃs tv ahaṃ munīn  Mn 
etad vo 'yaṃ bhṛguḥ śāstraṃ śrāvayiṣyaty aśesataḥ 
etad dhi matto 'dhijage sarvam eṣo 'khilaṃ muniḥ  Mn 
tatas tathā sa tenokto maharṣimanunā bhṛguḥ 
tān abravīd ṛṣīn sarvān prītātmā śrūyatām iti  Mn 
svāyaṃbhuvasyāsya manoḥ ṣaḍvaṃśyā manavo 'pare 
sṛṣṭavantaḥ prajāḥ svāḥ svā mahātmāno mahaujasaḥ  Mn 
svārociṣaś cottamaś ca tāmaso raivatas tathā 
cākṣuṣaś ca mahātejā vivasvatsuta eva ca  Mn 
svāyaṃbhuvādyāḥ saptaite manavo bhūritejasaḥ 
sve sve 'ntare sarvam idam utpādyāpuś carācaram  Mn 
nimeṣā daśa cāṣṭau ca kāṣṭhā triṃśat tu tāḥ kalā 
triṃśat kalā muhūrtaḥ syād ahorātraṃ tu tāvataḥ  Mn 
ahorātre vibhajate sūryo mānuṣadaivike 
rātriḥ svapnāya bhūtānāṃ ceṣṭāyai karmaṇām ahaḥ  Mn 
pitrye rātryahanī māsaḥ pravibhāgas tu pakṣayoḥ 
karmaceṣṭāsv ahaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī  Mn 
daive rātryahanī varṣaṃ pravibhāgas tayoḥ punaḥ 
ahas tatrodagayanaṃ rātriḥ syād dakṣiṇāyanam  Mn 
brāhmasya tu kṣapāhasya yat pramāṇaṃ samāsataḥ 
ekaikaśo yugānāṃ tu kramaśas tan nibodhata  Mn 
catvāry āhuḥ sahasrāṇi varsāṇāṃ tat kṛtaṃ yugam 
tasya tāvac chatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaś ca tathāvidhaḥ  Mn 
itareṣu sasaṃdhyeṣu sasaṃdhyāṃśeṣu ca triṣu 
ekāpāyena vartante sahasrāṇi śatāni ca  Mn 
yad etat parisaṃkhyātam ādāv eva caturyugam 
etad dvādaśasāhasraṃ devānāṃ yugam ucyate  Mn 
daivikānāṃ yugānāṃ tu sahasraṃ parisaṃkhyayā 
brāhmam ekam ahar jñeyaṃ tāvatīṃ rātrim eva ca  Mn 
tad vai yugasahasrāntaṃ brāhmaṃ puṇyam ahar viduḥ 
rātriṃ ca tāvatīm eva te 'horātravido janāḥ  Mn 
tasya so 'harniśasyānte prasuptaḥ pratibudhyate 
pratibuddhaś ca sṛjati manaḥ sadasadātmakam  Mn 
manaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ vikurute codyamānaṃ sisṛkṣayā 
ākāśaṃ jāyate tasmāt tasya śabdaṃ guṇaṃ viduḥ  Mn 
ākāśāt tu vikurvāṇāt sarvagandhavahaḥ śuciḥ 
balavāñ jāyate vāyuḥ sa vai sparśaguṇo mataḥ  Mn

jyotir utpadyate bhāsvat tad rūpaguṇam ucyate  Mn 
jyotiṣaś ca vikurvāṇād āpo rasaguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ 
adbhyo gandhaguṇā bhūmir ity eṣā sṛṣṭir āditaḥ  Mn 
yad prāg dvādaśasāhasram uditaṃ daivikaṃ yugam 
tad ekasaptatiguṇaṃ manvantaram ihocyate  Mn 
manvantarāṇy asaṃkhyāni sargaḥ saṃhāra eva ca 
krīḍann ivaitat kurute parameṣṭhī punaḥ punaḥ  Mn 
catuṣpāt sakalo dharmaḥ satyaṃ caiva kṛte yuge 
nādharmeṇāgamaḥ kaś cin manuṣyān prati vartate  Mn 
itareṣv āgamād dharmaḥ pādaśas tv avaropitaḥ 
caurikānṛtamāyābhir dharmaś cāpaiti pādaśaḥ  Mn 
arogāḥ sarvasiddhārthāś caturvarṣaśatāyuṣaḥ

vedoktam āyur martyānām āśiṣaś caiva karmaṇām 
phalanty anuyugaṃ loke prabhāvaś ca śarīriṇām  Mn

anye kaliyuge nṝṇāṃ yugahrāsānurūpataḥ  Mn

dvāpare yajñam evāhur dānam ekaṃ kalau yuge  Mn

mukhabāhūrupajjānāṃ pṛthakkarmāṇy akalpayat  Mn 
adhyāpanam adhyayanaṃ yajanaṃ yājanaṃ tathā

prajānāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ dānam ijyādhyayanam eva ca 
viṣayeṣv aprasaktiś ca kṣatriyasya samāsataḥ  Mn 
paśūnāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ dānam ijyādhyayanam eva ca 
vaṇikpathaṃ kusīdaṃ ca vaiśyasya kṛṣim eva ca  Mn 
ekam eva tu śūdrasya prabhuḥ karma samādiśat 
eteṣām eva varṇānāṃ śuśrūṣām anasūyayā  Mn 
ūrdhvaṃ nābher medhyataraḥ puruṣaḥ parikīrtitaḥ 
tasmān medhyatamaṃ tv asya mukham uktaṃ svayaṃbhuvā  Mn 
uttamāṅgodbhavāj jyeṣṭhyād brahmaṇaś caiva dhāraṇāt

taṃ hi svayaṃbhūḥ svād āsyāt tapas taptvādito 'sṛjat 
havyakavyābhivāhyāya sarvasyāsya ca guptaye  Mn 
yasyāsyena sadāśnanti havyāni tridivaukasaḥ 
kavyāni caiva pitaraḥ kiṃ bhūtam adhikaṃ tataḥ  Mn

buddhimatsu narāḥ śreṣṭhā nareṣu brāhmaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ  Mn 
brāhmaṇeṣu ca vidvāṃso vidvatsu kṛtabuddhayaḥ 
kṛtabuddhiṣu kartāraḥ kartṛṣu brahmavedinaḥ  Mn

svāyaṃbhuvo manur dhīmān idaṃ śāstram akalpayat  Mn

śiśyebhyaś ca pravaktavyaṃ samyaṅ nānyena kena cit  Mn

manovāggehajair nityaṃ karmadoṣair na lipyate  Mn

idaṃ svastyayanaṃ śreṣṭham idaṃ buddhivivardhanam

asmin dharmo 'khilenokto guṇadoṣau ca karmaṇām

deśadharmāñ jātidharmān kuladharmāṃś ca śāśvatān

sa sarvo 'bhihito vede sarvajñānamayo hi saḥ  Mn

arthakāmeṣv asaktānāṃ dharmajñānaṃ vidhīyate

ubhāv api hi tau dharmau samyag uktau manīṣibhiḥ  Mn 
udite 'nudite caiva samayādhyuṣite tathā 
sarvathā vartate yajña itīyaṃ vaidikī śrutiḥ  Mn 
niṣekādiśmaśānānto mantrair yasyodito vidhiḥ 
tasya śāstre 'dhikāro 'smiñ jñeyo nānyasya kasya cit  Mn 
sarasvatīdṛśadvatyor devanadyor yad antaram 
taṃ devanirmitaṃ deśaṃ brahmāvartaṃ pracakṣate  Mn 
tasmin deśe ya ācāraḥ pāramparyakramāgataḥ 
varṇānāṃ sāntarālānāṃ sa sadācāra ucyate  Mn 
kurukṣetraṃ ca matsyāś ca pañcālāḥ śūrasenakāḥ 
eṣa brahmarṣideśo vai brahmāvartād anantaraḥ  Mn 
etad deśaprasūtasya sakāśād agrajanmanaḥ 
svaṃ svaṃ caritraṃ śikṣeran pṛthivyāṃ sarvamānavāḥ  Mn 
himavadvindhyayor madhyaṃ yat prāg vinaśanād api 
pratyag eva prayāgāc ca madhyadeśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  Mn 
ā samudrāt tu vai pūrvād ā samudrāc ca paścimāt 
tayor evāntaraṃ giryor āryāvartaṃ vidur budhāḥ  Mn 
kṛṣṇasāras tu carati mṛgo yatra svabhāvataḥ 
sa jñeyo yajñiyo deśo mlecchadeśas tv ataḥ paraḥ  Mn 
etāṇ dvijātayo deśān saṃśrayeran prayatnataḥ 
śūdras tu yasmin kasmin vā nivased vṛttikarśitaḥ  Mn 
eṣā dharmasya vo yoniḥ samāsena prakīrtitā 
saṃbhavaś cāsya sarvasya varṇadharmān nibodhata  Mn 
vaidikaiḥ karmabhiḥ puṇyair niṣekādir dvijanmanām 
kāryaḥ śarīrasaṃskāraḥ pāvanaḥ pretya ceha ca  Mn 
gārbhair homair jātakarma cauḍamauñjīnibandhanaiḥ 
baijikaṃ gārbhikaṃ caino dvijānām apamṛjyate  Mn 
svādhyāyena vratair homais traividyenejyayā sutaiḥ 
mahāyajñaiś ca yajñaiś ca brāhmīyaṃ kriyate tanuḥ  Mn 
prāṅ nābhivardhanāt puṃso jātakarma vidhīyate 
mantravat prāśanaṃ cāsya hiraṇyamadhusarpiṣām  Mn 
nāmadheyaṃ daśamyāṃ tu dvādaśyāṃ vāsya kārayet 
puṇye tithau muhūrte vā nakṣatre vā guṇānvite  Mn 
maṅgalyaṃ brāhmaṇasya syāt kṣatriyasya balānvitam 
vaiśyasya dhanasaṃyuktaṃ śūdrasya tu jugupsitam  Mn 
śarmavad brāhmaṇasya syād rājño rakṣāsamanvitam 
vaiśyasya puṣṭisaṃyuktaṃ śūdrasya preṣyasaṃyutam  Mn 
strīṇāṃ sukhodyam akrūraṃ vispaṣṭārthaṃ manoharam 
maṅgalyaṃ dīrghavarṇāntam āśīrvādābhidhānavat  Mn 
caturthe māsi kartavyaṃ śiśor niṣkramaṇaṃ gṛhāt 
ṣaṣṭhe 'nnaprāśanaṃ māsi yad veṣṭaṃ maṅgalaṃ kule  Mn 
cūḍākarma dvijātīnāṃ sarveṣām eva dharmataḥ 
prathame 'bde tṛtīye vā kartavyaṃ śruticodanāt  Mn 
garbhāṣṭame 'bde kurvīta brāhmaṇasyopanāyanam 
garbhād ekādaśe rājño garbhāt tu dvādaśe viśaḥ  Mn 
brahmavarcasakāmasya kāryo viprasya pañcame 
rājño balārthinaḥ ṣaṣṭhe vaiśyasyehārthino 'ṣṭame  Mn 
ā ṣodaśād brāhmaṇasya sāvitrī nātivartate 
ā dvāviṃśāt kṣatrabandhor ā caturviṃśater viśaḥ  Mn 
ata ūrdhvaṃ trayo 'py ete yathākālam asaṃskṛtāḥ 
sāvitrīpatitā vrātyā bhavanty āryavigarhitāḥ  Mn 
naitair apūtair vidhivad āpady api hi karhi cit 
brāhmān yaunāṃś ca saṃbandhān nācared brāhmaṇaḥ saha  Mn 
kārṣṇarauravabāstāni carmāṇi brahmacāriṇaḥ 
vasīrann ānupūrvyeṇa śāṇakṣaumāvikāni ca  Mn 
mauñjī trivṛt samā ślakṣṇā kāryā viprasya mekhalā 
kṣatriyasya tu maurvī jyā vaiśyasya śaṇatāntavī  Mn 
muñjālābhe tu kartavyāḥ kuśāśmantakabalvajaiḥ 
trivṛtā granthinaikena tribhiḥ pañcabhir eva vā  Mn 
kārpāsam upavītaṃ syād viprasyordhvavṛtaṃ trivṛt 
śaṇasūtramayaṃ rājño vaiśyasyāvikasautrikam  Mn 
brāhmaṇo bailvapālāśau kṣatriyo vāṭakhādirau 
pailavāudumbarau vaiśyo daṇḍān arhanti dharmataḥ  Mn 
keśāntiko brāhmaṇasya daṇḍaḥ kāryaḥ pramāṇataḥ 
lalāṭasammito rājñaḥ syāt tu nāsāntiko viśaḥ  Mn 
ṛjavas te tu sarve syur avraṇāḥ saumyadarśanāḥ 
anudvegakarā nṝṇāṃ satvaco 'nagnidūṣitāḥ  Mn 
pratigṛhyepsitaṃ daṇḍam upasthāya ca bhāskaram 
pradakṣiṇaṃ parītyāgniṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ yathāvidhi  Mn 
bhavatpūrvaṃ cared bhaikṣam upanīto dvijottamaḥ 
bhavanmadhyaṃ tu rājanyo vaiśyas tu bhavaduttaram  Mn 
mātaraṃ vā svasāraṃ vā mātur vā bhaginīṃ nijām 
bhikṣeta bhikṣāṃ prathamaṃ yā cainaṃ nāvamānayet  Mn 
samāhṛtya tu tad bhaikṣaṃ yāvadannam amāyayā 
nivedya gurave 'śnīyād ācamya prāṅmukhaḥ śuciḥ  Mn 
āyuṣyaṃ prāṅmukho bhuṅkte yaśasyaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ 
śriyaṃ pratyaṅmukho bhuṅkte ṛtaṃ bhuṅkte hy udaṅmukhaḥ  Mn 
upaspṛśya dvijo nityam annam adyāt samāhitaḥ 
bhuktvā copaspṛśet samyag adbhiḥ khāni ca saṃspṛśet  Mn 
pūjayed aśanaṃ nityam adyāc caitad akutsayan 
dṛṣṭvā hṛṣyet prasīdec ca pratinandec ca sarvaśaḥ  Mn 
pūjitaṃ hy aśanaṃ nityaṃ balam ūrjaṃ ca yacchati 
apūjitaṃ tu tad bhuktam ubhayaṃ nāśayed idam  Mn 
nocchiṣṭaṃ kasya cid dadyān nādyād etat tathāntarā 
na caivātyaśanaṃ kuryān na cocchiṣṭaḥ kva cid vrajet  Mn 
anārogyam anāyuṣyam asvargyaṃ cātibhojanam 
apuṇyaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet  Mn 
brāhmeṇa vipras tīrthena nityakālam upaspṛśet 
kāyatraidaśikābhyāṃ vā na pitryeṇa kadā cana  Mn 
aṅguṣṭhamūlasya tale brāhmaṃ tīrthaṃ pracakṣate 
kāyam aṅgulimūle 'gre devaṃ pitryaṃ tayor adhaḥ  Mn 
trir ācāmed apaḥ pūrvaṃ dviḥ pramṛjyāt tato mukham 
khāni caiva spṛśed adbhir ātmānaṃ śira eva ca  Mn 
anuṣṇābhir aphenābhir adbhis tīrthena dharmavit 
śaucepsuḥ sarvadācāmed ekānte prāgudaṅmukhaḥ  Mn 
hṛdgābhiḥ pūyate vipraḥ kaṇṭhagābhis tu bhūmipaḥ 
vaiśyo 'dbhiḥ prāśitābhis tu śūdraḥ spṛṣṭābhir antataḥ  Mn 
uddhṛte dakṣine pāṇāv upavīty ucyate dvijaḥ 
savye prācīnāvītī nivītī kaṇṭhasajjane  Mn 
mekhalām ajinaṃ daṇḍam upavītaṃ kamaṇḍalum 
apsu prāsya vinaṣṭāni gṛhṇītānyāni mantravat  Mn 
keśāntaḥ ṣoḍaśe varṣe brāhmaṇasya vidhīyate 
rājanyabandhor dvāviṃśe vaiśyasya dvyadhike mataḥ  Mn 
amantrikā tu kāryeyaṃ strīṇām āvṛd aśeṣataḥ 
saṃskārārthaṃ śarīrasya yathākālaṃ yathākramam  Mn 
vaivāhiko vidhiḥ strīṇāṃ saṃskāro vaidikaḥ smṛtaḥ 
patisevā gurau vāso gṛhārtho 'gniparikriyā  Mn 
eṣa prokto dvijātīnām aupanāyaniko vidhiḥ 
utpattivyañjakaḥ puṇyaḥ karmayogaṃ nibodhata  Mn 
upanīya guruḥ śiṣyaṃ śikṣayec chaucam āditaḥ 
ācāram agnikāryaṃ ca saṃdhyopāsanam eva ca  Mn 
adhyeṣyamāṇas tv ācānto yathāśāstram udaṅmukhaḥ 
brahmāñjalikṛto 'dhyāpyo laghuvāsā jitendriyaḥ  Mn 
brahmārambhe 'vasāne ca pādau grāhyau guroḥ sadā 
saṃhatya hastāv adhyeyaṃ sa hi brahmāñjaliḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
vyatyastapāṇinā kāryam upasaṃgrahaṇaṃ guroḥ 
savyena savyaḥ spraṣṭavyo dakṣiṇena ca dakṣiṇaḥ  Mn 
adhyeṣyamāṇaṃ tu gurur nityakālam atandritaḥ 
adhīṣva bho iti brūyād virāmo 'stv iti cāramet  Mn 
brahmanaḥ praṇavaṃ kuryād ādāv ante ca sarvadā 
sravaty anoṃkṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ parastāc ca viśīryati  Mn 
prākkūlān paryupāsīnaḥ pavitraiś caiva pāvitaḥ 
prāṇāyāmais tribhiḥ pūtas tata oṃkāram arhati  Mn 
akāraṃ cāpy ukāraṃ ca makāraṃ ca prajāpatiḥ 
vedatrayān niraduhad bhūr bhuvaḥ svar itīti ca  Mn 
tribhya eva tu vedebhyaḥ pādaṃ pādam adūduhat 
tad ity ṛco 'syāḥ sāvitryāḥ parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ  Mn 
etad akṣaram etāṃ ca japan vyāhṛtipūrvikām 
saṃdhyayor vedavid vipro vedapuṇyena yujyate  Mn 
sahasrakṛtvas tv abhyasya bahir etat trikaṃ dvijaḥ 
mahato 'py enaso māsāt tvacevāhir vimucyate  Mn 
etayā rcā visaṃyuktaḥ kāle ca kriyayā svayā 
brahmakṣatriyaviśyonir garhaṇāṃ yāti sādhuṣu  Mn 
oṃkārapūrvikās tisro mahāvyāhṛtayo 'vyayāḥ 
tripadā caiva sāvitrī vijñeyaṃ brahmaṇo mukham  Mn 
yo 'dhīte 'hany ahany etāṃ trīṇi varṣāṇy atandritaḥ 
sa brahma param abhyeti vāyubhūtaḥ khamūrtimān  Mn 
ekākṣaraṃ paraṃ brahma prāṇāyāmaḥ paraṃ tapaḥ 
sāvitryās tu paraṃ nāsti maunāt satyaṃ viśiṣyate  Mn 
kṣaranti sarvā vaidikyo juhotiyajatikriyāḥ 
akṣaraṃ duṣkaraṃ jñeyaṃ brahma caiva prajāpatiḥ  Mn 
vidhiyajñāj japayajño viśiṣṭo daśabhir guṇaiḥ 
upāṃśuḥ syāc chataguṇaḥ sāhasro mānasaḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
ye pākayajñās catvāro vidhiyajñasamanvitāḥ 
sarve te japayajñasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm  Mn 
japyenaiva tu saṃsidhyed brāhmaṇo nātra saṃśayaḥ 
kuryād anyan na vā kuryān maitro brāhmaṇa ucyate  Mn 
indriyāṇāṃ vicaratāṃ viṣayeṣv apahāriṣu 
saṃyame yatnam ātiṣṭhed vidvān yanteva vājinām  Mn 
ekādaśendriyāṇy āhur yāni pūrve manīṣiṇaḥ 
tāni samyak pravakṣyāmi yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ  Mn 
śrotraṃ tvak cakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā caiva pañcamī 
pāyūpasthaṃ hastapādaṃ vāk caiva daśamī smṛtā  Mn 
buddhīndriyāṇi pañcaiṣāṃ śrotrādīny anupūrvaśaḥ 
karmendriyāṇi pañcaiṣāṃ pāyvādīni pracakṣate  Mn 
ekādaśaṃ mano jñeyaṃ svaguṇenobhayātmakam 
yasmin jite jitāv etau bhavataḥ pañcakau gaṇau  Mn 
indriyāṇāṃ prasaṅgena doṣam ṛcchaty asaṃśayam 
saṃniyamya tu tāny eva tataḥ siddhiṃ nigacchati  Mn 
na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati 
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate  Mn 
yaś caitān prāpnuyāt sarvān yaś caitān kevalāṃs tyajet 
prāpaṇāt sarvakāmānāṃ parityāgo viśiṣyate  Mn 
na tathaitāni śakyante saṃniyantum asevayā 
viṣayeṣu prajuṣṭāni yathā jñānena nityaśaḥ  Mn 
vedās tyāgaś ca yajñāś ca niyamāś ca tapāṃsi ca 
na vipraduṣṭabhāvasya siddhiṃ gacchati karhi cit  Mn 
śrutvā spṛṣṭvā ca dṛṣṭvā ca bhuktvā ghrātvā ca yo naraḥ 
na hṛṣyati glāyati vā sa vijñeyo jitendriyaḥ  Mn 
indriyāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ yady ekaṃ kṣaratīndriyam 
tenāsya kṣarati prajñā dṛteḥ pādād ivodakam  Mn 
vaśe kṛtvendriyagrāmaṃ saṃyamya ca manas tathā 
sarvān saṃsādhayed arthān akṣiṇvan yogatas tanum  Mn 
pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ japāṃs tiṣṭhet sāvitrīm ārkadarśanāt 
paścimāṃ tu samāsīnaḥ samyag ṛkṣavibhāvanāt  Mn 
pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ japaṃs tiṣṭhan naiśam eno vyapohati 
paścimāṃ tu samāsīno malaṃ hanti divākṛtam  Mn 
na tiṣṭhati tu yaḥ pūrvāṃ nopāste yaś ca paścimām 
sa śūdravad bahiṣkāryaḥ sarvasmād dvijakarmaṇaḥ  Mn 
apāṃ samīpe niyato naityakaṃ vidhim āsthitaḥ 
sāvitrīm apy adhīyīta gatvāraṇyaṃ samāhitaḥ  Mn 
vedopakaraṇe caiva svādhyāye caiva naityake 
nānurodho 'sty anadhyāye homamantreṣu caiva hi  Mn 
naityake nāsty anadhyāyo brahmasattraṃ hi tat smṛtam 
brahmāhutihutaṃ puṇyam anadhyāyavaṣaṭkṛtam  Mn 
yaḥ svādhyāyam adhīte 'bdaṃ vidhinā niyataḥ śuciḥ 
tasya nityaṃ kṣaraty eṣa payo dadhi ghṛtaṃ madhu  Mn 
agnīndhanaṃ bhaikṣacaryām adhaḥśayyāṃ guror hitam 
ā samāvartanāt kuryāt kṛtopanayano dvijaḥ  Mn 
ācāryaputraḥ śuśrūṣur jñānado dhārmikaḥ śuciḥ 
āptaḥ śakto 'rthadaḥ sādhuḥ svo 'dhyāpyā daśa dharmataḥ  Mn 
nāpṛṣṭaḥ kasya cid brūyān na cānyāyena pṛcchataḥ 
jānann api hi medhāvī jaḍaval loka ācaret  Mn 
adharmeṇa ca yaḥ prāha yaś cādharmeṇa pṛcchati 
tayor anyataraḥ praiti vidveṣaṃ vādhigacchati  Mn 
dharmārthau yatra na syātāṃ śuśrūṣā vāpi tadvidhā 
tatra vidyā na vaptavyā śubhaṃ bījam ivoṣare  Mn 
vidyayaiva samaṃ kāmaṃ martavyaṃ brahmavādinā 
āpady api hi ghorāyāṃ na tv enām iriṇe vapet  Mn 
vidyā brāhmaṇam etyāha śevadhis te 'smi rakṣa mām 
asūyakāya māṃ mādās tathā syāṃ vīryavattamā  Mn 
yam eva tu śuciṃ vidyān niyatabrahmacāriṇam 
tasmai māṃ brūhi viprāya nidhipāyāpramādine  Mn 
brahma yas tv ananujñātam adhīyānād avāpnuyāt 
sa brahmasteyasaṃyukto narakaṃ pratipadyate  Mn 
laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ vāpi tathādhyātmikam eva vā 
ādadīta yato jñānaṃ taṃ pūrvam abhivādayet  Mn 
sāvitrīmātrasāro 'pi varaṃ vipraḥ suyantritaḥ 
nāyantritas trivedo 'pi sarvāśī sarvavikrayī  Mn 
śayyāsane 'dhyācarite śreyasā na samāviśet 
śayyāsanasthaś caivainaṃ pratyutthāyābhivādayet  Mn 
ūrdhvaṃ prāṇā hy utkrāmanti yūnaḥ sthavira āyati 
pratyutthānābhivādābhyāṃ punas tān pratipadyate  Mn 
abhivādanaśīlasya nityaṃ vṛddhopasevinaḥ 
catvāri tasya vardhante āyur dharmo yaśo balam  Mn 
abhivādāt paraṃ vipro jyāyāṃsam abhivādayan 
asau nāmāham asmīti svaṃ nāma parikīrtayet  Mn 
nāmadheyasya ye ke cid abhivādaṃ na jānate 
tān prājño 'ham iti brūyāt striyaḥ sarvās tathaiva ca  Mn 
bhoḥśabdaṃ kīrtayed ante svasya nāmno 'bhivādane 
nāmnāṃ svarūpabhāvo hi bhobhāva ṛṣibhiḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
āyuṣmān bhava saumyeti vācyo vipro 'bhivādane 
akāraś cāsya nāmno 'nte vācyaḥ pūrvākṣaraḥ plutaḥ  Mn 
yo na vetty abhivādasya vipraḥ pratyabhivādanam 
nābhivādyaḥ sa viduṣā yathā śūdras tathaiva saḥ  Mn 
brāhmaṇaṃ kuśalaṃ pṛcchet kṣatrabandhum anāmayam 
vaiśyaṃ kṣemaṃ samāgamya śūdram ārogyam eva ca  Mn 
avācyo dīkṣito nāmnā yavīyān api yo bhavet 
bhobhavatpūrvakaṃ tv enam abhibhāṣeta dharmavit  Mn 
parapatnī tu yā strī syād asaṃbandhā ca yonitaḥ 
tāṃ brūyād bhavatīty evaṃ subhage bhaginīti ca  Mn 
mātulāṃś ca pitṛvyāṃś ca śvaśurān ṛtvijo gurūn 
asāv aham iti brūyāt pratyutthāya yavīyasaḥ  Mn 
mātṛśvasā mātulānī śvaśrūr atha pitṛśvasā 
saṃpūjyā gurupatnīvat samās tā gurubhāryayā  Mn 
bhrātur bhāryopasaṃgrāhyā savarṇāhany ahany api 
viproṣya tūpasaṃgrāhyā jñātisaṃbandhiyoṣitaḥ  Mn 
pitur bhaginyāṃ mātuś ca jyāyasyāṃ ca svasary api 
mātṛvad vṛttim ātiṣṭhen mātā tābhyo garīyasī  Mn 
daśābdākhyaṃ paurasakhyaṃ pañcābdākhyaṃ kalābhṛtām 
tryabdapūrvaṃ śrotriyāṇāṃ svalpenāpi svayoniṣu  Mn 
brāhmaṇaṃ daśavarṣaṃ tu śatavarṣaṃ tu bhūmipam 
pitāputrau vijānīyād brāhmaṇas tu tayoḥ pitā  Mn 
vittaṃ bandhur vayaḥ karma vidyā bhavati pañcamī 
etāni mānyasthānāni garīyo yad yad uttaram  Mn 
pañcānāṃ triṣu varṇeṣu bhūyāṃsi guṇavanti ca 
yatra syuḥ so 'tra mānārhaḥ śūdro 'pi daśamīṃ gataḥ  Mn 
cakriṇo daśamīsthasya rogiṇo bhāriṇaḥ striyāḥ 
snātakasya ca rājñaś ca panthā deyo varasya ca  Mn 
teṣāṃ tu samāvetānāṃ mānyau snātakapārthivau 
rājasnātakayoś caiva snātako nṛpamānabhāk  Mn 
upanīya tu yaḥ śiṣyaṃ vedam adhyāpayed dvijaḥ 
sakalpaṃ sarahasyaṃ ca tam ācāryaṃ pracakṣate  Mn 
ekadeśaṃ tu vedasya vedāṅgāny api vā punaḥ 
yo 'dhyāpayati vṛttyartham upādhyāyaḥ sa ucyate  Mn 
niṣekādīni karmāṇi yaḥ karoti yathāvidhi 
saṃbhāvayati cānnena sa vipro gurur ucyate  Mn 
agnyādheyaṃ pākayajñān agniṣṭomādikān makhān 
yaḥ karoti vṛto yasya sa tasya rtvig ihocyate  Mn 
ya āvṛṇoty avitathaṃ brahmaṇā śravaṇāv ubhau 
sa mātā sa pitā jñeyas taṃ na druhyet kadā cana  Mn 
upādhyāyān daśācārya ācāryāṇāṃ śataṃ pitā 
sahasraṃ tu pitṝn mātā gauraveṇātiricyate  Mn 
utpādakabrahmadātror garīyān brahmadaḥ pitā 
brahmajanma hi viprasya pretya ceha ca śāśvatam  Mn 
kāmān mātā pitā cainaṃ yad utpādayato mithaḥ 
saṃbhūtiṃ tasya tāṃ vidyād yad yonāv abhijāyate  Mn 
ācāryas tv asya yāṃ jātiṃ vidhivad vedapāragaḥ 
utpādayati sāvitryā sā satyā sājarāmarā  Mn 
alpaṃ vā bahu vā yasya śrutasyopakaroti yaḥ 
tam apīha guruṃ vidyāc chrutopakriyayā tayā  Mn 
brāhmasya janmanaḥ kartā svadharmasya ca śāsitā 
bālo 'pi vipro vṛddhasya pitā bhavati dharmataḥ  Mn 
adhyāpayām āsa pitṝn śiśur āṅgirasaḥ kaviḥ 
putrakā iti hovāca jñānena parigṛhya tān  Mn 
te tam artham apṛcchanta devān āgatamanyavaḥ 
devāś caitān sametyocur nyāyyaṃ vaḥ śiśur uktavān  Mn 
ajño bhavati vai bālaḥ pitā bhavati mantradaḥ 
ajñaṃ hi bālam ity āhuḥ pitety eva tu mantradam  Mn 
na hāyanair na palitair na vittena na bandhubhiḥ 
ṛṣayaś cakrire dharmaṃ yo 'nūcānaḥ sa no mahān  Mn 
viprāṇāṃ jñānato jyaiṣṭhyaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ tu vīryataḥ 
vaiśyānāṃ dhānyadhanataḥ śūdrāṇām eva janmataḥ  Mn 
na tena vṛddho bhavati yenāsya palitaṃ śiraḥ 
yo vai yuvāpy adhīyānas taṃ devāḥ sthaviraṃ viduḥ  Mn 
yathā kāṣṭhamayo hastī yathā carmamayo mṛgaḥ 
yaś ca vipro 'nadhīyānas trayas te nāma bibhrati  Mn 
yathā ṣaṇḍho 'phalaḥ strīṣu yathā gaur gavi cāphalā 
yathā cājñe 'phalaṃ dānaṃ tathā vipro 'nṛco 'phalaḥ  Mn 
ahiṃsayaiva bhūtānāṃ kāryaṃ śreyo 'nuśāsanam 
vāk caiva madhurā ślakṣṇā prayojyā dharmam icchatā  Mn 
yasya vāṅganasī śuddhe samyaggupte ca sarvadā 
sa vai sarvam avāpnoti vedāntopagataṃ phalam  Mn 
nāruṃtudaḥ syād ārto 'pi na paradrohakarmadhīḥ 
yayāsyodvijate vācā nālokyāṃ tām udīrayet  Mn 
sammānād brāhmaṇo nityam udvijeta viṣād iva 
amṛtasyeva cākāṅkṣed avamānasya sarvadā  Mn 
sukhaṃ hy avamataḥ śete sukhaṃ ca pratibudhyate 
sukhaṃ carati loke 'sminn avamantā vinaśyati  Mn 
anena kramayogena saṃskṛtātmā dvijaḥ śanaiḥ 
gurau vasan sañcinuyād brahmādhigamikaṃ tapaḥ  Mn 
tapoviśeṣair vividhair vrataiś ca vidhicoditaiḥ 
vedaḥ kṛtsno 'dhigantavyaḥ sarahasyo dvijanmanā  Mn 
vedam eva sadābhyasyet tapas tapsyan dvijottamaḥ 
vedābhyāso hi viprasya tapaḥ param ihocyate  Mn 
ā haiva sa nakhāgrebhyaḥ paramaṃ tapyate tapaḥ 
yaḥ sragvy api dvijo 'dhīte svādhyāyaṃ śaktito 'nvaham  Mn 
yo 'nadhītya dvijo vedam anyatra kurute śramam 
sa jīvann eva śūdratvam āśu gacchati sānvayaḥ  Mn 
mātur agre 'dhijananaṃ dvitīyaṃ mauñjibandhane 
tṛtīyaṃ yajñadīkṣāyāṃ dvijasya śruticodanāt  Mn 
tatra yad brahmajanmāsya mauñjībandhanacihnitam 
tatrāsya mātā sāvitrī pitā tv ācārya ucyate  Mn 
vedapradānād ācāryaṃ pitaraṃ paricakṣate 
na hy asmin yujyate karma kiñ cid ā mauñjibandhanāt  Mn 
nābhivyāhārayed brahma svadhāninayanād ṛte 
śūdreṇa hi samas tāvad yāvad vede na jāyate  Mn 
kṛtopanayanasyāsya vratādeśanam iṣyate 
brahmaṇo grahaṇaṃ caiva krameṇa vidhipūrvakam  Mn 
yady asya vihitaṃ carma yat sūtraṃ yā ca mekhalā 
yo daṇḍo yac ca vasanaṃ tat tad asya vrateṣv api  Mn 
sevetemāṃs tu niyamān brahmacārī gurau vasan 
sanniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ tapovṛddhyartham ātmanaḥ  Mn 
nityaṃ snātvā śuciḥ kuryād devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam 
devatābhyarcanaṃ caiva samidādhānam eva ca  Mn 
varjayen madhu māṃsaṃ ca gandhaṃ mālyaṃ rasān striyaḥ 
śuktāni yāni sarvāṇi prāṇināṃ caiva hiṃsanam  Mn 
abhyaṅgam añjanaṃ cākṣṇor upānacchatradhāraṇam 
kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca nartanaṃ gītavādanam  Mn 
dyūtaṃ ca janavādaṃ ca parivādaṃ tathānṛtam 
strīṇāṃ ca prekṣaṇālambham upaghātaṃ parasya ca  Mn 
ekaḥ śayīta sarvatra na retaḥ skandayet kva cit 
kāmād dhi skandayan reto hinasti vratam ātmanaḥ  Mn 
svapne siktvā brahmacārī dvijaḥ śukram akāmataḥ 
snātvārkam arcayitvā triḥ punar mām ity ṛcaṃ japet  Mn 
udakumbhaṃ sumanaso gośakṛnmṛttikākuśān 
āhared yāvad arthāni bhaikṣaṃ cāharahaś caret  Mn 
vedayajñair ahīnānāṃ praśastānāṃ svakarmasu 
brahmacāry āhared bhaikṣaṃ gṛhebhyaḥ prayato 'nvaham  Mn 
guroḥ kule na bhikṣeta na jñātikulabandhuṣu 
alābhe tv anyagehānāṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ vivarjayet  Mn 
sarvaṃ vāpi cared grāmaṃ pūrvoktānām asaṃbhave 
niyamya prayato vācam abhiśastāṃs tu varjayet  Mn 
dūrād āhṛtya samidhaḥ sannidadhyād vihāyasi 
sāyaM prātaś ca juhuyāt tābhir agnim atandritaḥ  Mn 
akṛtvā bhaikṣacaraṇam asamidhya ca pāvakaṃ 
anāturaḥ saptarātram avakīrṇivrataṃ caret  Mn 
bhaikṣeṇa vartayen nityaṃ naikānnādī bhaved vratī 
bhaikṣeṇa vratino vṛttir upavāsasamā smṛtā  Mn 
vratavad devadaivatye pitrye karmaṇy atha rṣivat 
kāmam abhyarthito 'śnīyād vratam asya na lupyate  Mn 
brāhmaṇasyaiva karmaitad upadiṣṭaṃ manīṣibhiḥ 
rājanyavaiśyayos tv evaṃ naitat karma vidhīyate  Mn 
codito guruṇā nityam apracodita eva vā 
kuryād adhyayane yatnam ācāryasya hiteṣu ca  Mn 
śarīraṃ caiva vācaṃ ca buddhīndriyamanāṃsi ca 
niyamya prāñjalis tiṣṭhed vīkṣamāṇo guror mukham  Mn 
nityam uddhṛtapāṇiḥ syāt sādhvācāraḥ susaṃvṛtaḥ 
āsyatām iti coktaḥ sann āsītābhimukhaṃ guroḥ  Mn 
hīnānnavastraveṣaḥ syāt sarvadā gurusannidhau 
uttiṣṭhet prathamaṃ cāsya caramaṃ caiva saṃviśet  Mn 
pratiśrāvaṇasaṃbhāṣe śayāno na samācaret 
nāsīno na ca bhuñjāno na tiṣṭhan na parāṅmukhaḥ  Mn 
āsīnasya sthitaḥ kuryād abhigacchaṃs tu tiṣṭhataḥ 
pratyudgamya tv āvrajataḥ paścād dhāvaṃs tu dhāvataḥ  Mn 
parāṅmukhasyābhimukho dūrasthasyaitya cāntikam 
praṇamya tu śayānasya nideśe caiva tiṣṭhataḥ  Mn 
nīcaṃ śayyāsanaṃ cāsya nityaṃ syād gurusannidhau 
guros tu cakṣurviṣaye na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet  Mn 
nodāhared asya nāma parokṣam api kevalam 
na caivāsyānukurvīta gatibhāṣitaceṣṭitam  Mn 
guror yatra parivādo nindā vāpi pravartate 
karṇau tatra pidhātavyau gantavyaṃ vā tato 'nyataḥ  Mn 
parīvādāt kharo bhavati śvā vai bhavati nindakaḥ 
paribhoktā kṛmir bhavati kīṭo bhavati matsarī  Mn 
dūrastho nārcayed enaṃ na kruddho nāntike striyāḥ 
yānāsanasthaś caivainam avaruhyābhivādayet  Mn 
prativāte 'nuvāte ca nāsīta guruṇā saha 
asaṃśrave caiva guror na kiṃ cid api kīrtayet  Mn 
go'śvoṣṭrayānaprāsāda prastareṣu kaṭeṣu ca 
āsīta guruṇā sārdhaṃ śilāphalakanauṣu ca  Mn 
guror gurau sannihite guruvad vṛttim ācaret 
na cānisṛṣṭo guruṇā svān gurūn abhivādayet  Mn 
vidyāguruṣv evam eva nityā vṛttiḥ svayoniṣu 
pratiṣedhatsu cādharmād dhitaṃ copadiśatsv api  Mn 
śreyaḥsu guruvad vṛttiṃ nityam eva samācaret 
guruputreṣu cāryeṣu guroś caiva svabandhuṣu  Mn 
bālaḥ samānajanmā vā śiṣyo vā yajñakarmaṇi 
adhyāpayan gurusuto guruvan mānam arhati  Mn 
utsādanaṃ ca gātrāṇāṃ snāpanocchiṣṭabhojane 
na kuryād guruputrasya pādayoś cāvanejanam  Mn 
guruvat pratipūjyāḥ syuḥ savarṇā guruyoṣitaḥ 
asavarṇās tu sampūjyāḥ pratyutthānābhivādanaiḥ  Mn 
abhyañjanaṃ snāpanaṃ ca gātrotsādanam eva ca 
gurupatnyā na kāryāṇi keśānāṃ ca prasādhanam  Mn 
gurupatnī tu yuvatir nābhivādyeha pādayoḥ 
pūrṇaviṃśativarṣeṇa guṇadoṣau vijānatā  Mn 
svabhāva eṣa nārīṇāṃ narāṇām iha dūṣaṇam 
ato 'rthān na pramādyanti pramadāsu vipaścitaḥ  Mn 
avidvāṃsam alaṃ loke vidvāṃsam api vā punaḥ 
pramadā hy utpathaṃ netuṃ kāmakrodhavaśānugam  Mn 
mātrā svasrā duhitrā vā na viviktāsano bhavet 
balavān indriyagrāmo vidvāṃsam api karṣati  Mn 
kāmaṃ tu gurupatnīnāṃ yuvatīnāṃ yuvā bhuvi 
vidhivad vandanaṃ kuryād asāv aham iti bruvan  Mn 
viproṣya pādagrahaṇam anvahaṃ cābhivādanam 
gurudāreṣu kurvīta satāṃ dharmam anusmaran  Mn 
yathā khanan khanitreṇa naro vāry adhigacchati 
tathā gurugatāṃ vidyāṃ śuśrūṣur adhigacchati  Mn 
muṇḍo vā jaṭilo vā syād atha vā syāc chikhājaṭaḥ 
nainaṃ grāme 'bhinimlocet sūryo nābhyudiyāt kva cit  Mn 
taṃ ced abhyudiyāt sūryaḥ śayānaṃ kāmacārataḥ 
nimloced vāpy avijñānāj japann upavased dinam  Mn 
sūryeṇa hy abhinirmuktaḥ śayāno 'bhyuditaś ca yaḥ 
prāyaścittam akurvāṇo yuktaḥ syān mahatainasā  Mn 
ācamya prayato nityam ubhe saṃdhye samāhitaḥ 
śucau deśe japañ japyam upāsīta yathāvidhi  Mn 
yadi strī yady avarajaḥ śreyaḥ kiṃ cit samācaret 
tat sarvam ācared yukto yatra cāsya ramen manaḥ  Mn 
dharmārthāv ucyate śreyaḥ kāmārthau dharma eva ca 
artha eveha vā śreyas trivarga iti tu sthitiḥ  Mn 
ācāryaś ca pitā caiva mātā bhrātā ca pūrvajaḥ 
nārtenāpy avamantavyā brāhmaṇena viśeṣataḥ  Mn 
ācāryo brahmaṇo mūrtiḥ pitā mūrtiḥ prajāpateḥ 
mātā pṛthivyā mūrtis tu bhrātā svo mūrtir ātmanaḥ  Mn 
yaṃ mātāpitarau kleśaṃ sahete saṃbhave nṛṇām 
na tasya niṣkṛtiḥ śakyā kartuṃ varṣaśatair api  Mn 
tayor nityaṃ priyaṃ kuryād ācāryasya ca sarvadā 
teṣv eva triṣu tuṣṭeṣu tapaḥ sarvaṃ samāpyate  Mn 
teṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ śuśrūṣā paramaṃ tapa ucyate 
na tair anabhyanujñāto dharmam anyaṃ samācaret  Mn 
ta eva hi trayo lokās ta eva traya āśramāḥ 
ta eva hi trayo vedās ta evoktās trayo 'gnayaḥ  Mn 
pitā vai gārhapatyo 'gnir mātāgnir dakṣiṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
gurur āhavanīyas tu sāgnitretā garīyasī  Mn 
triṣv apramādyann eteṣu trīn lokān vijayed gṛhī 
dīpyamānaḥ svavapuṣā devavad divi modate  Mn 
imaṃ lokaṃ mātṛbhaktyā pitṛbhaktyā tu madhyamam 
guruśuśrūṣayā tv evaṃ brahmalokaṃ samaśnute  Mn 
sarve tasyādṛtā dharmā yasyaite traya ādṛtāḥ 
anādṛtās tu yasyaite sarvās tasyāphalāḥ kriyāḥ  Mn 
yāvat trayas te jīveyus tāvan nānyaṃ samācaret 
teṣv eva nityaṃ śuśrūṣāṃ kuryāt priyahite rataḥ  Mn 
teṣām anuparodhena pāratryaṃ yad yad ācaret 
tat tan nivedayet tebhyo manovacanakarmabhiḥ  Mn 
triṣv eteṣv itikṛtyaṃ hi puruṣasya samāpyate 
eṣa dharmaḥ paraḥ sākṣād upadharmo 'nya ucyate  Mn 
śraddadhānaḥ śubhāṃ vidyām ādadītāvarād api 
anyād api paraṃ dharmaṃ strīratnaṃ duṣkulād api  Mn 
viṣād apy amṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ bālād api subhāṣitam 
amitrād api sadvṛttam amedhyād api kāñcanam  Mn 
striyo ratnāny atho vidyā dharmaḥ śaucaṃ subhāṣitam 
vividhāni ca śīlpāni samādeyāni sarvataḥ  Mn 
abrāhmaṇād adhyāyanam āpatkāle vidhīyate 
anuvrajyā ca śuśrūṣā yāvad adhyāyanaṃ guroḥ  Mn 
nābrāhmaṇe gurau śiṣyo vāsam ātyantikaṃ vaset 
brāhmaṇe vānanūcāne kāṅkṣan gatim anuttamām  Mn 
yadi tv ātyantikaṃ vāsaṃ rocayeta guroḥ kule 
yuktaḥ paricared enam ā śarīravimokṣaṇāt  Mn 
ā samāpteḥ śarīrasya yas tu śuśrūṣate gurum 
sa gacchaty añjasā vipro brahmaṇaḥ sadma śāśvatam  Mn 
na pūrvaṃ gurave kiṃ cid upakurvīta dharmavit 
snāsyaṃs tu guruṇājñaptaḥ śaktyā gurvartham āharet  Mn 
kṣetraṃ hiraṇyaṃ gām aśvaṃ chatropānaham āsanam 
dhānyaṃ śākaṃ ca vāsāṃsi gurave prītim āvahet  Mn 
ācārye tu khalu prete guruputre guṇānvite 
gurudāre sapiṇḍe vā guruvad vṛttim ācaret  Mn 
eteṣv avidyamāneṣu sthānāsanavihāravān 
prayuñjāno 'gniśuśrūṣāṃ sādhayed deham ātmanaḥ  Mn 
evaṃ carati yo vipro brahmacaryam aviplutaḥ 
sa gacchaty uttamasthānaṃ na ceha jāyate punaḥ  Mn 
ṣaṭtriṃśadābdikaṃ caryaṃ gurau traivedikaṃ vratam 
tadardhikaṃ pādikaṃ vā grahaṇāntikam eva vā  Mn 
vedān adhītya vedau vā vedaṃ vāpi yathākramam 
aviplutabrahmacaryo gṛhasthāśramam āvaset  Mn 
taṃ pratītaṃ svadharmeṇa brahmadāyaharaṃ pituḥ 
sragviṇaṃ talpa āsīnam arhayet prathamaṃ gavā  Mn 
guruṇānumataḥ snātvā samāvṛtto yathāvidhi 
udvaheta dvijo bhāryāṃ savarṇāṃ lakṣaṇānvitām  Mn 
asapiṇḍā ca yā mātur asagotrā ca yā pituḥ 
sā praśastā dvijātīnāṃ dārakarmaṇi maithune  Mn 
mahānty api samṛddhāni go'jāvidhanadhānyataḥ 
strīsaṃbandhe daśaitāni kulāni parivarjayet  Mn 
hīnakriyaṃ niṣpuruṣaṃ niśchando romaśārśasam 
kṣayāmayāvyapasmāri śvitrikuṣṭhikulāni ca  Mn 
nodvahet kapilāṃ kanyāṃ nādhikāṅgīṃ na rogiṇīm 
nālomikāṃ nātilomāṃ na vācāṭāṃ na piṅgalām  Mn 
na rkṣavṛkṣanadīnāmnīṃ nāntyaparvatanāmikām 
na pakṣyahipreṣyanāmnīṃ na ca bhīṣananāmikām  Mn 
avyaṅgāṅgīṃ saumyanāmnīṃ haṃsavāraṇagāminīm 
tanulomakeśadaśanāṃ mṛdvaṅgīm udvahet striyam  Mn 
yasyās tu na bhaved bhrātā na vijñāyeta vā pitā 
nopayaccheta tāṃ prājñaḥ putrikādharmaśaṅkayā  Mn 
savarṇāgre dvijātīnāṃ praśastā dārakarmaṇi 
kāmatas tu pravṛttānām imāḥ syuḥ kramaśo 'varāḥ  Mn 
śūdraiva bhāryā śūdrasya sā ca svā ca viśaḥ smṛte 
te ca svā caiva rājñaś ca tāś ca svā cāgrajanmanaḥ  Mn 
na brāhmaṇakṣatriyayor āpady api hi tiṣṭhatoḥ 
kasmiṃś cid api vṛttānte śūdrā bhāryopadiśyate  Mn 
hīnajātistriyaṃ mohād udvahanto dvijātayaḥ 
kulāny eva nayanty āśu sasantānāni śūdratām  Mn 
śūdrāvedī pataty atrer utathyatanayasya ca 
śaunakasya sutotpattyā tadapatyatayā bhṛgoḥ  Mn 
śūdrāṃ śayanam āropya brāhmaṇo yāty adhogatim 
janayitvā sutaṃ tasyāṃ brāhmaṇyād eva hīyate  Mn 
daivapitryātitheyāni tatpradhānāni yasya tu 
nāśnanti pitṛdevās tan na ca svargaṃ sa gacchati  Mn 
vṛṣalīphenapītasya niḥśvāsopahatasya ca 
tasyāṃ caiva prasūtasya niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate  Mn 
caturṇām api varṇānaṃ pretya ceha hitāhitān 
aṣṭāv imān samāsena strīvivāhān nibodhata  Mn 
brāhmo daivas tathaivārṣaḥ prājāpatyas tathāsuraḥ 
gāndharvo rākṣasaś caiva paiśācaś cāṣṭamo 'dhamaḥ  Mn 
yo yasya dharmyo varṇasya guṇadoṣau ca yasya yau 
tad vaḥ sarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi prasave ca guṇāguṇān  Mn 
ṣaḍ ānupūrvyā viprasya kṣatrasya caturo 'varān 
viṭśūdrayos tu tān eva vidyād dharmyān arākṣasān  Mn 
caturo brāhmaṇasyādyān praśastān kavayo viduḥ 
rākṣasaṃ kṣatriyasyaikam āsuraṃ vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ  Mn 
pañcānāṃ tu trayo dharmyā dvāv adharmyau smṛtāv iha 
paiśācaś cāsuraś caiva na kartavyau kadā cana  Mn 
pṛthak pṛthag vā miśrau vā vivāhau pūrvacoditau 
gāndharvo rākṣasaś caiva dharmyau kṣatrasya tau smṛtau  Mn 
ācchādya cārcayitvā ca śrutaśīlavate svayam 
āhūya dānaṃ kanyāyā brāhmo dharmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  Mn 
yajñe tu vitate samyag ṛtvije karma kurvate 
alaṅkṛtya sutādānaṃ daivaṃ dharmaṃ pracakṣate  Mn 
ekaṃ gomithunaṃ dve vā varād ādāya dharmataḥ 
kanyāpradānaṃ vidhivad ārṣo dharmaḥ sa ucyate  Mn 
sahobhau caratāṃ dharmam iti vācānubhāṣya ca 
kanyāpradānam abhyarcya prājāpatyo vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
jñātibhyo draviṇaṃ dattvā kanyāyai caiva śaktitaḥ 
kanyāpradānaṃ svācchandyād āsuro dharma ucyate  Mn 
icchayānyonyasaṃyogaḥ kanyāyāś ca varasya ca 
gāndharvaḥ sa tu vijñeyo maithunyaḥ kāmasaṃbhavaḥ  Mn 
hatvā chittvā ca bhittvā ca krośantīṃ rudantīṃ gṛhāt 
prasahya kanyāharaṇaṃ rākṣaso vidhir ucyate  Mn 
suptāṃ mattāṃ pramattāṃ vā raho yatropagacchati 
sa pāpiṣṭho vivāhānāṃ paiśācaś cāṣṭamo 'dhamaḥ  Mn 
adbhir eva dvijāgryāṇāṃ kanyādānaṃ viśiṣyate 
itareṣāṃ tu varṇānām itaretarakāmyayā  Mn 
yo yasyaiṣāṃ vivāhānāṃ manunā kīrtito guṇaḥ 
sarvaṃ śṛṇuta taṃ viprāḥ sarvaṃ kīrtayato mama  Mn 
daśa pūrvān parān vaṃśyān ātmānaṃ caikaviṃśakam 
brāhmīputraḥ sukṛtakṛn mocayaty enasaḥ pitṝn  Mn 
daivoḍhājaḥ sutaś caiva sapta sapta parāvarān 
ārṣoḍhājaḥ sutas trīṃs trīn ṣaṭ ṣaṭ kāyoḍhajaḥ sutaḥ  Mn 
brāhmādiṣu vivāheṣu caturṣv evānupūrvaśaḥ 
brahmavarcasvinaḥ putrā jāyante śiṣṭasammatāḥ  Mn 
rūpasattvaguṇopetā dhanavanto yaśasvinaḥ 
paryāptabhogā dharmiṣṭhā jīvanti ca śataṃ samāḥ  Mn 
itareṣu tu śiṣṭeṣu nṛśaṃsānṛtavādinaḥ 
jāyante durvivāheṣu brahmadharmadviṣaḥ sutāḥ  Mn 
aninditaiḥ strīvivāhair anindyā bhavati prajā 
ninditair ninditā nṝṇāṃ tasmān nindyān vivarjayet  Mn 
pāṇigrahaṇasaṃskāraḥ savarṇāsūpadiśyate 
asavarṇāsv ayaṃ jñeyo vidhir udvāhakarmaṇi  Mn 
śaraḥ kṣatriyayā grāhyaḥ pratodo vaiśyakanyayā 
vasanasya daśā grāhyā śūdrayotkṛṣṭavedane  Mn 
ṛtukālābhigāmī syāt svadāranirataḥ sadā 
parvavarjaṃ vrajec caināṃ tadvrato ratikāmyayā  Mn 
ṛtuḥ svābhāvikaḥ strīṇāṃ rātrayaḥ ṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ 
caturbhir itaraiḥ sārdham ahobhiḥ sadvigarhitaiḥ  Mn 
tāsām ādyāś catasras tu ninditaikādaśī ca yā 
trayodaśī ca śeṣās tu praśastā daśarātrayaḥ  Mn 
yugmāsu putrā jāyante striyo 'yugmāsu rātriṣu 
tasmād yugmāsu putrārthī saṃviśed ārtave striyam  Mn 
pumān puṃso 'dhike śukre strī bhavaty adhike striyāḥ 
same 'pumān puṃ striyau vā kṣīṇe 'lpe ca viparyayaḥ  Mn 
nindyāsv aṣṭāsu cānyāsu striyo rātriṣu varjayan 
brahmacāry eva bhavati yatra tatrāśrame vasan  Mn 
na kanyāyāḥ pitā vidvān gṛhṇīyāc chulkam aṇv api 
gṛhṇañ śulkaṃ hi lobhena syān naro 'patyavikrayī  Mn 
strīdhanāni tu ye mohād upajīvanti bāndhavāḥ 
nārī yānāni vastraṃ vā te pāpā yānty adhogatim  Mn 
ārṣe gomithunaṃ śulkaṃ ke cid āhur mṛṣaiva tat 
alpo 'py evaṃ mahān vāpi vikrayas tāvad eva saḥ  Mn 
yāsāṃ nādadate śulkaṃ jñātayo na sa vikrayaḥ 
arhaṇaṃ tat kumārīṇām ānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca kevalam  Mn 
pitṛbhir bhrātṛbhiś caitāḥ patibhir devarais tathā 
pūjyā bhūṣayitavyāś ca bahukalyāṇam īpsubhiḥ  Mn 
yatra nāryas tu pūjyante ramante tatra devatāḥ 
yatraitās tu na pūjyante sarvās tatrāphalāḥ kriyāḥ  Mn 
śocanti jāmayo yatra vinaśyaty āśu tat kulam 
na śocanti tu yatraitā vardhate tad dhi sarvadā  Mn 
jāmayo yāni gehāni śapanty apratipūjitāḥ 
tāni kṛtyāhatānīva vinaśyanti samantataḥ  Mn 
tasmād etāḥ sadā pūjyā bhūṣaṇācchādanāśanaiḥ 
bhūtikāmair narair nityaṃ satkareṣūtsaveṣu ca  Mn 
saṃtuṣṭo bhāryayā bhartā bhartrā bhāryā tathaiva ca 
yasminn eva kule nityaṃ kalyāṇaṃ tatra vai dhruvam  Mn 
yadi hi strī na roceta pumāṃsaṃ na pramodayet 
apramodāt punaḥ puṃsaḥ prajanaṃ na pravartate  Mn 
striyāṃ tu rocamānāyāṃ sarvaṃ tad rocate kulaṃ 
tasyāṃ tv arocamānāyāṃ sarvam eva na rocate  Mn 
kuvivāhaiḥ kriyālopair vedānadhyayanena ca 
kulāny akulatāṃ yānti brāhmaṇātikrameṇa ca  Mn 
śilpena vyavahāreṇa śūdrāpatyaiś ca kevalaiḥ 
gobhir aśvaiś ca yānaiś ca kṛṣyā rājopasevayā  Mn 
ayājyayājanaiś caiva nāstikyena ca karmaṇām 
kulāny āśu vinaśyanti yāni hīnāni mantrataḥ  Mn 
mantratas tu samṛddhāni kulāny alpadhanāny api 
kulasaṃkhyāṃ ca gacchanti karṣanti ca mahad yaśaḥ  Mn 
vaivāhike 'gnau kurvīta gṛhyaṃ karma yathāvidhi 
pañcayajñavidhānaṃ ca paktiṃ cānvāhikīṃ gṛhī  MnM 
pañca sūnā gṛhasthasya cullī peṣaṇy upaskaraḥ 
kaṇḍanī codakumbhaś ca badhyate yās tu vāhayan  MnM 
tāsāṃ krameṇa sarvāsāṃ niṣkṛtyarthaṃ maharṣibhiḥ 
pañca kḷptā mahāyajñāḥ pratyahaṃ gṛhamedhinām  MnM 
adhyāpanaṃ brahmayajñaḥ pitṛyajñas tu tarpaṇam 
homo daivo balir bhauto nṛyajño 'tithipūjanam  MnM 
pañcaitān yo mahāayajñān na hāpayati śaktitaḥ 
sa gṛhe 'pi vasan nityaṃ sūnādoṣair na lipyate  MnM 
devatātithibhṛtyānāṃ pitṝṇām ātmanaś ca yaḥ 
na nirvapati pañcānām ucchvasan na sa jīvati  MnM 
ahutaṃ ca hutaṃ caiva tathā prahutam eva ca 
brāhmyaṃ hutaṃ prāśitaṃ ca pañcayajñān pracakṣate  MnM 
japo 'huto huto homaḥ prahuto bhautiko baliḥ 
brāhmyaṃ hutaṃ dvijāgryārcā prāśitaṃ pitṛtarpaṇam  MnM 
svādhyāye nityayuktaḥ syād daive caiveha karmaṇi 
daivakarmaṇi yukto hi bibhartīdaṃ carācaram  MnM 
agnau prāstāhutiḥ samyag ādityam upatiṣṭhate 
ādityāj jāyate vṛṣṭir vṛṣṭer annaṃ tataḥ prajāḥ  MnM 
yathā vāyuṃ samāśritya vartante sarvajantavaḥ 
tathā gṛhastham āśritya vartante sarva āśramāḥ  MnM 
yasmāt trayo 'py āśramiṇo jñānenānnena cānvaham 
gṛhasthenaiva dhāryante tasmāj jyeṣṭhāśramo gṛhī  MnM 
sa saṃdhāryaḥ prayatnena svargam akṣayam icchatā 
sukhaṃ cehecchatātyantaṃ yo 'dhāryo durbalendriyaiḥ  MnM 
ṛṣayaḥ pitaro devā bhūtāny atithayas tathā 
āśāsate kuṭumbibhyas tebhyaḥ kāryaṃ vijānatā  MnM 
svādhyāyenārcayeta rṣīn homair devān yathāvidhi 
pitṝñ śrāddhaiś ca nṝn annair bhūtāni balikarmaṇā  MnM 
kuryād aharahaḥ śrāddham annādyenodakena vā 
payomūlaphalair vāpi pitṛbhyaḥ prītim āvahan  MnM 
ekam apy āśayed vipraṃ pitrarthe pāñcayajñike 
na caivātrāśayet kiṃ cid vaiśvadevaṃ prati dvijam  MnM 
vaiśvadevasya siddhasya gṛhye 'gnau vidhipūrvakam 
ābhyaḥ kuryād devatābhyo brāhmaṇo homam anvaham  MnM 
agneḥ somasya caivādau tayoś caiva samastayoḥ 
viśvebhyaś caiva devebhyo dhanvantaraya eva ca  MnM 
kuhvai caivānumatyai ca prajāpataya eva ca 
saha dyāvāpṛthivyoś ca tathā sviṣṭakṛte 'ntataḥ  MnM 
evaṃ samyagg havir hutvā sarvadikṣu pradakṣiṇam 
indrāntakāppatīndubhyaḥ sānugebhyo baliṃ haret  MnM 
marudbhya iti tu dvāri kṣiped apsv adbhya ity api 
vanaspatibhya ity evaṃ musalolūkhale haret  MnM 
ucchīrṣake śriyai kuryād bhadrakālyai ca pādataḥ 
brahmavāstoṣpatibhyāṃ tu vāstumadhye baliṃ haret  MnM 
viśvebhyaś caiva devebhyo balim ākāśa utkṣipet 
divācarebhyo bhūtebhyo naktaṃcāribhya eva ca  MnM 
pṛṣṭhavāstuni kurvīta baliṃ sarvātmabhūtaye 
pitṛbhyo baliśeṣaṃ tu sarvaṃ dakṣiṇato haret  MnM 
śūnāṃ ca patitānāṃ ca śvapacāṃ pāparogiṇām 
vayasānāṃ kṛmīṇāṃ ca śanakair nirvaped bhuvi  MnM 
evaṃ yaḥ sarvabhūtāni brāhmaṇo nityam arcati 
sa gacchati paraṃ sthānaṃ tejomūrtiḥ pathā rjunā  MnM 
kṛtvaitad balikarmaivam atithiṃ pūrvam āśayet 
bhikṣāṃ ca bhikṣave dadyād vidhivad brahmacāriṇe  MnM 
yat puṇyaphalam āpnoti gāṃ dattvā vidhivad guroḥ 
tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti bhikṣāṃ dattvā dvijo gṛhī  MnM 
bhikṣām apy udapātraṃ vā satkṛtya vidhipūrvakam 
vedatattvārthaviduṣe brāhmaṇāyopapādayet  MnM 
naśyanti havyakavyāni narāṇām avijānatām 
bhasmībhūteṣu vipreṣu mohād dattāni dātṛbhiḥ  MnM 
vidyātapaḥsamṛddheṣu hutaṃ vipramukhāgniṣu 
nistārayati durgāc ca mahataś caiva kilbiṣāt  MnM 
saṃprāptāya tv atithaye pradadyād āsanodake 
annaṃ caiva yathāśakti satkṛtya vidhipūrvakam  MnM 
śilān apy uñchato nityaṃ pañcāgnīn api juhvataḥ 
sarvaṃ sukṛtam ādatte brāhmaṇo 'narcito vasan  MnM 
tṛṇāni bhūmir udakaṃ vāk caturthī ca sūnṛtā 
etāny api satāṃ gehe nocchidyante kadā cana  MnM 
ekarātraṃ tu nivasann atithir brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ 
anityaṃ hi sthito yasmāt tasmād atithir ucyate  MnM 
naikagrāmīṇam atithiṃ vipraṃ sāṅgatikaṃ tathā 
upasthitaṃ gṛhe vidyād bhāryā yatrāgnayo 'pi vā  MnM 
upāsate ye gṛhasthāḥ parapākam abuddhayaḥ 
tena te pretya paśutāṃ vrajanty annādidāyinaḥ  MnM 
apraṇodyo 'tithiḥ sāyaṃ sūryoḍho gṛhamedhinā 
kāle prāptas tv akāle vā nāsyānaśnan gṛhe vaset  MnM 
na vai svayaṃ tad aśnīyād atithiṃ yan na bhojayet 
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ svargyaṃ vātithipūjanam  MnM 
āsanāvasathau śayyām anuvrajyām upāsanām 
uttameṣūttamaṃ kuryād dhīne hīnaṃ same samam  MnM 
vaiśvadeve tu nirvṛtte yady anyo 'tithir āvrajet 
tasyāpy annaṃ yathāśakti pradadyān na baliṃ haret  MnM 
na bhojanārthaṃ sve vipraḥ kulagotre nivedayet 
bhojanārthaṃ hi te śaṃsan vāntāśīty ucyate budhaiḥ  MnM 
na brāhmaṇasya tv atithir gṛhe rājanya ucyate 
vaiśyaśūdrau sakhā caiva jñātayo gurur eva ca  MnM 
yadi tv atithidharmeṇa kṣatriyo gṛham āvrajet 
bhuktavatsu ca vipreṣu kāmaṃ tam api bhojayet  MnM 
vaiśyaśūdrāv api prāptau kuṭumbe 'tithidharmiṇau 
bhojayet saha bhṛtyais tāv ānṛśaṃsyaṃ prayojayan  MnM 
itarān api sakhyādīn samprītyā gṛham āgatān 
prakṛtyānnaṃ yathāśakti bhojayet saha bhāryayā  MnM 
suvāsinīḥ kumārīś ca rogiṇo garbhiṇīḥ striyaḥ 
atithibhyo 'gra evaitān bhojayed avicārayan  MnM 
adattvā tu ya etebhyaḥ pūrvaṃ bhuṅkte 'vicakṣaṇaḥ 
sa bhuñjāno na jānāti śvagṛdhrair jagdhim ātmanaḥ  MnM 
bhuktavatsv atha vipreṣu sveṣu bhṛtyeṣu caiva hi 
bhuñjīyātāṃ tataḥ paścād avaśiṣṭaṃ tu dampatī  MnM 
devān ṛṣīn manuṣyāṃś ca pitṝn gṛhyāś ca devatāḥ 
pūjayitvā tataḥ paścād gṛhasthaḥ śeṣabhug bhavet  MnM 
aghaṃ sa kevalaṃ bhuṅkte yaḥ pacaty ātmakāraṇāt 
yajñaśiṣṭāśanaṃ hy etat satām annaṃ vidhīyate  MnM 
rājartviksnātakagurūn priyaśvaśuramātulān 
arhayen madhuparkeṇa parisaṃvatsarāt punaḥ  MnM 
rājā ca śrotriyaś caiva yajñakarmaṇy upasthitau 
madhuparkeṇa saṃpūjyau na tv ayajña iti sthitiḥ  MnM 
sāyaṃ tv annasya siddhasya patny amantraṃ baliṃ haret 
vaiśvadevaṃ hi nāmaitat sāyaṃ prātar vidhīyate  MnM 
pitṛyajñaṃ tu nirvartya vipraś candrakṣaye 'gnimān 
piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryān māsānumāsikam  MnM 
pitṝṇāṃ māsikaṃ śrāddham anvāhāryaṃ vidur budhāḥ 
tac cāmiṣeṇā kartavyaṃ praśastena prayatnataḥ  MnM 
tatra ye bhojanīyāḥ syur ye ca varjyā dvijottamāḥ 
yāvantaś caiva yaiś cānnais tān pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ  MnM 
dvau daive pitṛkārye trīn ekaikam ubhayatra vā 
bhojayet susamṛddho 'pi na prasajjeta vistare  MnM 
satkriyāṃ deśakālau ca śaucaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃpadaḥ 
pañcaitān vistaro hanti tasmān neheta vistaram  MnM 
prathitā pretakṛtyaiṣā pitryaṃ nāma vidhukṣaye 
tasmin yuktasyaiti nityaṃ pretakṛtyaiva laukikī  MnM 
śrotriyāyaiva deyāni havyakavyāni dātṛbhiḥ 
arhattamāya viprāya tasmai dattaṃ mahāphalam  MnM 
ekaikam api vidvāṃsaṃ daive pitrye ca bhojayet 
puṣkalaṃ phalam āpnoti nāmantrajñān bahūn api  MnM 
dūrād eva parīkṣeta brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam 
tīrthaṃ tad dhavyakavyānāṃ pradāne so 'tithiḥ smṛtaḥ  MnM 
sahasraṃ hi sahasrāṇām anṛcāṃ yatra bhuñjate 
ekas tān mantravit prītaḥ sarvān arhati dharmataḥ  MnM 
jñānotkṛṣṭāya deyāni kavyāni ca havīṃṣi ca 
na hi hastāv asṛgdigdhau rudhireṇaiva śudhyataḥ  MnM 
yāvato grasate grāsān havyakavyeṣv amantravit 
tāvato grasate preto dīptaśūlarṣṭyayoguḍān  MnM 
jñānaniṣṭhā dvijāḥ ke cit taponiṣṭhās tathāpare 
tapaḥsvādhyāyaniṣṭhāś ca karmaniṣṭhās tathāpare  MnM 
jñānaniṣṭheṣu kavyāni pratiṣṭhāpyāni yatnataḥ 
havyāni tu yathānyāyaṃ sarveṣv eva caturṣv api  MnM 
aśrotriyaḥ pitā yasya putraḥ syād vedapāragaḥ 
aśrotriyo vā putraḥ syāt pitā syād vedapāragaḥ  MnM 
jyāyāṃsam anayor vidyād yasya syāc chrotriyaḥ pitā 
mantrasaṃpūjanārthaṃ tu satkāram itaro 'rhati  MnM 
na śrāddhe bhojayen mitraṃ dhanaiḥ kāryo 'sya saṃgrahaḥ 
nāriṃ na mitraṃ yaṃ vidyāt taṃ śrāddhe bhojayed dvijam  MnM 
yasya mitrapradhānāni śrāddhāni ca havīṃṣi ca 
tasya pretya phalaṃ nāsti śrāddheṣu ca haviḥṣu ca  MnM 
yaḥ saṃgatāni kurute mohāc chrāddhena mānavaḥ 
sa svargāc cyavate lokāc chrāddhamitro dvijādhamaḥ  MnM 
saṃbhojāni sābhihitā paiśācī dakṣiṇā dvijaiḥ 
ihaivāste tu sā loke gaur andhevaikaveśmani  MnM 
yatheriṇe bījam uptvā na vaptā labhate phalam 
tathānṛce havir dattvā na dātā labhate phalam  MnM 
dātṝn pratigrahītṝṃś ca kurute phalabhāginaḥ 
viduṣe dakṣiṇāṃ dattvā vidhivat pretya ceha ca  MnM 
kāmaṃ śrāddhe 'rcayen mitraṃ nābhirūpam api tv arim 
dviṣatā hi havir bhuktaṃ bhavati pretya niṣphalam  MnM 
yatnena bhojayec chrāddhe bahvṛcaṃ vedapāragam 
śākhāntagam athādhvaryuṃ chandogaṃ tu samāptikam  MnM 
eṣām anyatamo yasya bhuñjīta śrāddham arcitaḥ 
pitṝṇāṃ tasya tṛptiḥ syāc chāśvatī sāptapauruṣī  MnM 
eṣa vai prathamaḥ kalpaḥ pradāne havyakavyayoḥ 
anukalpas tv ayaṃ jñeyaḥ sadā sadbhir anuṣṭhitaḥ  MnM 
mātāmahaṃ mātulaṃ ca svasrīyaṃ śvaśuraṃ gurum 
dauhitraṃ viṭpatiṃ bandhum ṛtvig yājyau ca bhojayet  MnM 
na brāhmaṇaṃ parīkṣeta daive karmaṇi dharmavit 
pitrye karmaṇi tu prāpte parīkṣeta prayatnataḥ  MnM 
ye stenapatitaklībā ye ca nāstikavṛttayaḥ 
tān havyakavyayor viprān anarhān manur abravīt  MnM 
jaṭilaṃ cānadhīyānaṃ durbālaṃ kitavaṃ tathā 
yājayanti ca ye pūgāṃs tāṃś ca śrāddhe na bhojayet  MnM 
cikitsakān devalakān māṃsavikrayiṇas tathā 
vipaṇena ca jīvanto varjyāḥ syur havyakavyayoḥ  MnM 
preṣyo grāmasya rājñaś ca kunakhī śyāvadantakaḥ 
pratiroddhā guroś caiva tyaktāgnir vārdhuṣis tathā  MnM 
yakṣmī ca paśupālaś ca parivettā nirākṛtiḥ 
brahmadviṭ parivittiś ca gaṇābhyantara eva ca  MnM 
kuśīlavo 'vakīrṇī ca vṛṣalīpatir eva ca 
paunarbhavaś ca kāṇaś ca yasya copapatir gṛhe  MnM 
bhṛtakādhyāpako yaś ca bhṛtakādhyāpitas tathā 
śūdraśiṣyo guruś caiva vāgduṣṭaḥ kuṇḍagolakau  MnM 
akāraṇe parityaktā mātāpitror guros tathā 
brāhmair yaunaiś ca saṃbandhaiḥ saṃyogaṃ patitair gataḥ  MnM 
agāradāhī garadaḥ kuṇḍāśī somavikrayī 
samudrayāyī bandī ca tailikaḥ kūṭakārakaḥ  MnM 
pitrā vivadamānaś ca kitavo madyapas tathā 
pāparogy abhiśastaś ca dāmbhiko rasavikrayī  MnM 
dhanuḥśarāṇāṃ kartā ca yaś cāgredidhiṣūpatiḥ 
mitradhrug dyūtavṛttiś ca putrācāryas tathaiva ca  MnM 
bhrāmarī ganḍamālī ca śvitry atho piśunas tathā 
unmatto 'ndhaś ca varjyāḥ syur vedanindaka eva ca  MnM 
hastigo'śvoṣṭradamako nakṣatrair yaś ca jīvati 
pakṣiṇāṃ poṣako yaś ca yuddhācāryas tathaiva ca  MnM 
srotasāṃ bhedako yaś ca teṣāṃ cāvaraṇe rataḥ 
gṛhasaṃveśako dūto vṛkṣāropaka eva ca  MnM 
śvakrīḍī śyenajīvī ca kanyādūṣaka eva ca 
hiṃsro vṛṣalavṛttiś ca gaṇānāṃ caiva yājakaḥ  MnM 
ācārahīnaḥ klībaś ca nityaṃ yācanakas tathā 
kṛṣijīvī ślīpadī ca sadbhir nindita eva ca  MnM 
aurabhriko māhiṣikaḥ parapūrvāpatis tathā 
pretaniryāpakaś caiva varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ  MnM 
etān vigarhitācārān apāṅkteyān dvijādhamān 
dvijātipravaro vidvān ubhayatra vivarjayet  MnM 
brāhmaṇo tv anadhīyānas tṛṇāgnir iva śāmyati 
tasmai havyaṃ na dātavyaṃ na hi bhasmani hūyate  MnM 
apāṅktadāne yo dātur bhavaty ūrdhvaṃ phalodayaḥ 
daive haviṣi pitrye vā taṃ pravaksyāmy aśeṣataḥ  MnM 
avratair yad dvijair bhuktaṃ parivetrādibhis tathā 
apāṅkteyair yad anyaiś ca tad vai rakṣāṃsi bhuñjate  MnM 
dārāgnihotrasaṃyogaṃ kurute yo 'graje sthite 
parivettā sa vijñeyaḥ parivittis tu pūrvajaḥ  MnM 
parivittiḥ parivettā yayā ca parividyate 
sarve te narakaṃ yānti dātṛyājakapañcamāḥ  MnM 
bhrātur mṛtasya bhāryāyāṃ yo 'nurajyeta kāmataḥ 
dharmeṇāpi niyuktāyāṃ sa jñeyo didhiṣūpatiḥ  MnM 
paradāreṣu jāyete dvau sutau kuṇḍagolakau 
patyau jīvati kuṇḍaḥ syān mṛte bhartari golakaḥ  MnM 
tau tu jātau parakṣetre prāṇinau pretya ceha ca 
dattāni havyakavyāni nāśayanti pradāyinām  MnM 
apāṅktyo yāvataḥ paṅktyān bhuñjānān anupaśyati 
tāvatāṃ na phalaṃ tatra dātā prāpnoti bāliśaḥ  MnM 
vīkṣyāndho navateḥ kāṇaḥ ṣaṣṭeḥ śvitrī śatasya tu 
pāparogī sahasrasya dātur nāśayate phalam  MnM 
yāvataḥ saṃspṛśed aṅgair brāhmaṇāñ śūdrayājakaḥ 
tāvatāṃ na bhaved dātuḥ phalaṃ dānasya paurtikam  MnM

somavikrayiṇe viṣṭhā bhiṣaje pūyaśoṇitam 
naṣṭaṃ devalake dattam apratiṣṭhaṃ tu vārdhuṣau  MnM 
yat tu vāṇijake dattaṃ neha nāmutra tad bhavet 
bhasmanīva hutaṃ dravyaṃ tathā paunarbhave dvije  MnM 
itareṣu tv apāṅktyeṣu yathoddiṣṭeṣv asādhuṣu 
medo'sṛṅmāṃsamajjāsthi vadanty annaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ  MnM 
apāṅktyopahatā paṅktiḥ pāvyate yair dvijottamaiḥ 
tān nibodhata kārtsnyena dvijāgryān paṅktipāvanān  MnM 
agryāḥ sarveṣu vedeṣu sarvapravacaneṣu ca 
śrotriyānvayajāś caiva vijñeyāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ  MnM 
triṇāciketaḥ pañcāgnis trisuparṇaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavit 
brahmadeyātmasantāno jyeṣṭhasāmaga eva ca  MnM 
vedārthavit pravaktā ca brahmacārī sahasradaḥ 
śatāyuś caiva vijñeyā brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ  MnM 
pūrvedyur aparedyur vā śrāddhakarmaṇy upasthite 
nimantrayeta tryavarān samyag viprān yathoditān  MnM

vāyuvac cānugacchanti tathāsīnān upāsate  MnM

kathaṃ cid apy atikrāman pāpaḥ sūkaratāṃ vrajet  MnM

akrodhanāḥ śaucaparāḥ satataṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ 
nyastaśastrā mahābhāgāḥ pitaraḥ pūrvadevatāḥ  MnM

ye ca yair upacaryāḥ syur niyamais tān nibodhata  MnM 
manor hairaṇyagarbhasya ye marīcyādayaḥ sutāḥ 
teṣām ṛṣīṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ putrāḥ pitṛgaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ  MnM 
virāṭsutāḥ somasadaḥ sādhyānāṃ pitaraḥ smṛtāḥ 
agniṣvāttāś ca devānāṃ mārīcā lokaviśrutāḥ  MnM 
daityadānavayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām 
suparṇakinnarāṇāṃ ca smṛtā barhiṣado 'trijāḥ  MnM

vaiśyānām ājyapā nāma śūdrāṇāṃ tu sukālinaḥ  MnM

pulastyasyājyapāḥ putrā vasiṣṭhasya sukālinaḥ  MnM 
agnidagdhānagnidagdhān kāvyān barhiṣadas tathā

ya ete tu gaṇā mukhyāḥ pitṝṇāṃ parikīrtitāḥ 
teṣām apīha vijñeyaṃ putrapautram anantakam  MnM 
ṛṣibhyaḥ pitaro jātāḥ pitṛbhyo devamānavāḥ 
devebhyas tu jagat sarvaṃ caraṃ sthāṇv anupūrvaśaḥ  MnM 
rājatair bhājanair eṣām atho vā rajatānvitaiḥ 
vāry api śraddhayā dattam akṣayāyopakalpate  MnM 
daivakāryād dvijātīnāṃ pitṛkāryaṃ viśiṣyate 
daivaṃ hi pitṛkāryasya pūrvam āpyāyanaṃ smṛtam  MnM 
teṣām ārakṣabhūtaṃ tu pūrvaṃ daivaṃ niyojayet 
raksāṃsi vipralumpanti śrāddham ārakṣavarjitam  MnM 
daivādyantaṃ tad īheta pitrādyantaṃ na tad bhavet 
pitrādyantaṃ tv īhamānaḥ kṣipraṃ naśyati sānvayaḥ  MnM 
śuciṃ deśaṃ viviktaṃ ca gomayenopalepayet 
dakṣināpravaṇaṃ caiva prayatnenopapādayet  MnM 
avakāśeṣu cokṣeṣu jalatīreṣu caiva hi 
vivikteṣu ca tuṣyanti dattena pitaraḥ sadā  MnM 
āsaneṣūpakḷpteṣu barhiṣmatsu pṛthakpṛthak 
upaspṛṣṭodakān samyag viprāṃs tān upaveśayet  MnM

agnau kuryād anujñāto brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇaiḥ saha  MnM 
agneḥ somayamābhyāṃ ca kṛtvāpyāyanam āditaḥ 
havirdānena vidhivat paścāt saṃtarpayet pitṝn  MnM 
agnyabhāve tu viprasya pāṇāv evopapādayet 
yo hy agniḥ sa dvijo viprair mantradarśibhir ucyate  MnM 
akrodhanān suprasādān vadanty etān purātanān 
lokasyāpyāyane yuktān śrāddhadevān dvijottamān  MnM 
apasavyam agnau kṛtvā sarvam āvṛtya vikramam 
apasavyena hastena nirvaped udakaṃ bhuvi  MnM 
trīṃs tu tasmād dhaviḥśeṣāt piṇḍān kṛtvā samāhitaḥ 
audakenaiva vidhinā nirvaped dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ  MnM 
nyupya piṇḍāṃs tatas tāṃs tu prayato vidhipūrvakam 
teṣu darbheṣu taṃ hastaṃ nirmṛjyāl lepabhāginām  MnM 
ācamyodakparāvṛtya trir āyamya śanair asūn 
ṣaḍ ṛtūṃś ca namaskuryāt pitṝn eva ca mantravat  MnM 
udakaṃ ninayec cheṣaṃ śanaiḥ piṇḍāntike punaḥ 
avajighrec ca tān piṇḍān yathānyuptān samāhitaḥ  MnM 
piṇḍebhyas tv alpikāṃ mātrāṃ samādāyānupūrvaśaḥ 
tān eva viprān āsīnān vidhivat pūrvam āśayet  MnM 
dhriyamāṇe tu pitari pūrveṣām eva nirvapet 
vipravad vāpi taṃ śrāddhe svakaṃ pitaram āśayet  MnM 
pitā yasya nivṛttaḥ syāj jīvec cāpi pitāmahaḥ 
pituḥ sa nāma saṅkīrtya kīrtayet prapitāmaham  MnM 
pitāmaho vā tacchrāddhaṃ bhuñjītety abravīn manuḥ 
kāmaṃ vā samanujñātaḥ svayam eva samācaret  MnM 
teṣāṃ dattvā tu hasteṣu sapavitraṃ tilodakam 
tatpiṇḍāgraṃ prayaccheta svadhaiṣām astv iti bruvan  MnM 
pāṇibhyāṃ tūpasaṃgṛhya svayam annasya vardhitam 
viprāntike pitṝn dhyāyan śanakair upanikṣipet  MnM 
ubhayor hastayor muktaṃ yad annam upanīyate 
tad vipralumpanty asurāḥ sahasā duṣṭacetasaḥ  MnM 
guṇāṃś ca sūpaśākādyān payo dadhi ghṛtaṃ madhu 
vinyaset prayataḥ pūrvaṃ bhūmāv eva samāhitaḥ  MnM 
bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ ca vividhaṃ mūlāni ca phalāni ca 
hṛdyāni caiva māṃsāni pānāni surabhīṇi ca  MnM 
upanīya tu tat sarvaṃ śanakaiḥ susamāhitaḥ 
pariveṣayeta prayato guṇān sarvān pracodayan  MnM 
nāsram āpātayej jātu na kupyen nānṛtaṃ vadet 
na pādena spṛśed annaṃ na caitad avadhūnayet  MnM 
asraṃ gamayati pretān kopo 'rīn anṛtaṃ śunaḥ 
pādasparśas tu rakṣāṃsi duṣkṛtīn avadhūnanam  MnM 
yad yad roceta viprebhyas tat tad dadyād amatsaraḥ 
brahmodyāś ca kathāḥ kuryāt pitṝṇām etad īpsitam  MnM

trīṇi cātra praśaṃsanti śaucam akrodham atvarām  MnM 
atyuṣṇaṃ sarvam annaṃ syād bhuñjīraṃs te ca vāgyatāḥ 
na ca dvijātayo brūyur dātrā pṛṣṭā havirguṇān  MnM 
yāvad uṣmā bhavaty annaṃ yāvad aśnanti vāgyatāḥ 
pitaras tāvad aśnanti yāvan noktā havirguṇāḥ  MnM 
yad veṣṭitaśirā bhuṅkte yad bhuṅkte dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ 
sopānatkaś ca yad bhuṅkte tad vai rakṣāṃsi bhuñjate  MnM 
cāṇḍālaś ca varāhaś ca kukkuṭaḥ śvā tathaiva ca 
rajasvalā ca ṣaṇḍhaś ca nekṣerann aśnato dvijān  MnM 
home pradāne bhojye ca yad ebhir abhivīkṣyate 
daive haviṣi pitrye vā tad gacchaty ayathātatham  MnM 
ghrāṇena sūkaro hanti pakṣavātena kukkuṭaḥ

khañjo vā yadi vā kāṇo dātuḥ preṣyo 'pi vā bhavet 
hīnātiriktagātro vā tam apy apanayet punaḥ  MnM 
brāhmaṇaṃ bhikṣukaṃ vāpi bhojanārtham upasthitam 
brāhmaṇair abhyanujñātaḥ śaktitaḥ pratipūjayet  MnM 
sārvavarṇikam annādyaṃ saṃnīyāplāvya vāriṇā 
samutsṛjed bhuktavatām agrato vikiran bhuvi  MnM 
asaṃskṛtapramītānāṃ tyāgināṃ kulayoṣitām

anayaivāvṛtā kāryaṃ piṇḍanirvapanaṃ sutaiḥ  MnM

śrāddhabhug vṛṣalītalpaṃ tad ahar yo 'dhigacchati

ācāntāṃś cānujānīyād abhito ramyatām iti  MnM

aparāhṇas tathā darbhā vāstusaṃpādanaṃ tilāḥ 
sṛṣṭir mṛṣṭir dvijāś cāgryāḥ śrāddhakarmasu saṃpadaḥ  MnM 
darbhāḥ pavitraṃ pūrvāhṇo haviṣyāṇi ca sarvaśaḥ 
pavitraṃ yac ca pūrvoktaṃ vijñeyā havyasaṃpadaḥ  MnM 
munyannāni payaḥ somo māṃsaṃ yac cānupaskṛtam 
aksāralavaṇaṃ caiva prakṛtyā havir ucyate  MnM 
visṛjya brāhmaṇāṃs tāṃs tu niyato vāgyataḥ śuciḥ

pativratā dharmapatnī pitṛpūjanatatparā

āyuṣmantaṃ sutaṃ sūte yaśomedhāsamanvitam 
dhanavantaṃ prajāvantaṃ sāttvikaṃ dhārmikaṃ tathā  MnM

tato gṛhabaliṃ kuryād iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ  MnM 
havir yac cirarātrāya yac cānantyāya kalpate

ṣaṇmāsāṃś chāgamāṃsena pārṣatena ca sapta vai

daśamāsāṃs tu tṛpyanti varāhamahiṣāmiṣaiḥ 
śaśakūrmayos tu māṃsena māsān ekādaśaiva tu  MnM 
saṃvatsaraṃ tu gavyena payasā pāyasena ca

kālaśākaṃ mahāśalkāḥ khaṅgalohāmiṣaṃ madhu 
ānantyāyaiva kalpyante munyannāni ca sarvaśaḥ  MnM

tad apy akṣayam eva syād varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca  MnM

pāyasaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ prāk chāye kuñjarasya ca  MnM

tat tat pitṝṇāṃ bhavati paratrānantam akṣayam  MnM 
kṛṣṇapakṣe daśamyādau varjayitvā caturdaśīm 
śrāddhe praśastās tithayo yathaitā na tathetarāḥ  MnM

ayukṣu tu pitṝn sarvān prajāṃ prāpnoti puṣkalām  MnM

prācīnāvītinā samyag apasavyam atandriṇā

anena vidhinā śrāddhaṃ trir abdasyeha nirvapet

etad vo 'bhihitaṃ sarvaṃ vidhānaṃ pāñcayajñikam

caturtham āyuṣo bhāgam uṣitvādyaṃ gurau dvijāḥ

yā vṛttis tāṃ samāsthāya vipro jīved anāpadi  Mn

iṣṭīḥ pārvāyaṇāntīyāḥ kevalā nirvapet sadā  Mn

ajihmām aśathāṃ śuddhāṃ jīved brāhmaṇajīvikām  Mn

ato 'nyatamayā vṛttyā jīvaṃs tu snātako dvijaḥ 
svargāyuṣyayaśasyāni vratāṇīmāni dhārayet  Mn

tad dhi kurvan yathāśakti prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim  Mn 
nehetārthān prasaṅgena na viruddhena karmaṇā 
na vidyamāneṣv artheṣu nārtyām api yatas tataḥ  Mn 
indriyārtheṣu sarveṣu na prasajyeta kāmataḥ 
atiprasaktiṃ caiteṣāṃ manasā saṃnivartayet  Mn

yathā tathādhyāpayaṃs tu sā hy asya kṛtakṛtyatā  Mn

nityaṃ śāstrāṇy avekṣeta nigamāṃś caiva vaidikān  Mn 
yathā yathā hi puruṣaḥ śāstraṃ samadhigacchati 
tathā tathā vijānāti vijñānaṃ cāsya rocate  Mn 
ṛṣiyajñaṃ devayajñaṃ bhūtayajñaṃ ca sarvadā 
nṛyajñaṃ pitṛyajñaṃ ca yathāśakti na hāpayet  Mn 
etān eke mahāyajñān yajñaśāstravido janāḥ 
anīhamānāḥ satatam indriyeṣv eva juhvati  Mn 
vācy eke juhvati prāṇaṃ prāṇe vācaṃ ca sarvadā 
vāci prāṇe ca paśyanto yajñanirvṛttim akṣayām  Mn 
jñānenaivāpare viprā yajanty etair makhaiḥ sadā 
jñānamūlāṃ kriyām eṣāṃ paśyanto jñānacakṣuṣā  Mn 
agnihotraṃ ca juhuyād ādyante dyuniśoḥ sadā 
darśena cārdhamāsānte paurṇāmāsena caiva hi  Mn 
sasyānte navasasyeṣṭyā tathā rtvante dvijo 'dhvaraiḥ 
paśunā tv ayanasyādau samānte saumikair makhaiḥ  Mn 
nāniṣṭvā navasasyeṣṭyā paśunā cāgnimān dvijaḥ 
navānnam adyān māṃsaṃ vā dīrgham āyur jijīviṣuḥ  Mn 
navenānarcitā hy asya paśuhavyena cāgnayaḥ 
prāṇān evāttum icchanti navānnāmiṣagardhinaḥ  Mn 
āsanāśanaśayyābhir adbhir mūlaphalena vā 
nāsya kaś cid vased gehe śaktito 'narcito 'tithiḥ  Mn 
pāṣāṇḍino vikarmasthān baiḍālavratikāñ śaṭhān 
haitukān bakavṛttīṃś ca vāṅgātreṇāpi nārcayet  Mn 
vedavidyāvratasnātāñ śrotriyān gṛhamedhinaḥ 
pūjayed dhavyakavyena viparītāṃś ca varjayet  Mn 
śaktito 'pacamānebhyo dātavyaṃ gṛhamedhinā 
saṃvibhāgaś ca bhūtebhyaḥ kartavyo 'nuparodhataḥ  Mn

yājyāntevāsinor vāpi na tv anyata iti sthitiḥ  Mn 
na sīdet snātako vipraḥ kṣudhā śaktaḥ kathaṃ cana 
na jīrṇamalavadvāsā bhavec ca vibhave sati  Mn 
kḷptakeśanakhaśmaśrur dāntaḥ śuklāmbaraḥ śuciḥ 
svādhyāye caiva yuktaḥ syān nityam ātmahiteṣu ca  Mn 
vaiṇavīṃ dhārayed yaṣṭiṃ sodakaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum 
yajñopavītaṃ vedaṃ ca śubhaṃ raukme ca kuṇḍale  Mn 
nekṣetodyantam ādityaṃ nāstaṃ yāntaṃ kadā cana 
nopasṛṣṭaṃ na vāristhaṃ na madhyaṃ nabhaso gatam  Mn 
na laṅghayed vatsatantrīṃ na pradhāvec ca varṣati 
na codake nirīkṣeta svarūpam iti dhāraṇā  Mn 
mṛdaṃ gāṃ daivataṃ vipraṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu catuṣpatham 
pradakṣiṇāni kurvīta prajñātāṃś ca vanaspatīn  Mn 
nopagacchet pramatto 'pi striyam ārtavadarśane 
samānaśayane caiva na śayīta tayā saha  Mn 
rajasābhiplutāṃ nārīṃ narasya hy upagacchataḥ 
prajñā tejo balaṃ cakṣur āyuś caiva prahīyate  Mn 
tāṃ vivarjayatas tasya rajasā samabhiplutām 
prajñā tejo balaṃ cakṣur āyuś caiva pravardhate  Mn 
nāśnīyād bhāryayā sārdhaṃ nainām īkṣeta cāśnatīm 
kṣuvatīṃ jṛmbhamāṇāṃ vā na cāsīnāṃ yathāsukham  Mn 
nāñjayantīṃ svake netre na cābhyaktām anāvṛtām 
na paśyet prasavantīṃ ca tejaskāmo dvijottamaḥ  Mn 
nānnam adyād ekavāsā na nagnaḥ snānam ācaret 
na mūtraṃ pathi kurvīta na bhasmani na govraje  Mn 
na phālakṛṣṭe na jale na cityāṃ na ca parvate 
na jīrṇadevāyatane na valmīke kadā cana  Mn 
na sasattveṣu garteṣu na gacchann api na sthitaḥ 
na nadītīram āsādya na ca parvatamastake  Mn 
vāyvagnivipram ādityam apaḥ paśyaṃs tathaiva gāḥ 
na kadā cana kurvīta viṇmūtrasya visarjanam  Mn 
tiraskṛtyoccaret kāṣṭha loṣṭhapatratṛṇādinā 
niyamya prayato vācaṃ saṃvītāṅgo 'vaguṇṭhitaḥ  MnKM 
mūtroccārasamutsargaṃ divā kuryād udaṅmukhaḥ 
dakṣiṇābhimukho rātrau saṃdhyāyoś ca yathā divā  MnKM 
chāyāyām andhakāre vā rātrāv ahani vā dvijaḥ 
yathāsukhamukhaḥ kuryāt prāṇabādhabhayeṣu ca  MnKM 
pratyagniṃ pratisūryaṃ ca pratisomodakadvijam 
pratigu prativātaṃ ca prajñā naśyati mehataḥ  MnKM 
nāgniṃ mukhenopadhamen nagnāṃ nekṣeta ca striyam 
nāmedhyaṃ prakṣiped agnau na ca pādau pratāpayet  Mn 
adhastān nopadadhyāc ca na cainam abhilaṅghayet 
na cainaṃ pādataḥ kuryān na prāṇābādham ācaret  Mn 
nāśnīyāt saṃdhivelāyāṃ na gacchen nāpi saṃviśet 
na caiva pralikhed bhūmiṃ nātmano 'paharet srajam  Mn 
nāpsu mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ vā ṣṭhīvanaṃ vā samutsṛjet 
amedhyaliptam anyad vā lohitaṃ vā viṣāṇi vā  Mn 
naikaḥ supyāc chūnyagehe na śreyāṃsaṃ prabodhayet 
nodakyayābhibhāṣeta yajñaṃ gacchen na cāvṛtaḥ  Mn 
agnyagāre gavāṃ goṣṭhe brāhmaṇānāṃ ca saṃnidhau 
svādhyāye bhojane caiva dakṣinaṃ pāṇim uddharet  Mn 
na vārayed gāṃ dhayantīṃ na cācakṣīta kasya cit 
na divīndrāyudhaṃ dṛṣṭvā kasya cid darśayed budhaḥ  Mn 
nādharmike vased grāme na vyādhibahule bhṛśam 
naikaḥ prapadyetādhvānaṃ na ciraṃ parvate vaset  Mn 
na śūdrarājye nivasen nādhārmikajanāvṛte 
na pāṣaṇḍigaṇākrānte nopasṣṛṭe 'ntyajair nṛbhiḥ  Mn 
na bhuñjītoddhṛtasnehaṃ nātisauhityam ācaret 
nātiprage nātisāyaṃ na sāyaṃ prātarāśitaḥ  Mn 
na kurvīta vṛthāceṣṭāṃ na vāry añjalinā pibet 
notsaṅge bhakṣayed bhakṣyān na jātu syāt kutūhalī  Mn 
na nṛtyed atha vā gāyen na vāditrāṇi vādayet 
nāsphoṭayen na ca kṣveḍen na ca rakto virāvayet  Mn 
na pādau dhāvayet kāṃsye kadā cid api bhājane 
na bhinnabhāṇḍe bhuñjīta na bhāvapratidūṣite  Mn 
upānahau ca vāsaś ca dhṛtam anyair na dhārayet 
upavītam alaṅkāraṃ srajaṃ karakam eva ca  Mn 
nāvinītair bhajed dhuryair na ca kṣudhvyādhipīḍitaiḥ 
na bhinnaśṛṅgākṣikhurair na vāladhivirūpitaiḥ  Mn 
vinītais tu vrajen nityam āśugair lakṣaṇānvitaiḥ 
varṇarūpopasaṃpannaiḥ pratodenātudan bhṛśam  Mn 
bālātapaḥ pretadhūmo varjyaṃ bhinnaṃ tathāsanam 
na chindyān nakharomāṇi dantair notpāṭayen nakhān  Mn 
na mṛlloṣṭhaṃ ca mṛdnīyān na chindyāt karajais tṛṇam 
na karma niṣphalaṃ kuryān nāyatyām asukhodayam  Mn 
loṣṭhamardī tṛṇacchedī nakhakhādī ca yo naraḥ 
sa vināśaṃ vrajaty āśu sūcakāśucir eva ca  Mn 
na vigarhya kathāṃ kuryād bahir mālyaṃ na dhārayet 
gavāṃ ca yānaṃ pṛṣṭhena sarvathaiva vigarhitam  Mn 
advāreṇa ca nātīyād grāmaṃ vā veśma vāvṛtam 
rātrau ca vṛkṣamūlāni dūrataḥ parivarjayet  Mn 
nākṣair dīvyet kadā cit tu svayaṃ nopānahau haret 
śayanastho na bhuñjīta na pāṇisthaṃ na cāsane  Mn 
sarvaṃ ca tilasaṃbaddhaṃ nādyād astam ite ravau 
na ca nagnaḥ śayīteha na cocchiṣṭaḥ kva cid vrajet  Mn 
ārdrapādas tu bhuñjīta nārdrapādas tu saṃviśet 
ārdrapādas tu bhuñjāno dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt  Mn 
acakṣurviṣayaṃ durgaṃ  na prapadyeta karhi cit 
na viṇmūtram udīkṣeta na bāhubhyāṃ nadīṃ taret  Mn 
adhitiṣṭhen na keśāṃs tu na bhasmāsthikapālikāḥ 
na kārpāsāsthi na tuṣān dīrgham āyur jijīviṣuḥ  Mn 
na saṃvasec ca patitair na cāṇḍālair na pulkasaiḥ 
na mūrkhair nāvaliptaiś ca nāntyair nāntyāvasāyibhiḥ  Mn 
na śūdrāya matiṃ dadyān nocchiṣṭaṃ na haviṣkṛtam 
na cāsyopadiśed dharmaṃ na cāsya vratam ādiśet  Mn 
yo hy asya dharmam ācaṣṭe yaś caivādiśati vratam 
so 'saṃvṛtaṃ nāma tamaḥ saha tenaiva majjati  Mn 
na saṃhatābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ kaṇḍūyed ātmanaḥ śiraḥ 
na spṛśec caitad ucchiṣṭo na ca snāyād vinā tataḥ  Mn 
keśagrahān prahārāṃś ca śirasy etān vivarjayet 
śiraḥsnātaś ca tailena nāṅgaṃ kiṃ cid api spṛśet  Mn 
na rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇīyād arājanyaprasūtitaḥ 
sūnācakradhvajavatāṃ veśenaiva ca jīvatām  Mn 
daśasūnāsamaṃ cakraṃ daśacakrasamo dhvajaḥ 
daśadhvajasamo veśo daśaveśasamo nṛpaḥ  Mn 
daśa sūṇāsahasrāṇi yo vāhayati saunikaḥ 
tena tulyaḥ smṛto rājā ghoras tasya pratigrahaḥ  Mn 
yo rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇāti lubdhasyocchāstravartinaḥ 
sa paryāyeṇa yātīmān narakān ekaviṃśatim  Mn 
tāmisram andhatāmisraṃ mahārauravarauravau 
narakaṃ kālasūtraṃ ca mahānarakam eva ca  Mn 
saṃjīvanaṃ mahāvīciṃ tapanaṃ saṃpratāpanam 
saṃhātaṃ ca sakākolaṃ kuḍmalaṃ pratimūrtikam  Mn 
lohaśaṅkum ṛjīṣaṃ ca panthānaṃ śālmalīṃ nadīm 
asipatravanaṃ caiva lohadārakam eva ca  Mn 
etad vidanto vidvāṃso brāhmaṇā brahmavādinaḥ 
na rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇanti pretya śreyo 'bhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ  Mn 
brāhme muhūrte budhyeta dharmārthau cānucintayet 
kāyakleśāṃś ca tanmūlān vedatattvārtham eva ca  Mn 
utthāyāvaśyakaṃ kṛtvā kṛtaśaucaḥ samāhitaḥ 
pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ japaṃs tiṣṭhet svakāle cāparāṃ ciram  Mn 
ṛṣayo dīrghasaṃdhyatvād dīrgham āyur avāpnuyuḥ 
prajñāṃ yaśaś ca kīrtiṃ ca brahmavarcasam eva ca  Mn 
śrāvaṇyāṃ prauṣṭhapadyāṃ vāpy upākṛtya yathāvidhi

puṣye tu chandasāṃ kuryād bahir utsarjanaṃ dvijaḥ 
māghaśuklasya vā prāpte pūrvāhṇe prathame 'hani  Mn 
yathāśāstraṃ tu kṛtvaivam utsargaṃ chandasāṃ bahiḥ 
viramet pakṣiṇīṃ rātriṃ tad evaikam aharniśam  Mn 
ata ūrdhvaṃ tu chandāṃsi śukleṣu niyataḥ paṭhet

nāvispaṣṭam adhīyīta na śūdrajanasannidhau 
na niśānte pariśrānto brahmādhītya punaḥ svapet  Mn 
yathoditena vidhinā nityaṃ chandaskṛtaṃ paṭhet 
brahma chandaskṛtaṃ caiva dvijo yukto hy anāpadi  Mn 
imān nityam anadhyāyān adhīyāno vivarjayet 
adhyāpanaṃ ca kurvāṇaḥ śiṣyāṇāṃ vidhipūrvakam  Mn 
karṇaśrave 'nile rātrau divā pāṃsusamūhane 
etau varṣāsv anadhyāyāv adhyāyajñāḥ pracakṣate  Mn 
vidyutstanitavarṣeṣu maholkānāṃ ca saṃplave 
ākālikam anadhyāyam eteṣu manur abravīt  Mn 
etāṃs tv abhyuditān vidyād yadā prāduṣkṛtāgniṣu 
tadā vidyād anadhyāyam anṛtau cābhradarśane  Mn 
nirghāte bhūmicalane jyotiṣāṃ copasarjane 
etān ākālikān vidyād anadhyāyān ṛtāv api  Mn 
prāduṣkṛteṣv agniṣu tu vidyutstanitaniḥsvane 
sajyotiḥ syād anadhyāyaḥ śeṣe rātrau yathā divā  Mn 
nityānadhyāya eva syād grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca 
dharmanaipuṇyakāmānāṃ pūtigandhe ca sarvadā  Mn

udake madhyarātre ca viṇmūtrasya visarjane 
ucchiṣṭaḥ śrāddhabhuk caiva manasāpi na cintayet  Mn 
pratigṛhya dvijo vidvān ekoddiṣṭasya ketanam 
tryahaṃ na kīrtayed brahma rājño rāhoś ca sūtake  Mn 
yāvad ekānudiṣṭasya gandho lepaś ca tiṣṭhati 
viprasya viduṣo dehe tāvad brahma na kīrtayet  Mn 
śayānaḥ prauḍhapādaś ca kṛtvā caivāvasakthikām

nīhāre bāṇaśabde ca saṃdhyayor eva cobhayoḥ 
amāvāsyācaturdaśyoḥ paurṇamāsyaṣṭakāsu ca  Mn 
amāvāsyā guruṃ hanti śiṣyaṃ hanti caturdaśī 
brahmāṣṭakapaurṇamāsyau tasmāt tāḥ parivarjayet  Mn 
pāṃsuvarṣe diśāṃ dāhe gomāyuvirute tathā 
śvakharoṣṭre ca ruvati paṅktau ca na paṭhed dvijaḥ  Mn

vasitvā maithunaṃ vāsaḥ śrāddhikaṃ pratigṛhya ca  Mn

corair upadrute grāme saṃbhrame cāgnikārite 
ākālikam anadhyāyaṃ vidyāt sarvādbhuteṣu ca  Mn 
upākarmaṇi cotsarge trirātraṃ kṣepaṇaṃ smṛtam 
aṣṭakāsu tv ahorātram ṛtvantāsu ca rātriṣu  Mn 
nādhīyītāśvam ārūḍho na vṛkṣaṃ na ca hastinam 
na nāvaṃ na kharaṃ noṣṭraṃ neriṇastho na yānagaḥ  Mn 
na vivāde na kalahe na senāyāṃ na saṃgare 
na bhuktamātre nājīrṇe na vamitvā na śuktake  Mn 
atithiṃ cānanujñāpya mārute vāti vā bhṛśam

kramataḥ pūrvam abhyasya paścād vedam adhīyate  Mn

antarāgamane vidyād anadhyāyam aharniśam  Mn 
dvāv eva varjayen nityam anadhyāyau prayatnataḥ 
svādhyāyabhūmiṃ cāśuddham ātmānaṃ cāśuciṃ dvijaḥ  Mn

na vāsobhiḥ sahājasraṃ nāvijñāte jalāśaye  Mn

saṃdhyayor ubhayoś caiva na seveta catuṣpatham  Mn 
udvartanam apasnānaṃ viṇmūtre raktam eva ca

adhārmikaṃ taskaraṃ ca parasyaiva ca yoṣitaṃ  Mn 
na hīdṛśam anāyuṣyaṃ loke kiṃ cana vidyate 
yādṛśaṃ puruṣasyeha paradāropasevanam  Mn 
kṣatriyaṃ caiva sarpaṃ ca brāhmaṇaṃ ca bahuśrutam 
nāvamanyeta vai bhūṣṇuḥ kṛśān api kadā cana  Mn

tasmād etat trayaṃ nityaṃ nāvamanyeta buddhimān  Mn 
nātmānam avamanyeta purvābhir asamṛddhibhiḥ 
ā mṛtyoḥ śriyam anvicchen naināṃ manyeta durlabhām  Mn 
satyaṃ brūyāt priyaṃ brūyān na brūyāt satyam apriyam 
priyaṃ ca nānṛtaṃ brūyād eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ  Mn 
bhadraṃ bhadram iti brūyād bhadram ity eva vā vadet 
śuṣkavairaṃ vivādaṃ ca na kuryāt kena cit saha  Mn 
nātikalyaṃ nātisāyaṃ nātimadhyaṃdine sthite 
nājñātena samaṃ gacchen naiko na vṛṣalaiḥ saha  Mn 
hīnāṅgān atiriktāṅgān vidyāhīnān vayo'dhikān 
rūpadraviṇahīnāṃś ca jātihīnāṃś ca nākṣipet  Mn 
na spṛśet pāṇinocchiṣṭo vipro gobrāhmaṇānalāṇ 
na cāpi paśyed aśuciḥ sustho jyotirgaṇān divā  Mn 
spṛṣṭvaitān aśucir nityam adbhiḥ prāṇān upaspṛśet 
gātrāṇi caiva sarvāṇi nābhiṃ pāṇitalena tu  Mn 
anāturaḥ svāni khāni na spṛśed animittataḥ 
romāṇi ca rahasyāni sarvāṇy eva vivarjayet  Mn 
maṅgalācārayuktaḥ syāt prayatātmā jitendriyaḥ 
japec ca juhuyāc caiva nityam agnim atandritaḥ  Mn 
maṅgalācārayuktānāṃ nityaṃ ca prayatātmanām 
japatāṃ juhvatāṃ caiva vinipāto na vidyate  Mn 
vedam evābhyasen nityaṃ yathākālam atandritaḥ 
taṃ hy asyāhuḥ paraṃ dharmam upadharmo 'nya ucyate  Mn ḥḥ
vedābhyāsena satataṃ śaucena tapasaiva ca 
adroheṇa ca bhūtānāṃ jātiṃ smarati paurvikīm  Mn 
paurvikīṃ saṃsmaran jātiṃ brahmaivābhyasyate punaḥ 
brahmābhyāsena cājasram anantaṃ sukham aśnute  Mn 
sāvitrāñ śāntihomāṃś ca kuryāt parvasu nityaśaḥ 
pitṝṃś caivāṣṭakāsv arcen nityam anvaṣṭakāsu ca  Mn 
dūrād āvasathān mūtraṃ dūrāt pādāvasecanam 
ucchiṣṭānnaniṣekaṃ ca dūrād eva samācaret  Mn 
maitraṃ prasādhanaṃ snānaṃ dantadhāvanam añjanam 
pūrvāhṇa eva kurvīta devatānāṃ ca pūjanam  Mn 
daivatāny abhigacchet tu dhārmikāṃś ca dvijottamān 
īśvaraṃ caiva rakṣārthaṃ gurūn eva ca parvasu  Mn 
abhivādayed vṛddhāṃś ca dadyāc caivāsanaṃ svakam 
kṛtāñjalir upāsīta gacchataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nviyāt  Mn 
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ samyaṅ nibaddhaṃ sveṣu karmasu 
dharmamūlaṃ niṣeveta sadācāram atandritaḥ  Mn 
ācārāl labhate hy āyur ācārād īpsitāḥ prajāḥ 
ācārād dhanam akṣayyam ācāro hanty alakṣaṇam  Mn 
durācāro hi puruṣo loke bhavati ninditaḥ 
duḥkhabhāgī ca satataṃ vyādhito 'lpāyur eva ca  Mn 
sarvalakṣaṇahīno 'pi yaḥ sadācāravān naraḥ 
śraddadhāno 'nasūyaś ca śataṃ varṣāṇi jīvati  Mn 
yad yat paravaśaṃ karma tat tad yatnena varjayet 
yad yad ātmavaśaṃ tu syāt tat tat seveta yatnataḥ  Mn 
sarvaṃ paravaśaṃ duḥkhaṃ sarvam ātmavaśaṃ sukham 
etad vidyāt samāsena lakṣaṇaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ  Mn 
yat karma kurvato 'sya syāt paritoṣo 'ntarātmanaḥ 
tat prayatnena kurvīta viparītaṃ tu varjayet  Mn 
ācāryaṃ ca pravaktāraṃ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ gurum 
na hiṃsyād brāhmaṇān gāś ca sarvāṃś caiva tapasvinaḥ  Mn 
nāstikyaṃ vedanindāṃ ca devatānāṃ ca kutsanam 
dveṣaṃ dambhaṃ ca mānaṃ ca krodhaṃ taikṣṇyaṃ ca varjayet  Mn 
parasya daṇḍaṃ nodyacchet kruddho nainaṃ nipātayet 
anyatra putrāc chiṣyād vā śiṣṭyarthaṃ tāḍayet tu tau  Mn 
brāhmaṇāyāvaguryaiva dvijātir vadhakāmyayā 
śataṃ varṣāṇi tāmisre narake parivartate  Mn 
tāḍayitvā tṛṇenāpi saṃrambhān matipūrvakam 
ekaviṃśatīm ājātīḥ pāpayoniṣu jāyate  Mn 
ayudhyamānasyotpādya brāhmaṇasyāsṛg aṅgataḥ 
duḥkhaṃ sumahad āpnoti pretyāprājñatayā naraḥ  Mn 
śoṇitaṃ yāvataḥ pāṃsūn saṃgṛhṇāti mahītalāt 
tāvato 'bdān amutrānyaiḥ śoṇitotpādako 'dyate  Mn 
na kadā cid dvije tasmād vidvān avagured api 
na tāḍayet tṛṇenāpi na gātrāt srāvayed asṛk  Mn 
adhārmiko naro yo hi yasya cāpy anṛtaṃ dhanam 
hiṃsārataś ca yo nityaṃ nehāsau sukham edhate  Mn 
na sīdann api dharmeṇa mano 'dharme niveśayet 
adhārmikānāṃ pāpānām āśu paśyan viparyayam  Mn 
nādharmaś carito loke sadyaḥ phalati gaur iva 
śanair āvartyamānas tu kartur mūlāni kṛntati  Mn 
yadi nātmani putreṣu na cet putreṣu naptṛṣu 
na tv eva tu kṛto 'dharmaḥ kartur bhavati niṣphalaḥ  Mn 
adharmeṇaidhate tāvat tato bhadrāṇi paśyati 
tataḥ sapatnān jayati samūlas tu vinaśyati  Mn 
satyadharmāryavṛtteṣu śauce caivāramet sadā 
śiṣyāṃś ca śiṣyād dharmeṇa vāgbāhūdarasaṃyataḥ  Mn 
parityajed arthakāmau yau syātāṃ dharmavarjitau 
dharmaṃ cāpy asukhodarkaṃ lokasaṃkruṣṭam eva ca  Mn 
na pāṇipādacapalo na netracapalo 'nṛjuḥ 
na syād vākcapalaś caiva na paradrohakarmadhīḥ  Mn 
yenāsya pitaro yātā yena yātāḥ pitāmahāḥ 
tena yāyāt satāṃ mārgaṃ tena gacchan na riṣyati  Mn 
ṛtvikpurohitācāryair mātulātithisaṃśritaiḥ 
bālavṛddhāturair vaidyair jñātisaṃbandhibāndhavaiḥ  Mn 
mātāpitṛbhyāṃ jāmībhir bhrātrā putreṇa bhāryayā 
duhitrā dāsavargeṇa vivādaṃ na samācaret  Mn 
etair vivādān saṃtyajya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate 
etair jitaiś ca jayati sarvāṃl lokān imān gṛhī  Mn 
ācāryo brahmalokeśaḥ prājāpatye pitā prabhuḥ 
atithis tv indralokeśo devalokasya ca rtvijaḥ  Mn 
jāmayo 'psarasāṃ loke vaiśvadevasya bāndhavāḥ 
saṃbandhino hy apāṃ loke pṛthivyāṃ mātṛmātulau  Mn 
ākāśeśās tu vijñeyā bālavṛddhakṛśāturāḥ 
bhrātā jyeṣṭhaḥ samaḥ pitrā bhāryā putraḥ svakā tanuḥ  Mn 
chāyā svo dāsavargaś ca duhitā kṛpaṇaṃ param 
tasmād etair adhikṣiptaḥ sahetāsaṃjvaraḥ sadā  Mn 
pratigrahasamartho 'pi prasaṅgaṃ tatra varjayet 
pratigraheṇa hy asyāśu brāhmaṃ tejaḥ praśāmyati  Mn 
na dravyāṇām avijñāya vidhiṃ dharmyaṃ pratigrahe 
prājñaḥ pratigrahaṃ kuryād avasīdann api kṣudhā  Mn 
hiraṇyaṃ bhūmim aśvaṃ gām annaṃ vāsas tilān ghṛtam 
pratigṛhṇann avidvāṃs tu bhasmībhavati dāruvat  Mn 
hiraṇyam āyur annaṃ ca bhūr gauś cāpy oṣatas tanum 
aśvaś cakṣus tvacaṃ vāso ghṛtaṃ tejas tilāh prajāḥ  Mn 
atapās tv anadhīyānaḥ pratigraharucir dvijaḥ 
ambhasy aśmaplaveneva saha tenaiva majjati  Mn 
tasmād avidvān bibhiyād yasmāt tasmāt pratigrahāt 
svalpakenāpy avidvān hi paṅke gaur iva sīdati  Mn 
na vāry api prayacchet tu baiḍālavratike dvije 
na bakavratike pāpe nāvedavidi dharmavit  Mn 
triṣv apy eteṣu dattaṃ hi vidhināpy arjitaṃ dhanam 
dātur bhavaty anarthāya paratrādātur eva ca  Mn 
yathā plavenāupalena nimajjaty udake taran 
tathā nimajjato 'dhastād ajñau dātṛpratīcchakau  Mn 
dharmadhvajī sadā lubdhaś chādmiko lokadambhakaḥ 
baiḍālavratiko jñeyo hiṃsraḥ sarvābhisaṃdhakaḥ  Mn 
adhodṛṣṭir naiṣkṛtikaḥ svārthasādhanatatparaḥ 
śaṭho mithyāvinītaś ca bakavratacaro dvijaḥ  MnM 
ye bakavratino viprā ye ca mārjāraliṅginaḥ 
te patanty andhatāmisre tena pāpena karmaṇā  MnM 
na dharmasyāpadeśena pāpaṃ kṛtvā vrataṃ caret 
vratena pāpaṃ pracchādya kurvan strīśūdradambhanam  MnM 
pretyeha cedṛśā viprā garhyante brahmavādibhiḥ 
chadmanā caritaṃ yac ca vrataṃ rakṣāṃsi gacchati  MnM 
aliṅgī liṅgiveṣeṇa yo vṛttim upajīvati 
sa liṅgināṃ haraty enas tiryagyonau ca jāyate  MnM 
parakīyanipāneṣu na snāyād dhi kadā cana 
nipānakartuḥ snātvā tu duṣkṛtāṃśena lipyate  MnM 
yānaśayyāsanāny asya kūpodyānagṛhāṇi ca 
adattāny upayuñjāna enasaḥ syāt turīyabhāk  MnM 
nadīṣu devakhāteṣu taḍāgeṣu saraḥsu ca 
snānaṃ samācaren nityaṃ gartaprasravaṇeṣu ca  MnM 
yamān seveta satataṃ na nityaṃ niyamān budhaḥ 
yamān pataty akurvāṇo niyamān kevalān bhajan  MnM 
nāśrotriyatate yajñe grāmayājikṛte tathā 
striyā klībena ca hute bhuñjīta brāhmaṇaḥ kva cit  MnM 
aślīkam etat sādhūnāṃ yatra juhvaty amī haviḥ 
pratīpam etad devānāṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet  MnM 
mattakruddhāturāṇāṃ ca na bhuñjīta kadā cana 
keśakīṭāvapannaṃ ca padā spṛṣṭaṃ ca kāmataḥ  MnM 
bhrūṇaghnāvekṣitaṃ caiva saṃspṛṣṭaṃ cāpy udakyayā 
patatriṇāvalīḍhaṃ ca śunā saṃspṛṣṭam eva ca  MnM 
gavā cānnam upaghrātaṃ ghuṣṭānnaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ 
gaṇānnaṃ gaṇikānnaṃ ca viduṣā ca jugupsitam  MnM 
stenagāyanayoś cānnaṃ takṣṇo vārdhuṣikasya ca 
dīkṣitasya kadaryasya baddhasya nigaḍasya ca  MnM 
abhiśastasya ṣaṇḍhasya puṃścalyā dāmbhikasya ca 
śuktaṃ paryuṣitaṃ caiva śūdrasyocchiṣṭam eva ca  MnM 
cikitsakasya mṛgayoḥ krūrasyocchiṣṭabhojinaḥ 
ugrānnaṃ sūtikānnaṃ ca paryācāntam anirdaśam  MnM 
anarcitaṃ vṛthāmāṃsam avīrāyāś ca yoṣitaḥ 
dviṣadannaṃ nagaryannaṃ patitānnam avakṣutam  MnM 
piśunānṛtinoś cānnaṃ kratuvikrayiṇas tathā 
śailūṣatunnavāyānnaṃ kṛtaghnasyānnam eva ca  MnM 
karmārasya niṣādasya raṅgāvatārakasya ca 
suvarṇakartur veṇasya śastravikrayiṇas tathā  MnM 
śvavatāṃ śauṇḍikānāṃ ca cailanirṇejakasya ca 
rañjakasya nṛśaṃsasya yasya copapatir gṛhe  MnM 
mṛṣyanti ye copapatiṃ strījitānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ 
anirdaśaṃ ca pretānnam atuṣṭikaram eva ca  MnM 
rājānnaṃ teja ādatte śūdrānnaṃ brahmavarcasam 
āyuḥ suvarṇakārānnaṃ yaśaś carmāvakartinaḥ  MnM 
kārukānnaṃ prajāṃ hanti balaṃ nirṇejakasya ca 
gaṇānnaṃ gaṇikānnaṃ ca lokebhyaḥ parikṛntati  MnM 
pūyaṃ cikitsakasyānnaṃ puṃścalyās tv annam indriyam 
viṣṭhā vārdhuṣikasyānnaṃ śastravikrayiṇo malam  MnM 
ya ete 'nye tv abhojyānnāḥ kramaśaḥ parikīrtitāḥ 
teṣāṃ tvagasthiromāṇi vadanty annaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ  MnM 
bhuktvāto 'nyatam asyānnam amatyā kṣapaṇaṃ tryaham 
matyā bhuktvācaret kṛcchraṃ retoviṇmūtram eva ca  MnM 
nādyāc chūdrasya pakvānnaṃ vidvān aśrāddhino dvijaḥ 
ādadītāmam evāsmād avṛttāv ekarātrikam  MnM 
śrotriyasya kadaryasya vadānyasya ca vārdhuṣeḥ 
mīmāṃsitvobhayaṃ devāḥ samam annam akalpayan  MnM 
tān prajāpatir āhaitya mā kṛdhvaṃ viṣamaṃ samam 
śraddhāpūtaṃ vadānyasya hatam aśraddhayetarat  MnM 
śraddhayeṣṭaṃ ca pūrtaṃ ca nityaṃ kuryād atandritaḥ 
śraddhākṛte hy akṣaye te bhavataḥ svāgatair dhanaiḥ  MnM 
dānadharmaṃ niṣeveta nityam aiṣṭikapaurtikam 
parituṣṭena bhāvena pātram āsādya śaktitaḥ  MnM 
yat kiṃ cid api dātavyaṃ yācitenānasūyayā 
utpatsyate hi tat pātraṃ yat tārayati sarvataḥ  MnM 
vāridas tṛptim āpnoti sukham akṣayyam annadaḥ 
tilapradaḥ prajām iṣṭāṃ dīpadaś cakṣur uttamam  MnM 
bhūmido bhūmim āpnoti dīrgham āyur hiraṇyadaḥ 
gṛhado 'gryāṇi veśmāni rūpyado rūpam uttamam  MnM 
vāsodaś candrasālokyam aśvisālokyam aśvadaḥ 
anaḍuhaḥ śriyaṃ puṣṭāṃ godo bradhnasya viṣṭapam  MnM 
yānaśayyāprado bhāryām aiśvaryam abhayapradaḥ 
dhānyadaḥ śāśvataṃ saukhyaṃ brahmado brahmasārṣṭitām  MnM 
sarveṣām eva dānānāṃ brahmadānaṃ viśiṣyate 
vāryannagomahīvāsas tilakāñcanasarpiṣām  MnM 
yena yena tu bhāvena yad yad dānaṃ prayacchati 
tat tat tenaiva bhāvena prāpnoti pratipūjitaḥ  MnM 
yo 'rcitaṃ pratigṛhṇāti dadāty arcitam eva vā 
tāv ubhau gacchataḥ svargaṃ narakaṃ tu viparyaye  MnM 
na vismayeta tapasā vaded iṣṭvā ca nānṛtam 
nārto 'py apavaded viprān na dattvā parikīrtayet  MnM 
yajño 'nṛtena kṣarati tapaḥ kṣarati vismayāt 
āyur viprāpavādena dānaṃ ca parikīrtanāt  MnM 
dharmaṃ śanaiḥ saṃcinuyād valmīkam iva puttikāḥ 
paralokasahāyārthaṃ sarvabhūtāny apīḍayan  MnM 
nāmutra hi sahāyārthaṃ pitā mātā ca tiṣṭhataḥ 
na putradāraṃ na jñātir dharmas tiṣṭhati kevalaḥ  MnM 
ekaḥ prajāyate jantur eka eva pralīyate 
eko 'nubhuṅkte sukṛtam eka eva ca duṣkṛtam  MnM 
mṛtaṃ śarīram utsṛjya kāṣṭhaloṣṭasamaṃ kṣitau 
vimukhā bāndhavā yānti dharmas tam anugacchati  MnM 
tasmād dharmaṃ sahāyārthaṃ nityaṃ saṃcinuyāc chanaiḥ 
dharmeṇa hi sahāyena tamas tarati dustaram  MnM 
dharmapradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ tapasā hatakilbiṣam 
paralokaṃ nayaty āśu bhāsvantaṃ khaśarīriṇam  MnM 
uttamair uttamair nityaṃ saṃbandhān ācaret saha 
ninīṣuḥ kulam utkarṣam adhamān adhamāṃs tyajet  MnM 
uttamān uttamān eva gacchan hīnāṃs tu varjayan 
brāhmaṇaḥ śreṣṭhatām eti pratyavāyena śūdratām  MnM 
dṛḍhakārī mṛdur dāntaḥ krūrācārair asaṃvasan 
ahiṃsro damadānābhyāṃ jayet svargaṃ tathāvrataḥ  MnM 
edhodakaṃ mūlaphalam annam abhyudyataṃ ca yat 
sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyān madhv athābhayadakṣiṇām  MnM 
āhṛtābhyudyatāṃ bhikṣāṃ purastād apracoditām 
mene prajāpatir grāhyām api duṣkṛtakarmaṇaḥ  MnM 
nāśnanti pitaras tasya daśavarṣāṇi pañca ca 
na ca havyaṃ vahaty agnir yas tām abhyavamanyate  MnM 
śayyāṃ gṛhān kuśān gandhān apaḥ puṣpaṃ maṇīn dadhi 
dhānā matsyān payo māṃsaṃ śākaṃ caiva na nirṇudet  MnM 
gurūn bhṛtyāṃś cojjihīrṣann arciṣyan devatātithīn 
sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyān na tu tṛpyet svayaṃ tataḥ  MnM 
guruṣu tv abhyatīteṣu vinā vā tair gṛhe vasan 
ātmano vṛttim anvicchan gṛhṇīyāt sādhutaḥ sadā  MnM 
ārdhikaḥ kulamitraṃ ca gopālo dāsanāpitau 
ete śūdreṣu bhojyānnā yāś cātmānaṃ nivedayet  MnM 
yādṛśo 'sya bhaved ātmā yādṛśaṃ ca cikīrṣitam 
yathā copacared enaṃ tathātmānaṃ nivedayet  MnM 
yo 'nyathā santam ātmānam anyathā satsu bhāṣate
