sa pāpakṛttamo loke stena ātmāpahārakaḥ  MnM 
vācy arthā niyatāḥ sarve vāṅgūlā vāgviniḥsṛtāḥ 
tāṃs tu yaḥ stenayed vācaṃ sa sarvasteyakṛn naraḥ  MnM 
maharṣipitṛdevānāṃ gatvānṛṇyaṃ yathāvidhi 
putre sarvaṃ samāsajya vasen mādhyasthyam āśritaḥ  MnM 
ekākī cintayen nityaṃ vivikte hitam ātmanaḥ 
ekākī cintayāno hi paraṃ śreyo 'dhigacchati  MnM 
eṣoditā gṛhasthasya vṛttir viprasya śāśvatī 
snātakavratakalpaś ca sattvavṛddhikaraḥ śubhaḥ  MnM 
anena vipro vṛttena vartayan vedaśāstravit 
vyapetakalmaṣo nityaṃ brahmaloke mahīyate  MnM 
śrutvaitān ṛṣayo dharmān snātakasya yathoditān 
idam ūcur mahātmānam analaprabhavaṃ bhṛgum  Mn 
evaṃ yathoktaṃ viprāṇāṃ svadharmam anutiṣṭhatām 
kathaṃ mṛtyuḥ prabhavati vedaśāstravidāṃ prabho  Mn 
sa tān uvāca dharmātmā maharṣīn mānavo bhṛguḥ 
śrūyatāṃ yena doṣeṇa mṛtyur viprān jighāṃsati  Mn 
anabhyāsena vedānām ācārasya ca varjanāt 
ālasyād annadoṣāc ca mṛtyur viprāñ jighāṃsati  Mn 
laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva palāṇḍuṃ kavakāni ca 
abhakṣyāṇi dvijātīnām amedhyaprabhavāni ca  Mn 
lohitān vṛkṣaniryāsān vṛścanaprabhavāṃs tathā 
śeluṃ gavyaṃ ca peyūṣaṃ prayatnena vivarjayet  Mn 
vṛthā kṛsarasaṃyāvaṃ pāyasāpūpam eva ca 
anupākṛtamāṃsāni devānnāni havīṃṣi ca  Mn 
anirdaśāyā goḥ kṣīram auṣṭram aikaśaphaṃ tathā 
āvikaṃ saṃdhinīkṣīraṃ vivatsāyāś ca goḥ payaḥ  Mn 
āraṇyānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ mṛgāṇāṃ māhiṣaṃ vinā 
strīkṣīraṃ caiva varjyāni sarvaśuktāni caiva hi  Mn 
dadhi bhakṣyaṃ ca śukteṣu sarvaṃ ca dadhisaṃbhavam 
yāni caivābhiṣūyante puṣpamūlaphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ  Mn 
kravyādāñ śakunān sarvāṃs tathā grāmanivāsinaḥ 
anirdiṣṭāṃś caikaśaphāṃṣ ṭiṭṭibhaṃ ca vivarjayet  Mn 
kalaviṅkaṃ plavaṃ haṃsaṃ cakrāhvaṃ grāmakukkuṭam 
sārasaṃ rajjuvālaṃ ca dātyūhaṃ śukasārike  Mn 
pratudāñ jālapādāṃś ca koyaṣṭinakhaviṣkirān 
nimajjataś ca matsyādān saunaṃ vallūram eva ca  Mn 
bakaṃ caiva balākāṃ ca kākolaṃ khañjarīṭakam 
matsyādān viḍvarāhāṃś ca matsyān eva ca sarvaśaḥ  Mn 
yo yasya māṃsam aśnāti sa tanmāṃsāda ucyate 
matsyādaḥ sarvamāṃsādas tasmān matsyān vivarjayet  Mn 
pāṭhīnarohitāv ādyau niyuktau havyakavyayoḥ 
rājīvān siṃhatuṇḍāś ca saśalkāś caiva sarvaśaḥ  Mn 
na bhakṣayed ekacarān ajñātāṃś ca mṛgadvijān 
bhakṣyeṣv api samuddiṣṭān sarvān pañcanakhāṃs tathā  Mn 
śvāvidhaṃ śalyakaṃ godhāṃ khaḍgakūrmaśaśāṃs tathā 
bhakṣyān pañcanakheṣv āhur anuṣṭrāṃś caikatodatah  Mn 
chatrākaṃ viḍvarāhaṃ ca laśunaṃ grāmakukkuṭam 
palāṇḍuṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva matyā jagdhvā pated dvijaḥ  Mn 
amatyaitāni ṣaḍ jagdhvā kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ caret 
yaticāndrāyāṇaṃ vāpi śeṣeṣūpavased ahaḥ  Mn 
saṃvatsarasyaikam api caret kṛcchraṃ dvijottamaḥ 
ajñātabhuktaśuddhyarthaṃ jñātasya tu viṣeśataḥ  Mn 
yajñārthaṃ brāhmaṇair vadhyāḥ praśastā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ 
bhṛtyānāṃ caiva vṛttyartham agastyo hy ācarat purā  Mn 
babhūvur hi puroḍāśā bhakṣyāṇāṃ mṛgapakṣiṇām 
purāṇeṣv api yajñeṣu brahmakṣatrasaveṣu ca  Mn 
yat kiṃ cit snehasaṃyuktaṃ bhakṣyaṃ bhojyam agarhitam 
tat paryuṣitam apy ādyaṃ haviḥśeṣaṃ ca yad bhavet  Mn 
cirasthitam api tv ādyam asnehāktaṃ dvijātibhiḥ 
yavagodhūmajaṃ sarvaṃ payasaś caiva vikriyā  Mn 
etad uktaṃ dvijātīnāṃ bhakṣyābhakṣyam aśeṣataḥ 
māṃsasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ bhakṣaṇavarjane  Mn 
prokṣitaṃ bhakṣayen māṃsaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca kāmyayā 
yathāvidhi niyuktas tu prāṇānām eva cātyaye  Mn 
prāṇasyānnam idaṃ sarvaṃ prajāpatir akalpayat 
sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva sarvaṃ prāṇasya bhojanam  Mn 
carāṇām annam acarā daṃṣṭriṇām apy adaṃṣṭriṇaḥ 
ahastāś ca sahastānāṃ śūrāṇāṃ caiva bhīravaḥ  Mn 
nāttā duṣyaty adann ādyān prāṇino 'hanyahany api 
dhātraiva sṛṣṭā hy ādyāś ca prāṇino 'ttāra eva ca  Mn 
yajñāya jagdhir māṃsasyety eṣa daivo vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ 
ato 'nyathā pravṛttis tu rākṣaso vidhir ucyate  Mn 
krītvā svayaṃ vāpy utpādya paropakṛtam eva vā 
devān pitṝṃś cārcayitvā khādan māṃsaṃ na duṣyati  Mn 
nādyād avidhinā māṃsaṃ vidhijño 'nāpadi dvijaḥ 
jagdhvā hy avidhinā māṃsaṃ pretas tair adyate 'vaśaḥ  Mn 
na tādṛśaṃ bhavaty eno mṛgahantur dhanārthinaḥ 
yādṛśaṃ bhavati pretya vṛthāmāṃsāni khādataḥ  Mn 
niyuktas tu yathānyāyaṃ yo māṃsaṃ nātti mānavaḥ 
sa pretya paśutāṃ yāti saṃbhavān ekaviṃśatim  Mn 
asaṃskṛtān paśūn mantrair nādyād vipraḥ kadā cana 
mantrais tu saṃskṛtān adyāc chāśvataṃ vidhim āsthitaḥ  Mn 
kuryād ghṛtapaśuṃ saṅge kuryāt piṣṭapaśuṃ tathā 
na tv eva tu vṛthā hantuṃ paśum icchet kadā cana  Mn 
yāvanti paśuromāṇi tāvatkṛtvo ha māraṇam 
vṛthāpaśughnaḥ prāpnoti pretya janmani janmani  Mn 
yajñārthaṃ paśavaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayam eva svayaṃbhuvā 
yajño 'sya bhūtyai sarvasya tasmād yajñe vadho 'vadhaḥ  Mn 
oṣadhyaḥ paśavo vṛkṣās tiryañcaḥ pakṣiṇas tathā 
yajñārthaṃ nidhanaṃ prāptāḥ prāpnuvanty utsṛtīḥ punaḥ  Mn 
madhuparke ca yajñe ca pitṛdaivatakarmaṇi 
atraiva paśavo hiṃsyā nānyatrety abravīn manuḥ  Mn 
eṣv artheṣu paśūn hiṃsan vedatattvārthavid dvijaḥ 
ātmānaṃ ca paśuṃ caiva gamayaty uttamaṃ gatim  Mn 
gṛhe gurāv araṇye vā nivasann ātmavān dvijaḥ 
nāvedavihitāṃ hiṃsām āpady api samācaret  Mn 
yā vedavihitā hiṃsā niyatāsmiṃś carācare 
ahiṃsām eva tāṃ vidyād vedād dharmo hi nirbabhau  Mn 
yo 'hiṃsakāni bhūtāni hinasty ātmasukhecchayā 
sa jīvāṃś ca mṛtaś caiva na kva cit sukham edhate  Mn 
yo bandhanavadhakleśān prāṇināṃ na cikīrṣati 
sa sarvasya hitaprepsuḥ sukham atyantam aśnute  Mn 
yad dhyāyati yat kurute ratiṃ badhnāti yatra ca 
tad avāpnoty ayatnena yo hinasti na kiṃ cana  Mn 
nākṛtvā prāṇināṃ hiṃsāṃ māṃsam utpadyate kva cit 
na ca prāṇivadhaḥ svargyas tasmān māṃsaṃ vivarjayet  Mn 
samutpattiṃ ca māṃsasya vadhabandhau ca dehinām 
prasamīkṣya nivarteta sarvamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇāt  Mn 
na bhakṣayati yo māṃsaṃ vidhiṃ hitvā piśācavat 
na loke priyatāṃ yāti vyādhibhiś ca na pīḍyate  Mn 
anumantā viśasitā nihantā krayavikrayī 
saṃskartā copahartā ca khādakaś ceti ghātakāḥ  Mn 
svamāṃsaṃ paramāṃsena yo vardhayitum icchati 
anabhyarcya pitṝn devāṃs tato 'nyo nāsty apuṇyakṛt  Mn 
varṣe varṣe 'śvamedhena yo yajeta śataṃ samāḥ 
māṃsāni ca na khāded yas tayoḥ puṇyaphalaṃ samam  Mn 
phalamūlāśanair medhyair munyannānāṃ ca bhojanaiḥ 
na tat phalam avāpnoti yan māṃsaparivarjanāt  Mn 
māṃ sa bhakṣayitāmutra yasya māṃsam ihādmy aham 
etan māṃsasya māṃsatvaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ  Mn 
na māṃsabhakṣaṇe doṣo na madye na ca maithune 
pravṛttir eṣā bhūtānāṃ nivṛttis tu mahāphalā  Mn 
pretaśuddhiṃ pravakṣyāmi dravyaśuddhiṃ tathaiva ca 
caturṇām api varṇānāṃ yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ  Mn 
dantajāte 'nujāte ca kṛtacūḍe ca saṃsthite 
aśuddhā bāndhavāḥ sarve sūtake ca tathocyate  Mn ḥḥ
daśāhaṃ śāvam āśaucaṃ sapiṇḍeṣu vidhīyate 
arvāk saṃcayanād asthnāṃ tryaham ekāham eva vā  Mn 
sapiṇḍatā tu puruṣe saptame vinivartate 
samānodakabhāvas tu janmanāmnor avedane  Mn 
yathedaṃ śāvam āśaucaṃ sapiṇḍeṣu vidhīyate 
janane 'py evam eva syān nipuṇaṃ śuddhim icchatām  Mn 
sarveṣāṃ śāvam āśaucaṃ mātāpitros tu sūtakam 
sūtakaṃ mātur eva syād upaspṛśya pitā śuciḥ  MnM 
nirasya tu pumāñ śukram upaspṛsyaiva śudhyati 
baijikād abhisaṃbandhād anurundhyād aghaṃ tryaham  MnM 
ahnā caikena rātryā ca trirātrair eva ca tribhiḥ 
śavaspṛśo viśudhyanti tryahād udakadāyinaḥ  MnM 
guroḥ pretasya śiṣyas tu pitṛmedhaṃ samācaran 
pretahāraiḥ samaṃ tatra daśarātreṇa śudhyati  MnM 
rātribhir māsatulyābhir garbhasrāve viśudhyati 
rajasy uparate sādhvī snānena strī rajasvalā  MnM 
nṛṇām akṛtacūḍānāṃ viśuddhir naiśikī smṛtā 
nirvṛttacūḍakānāṃ tu trirātrāc chuddhir iṣyate  MnM 
ūnadvivārṣikaṃ pretaṃ nidadhyur bāndhavā bahiḥ 
alaṃkṛtya śucau bhūmāv asthisaṃcayanād ṛte  MnM 
nāsya kāryo 'gnisaṃskāro na ca kāryodakakriyā 
araṇye kāṣṭhavat tyaktvā kṣapeyus tryaham eva tu  MnM 
nātrivarṣasya kartavyā bāndhavair udakakriyā 
jātadantasya vā kuryur nāmni vāpi kṛte sati  MnM 
sabrahmacāriṇy ekāham atīte kṣapaṇaṃ smṛtam 
janmany ekodakānāṃ tu trirātrāc chuddhir iṣyate  MnM 
strīṇām asaṃskṛtānāṃ tu tryahāc chudhyanti bāndhavāḥ 
yathoktenaiva kalpena śudhyanti tu sanābhayaḥ  MnM 
akṣāralavaṇānnāḥ syur nimajjeyuś ca te tryaham 
māṃsāśanaṃ ca nāśnīyuḥ śayīraṃś ca pṛthak kṣitau  MnM 
saṃnidhāv eṣa vai kalpaḥ śāvāśaucasya kīrtitaḥ 
asaṃnidhāv ayaṃ jñeyo vidhiḥ saṃbandhibāndhavaiḥ  MnM 
vigataṃ tu videśasthaṃ śṛṇuyād yo hy anirdaśam 
yac cheṣaṃ daśarātrasya tāvad evāśucir bhavet  MnM 
atikrānte daśāhe ca trirātram aśucir bhavet 
saṃvatsare vyatīte tu spṛṣṭvaivāpo viśudhyati  MnM 
nirdaśaṃ jñātimaraṇaṃ śrutvā putrasya janma ca 
savāsā jalam āplutya śuddho bhavati mānavaḥ  MnM 
bāle deśāntarasthe ca pṛthakpiṇḍe ca saṃsthite 
savāsā jalam āplutya sadya eva viśudhyati  MnM 
antardaśāhe syātāṃ cet punar maraṇajanmanī 
tāvat syād aśucir vipro yāvat tat syād anirdaśam  MnM 
trirātram āhur āśaucam ācārye saṃsthite sati 
tasya putre ca patnyāṃ ca divārātram iti sthitiḥ  MnM 
śrotriye tūpasaṃpanne trirātram aśucir bhavet 
mātule pakṣiṇīṃ rātriṃ śiṣyartvigbāndhaveṣu ca  MnM 
prete rājani sajyotir yasya syād viṣaye sthitaḥ 
aśrotriye tv ahaḥ kṛtsnam anūcāne tathā gurau  MnM 
śuddhyed vipro daśāhena dvādaśāhena bhūmipaḥ 
vaiśyaḥ pañcadaśāhena śūdro māsena śudhyati  MnM 
na vardhayed aghāhāni pratyūhen nāgniṣu kriyāḥ 
na ca tatkarma kurvāṇaḥ sanābhyo 'py aśucir bhavet  MnM 
divākīrtim udakyāṃ ca patitaṃ sūtikāṃ tathā 
śavaṃ tatspṛṣṭinaṃ caiva spṛṣṭvā snānena śudhyati  MnM 
ācamya prayato nityaṃ japed aśucidarśane 
saurān mantrān yathotsāhaṃ pāvamānīś ca śaktitaḥ  MnM 
nāraṃ spṛṣṭvāsthi sasnehaṃ snātvā vipro viśudhyati 
ācamyaiva tu niḥsnehaṃ gām ālabhyārkam īkṣya vā  MnM 
ādiṣṭī nodakaṃ kuryād ā vratasya samāpanāt 
samāpte tūdakaṃ kṛtvā trirātreṇaiva śudhyati  MnM 
vṛthāsaṃkarajātānāṃ pravrajyāsu ca tiṣṭhatām 
ātmanas tyāgināṃ caiva nivartetodakakriyā  MnM 
pāṣaṇḍam āśritānāṃ ca carantīnāṃ ca kāmataḥ 
garbhabhartṛdruhāṃ caiva surāpīnāṃ ca yoṣitām  MnM 
ācāryaṃ svam upādhyāyaṃ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ gurum 
nirhṛtya tu vratī pretān na vratena viyujyate  MnM 
dakṣiṇena mṛtaṃ śūdraṃ puradvāreṇa nirharet 
paścimottarapūrvais tu yathāyogaṃ dvijanmanaḥ  MnM 
na rājñām aghadoṣo 'sti vratināṃ na ca sattriṇām 
aindraṃ sthānam upāsīnā brahmabhūtā hi te sadā  MnM 
rājño mahātmike sthāne sadyaḥśaucaṃ vidhīyate 
prajānāṃ parirakṣārtham āsanaṃ cātra kāraṇam  MnM 
ḍimbhāhavahatānāṃ ca vidyutā pārthivena ca 
gobrāhmaṇasya caivārthe yasya cecchati pārthivaḥ  MnM 
somāgnyarkānilendrāṇāṃ vittāppatyor yamasya ca 
aṣṭānāṃ lokapālānāṃ vapur dhārayate nṛpaḥ  MnM 
lokeśādhiṣṭhito rājā nāsyāśaucaṃ vidhīyate 
śaucāśaucaṃ hi martyānāṃ lokebhyaḥ prabhavāpyayau  MnM 
udyatair āhave śastraiḥ kṣatradharmahatasya ca 
sadyaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate yajñas tathāśaucam iti sthitiḥ  MnM 
vipraḥ śudhyaty apaḥ spṛṣṭvā kṣatriyo vāhanāyudham 
vaiśyaḥ pratodaṃ raśmīn vā yaṣṭiṃ śūdraḥ kṛtakriyaḥ  MnM 
etad vo 'bhihitaṃ śaucaṃ sapiṇḍeṣu dvijottamāḥ 
asapiṇḍeṣu sarveṣu pretaśuddhiṃ nibodhata  MnM 
asapiṇḍaṃ dvijaṃ pretaṃ vipro nirhṛtya bandhuvat 
viśudhyati trirātreṇa mātur āptāṃś ca bāndhavān  MnM 
yady annam atti teṣāṃ tu daśāhenaiva śudhyati 
anadann annam ahnaiva na cet tasmin gṛhe vaset  MnM 
anugamyecchayā pretaṃ jñātim ajñātim eva ca 
snātvā sacailaḥ spṛṣṭvāgniṃ ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyati  MnM 
na vipraṃ sveṣu tiṣṭhatsu mṛtaṃ śūdreṇa nāyayet 
asvargyā hy āhutiḥ sā syāc chūdrasaṃsparśadūṣitā  MnM 
jñānaṃ tapo 'gnir āhāro mṛn mano vāry upāñjanam 
vāyuḥ karmārkakālau ca śuddheḥ kartṝṇi dehinām  MnM 
sarveṣām eva śaucānām arthaśaucaṃ paraṃ smṛtaṃ 
yo 'rthe śucir hi sa śucir na mṛdvāriśuciḥ śuciḥ  MnM 
kṣāntyā śudhyanti vidvāṃso dānenākāryakāriṇaḥ 
pracchannapāpā japyena tapasā vedavittamāḥ  MnM 
mṛttoyaiḥ śudhyate śodhyaṃ nadī vegena śudhyati 
rajasā strī manoduṣṭā saṃnyāsena dvijottamāḥ  MnM 
adbhir gātrāṇi śudhyanti manaḥ satyena śudhyati 
vidyātapobhyāṃ bhūtātmā buddhir jñānena śudhyati  MnM 
eṣa śaucasya vaḥ proktaḥ śarīrasya vinirṇayaḥ 
nānāvidhānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ śuddheḥ śṛṇuta nirṇayam  MnM 
taijasānāṃ maṇīnāṃ ca sarvasyāśmamayasya ca 
bhasmanādbhir mṛdā caiva śuddhir uktā manīṣibhiḥ  MnM 
nirlepaṃ kāñcanaṃ bhāṇḍam adbhir eva viśudhyati 
abjam aśmamayaṃ caiva rājataṃ cānupaskṛtam  MnM 
apām agneś ca saṃyogād dhaimaṃ raupyaṃ ca nirbabhau 
tasmāt tayoḥ svayonyaiva nirṇeko guṇavattaraḥ  MnM 
tāmrāyaḥkāṃsyaraityānāṃ trapuṇaḥ sīsakasya ca 
śaucaṃ yathārhaṃ kartavyaṃ kṣārāmlodakavāribhiḥ  MnM 
dravāṇāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ śuddhir utpavanaṃ smṛtam 
prokṣaṇaṃ saṃhatānāṃ ca dāravāṇāṃ ca takṣaṇam  MnM 
mārjanaṃ yajñapātrāṇāṃ pāṇinā yajñakarmaṇi 
camasānāṃ grahāṇāṃ ca śuddhiḥ prakṣālanena tu  MnM 
carūṇāṃ sruksruvāṇāṃ ca śuddhir uṣṇena vāriṇā 
sphyaśūrpaśakaṭānāṃ ca musalolūkhalasya ca  MnM 
adbhis tu prokṣaṇaṃ śaucaṃ bahūnāṃ dhānyavāsasām 
prakṣālanena tv alpānām adbhiḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate  MnM 
cailavac carmaṇāṃ śuddhir vaidalānāṃ tathaiva ca 
śākamūlaphalānāṃ ca dhānyavac chuddhir iṣyate  MnM 
kauśeyāvikayor ūṣaiḥ kutapānām ariṣṭakaiḥ 
śrīphalair aṃśupaṭṭānāṃ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ  MnM 
kṣaumavac chaṅkhaśṛṅgāṇām asthidantamayasya ca 
śuddhir vijānatā kāryā gomūtreṇodakena vā  MnM 
prokṣaṇāt tṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca palālaṃ caiva śudhyati 
mārjanopāñjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛnmayam  MnM 
madyair mūtraiḥ purīṣair vā ṣṭhīvanaih pūyaśoṇitaiḥ 
saṃspṛṣṭaṃ naiva śuddhyeta punaḥpākena mṛnmayam  Mn 
saṃmārjanopāñjanena sekenollekhanena ca 
gavāṃ ca parivāsena bhūmiḥ śudhyati pañcabhiḥ  MnM 
pakṣijagdhaṃ gavā ghrātam avadhūtam avakṣutam 
dūṣitaṃ keśakīṭaiś ca mṛtprakṣepeṇa śudhyati  MnM 
yāvan nāpaity amedhyāktād gandho lepaś ca tatkṛtaḥ 
tāvan mṛdvāri cādeyaṃ sarvāsu dravyaśuddhiṣu  MnM 
trīṇi devāḥ pavitrāṇi brāhmaṇānām akalpayan 
adṛṣṭam adbhir nirṇiktaṃ yac ca vācā praśasyate  MnM 
āpaḥ śuddhā bhūmigatā vaitṛṣṇyaṃ yāsu gor bhavet 
avyāptāś ced amedhyena gandhavarṇarasānvitāḥ  MnM 
nityaṃ śuddhaḥ kāruhastaḥ paṇye yac ca prasāritam 
brahmacārigataṃ bhaikṣyaṃ nityaṃ medhyam iti sthitiḥ  MnM 
nityam āsyaṃ śuci strīṇāṃ śakuniḥ phalapātane 
prasrave ca śucir vatsaḥ śvā mṛgagrahaṇe śuciḥ  MnM 
śvabhir hatasya yan māṃsaṃ śuci tan manur abravīt 
kravyādbhiś ca hatasyānyaiś caṇḍālādyaiś ca dasyubhiḥ  MnM 
ūrdhvaṃ nābher yāni khāni tāni medhyāni sarvaśaḥ 
yāny adhas tāny amedhyāni dehāc caiva malāś cyutāḥ  MnM 
makṣikā vipruṣaś chāyā gaur aśvaḥ sūryaraśmayaḥ 
rajo bhūr vāyur agniś ca sparśe medhyāni nirdiśet  MnM 
viṇmūtrotsargaśuddhyarthaṃ mṛdvāry ādeyam arthavat 
daihikānāṃ malānāṃ ca śuddhiṣu dvādaśasv api  MnM 
vasā śukram asṛṅ majjā mūtraviṭ ghrāṇakarṇaviṭ 
śleśma aśru dūṣikā svedo dvādaśaite nṛṇāṃ malāḥ  MnM 
ekā liṅge gude tisras tathaikatra kare daśa 
ubhayoḥ sapta dātavyā mṛdaḥ śuddhim abhīpsatā  MnM 
etac chaucaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ dviguṇaṃ brahmacāriṇām 
triguṇaṃ syād vanasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ tu caturguṇam  MnM 
kṛtvā mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ vā khāny ācānta upaspṛśet 
vedam adhyeṣyamāṇaś ca annam aśnaṃś ca sarvadā  MnM 
trir ācāmed apaḥ pūrvaṃ dviḥ pramṛjyāt tato mukham 
śarīraṃ śaucam icchan hi strī śūdras tu sakṛt sakṛt  MnM 
śūdrāṇāṃ māsikaṃ kāryaṃ vapanaṃ nyāyavartinām 
vaiśyavac chaucakalpaś ca dvijocchiṣṭaṃ ca bhojanam  MnM 
nocchiṣṭaṃ kurvate mukhyā vipruṣo 'ṅgaṃ na yānti yāḥ 
na śmaśrūṇi gatāny āsyaṃ na dantāntaradhiṣṭhitam  MnM 
spṛśanti bindavaḥ pādau ya ācāmayataḥ parān 
bhaumikais te samā jñeyā na tair āprayato bhavet  MnM 
ucchiṣṭena tu saṃspṛṣṭo dravyahastaḥ kathaṃ cana 
anidhāyaiva tad dravyam ācāntaḥ śucitām iyāt  MnM 
vānto viriktaḥ snātvā tu ghṛtaprāśanam ācaret 
ācāmed eva bhuktvānnaṃ snānaṃ maithuninaḥ smṛtam  MnM 
suptvā kṣutvā ca bhuktvā ca niṣṭhīvyoktvānṛtāni ca 
pītvāpo 'dhyeṣyamāṇaś ca ācāmet prayato 'pi san  MnM 
eṣāṃ śaucavidhiḥ kṛtsno dravyaśuddhis tathaiva ca 
ukto vaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ strīṇāṃ dharmān nibodhata  MnM 
bālayā vā yuvatyā vā vṛddhayā vāpi yoṣitā 
na svātantryeṇa kartavyaṃ kiṃ cid kāryaṃ gṛheṣv api  MnM 
bālye pitur vaśe tiṣṭhet pāṇigrāhasya yauvane 
putrāṇāṃ bhartari prete na bhajet strī svatantratām  MnM 
pitrā bhartrā sutair vāpi necched viraham ātmanaḥ 
eṣāṃ hi viraheṇa strī garhye kuryād ubhe kule  MnM 
sadā prahṛṣṭayā bhāvyaṃ gṛhakārye ca dakṣayā 
susaṃskṛtopaskarayā vyaye cāmuktahastayā  MnM 
yasmai dadyāt pitā tv enāṃ bhrātā vānumate pituḥ 
taṃ śuśrūṣeta jīvantaṃ saṃsthitaṃ ca na laṅghayet  MnM 
maṅgalārthaṃ svastyayanaṃ yajñaś cāsāṃ prajāpateḥ 
prayujyate vivāhe tu pradānaṃ svāmyakāraṇam  MnM 
anṛtāv ṛtukāle ca mantrasaṃskārakṛt patiḥ 
sukhasya nityaṃ dāteha paraloke ca yoṣitaḥ  MnM 
viśīlaḥ kāmavṛtto vā guṇair vā parivarjitaḥ 
upacāryaḥ striyā sādhvyā satataṃ devavat patiḥ  MnM 
nāsti strīṇāṃ pṛthag yajño na vrataṃ nāpy upoṣaṇam 
patiṃ śuśrūṣate yena tena svarge mahīyate  MnM 
pāṇigrāhasya sādhvī strī jīvato vā mṛtasya vā 
patilokam abhīpsantī nācaret kiṃ cid apriyam  MnM 
kāmaṃ tu ksapayed dehaṃ puṣpamūlaphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ 
na tu nāmāpi gṛhṇīyāt patyau prete parasya tu  MnM 
āsītā maraṇāt ksāntā niyatā brahmacāriṇī 
yo dharma ekapatnīnāṃ kāṅkṣantī tam anuttamam  MnM 
anekāni sahasrāṇi kumārabrahmacāriṇām 
divaṃ gatāni viprāṇām akṛtvā kulasaṃtatim  MnM 
mṛte bhartari sāḍhvī strī brahmacarye vyavasthitā 
svargaṃ gacchaty aputrāpi yathā te brahmacāriṇaḥ  MnM 
apatyalobhād yā tu strī bhartāram ativartate 
seha nindām avāpnoti paralokāc ca hīyate  MnM 
nānyotpannā prajāstīha na cāpy anyaparigrahe 
na dvitīyaś ca sādhvīnāṃ kva cid bhartopadiśyate  MnM 
patiṃ hitvāpakṛṣṭaṃ svam utkṛṣṭaṃ yā niṣevate 
nindyaiva sā bhavel loke parapūrveti cocyate  MnM 
vyabhicārāt tu bhartuḥ strī loke prāpnoti nindyatām 
śṛgālayoniṃ prāpnoti pāparogaiś ca pīḍyate  MnM 
patiṃ yā nābhicarati manovāgdehasaṃyutā 
sā bhartṛlokam āpnoti sadbhiḥ sādhvīti cocyate  MnM 
anena nārī vṛttena manovāgdehasaṃyatā 
ihāgryāṃ kīrtim āpnoti patilokaṃ paratra ca  MnM 
evaṃ vṛttāṃ savarṇāṃ strīṃ dvijātiḥ pūrvamāriṇīm 
dāhayed agnihotreṇa yajñapātraiś ca dharmavit  MnM 
bhāryāyai pūrvamāriṇyai dattvāgnīn antyakarmaṇi 
punar dārakriyāṃ kuryāt punar ādhānam eva ca  MnM 
anena vidhinā nityaṃ pañcayajñān na hāpayet 
dvitīyam āyuṣo bhāgaṃ kṛtadāro gṛhe vaset  MnM 
evaṃ gṛhāśrame sthitvā vidhivat snātako dvijaḥ 
vane vaset tu niyato yathāvad vijitendriyaḥ  Mn 
gṛhasthas tu yathā paśyed valīpalitam ātmanaḥ 
apatyasyaiva cāpatyaṃ tadāraṇyaṃ samāśrayet  Mn 
saṃtyajya grāmyam āhāraṃ sarvaṃ caiva paricchadam 
putreṣu bhāryāṃ nikṣipya vanaṃ gacchet sahaiva vā  Mn 
agnihotraṃ samādāya gṛhyaṃ cāgniparicchadam 
grāmād araṇyaṃ niḥsṛtya nivasen niyatendriyaḥ  Mn 
munyannair vividhair medhyaiḥ śākamūlaphalena vā 
etān eva mahāyajñān nirvaped vidhipūrvakam  Mn 
vasīta carma cīraṃ vā sāyaṃ snāyāt prage tathā 
jaṭāś ca bibhṛyān nityaṃ śmaśrulomanakhāni ca  Mn 
yadbhakṣyaṃ syād tato dadyād baliṃ bhikṣāṃ ca śaktitaḥ 
ammūlaphalabhikṣābhir arcayed āśramāgatān  Mn 
svādhyāye nityayuktaḥ syād dānto maitraḥ samāhitaḥ 
dātā nityam anādātā sarvabhūtānukampakaḥ  Mn 
vaitānikaṃ ca juhuyād agnihotraṃ yathāvidhi 
darśam askandayan parva paurṇamāsaṃ ca yogataḥ  Mn 
ṛkṣeṣṭyāgrayaṇaṃ caiva cāturmāsyāni cāharet 
turāyaṇaṃ ca kramaśo dakṣasyāyanam eva ca  Mn 
vāsantaśāradair medhyair munyannaiḥ svayam āhṛtaiḥ 
puroḍāśāṃś carūṃś caiva vidhivan nirvapet pṛthak  Mn 
devatābhyas tu tad dhutvā vanyaṃ medhyataraṃ haviḥ 
śeṣam ātmani yuñjīta lavaṇaṃ ca svayaṃ kṛtam  Mn 
sthalajāudakaśākāni puṣpamūlaphalāni ca 
medhyavṛkṣodbhavāny adyāt snehāṃś ca phalasaṃbhavān  Mn 
varjayen madhu māṃsaṃ ca bhaumāni kavakāni ca 
bhūstṛṇaṃ śigrukaṃ caiva śleśmātakaphalāni ca  Mn 
tyajed āśvayuje māsi munyannaṃ pūrvasaṃcitam 
jīrṇāni caiva vāsāṃsi śākamūlaphalāni ca  Mn 
na phālakṛṣṭam aśnīyād utsṛṣṭam api kena cit 
na grāmajātāny ārto 'pi mūlāṇi ca phalāni ca  Mn 
agnipakvāśano vā syāt kālapakvabhug eva vā 
aśmakuṭṭo bhaved vāpi dantolūkhaliko 'pi vā  Mn 
sadyaḥ prakṣālako vā syān māsasaṃcayiko 'pi vā 
ṣaṇmāsanicayo vā syāt samānicaya eva vā  Mn 
naktaṃ cānnaṃ samaśnīyād divā vāhṛtya śaktitaḥ 
caturthakāliko vā syāt syād vāpy aṣṭamakālikaḥ  Mn 
cāndrāyaṇavidhānair vā śuklakṛṣṇe ca vartayet 
pakṣāntayor vāpy aśnīyād yavāgūṃ kvathitāṃ sakṛt  Mn 
puṣpamūlaphalair vāpi kevalair vartayet sadā 
kālapakvaiḥ svayaṃ śīrṇair vaikhānasamate sthitaḥ  Mn 
bhūmau viparivarteta tiṣṭhed vā prapadair dinam 
sthānāsanābhyāṃ viharet savaneṣūpayann apaḥ  Mn 
grīṣme pañcatapās tu syād varṣāsv abhrāvakāśikaḥ 
ārdravāsās tu hemante kramaśo vardhayaṃs tapaḥ  Mn 
upaspṛśaṃs triṣavaṇaṃ pitṝn devāṃś ca tarpayet 
tapaś caraṃś cogrataraṃ śoṣayed deham ātmanaḥ  Mn 
agnīn ātmani vaitānān samāropya yathāvidhi 
anagnir aniketaḥ syān munir mūlaphalāśanaḥ  Mn 
aprayatnaḥ sukhārtheṣu brahmacārī dharāśayaḥ 
śaraṇeṣv amamaś caiva vṛkṣamūlaniketanaḥ  Mn 
tāpaseṣv eva vipreṣu yātrikaṃ bhaikṣam āharet 
gṛhamedhiṣu cānyeṣu dvijeṣu vanavāsiṣu  Mn 
grāmād āhṛtya vāśnīyād aṣṭau grāsān vane vasan 
pratigṛhya puṭenaiva pāṇinā śakalena vā  Mn 
etāś cānyāś ca seveta dīkṣā vipro vane vasan 
vividhāś cāupaniṣadīr ātmasaṃsiddhaye śrutīḥ  Mn 
ṛṣibhir brāhmaṇaiś caiva gṛhasthair eva sevitāḥ 
vidyātapovivṛddhyarthaṃ śarīrasya ca śuddhaye  Mn 
aparājitāṃ vāsthāya vrajed diśam ajihmagaḥ 
ā nipātāc charīrasya yukto vāryanilāśanaḥ  Mn 
āsāṃ maharṣicaryāṇāṃ tyaktvānyatamayā tanum 
vītaśokabhayo vipro brahmaloke mahīyate  Mn 
vaneṣu ca vihṛtyaivaṃ tṛtīyaṃ bhāgam āyuṣaḥ 
caturtham āyuṣo bhāgaṃ tyakvā saṅgān parivrajet  Mn 
āśramād āśramaṃ gatvā hutahomo jitendriyaḥ 
bhikṣābalipariśrāntaḥ pravrajan pretya vardhate  Mn 
ṛṇāni trīṇy apākṛtya mano mokṣe niveśayet 
anapākṛtya mokṣaṃ tu sevamāno vrajaty adhaḥ  Mn 
adhītya vidhivad vedān putrāṃś cotpādya dharmataḥ 
iṣṭvā ca śaktito yajñair mano mokṣe niveśayet  Mn 
anadhītya dvijo vedān anutpādya tathā sutān 
aniṣṭvā caiva yajñaiś ca mokṣam icchan vrajaty adhaḥ  Mn 
prājāpatyaṃ nirupyeṣṭiṃ sarvavedasadakṣiṇām 
ātmany agnīn samāropya brāhmaṇaḥ pravrajed gṛhāt  Mn 
yo dattvā sarvabhūtebhyaḥ pravrajaty abhayaṃ gṛhāt 
tasya tejomayā lokā bhavanti brahmavādinaḥ  Mn 
yasmād aṇv api bhūtānāṃ dvijān notpadyate bhayam 
tasya dehād vimuktasya bhayaṃ nāsti kutaś cana  Mn 
agārād abhiniṣkrāntaḥ pavitropacito muniḥ 
samupoḍheṣu kāmeṣu nirapekṣaḥ parivrajet  Mn 
eka eva caren nityaṃ siddhyartham asahāyavān 
siddhim ekasya saṃpaśyan na jahāti na hīyate  Mn 
anagnir aniketaḥ syād grāmam annārtham āśrayet 
upekṣako 'saṃkusuko munir bhāvasamāhitaḥ  Mn 
kapālaṃ vṛkṣamūlāni kucelam asahāyatā 
samatā caiva sarvasminn etan muktasya lakṣaṇam  Mn 
nābhinandeta maraṇaṃ nābhinandeta jīvitam 
kālam eva pratīkṣeta nirveśaṃ bhṛtako yathā  Mn 
dṛṣṭipūtaṃ nyaset pādaṃ vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ pibet 
satyapūtāṃ vaded vācaṃ manaḥpūtaṃ samācaret  Mn 
ativādāṃs titikṣeta nāvamanyeta kaṃ cana 
na cemaṃ deham āśritya vairaṃ kurvīta kena cit  Mn 
kruddhyantaṃ na pratikrudhyed ākruṣṭaḥ kuśalaṃ vadet 
saptadvārāvakīrṇāṃ ca na vācam anṛtāṃ vadet  Mn 
adhyātmaratir āsīno nirapekṣo nirāmiṣaḥ 
ātmanaiva sahāyena sukhārthī vicared iha  Mn 
na cotpātanimittābhyāṃ na nakṣatrāṅgavidyayā 
nānuśāsanavādābhyāṃ bhikṣāṃ lipseta karhi cit  Mn 
na tāpasair brāhmaṇair vā vayobhir api vā śvabhiḥ 
ākīrṇaṃ bhikṣukair vānyair agāram upasaṃvrajet  Mn 
kḷptakeśanakhaśmaśruḥ pātrī daṇḍī kusumbhavān 
vicaren niyato nityaṃ sarvabhūtāny apīḍayan  Mn 
ataijasāni pātrāṇi tasya syur nirvraṇāni ca 
teṣām adbhiḥ smṛtaṃ śaucaṃ camasānām ivādhvare  Mn 
alābuṃ dārupātraṃ ca mṛṇmayaṃ vaidalaṃ tathā 
etāṇi yatipātrāṇi manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo 'bravīt  Mn 
ekakālaṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ na prasajjeta vistare 
bhaikṣe prasakto hi yatir viṣayeṣv api sajjati  Mn 
vidhūme sannamusale vyaṅgāre bhuktavajjane 
vṛtte śarāvasaṃpāte bhikṣāṃ nityaṃ yatiś caret  Mn 
alābhe na viṣadī syāl lābhe caiva na harṣayet 
prāṇayātrikamātraḥ syān mātrāsaṅgād vinirgataḥ  Mn 
abhipūjitalābhāṃs tu jugupsetaiva sarvaśaḥ 
abhipūjitalābhaiś ca yatir mukto 'pi badhyate  Mn 
alpānnābhyavahāreṇa rahaḥsthānāsanena ca 
hriyamāṇāni viṣayair indriyāṇi nivartayet  Mn 
indriyāṇāṃ nirodhena rāgadveśakṣayeṇa ca 
ahiṃsayā ca bhūtānām amṛtatvāya kalpate  Mn 
avekṣeta gatīr nṝṇāṃ karmadoṣasamudbhavāḥ 
niraye caiva patanaṃ yātanāś ca yamakṣaye  Mn 
viprayogaṃ priyaiś caiva saṃyogaṃ ca tathāpriyaiḥ 
jarayā cābhibhavanaṃ vyādhibhiś copapīḍanaṃ  Mn 
dehād utkramaṇaṃ cāṣmāt punar garbhe ca saṃbhavam 
yonikoṭisahasreṣu sṛtīś cāsyāntarātmanaḥ  Mn 
adharmaprabhavaṃ caiva duḥkhayogaṃ śarīriṇām 
dharmārthaprabhavaṃ caiva sukhasaṃyogam akṣayam  Mn 
sūkṣmatāṃ cānvavekṣeta yogena paramātmanaḥ 
deheṣu ca samutpattim uttameṣv adhameṣu ca  Mn 
dūṣito 'pi cared dharmaṃ yatra tatrāśrame rataḥ 
samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu na liṅgaṃ dharmakāraṇam  Mn 
phalaṃ katakavṛkṣasya yady apy ambuprasādakam 
na nāmagrahaṇād eva tasya vāri prasīdati  Mn 
saṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ jantūnāṃ rātrāv ahani vā sadā 
śarīrasyātyaye caiva samīkṣya vasudhāṃ caret  Mn 
ahnā rātryā ca yāñ jantūn hinasty ajñānato yatiḥ 
teṣāṃ snātvā viśuddhyarthaṃ prāṇāyāmān ṣaḍ ācaret  Mn 
prāṇāyāmā brāhmaṇasya trayo 'pi vidhivat kṛtāḥ 
vyāhṛtipraṇavair yuktā vijñeyaṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ  Mn 
dahyante dhmāyamānānāṃ dhātūnāṃ hi yathā malāḥ 
tathendriyāṇāṃ dahyante doṣāḥ prāṇasya nigrahāt  Mn 
prāṇāyamair dahed doṣān dhāraṇābhiś ca kilbiṣam 
pratyāhāreṇa saṃsargān dhyānenānīśvarān guṇān  Mn 
uccāvaceṣu bhūteṣu durjñeyām akṛtātmabhiḥ 
dhyānayogena saṃpaśyed gatim asyāntarātmanaḥ  Mn 
samyagdarśanasaṃpannaḥ karmabhir na nibadhyate 
darśanena vihīnas tu saṃsāraṃ pratipadyate  Mn 
ahiṃsayendriyāsaṅgair vaidikaiś caiva karmabhiḥ 
tapasaś caraṇaiś cograiḥ sādhayantīha tatpadam  Mn 
asthisthūṇaṃ snāyuyutaṃ māṃsaśoṇitalepanam 
carmāvanaddhaṃ durgandhi pūrṇaṃ mūtrapurīṣayoḥ  Mn 
jarāśokasamāviṣṭaṃ rogāyatanam āturam 
rajasvalam anityaṃ ca bhūtāvāsam imaṃ tyajet  Mn 
nadīkūlaṃ yathā vṛkṣo vṛkṣaṃ vā śakunir yathā 
tathā tyajann imaṃ dehaṃ kṛcchrād grāhād vimucyate  Mn 
priyeṣu sveṣu sukṛtam apriyeṣu ca duṣkṛtam 
visṛjya dhyānayogena brahmābhyeti sanātanam  Mn 
yadā bhāvena bhavati sarvabhāveṣu niḥspṛhaḥ 
tadā sukham avāpnoti pretya ceha ca śāśvatam  Mn 
anena vidhinā sarvāṃs tyaktvā saṅgāñ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ 
sarvadvandvavinirmukto brahmaṇy evāvatiṣṭhate  Mn 
dhyānikaṃ sarvam evaitad yad etad abhiśabditam 
na hy anadhyātmavit kaś cit kriyāphalam upāśnute  Mn 
adhiyajñaṃ brahma japed ādhidaivikam eva ca 
ādhyātmikaṃ ca satataṃ vedāntābhihitaṃ ca yat  Mn 
idaṃ śaraṇam ajñānām idam eva vijānatām 
idam anvicchatāṃ svargam idam ānantyam icchatām  Mn 
anena kramayogena parivrajati yo dvijaḥ 
sa vidhūyeha pāpmānaṃ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati  Mn 
eṣa dharmo 'nuśiṣṭo vo yatīnāṃ niyatātmanām 
vedasaṃnyāsikānāṃ tu karmayogaṃ nibodhata  Mn 
brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca vānaprastho yatis tathā 
ete gṛhasthaprabhavāś catvāraḥ pṛthag āśramāḥ  Mn 
sarve 'pi kramaśas tv ete yathāśāstraṃ niṣevitāḥ 
yathoktakāriṇaṃ vipraṃ nayanti paramāṃ gatim  Mn 
sarveṣām api caiteṣāṃ vedasmṛtividhānataḥ 
gṛhastha ucyate śreṣṭhaḥ sa trīn etān bibharti hi  Mn 
yathā nadīnadāḥ sarve sāgare yānti saṃsthitim 
tathaivāśramiṇaḥ sarve gṛhasthe yānti saṃsthitim  Mn 
caturbhir api caivaitair nityam āśramibhir dvijaiḥ 
daśalakṣaṇako dharmaḥ sevitavyaḥ prayatnataḥ  Mn 
dhṛtiḥ kṣamā damo 'steyaṃ śaucam indriyanigrahaḥ 
dhīr vidyā satyam akrodho daśakaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam  Mn 
daśa lakṣaṇāni dharmasya ye viprāḥ samadhīyate 
adhītya cānuvartante te yānti paramāṃ gatim  Mn 
daśalakṣaṇakaṃ dharmam anutiṣṭhan samāhitaḥ 
vedāntaṃ vidhivac chrutvā saṃnyased anṛṇo dvijaḥ  Mn 
saṃnyasya sarvakarmāṇi karmadoṣān apānudan 
niyato vedam abhyasya putraiśvarye sukhaṃ vaset  Mn 
evaṃ saṃnyasya karmāṇi svakāryaparamo 'spṛhaḥ 
saṃnyāsenāpahatyainaḥ prāpnoti paramaṃ gatim  Mn 
eṣa vo 'bhihito dharmo brāhmaṇasya caturvidhaḥ 
puṇyo 'kṣayaphalaḥ pretya rājñāṃ dharmaṃ nibodhata  Mn 
rājadharmān pravakṣyāmi yathāvṛtto bhaven nṛpaḥ 
saṃbhavaś ca yathā tasya siddhiś ca paramā yathā  Mn 
brāhmaṃ prāptena saṃskāraṃ kṣatriyeṇa yathāvidhi 
sarvasyāsya yathānyāyaṃ kartavyaṃ parirakṣaṇam  Mn 
arājake hi loke 'smin sarvato vidruto bhayāt 
rakṣārtham asya sarvasya rājānam asṛjat prabhuḥ  Mn 
indrānilayamārkāṇām agneś ca varuṇasya ca 
candravitteśayoś caiva mātrā nirhṛtya śāśvatīḥ  Mn 
yasmād eṣāṃ surendrāṇāṃ mātrābhyo nirmito nṛpaḥ 
tasmād abhibhavaty eṣa sarvabhūtāni tejasā  Mn 
tapaty ādityavac caiṣa cakṣūṃṣi ca manāṃsi ca 
na cainaṃ bhuvi śaknoti kaś cid apy abhivīkṣitum  Mn 
so 'gnir bhavati vāyuś ca so 'rkaḥ somaḥ sa dharmarāṭ 
sa kuberaḥ sa varuṇaḥ sa mahendraḥ prabhāvataḥ  Mn 
bālo 'pi nāvamāntavyo manuṣya iti bhūmipaḥ 
mahatī devatā hy eṣā nararūpeṇa tiṣṭhati  Mn 
ekam eva dahaty agnir naraṃ durupasarpiṇam 
kulaṃ dahati rājāgniḥ sapaśudravyasaṃcayam  Mn 
kāryaṃ so 'vekṣya śaktiṃ ca deśakālau ca tattvataḥ 
kurute dharmasiddhyarthaṃ viśvarūpaṃ punaḥ punaḥ  Mn 
yasya prasāde padmā śrīr vijayaś ca parākrame 
mṛtyuś ca vasati krodhe sarvatejomayo hi saḥ  Mn 
taṃ yas tu dveṣṭi saṃmohāt sa vinaśyaty asaṃśayam 
tasya hy āśu vināśāya rājā prakurute manaḥ  Mn 
tasmād dharmaṃ yam iṣṭeṣu sa vyavasyen narādhipaḥ 
aniṣṭaṃ cāpy aniṣṭeṣu taṃ dharmaṃ na vicālayet  Mn 
tasyārthe sarvabhūtānāṃ goptāraṃ dharmam ātmajam 
brahmatejomayaṃ daṇḍam asṛjat pūrvam īśvaraḥ  Mn 
tasya sarvāṇi bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca 
bhayād bhogāya kalpante svadharmān na calanti ca  Mn 
taṃ deśakālau śaktiṃ ca vidyāṃ cāvekṣya tattvataḥ 
yathārhataḥ saṃpraṇayen nareṣv anyāyavartiṣu  Mn 
sa rājā puruṣo daṇḍaḥ sa netā śāsitā ca saḥ 
caturṇām āśramāṇāṃ ca dharmasya pratibhūḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
daṇḍaḥ śāsti prajāḥ sarvā daṇḍa evābhirakṣati 
daṇḍaḥ supteṣu jāgarti daṇḍaṃ dharmaṃ vidur budhāḥ  Mn 
samīkṣya sa dhṛtaḥ samyak sarvā rañjayati prajāḥ 
asamīkṣya praṇītas tu vināśayati sarvataḥ  Mn 
yadi na praṇayed rājā daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣv atandritaḥ 
śūle matsyān ivāpakṣyan durbalān balavattarāḥ  Mn 
adyāt kākaḥ puroḍāśaṃ śvā ca lihyād dhavis tathā 
svāmyaṃ ca na syāt kasmiṃś cit pravartetādharottaram  Mn 
sarvo daṇḍajito loko durlabho hi śucir naraḥ 
daṇḍasya hi bhayāt sarvaṃ jagad bhogāya kalpate  Mn 
devadānavagandharvā rakṣāṃsi patagoragāḥ 
te 'pi bhogāya kalpante daṇḍenaiva nipīḍitāḥ  Mn 
duṣyeyuḥ sarvavarṇāś ca bhidyeran sarvasetavaḥ 
sarvalokaprakopaś ca bhaved daṇḍasya vibhramāt  Mn 
yatra śyāmo lohitākṣo daṇḍaś carati pāpahā 
prajās tatra na muhyanti netā cet sādhu paśyati  Mn 
tasyāhuḥ saṃpraṇetāraṃ rājānaṃ satyavādinam 
samīkṣyakāriṇaṃ prājñaṃ dharmakāmārthakovidam  Mn 
taṃ rājā praṇayan samyak trivargeṇābhivardhate 
kāmātmā viṣamaḥ kṣudro daṇḍenaiva nihanyate  Mn 
daṇḍo hi sumahattejo durdharaś cākṛtātmabhiḥ 
dharmād vicalitaṃ hanti nṛpam eva sabāndhavam  Mn 
tato durgaṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca lokaṃ ca sacarācaram 
antarikṣagatāṃś caiva munīn devāṃś ca pīḍayet  Mn 
so 'sahāyena mūḍhena lubdhenākṛtabuddhinā 
na śakyo nyāyato netuṃ saktena viṣayeṣu ca  Mn 
śucinā satyasaṃdhena yathāśāstrānusāriṇā 
praṇetuṃ śakyate daṇḍaḥ susahāyena dhīmatā  Mn 
svarāṣṭre nyāyavṛttaḥ syād bhṛśadaṇḍaś ca śatruṣu 
suhṛtsv ajihmaḥ snigdheṣu brāhmaṇeṣu kṣamānvitaḥ  Mn 
evaṃvṛttasya nṛpateḥ śiloñchenāpi jīvataḥ 
vistīryate yaśo loke tailabindur ivāmbhasi  Mn 
atas tu viparītasya nṛpater ajitātmanaḥ 
saṃkṣipyate yaśo loke ghṛtabindur ivāmbhasi  Mn 
sve sve dharme niviṣṭānāṃ sarveṣām anupūrvaśaḥ 
varṇānām āśramāṇāṃ ca rājā sṛṣṭo 'bhirakṣitā  Mn 
tena yad yat sabhṛtyena kartavyaṃ rakṣatā prajāḥ 
tat tad vo 'haṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ  Mn 
brāhmaṇān paryupāsīta prātar utthāya pārthivaḥ 
traividyavṛddhān viduṣas tiṣṭhet teṣāṃ ca śāsane  Mn 
vṛddhāṃś ca nityaṃ seveta viprān vedavidaḥ śucīn 
vṛddhasevī hi satataṃ rakṣobhir api pūjyate  Mn 
tebhyo 'dhigacched vinayaṃ vinītātmāpi nityaśaḥ 
vinītātmā hi nṛpatir na vinaśyati karhi cit  Mn 
bahavo 'vinayān naṣṭā rājānaḥ saparicchadāḥ 
vanasthā api rājyāni vinayāt pratipedire  Mn 
veno vinaṣṭo 'vinayān nahuṣaś caiva pārthivaḥ 
sudāḥ paijavanaś caiva sumukho nimir eva ca  Mn 
pṛthus tu vinayād rājyaṃ prāptavān manur eva ca 
kuberaś ca dhanaiśvaryaṃ brāhmaṇyaṃ caiva gādhijaḥ  Mn 
traividyebhyas trayīṃ vidyāṃ daṇḍanītiṃ ca śāśvatīm 
ānvīkṣikīṃ cātmavidyāṃ vārtārambhāṃś ca lokataḥ  Mn 
indriyāṇāṃ jaye yogaṃ samātiṣṭhed divāniśam 
jitendriyo hi śaknoti vaśe sthāpayituṃ prajāḥ  Mn 
daśa kāmasamutthāni tathāṣṭau krodhajāni ca 
vyasanāni durantāni prayatnena vivarjayet  Mn 
kāmajeṣu prasakto hi vyasaneṣu mahīpatiḥ 
viyujyate 'rthadharmābhyāṃ krodhajeṣv ātmanaiva tu  Mn 
mṛgayākṣo divāsvapnaḥ parivādaḥ striyo madaḥ 
tauryatrikaṃ vṛthāṭyā ca kāmajo daśako gaṇaḥ  Mn 
paiśunyaṃ sāhasaṃ droha īrṣyāsūyārthadūṣaṇam 
vāgdaṇḍajaṃ ca pāruṣyaṃ krodhajo 'pi gaṇo 'ṣṭakaḥ  Mn 
dvayor apy etayor mūlaṃ yaṃ sarve kavayo viduḥ 
taṃ yatnena jayel lobhaṃ tajjāv etāv ubhau gaṇau  Mn 
pānam akṣāḥ striyaś caiva mṛgayā ca yathākramam 
etat kaṣṭatamaṃ vidyāc catuṣkaṃ kāmaje gaṇe  Mn 
daṇḍasya pātanaṃ caiva vākpāruṣyārthadūṣaṇe 
krodhaje 'pi gaṇe vidyāt kaṣṭam etat trikaṃ sadā  Mn 
saptakasyāsya vargasya sarvatraivānuṣaṅgiṇaḥ 
pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ gurutaraṃ vidyād vyasanam ātmavān  Mn 
vyasanasya ca mṛtyoś ca vyasanaṃ kaṣṭam ucyate 
vyasany adho 'dho vrajati svar yāty avyasanī mṛtaḥ  Mn 
maulāñ śāstravidaḥ śūrāṃl labdhalakṣān kulodbhavān 
sacivān sapta cāṣṭau vā prakurvīta parīkṣitān  Mn 
api yat sukaraṃ karma tad apy ekena duṣkaram 
viśeṣato 'sahāyena kiṃ tu rājyaṃ mahodayam  Mn 
taiḥ sārdhaṃ cintayen nityaṃ sāmānyaṃ saṃdhivigraham 
sthānaṃ samudayaṃ guptiṃ labdhapraśamanāni ca  Mn 
teṣāṃ svaṃ svam abhiprāyam upalabhya pṛthak pṛthak 
samastānāṃ ca kāryeṣu vidadhyād dhitam ātmanaḥ  Mn 
sarveṣāṃ tu viśiṣṭena brāhmaṇena vipaścitā 
mantrayet paramaṃ mantraṃ rājā ṣāḍguṇyasaṃyutam  Mn 
nityaṃ tasmin samāśvastaḥ sarvakāryāṇi niḥkṣipet 
tena sārdhaṃ viniścitya tataḥ karma samārabhet  Mn 
anyān api prakurvīta śucīn prājñān avasthitān 
samyag arthasamāhartṝn amātyān suparīkṣitān  Mn 
nirvartetāsya yāvadbhir itikartavyatā nṛbhiḥ 
tāvato 'tandritān dakṣān prakurvīta vicakṣaṇān  Mn 
teṣām arthe niyuñjīta śūrān dakṣān kulodgatān 
śucīn ākarakarmānte bhīrūn antarniveśane  Mn 
dūtaṃ caiva prakurvīta sarvaśāstraviśāradam 
iṅgitākāraceṣṭajñaṃ śuciṃ dakṣaṃ kulodgatam  Mn 
anuraktaḥ śucir dakṣaḥ smṛtimān deśakālavit 
vapuṣmān vītabhīr vāgmī dūto rājñaḥ praśasyate  Mn 
amātye daṇḍa āyatto daṇḍe vainayikī kriyā 
nṛpatau kośarāṣṭre ca dūte saṃdhiviparyayau  Mn 
dūta eva hi saṃdhatte bhinatty eva ca saṃhatān 
dūtas tat kurute karma bhidyante yena mānavaḥ  Mn 
sa vidyād asya kṛtyeṣu nirgūḍheṅgitaceṣṭitaiḥ 
ākāram iṅgitaṃ ceṣṭāṃ bhṛtyeṣu ca cikīrṣitam  Mn 
buddhvā ca sarvaṃ tattvena pararājacikīrṣitam 
tathā prayatnam ātiṣṭhed yathātmānaṃ na pīḍayet  Mn 
jāṅgalaṃ sasyasaṃpannam āryaprāyam anāvilam 
ramyam ānatasāmantaṃ svājīvyaṃ deśam āvaset  Mn 
dhanvadurgaṃ mahīdurgam abdurgaṃ vārkṣam eva vā 
nṛdurgaṃ giridurgaṃ vā samāśritya vaset puram  Mn 
sarveṇa tu prayatnena giridurgaṃ samāśrayet 
eṣāṃ hi bāhuguṇyena giridurgaṃ viśiṣyate  Mn 
triṇy ādyāny āśritās tv eṣāṃ mṛgagartāśrayāpcarāḥ 
trīṇy uttarāṇi kramaśaḥ plavaṃgamanarāmarāḥ  Mn 
yathā durgāśritān etān nopahiṃsanti śatravaḥ 
tathārayo na hiṃsanti nṛpaṃ durgasamāśritam  Mn 
ekaḥ śataṃ yodhayati prākārastho dhanurdharaḥ 
śataṃ daśasahasrāṇi tasmād durgaṃ vidhīyate  Mn 
tat syād āyudhasaṃpannaṃ dhanadhānyena vāhanaiḥ 
brāhmaṇaiḥ śilpibhir yantrair yavasenodakena ca  Mn 
tasya madhye suparyāptaṃ kārayed gṛham ātmanaḥ 
guptaṃ sarvartukaṃ śubhraṃ jalavṛkṣasamanvitam  Mn 
tad adhyāsyodvahed bhāryāṃ savarṇāṃ lakṣaṇānvitām 
kule mahati saṃbhūtāṃ hṛdyāṃ rūpaguṇānvītām  Mn 
purohitaṃ ca kurvīta vṛṇuyād eva ca rtvijaḥ 
te 'sya gṛhyāṇi karmāṇi kuryur vaitānikāni ca  Mn 
yajeta rājā kratubhir vividhair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ 
dharmārthaṃ caiva viprebhyo dadyād bhogān dhanāni ca  Mn 
sāṃvatsarikam āptaiś ca rāṣṭrād āhārayed balim 
syāc cāmnāyaparo loke varteta pitṛvan nṛṣu  Mn 
adhyakṣān vividhān kuryāt tatra tatra vipaścitaḥ 
te 'sya sarvāṇy avekṣeran nṛṇāṃ kāryāṇi kurvatām  Mn 
āvṛttānāṃ gurukulād viprāṇāṃ pūjako bhavet 
nṛpāṇām akṣayo hy eṣa nidhir brāhmo 'bhidhīyate  Mn 
na taṃ stenā na cāmitrā haranti na ca naśyati 
tasmād rājñā nidhātavyo brāhmaṇeṣv akṣayo nidhiḥ  Mn 
na skandate na vyathate na vinaśyati karhi cit 
variṣṭham agnihotrebhyo brāhmaṇasya mukhe hutam  Mn 
samam abrāhmaṇe dānaṃ dviguṇaṃ brāhmaṇabruve 
prādhīte śatasāhasram anantaṃ vedapārage  Mn 
pātrasya hi viśeṣeṇa śraddadhānatayaiva ca 
alpaṃ vā bahu vā pretya dānasya phalam aśnute  Mn 
deśakālavidhānena dravyaṃ śraddhāsamanvitam 
pātre pradīyate yat tu tad dharmasya prasādhanam  MnM 
samottamādhamai rājā tv āhūtaḥ pālayan prajāḥ 
na nivarteta saṃgrāmāt kṣātraṃ dharmam anusmaran  MnM 
saṃgrāmeṣv anivartitvaṃ prajānāṃ caiva pālanam 
śuśrūṣā brāhmaṇānāṃ ca rājñāṃ śreyaskaraṃ param  MnM 
āhaveṣu mitho 'nyonyaṃ jighāṃsanto mahīkṣitaḥ 
yudhyamānāḥ paraṃ śaktyā svargaṃ yānty aparāṅmukhāḥ  MnM 
na kūṭair āyudhair hanyād yudhyamāno raṇe ripūn 
na karṇibhir nāpi digdhair nāgnijvalitatejanaiḥ  MnM 
na ca hanyāt sthalārūḍhaṃ na klībaṃ na kṛtāñjalim 
na muktakeśaṃ nāsīnaṃ na tavāsmīti vādinam  MnM 
na suptaṃ na visaṃnāhaṃ na nagnaṃ na nirāyudham 
nāyudhyamānaṃ paśyantaṃ na pareṇa samāgatam  MnM 
nāyudhavyasanaprāptaṃ nārtaṃ nātiparikṣataṃ 
na bhītaṃ na parāvṛttaṃ satāṃ dharmam anusmaran  MnM 
yas tu bhītaḥ parāvṛttaḥ saṃgrāme hanyate paraiḥ 
bhartur yad duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃ cit tat sarvaṃ pratipadyate  MnM 
yac cāsya sukṛtaṃ kiṃ cid amutrārtham upārjitam 
bhartā tat sarvam ādatte parāvṛttahatasya tu  MnM 
rathāśvaṃ hastinaṃ chatraṃ dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ paśūn striyaḥ 
sarvadravyāṇi kupyaṃ ca yo yaj jayati tasya tat  MnM 
rājñaś ca dadyur uddhāram ity eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ 
rājñā ca sarvayodhebhyo dātavyam apṛthagjitam  MnM 
eṣo 'nupaskṛtaḥ prokto yodhadharmaḥ sanātanaḥ 
asmād dharmān na cyaveta kṣatriyo ghnan raṇe ripūn  MnM 
alabdhaṃ caiva lipseta labdhaṃ rakṣet prayatnataḥ 
rakṣitaṃ vardhayec caiva vṛddhaṃ pātreṣu nikṣipet  MnM 
etac caturvidhaṃ vidyāt puruṣārthaprayojanam 
asya nityam anuṣṭhānaṃ samyak kuryād atandritaḥ  MnM 
alabdham icched daṇḍena labdhaṃ rakṣed avekṣayā 
rakṣitaṃ vardhayed vṛddhyā vṛddhaṃ pātreṣu nikṣipet  MnM 
nityam udyatadaṇḍaḥ syān nityaṃ vivṛtapauruṣaḥ 
nityaṃ saṃvṛtasaṃvāryo nityaṃ chidrānusāry areḥ  MnM 
nityam udyatadaṇḍasya kṛtsnam udvijate jagat 
tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni daṇḍenaiva prasādhayet  MnM 
amāyayaiva varteta na kathaṃ cana māyayā 
budhyetāriprayuktāṃ ca māyāṃ nityaṃ susaṃvṛtaḥ  MnM 
nāsya chidraṃ paro vidyād vidyāc chidraṃ parasya ca 
gūhet kūrma ivāṅgāni rakṣed vivaram ātmanaḥ  MnM 
bakavac cintayed arthān siṃhavac ca parākrame 
vṛkavac cāvalumpeta śaśavac ca viniṣpatet  MnM 
evaṃ vijayamānasya ye 'sya syuḥ paripanthinaḥ 
tān ānayed vaśaṃ sarvān sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ  MnM 
yadi te tu na tiṣṭheyur upāyaiḥ prathamais tribhiḥ 
daṇḍenaiva prasahyaitāñ śanakair vaśam ānayet  MnM 
sāmādīnām upāyānāṃ caturṇām api paṇḍitāḥ 
sāmadaṇḍau praśaṃsanti nityaṃ rāṣṭrābhivṛddhaye  MnM 
yathoddharati nirdātā kakṣaṃ dhānyaṃ ca rakṣati 
tathā rakṣen nṛpo rāṣṭraṃ hanyāc ca paripanthinaḥ  MnM 
mohād rājā svarāṣṭraṃ yaḥ karṣayaty anavekṣayā 
so 'cirād bhraśyate rājyāj jīvitāc ca sabāndhavaḥ  MnM 
śarīrakarṣaṇāt prāṇāḥ kṣīyante prāṇināṃ yathā 
tathā rājñām api prāṇāḥ kṣīyante rāṣṭrakarṣaṇāt  MnM 
rāṣṭrasya saṃgrahe nityaṃ vidhānam idam ācaret 
susaṃgṛhītarāṣṭre hi pārthivaḥ sukham edhate  MnM 
dvayos trayāṇāṃ pañcānāṃ madhye gulmam adhiṣṭhitam 
tathā grāmaśatānāṃ ca kuryād rāṣṭrasya saṃgraham  MnM 
grāmasyādhipatiṃ kuryād daśagrāmapatiṃ tathā 
viṃśatīśaṃ śateśaṃ ca sahasrapatim eva ca  MnM 
grāmadoṣān samutpannān grāmikaḥ śanakaiḥ svayam 
śaṃsed grāmadaśeśāya daśeśo viṃśatīśine  MnM 
viṃśatīśas tu tat sarvaṃ śateśāya nivedayet 
śaṃsed grāmaśateśas tu sahasrapataye svayam  MnM 
yāni rājapradeyāni pratyahaṃ grāmavāsibhiḥ 
annapānendhanādīni grāmikas tāny avāpnuyāt  MnM 
daśī kulaṃ tu bhuñjīta viṃśī pañca kulāni ca 
grāmaṃ grāmaśatādhyakṣaḥ sahasrādhipatiḥ puram  MnM 
teṣāṃ grāmyāṇi kāryāni pṛthakkāryāṇi caiva hi 
rājño 'nyaḥ sacivaḥ snigdhas tāni paśyed atandritaḥ  MnM 
nagare nagare caikaṃ kuryāt sarvārthacintakam 
uccaiḥsthānaṃ ghorarūpaṃ nakṣatrāṇām iva graham  MnM 
sa tān anuparikrāmet sarvān eva sadā svayam 
teṣāṃ vṛttaṃ pariṇayet samyag rāṣṭreṣu taccaraiḥ  MnM 
rājño hi rakṣādhikṛtāḥ parasvādāyinaḥ śaṭhāḥ 
bhṛtyā bhavanti prāyeṇa tebhyo rakṣed imāḥ prajāḥ  MnM 
ye kāryikebhyo 'rtham eva gṛhṇīyuḥ pāpacetasaḥ 
teṣāṃ sarvasvam ādāya rājā kuryāt pravāsanam  MnM 
rājā karmasu yuktānāṃ strīṇāṃ preṣyajanasya ca 
pratyahaṃ kalpayed vṛttiṃ sthānaṃ karmānurūpataḥ  MnM 
paṇo deyo 'vakṛṣṭasya ṣaḍ utkṛṣṭasya vetanam 
ṣāṇmāsikas tathācchādo dhānyadroṇas tu māsikaḥ  MnM 
krayavikrayam adhvānaṃ bhaktaṃ ca saparivyayam 
yogakṣemaṃ ca saṃprekṣya vaṇijo dāpayet karān  MnM 
yathā phalena yujyeta rājā kartā ca karmaṇām 
tathāvekṣya nṛpo rāṣṭre kalpayet satataṃ karān  MnM 
yathālpālpam adanty ādyaṃ vāryokovatsaṣaṭpadāḥ 
tathālpālpo grahītavyo rāṣṭrād rājñābdikaḥ karaḥ  MnM 
pañcāśadbhāga ādeyo rājñā paśuhiraṇyayoḥ 
dhānyānām aṣṭamo bhāgaḥ ṣaṣṭho dvādaśa eva vā  MnM 
ādadītātha ṣaḍbhāgaṃ drumāṃsamadhusarpiṣām 
gandhauṣadhirasānāṃ ca puṣpamūlaphalasya ca  MnM 
patraśākatṛṇānāṃ ca carmaṇāṃ vaidalasya ca 
mṛnmayānāṃ ca bhāṇḍānāṃ sarvasyāśmamayasya ca  MnM 
mriyamāṇo 'py ādadīta na rājā śrotriyāt karam 
na ca kṣudhāsya saṃsīdec chrotriyo viṣaye vasan  MnM 
yasya rājñas tu viṣaye śrotriyaḥ sīdati kṣudhā 
tasyāpi tat kṣudhā rāṣṭram acirenaiva sīdati  MnM 
śrutavṛtte viditvāsya vṛttiṃ dharmyāṃ prakalpayet 
saṃrakṣet sarvataś cainaṃ pitā putram ivāurasam  MnM 
saṃrakṣyamāṇo rājñā yaṃ kurute dharmam anvaham 
tenāyur vardhate rājño draviṇaṃ rāṣṭram eva ca  MnM 
yat kiṃ cid api varṣasya dāpayet karasaṃjñitam 
vyavahāreṇa jīvantaṃ rājā rāṣṭre pṛthagjanam  MnM 
kārukāñ śilpinaś caiva śūdrāṃs cātmopajīvinaḥ 
ekaikaṃ kārayet karma māsi māsi mahīpatiḥ  MnM 
nocchindyād ātmano mūlaṃ pareṣāṃ cātitṛṣṇayā 
ucchindan hy ātmano mūlam āṭmānaṃ tāṃś ca pīdayet  MnM 
tīkṣṇaś caiva mṛduś ca syāt kāryaṃ vīkṣya mahīpatiḥ 
tīkṣṇaś caiva mṛduś caiva rāja bhavati sammataḥ  MnM 
amātyamukhyaṃ dharmajñaṃ prājñaṃ dāntaṃ kulodgatam 
sthāpayed āsane tasmin khinnaḥ kāryekṣaṇe nṛṇām  MnM 
evaṃ sarvaṃ vidhāyedam itikartavyam ātmanaḥ 
yuktaś caivāpramattaś ca parirakṣed imāḥ prajāḥ  MnM 
vikrośantyo yasya rāṣṭrād hriyante dasyubhiḥ prajāḥ 
saṃpaśyataḥ sabhṛtyasya mṛtaḥ sa na tu jīvati  MnM 
kṣatriyasya paro dharmaḥ prājānām eva pālanam 
nirdiṣṭaphalabhoktā hi rājā dharmeṇa yujyate  MnM 
utthāya paścime yāme kṛtaśaucaḥ samāhitaḥ 
hutāgnir brāhmaṇāṃś cārcya praviśet sa śubhāṃ sabhām  MnM 
tatra sthitaḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ pratinandya visarjayet 
visṛjya ca prajāḥ sarvā mantrayet saha mantribhiḥ  MnM 
giripṛṣṭhaṃ samāruhya prasādaṃ vā rahogataḥ 
araṇye niḥśalāke vā mantrayed avibhāvitaḥ  MnM 
yasya mantraṃ na jānanti samāgamya pṛthagjanāḥ 
sa kṛtsnāṃ pṛthivīṃ bhuṅkte kośahīno 'pi pārthivaḥ  MnM 
jaḍamūkāndhabadhirāṃs tairyagyonān vayo'tigān 
strīmlecchavyādhitavyaṅgān mantrakāle 'pasārayet  MnM 
bhindanty avamatā mantraṃ tairyagyonās tathaiva ca 
striyaś caiva viśeṣeṇa tasmāt tatrādṛto bhavet  MnM 
madhyaṃdine 'rdharātre vā viśrānto vigataklamaḥ 
cintayed dharmakāmārthān sārdhaṃ tair eka eva vā  MnM 
parasparaviruddhānāṃ teṣāṃ ca samupārjanam 
kanyānāṃ saṃpradānaṃ ca kumārāṇāṃ ca rakṣaṇaṃ  MnM 
dūtasaṃpreṣaṇaṃ caiva kāryaśeṣaṃ tathaiva ca 
antaḥpurapracāraṃ ca praṇidhīnāṃ ca ceṣṭitam  MnM 
kṛtsnaṃ cāṣṭavidhaṃ karma pañcavargaṃ ca tattvataḥ 
anurāgāparāgau ca pracāraṃ maṇḍalasya ca  MnM 
madhyamasya pracāraṃ ca vijīgiṣoś ca ceṣṭitam 
udāsīnapracāraṃ ca śatroś caiva prayatnataḥ  MnM 
etāḥ prakṛtayo mūlaṃ maṇḍalasya samāsataḥ 
aṣṭau cānyāḥ samākhyātā dvādaśaiva tu tāḥ smṛtāḥ  MnM 
amātyarāṣṭradurgārtha daṇḍākhyāḥ pañca cāparāḥ 
pratyekaṃ kathitā hy etāḥ saṃkṣepeṇa dvisaptatiḥ  MnM 
anantaram ariṃ vidyād arisevinam eva ca 
arer anantaraṃ mitram udāsīnaṃ tayoḥ param  MnM 
tān sarvān abhisaṃdadhyāt sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ 
vyastaiś caiva samastaiś ca pauruṣeṇa nayena ca  MnM 
saṃdhiṃ ca vigrahaṃ caiva yānam āsanam eva ca 
dvaidhībhāvaṃ saṃśrayaṃ ca ṣaḍguṇāṃś cintayet sadā  MnM 
āsanaṃ caiva yānaṃ ca saṃdhiṃ vigraham eva ca 
kāryaṃ vīkṣya prayuñjīta dvaidhaṃ saṃśrayam eva ca  MnM 
saṃdhiṃ tu dvividhaṃ vidyād rājā vigraham eva ca 
ubhe yānāsane caiva dvividhaḥ saṃśrayaḥ smṛtaḥ  MnM 
samānayānakarmā ca viparītas tathaiva ca 
tadā tv āyatisaṃyuktaḥ saṃdhir jñeyo dvilakṣaṇaḥ  MnM 
svayaṃkṛtaś ca kāryārtham akāle kāla eva vā 
mitrasya caivāpakṛte dvividho vigrahaḥ smṛtaḥ  MnM 
ekākinaś cātyayike kārye prāpte yadṛcchayā 
saṃhatasya ca mitreṇa dvividhaṃ yānam ucyate  MnM 
kṣīṇasya caiva kramaśo daivāt pūrvakṛtena vā 
mitrasya cānurodhena dvividhaṃ smṛtam āsanam  MnM 
balasya svāminaś caiva sthitiḥ kāryārthasiddhaye 
dvividhaṃ kīrtyate dvaidhaṃ ṣāḍguṇyaguṇavedibhiḥ  MnM 
arthasaṃpādanārthaṃ ca pīḍyamānasya śatrubhiḥ 
sādhuṣu vyapadeśaś ca dvividhaḥ saṃśrayaḥ smṛtaḥ  MnM 
yadāvagacched āyatyām ādhikyaṃ dhruvam ātmanaḥ 
tadātve cālpikāṃ pīḍāṃ tadā saṃdhiṃ samāśrayet  MnM 
yadā prahṛṣṭā manyeta sarvās tu prakṛtīr bhṛśam 
atyucchritaṃ tathātmānaṃ tadā kurvīta vigraham  MnM 
yadā manyeta bhāvena hṛṣṭaṃ puṣṭaṃ balaṃ svakam 
parasya viparītaṃ ca tadā yāyād ripuṃ prati  MnM 
yadā tu syāt parikṣīṇo vāhanena balena ca 
tadāsīta prayatnena śanakaiḥ sāntvayann arīn  MnM 
manyetāriṃ yadā rājā sarvathā balavattaram 
tadā dvidhā balaṃ kṛtvā sādhayet kāryam ātmanaḥ  MnM 
yadā parabalānāṃ tu gamanīyatamo bhavet 
tadā tu saṃśrayet kṣipraṃ dhārmikaṃ balinaṃ nṛpam  MnM 
nigrahaṃ prakṛtīnāṃ ca kuryād yo 'ribalasya ca 
upaseveta taṃ nityaṃ sarvayatnair guruṃ yathā  MnM 
yadi tatrāpi saṃpaśyed doṣaṃ saṃśrayakāritam 
suyuddham eva tatrāpi nirviśaṅkaḥ samācaret  MnM 
sarvopāyais tathā kuryān nītijñaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ 
yathāsyābhyadhikā na syur mitrodāsīnaśatravaḥ  MnM 
āyatiṃ sarvakāryāṇāṃ tadātvaṃ ca vicārayet 
atītānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ guṇadoṣau ca tattvataḥ  MnM 
āyatyāṃ guṇadoṣajñas tadātve kṣipraniścayaḥ 
atīte kāryaśeṣajñaḥ śatrubhir nābhibhūyate  MnM 
yathainaṃ nābhisaṃdadhyur mitrodāsīnaśatravaḥ 
tathā sarvaṃ saṃvidadhyād eṣa sāmāsiko nayaḥ  MnM 
tadā tu yānam ātiṣṭhed arirāṣṭraṃ prati prabhuḥ 
tadānena vidhānena yāyād aripuraṃ śanaiḥ  MnM 
mārgaśīrṣe śubhe māsi yāyād yātrāṃ mahīpatiḥ 
phālgunaṃ vātha caitraṃ vā māsau prati yathābalam  MnM 
anyeṣv api tu kāleṣu yadā paśyed dhruvaṃ jayam 
tadā yāyād vigṛhyaiva vyasane cotthite ripoḥ  MnM 
kṛtvā vidhānaṃ mūle tu yātrikaṃ ca yathāvidhi 
upagṛhyāspadaṃ caiva cārān samyag vidhāya ca  MnM 
saṃśodhya trividhaṃ mārgaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ ca balaṃ svakam 
sāṃparāyikakalpena yāyād aripuraṃ prati  MnM 
śatrusevini mitre ca gūḍhe yuktataro bhavet 
gatapratyāgate caiva sa hi kaṣṭataro ripuḥ  MnM 
daṇḍavyūhena tan mārgaṃ yāyāt tu śakaṭena vā 
varāhamakarābhyāṃ vā sūcyā vā garuḍena vā  MnM 
yataś ca bhayam āśaṅket tato vistārayed balam 
padmena caiva vyūhena niviśeta sadā svayam  MnM 
senāpatibalādhyakṣau sarvadikṣu niveśayet 
yataś ca bhayam āśaṅket prācīṃ tāṃ kalpayed diśam  MnM 
gulmāṃś ca sthāpayed āptān kṛtasaṃjñān samantataḥ 
sthāne yuddhe ca kuśalān abhīrūn avikāriṇaḥ  MnM 
saṃhatān yodhayed alpān kāmaṃ vistārayed bahūn 
sūcyā vajreṇa caivaitān vyūhena vyūhya yodhayet  MnM 
syandanāśvaiḥ same yudhyed anūpe nau dvipais tathā 
vṛkṣagulmāvṛte cāpair asicarmāyudhaiḥ sthale  MnM 
kurukṣetrāṃś ca matsyāṃś ca pañcālāñ śūrasenajān 
dīrghāṃl laghūṃś caiva narān agrānīkeṣu yojayet  MnM 
praharṣayed balaṃ vyūhya tāṃś ca samyak parīkṣayet 
ceṣṭāś caiva vijānīyād arīn yodhayatām api  MnM 
uparudhyārim āsīta rāṣṭraṃ cāsyopapīḍayet 
dūṣayec cāsya satataṃ yavasānnodakendhanam  MnM 
bhindyāc caiva taḍāgāni prākāraparikhās tathā 
samavaskandayec cainaṃ rātrau vitrāsayet tathā  MnM 
upajapyān upajaped budhyetaiva ca tatkṛtam 
yukte ca daive yudhyeta jayaprepsur apetabhīḥ  MnM 
sāmnā dānena bhedena samastair atha vā pṛthak 
vijetuṃ prayatetārīn na yuddhena kadā cana  MnM 
anityo vijayo yasmād dṛśyate yudhyamānayoḥ 
parājayaś ca saṃgrāme tasmād yuddhaṃ vivarjayet  MnM 
trayāṇām apy upāyānāṃ pūrvoktānām asaṃbhave 
tathā yudhyeta saṃpanno vijayeta ripūn yathā  MnM 
jitvā saṃpūjayed devān brāhmaṇāṃś caiva dhārmikān 
pradadyāt parihārārthaṃ khyāpayed abhayāni ca  MnM 
sarveṣāṃ tu viditvaiṣāṃ samāsena cikīrṣitam 
sthāpayet tatra tadvaṃśyaṃ kuryāc ca samayakriyām  MnM 
pramāṇāni ca kurvīta teṣāṃ dharmān yathoditān 
ratnaiś ca pūjayed enaṃ pradhānapuruṣaiḥ saha  MnM 
ādānam apriyakaraṃ dānaṃ ca priyakārakam 
abhīpsitānām arthānāṃ kāle yuktaṃ praśasyate  MnM 
sarvaṃ karmedam āyattaṃ vidhāne daivamānuṣe 
tayor daivam acintyaṃ tu mānuṣe vidyate kriyā  MnM 
daivena vidhinā yuktaṃ mānuṣyaṃ yat pravartate 
parikleśena mahatā tadarthasya samādhakam  MnM 
saṃyuktasyāpi daivena puruṣakāreṇa varjitam 
vinā puruṣakāreṇa phalaṃ kṣetraṃ prayacchati  MnM 
candrārkādyā grahā vāyur agnir āpas tathaiva ca 
iha daivena sādhyante pauruṣeṇa prayatnataḥ  MnM 
saha vāpi vrajed yuktaḥ saṃdhiṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ 
mitraṃ hiraṇyaṃ bhūmiṃ vā saṃpaśyaṃs trividhaṃ phalam  MnM 
pārṣṇigrāhaṃ ca saṃprekṣya tathākrandaṃ ca maṇḍale 
mitrād athāpy amitrād vā yātrāphalam avāpnuyāt  MnM 
hiraṇyabhūmisaṃprāptyā pārthivo na tathaidhate 
yathā mitraṃ dhruvaṃ labdhvā kṛśam apy āyatikṣamam  MnM 
dharmajñaṃ ca kṛtajñaṃ ca tuṣṭaprakṛtim eva ca 
anuraktaṃ sthirārambhaṃ laghumitraṃ praśasyate  MnM 
prājñaṃ kulīnaṃ śūraṃ ca dakṣaṃ dātāram eva ca 
kṛtajñaṃ dhṛtimantaṃ ca kaṣṭam āhur ariṃ budhāḥ  MnM 
āryatā puruṣajñānaṃ śauryaṃ karuṇaveditā 
sthaulalakṣyaṃ ca satatam udāsīnaguṇodayaḥ  MnM 
ksemyāṃ sasyapradāṃ nityaṃ paśuvṛddhikarīm api 
parityajen nṛpo bhūmim ātmārtham avicārayan  MnM 
āpadarthaṃ dhanaṃ rakṣed dārān rakṣed dhanair api 
ātmānaṃ satataṃ rakṣed dārair api dhanair api  MnM 
saha sarvāḥ samutpannāḥ prasamīkṣyāpado bhṛśam 
saṃyuktāṃś ca viyuktāṃś ca sarvopāyān sṛjed budhaḥ  MnM 
upetāram upeyaṃ ca sarvopāyāṃś ca kṛtsnaśaḥ 
etat trayaṃ samāśritya prayatetārthasiddhaye  MnM 
evaṃ sarvam idaṃ rājā saha sammantrya mantribhiḥ 
vyāyamyāplutya madhyāhne bhoktum antaḥpuraṃ viśet  MnM 
tatrātmabhūtaiḥ kālajñair ahāryaiḥ paricārakaiḥ 
suparīkṣitam annādyam adyān mantrair viṣāpahaiḥ  MnM 
viṣaghnair agadaiś cāsya sarvadravyāṇi yojayet 
viṣaghnāni ca ratnāni niyato dhārayet sadā  MnM 
parīkṣitāḥ striyaś cainaṃ vyajanodakadhūpanaiḥ 
veṣābharaṇasaṃśuddhāḥ spṛśeyuḥ susamāhitāḥ  MnM 
evaṃ prayatnaṃ kurvīta yānaśayyāsanāśane 
snāne prasādhane caiva sarvālaṅkārakeṣu ca  MnM 
bhuktavān viharec caiva strībhir antaḥpure saha 
vihṛtya tu yathākālaṃ punaḥ kāryāṇi cintayet  MnM 
alaṃkṛtaś ca saṃpaśyed āyudhīyaṃ punar janam 
vāhanāni ca sarvāṇi śastrāṇy ābharaṇāni ca  MnM 
saṃdhyāṃ copāsya śṛṇuyād antarveśmani śastrabhṛt 
rahasyākhyāyināṃ caiva praṇidhīnāṃ ca ceṣṭitam  MnM 
gatvā kakṣāntaraṃ tv anyat samanujñāpya taṃ janam 
praviśed bhojanārthaṃ ca strīvṛto 'ntaḥpuraṃ punaḥ  MnM 
tatra bhuktvā punaḥ kiṃ cit tūryaghoṣaiḥ praharṣitaḥ 
saṃviśet taṃ yathākālam uttiṣṭhec ca gataklamaḥ  MnM 
etadvidhānam ātiṣṭhed arogaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ 
asvasthaḥ sarvam etat tu bhṛtyeṣu viniyojayet  MnM 
vyavahārān didṛkṣus tu brāhmaṇaiḥ saha pārthivaḥ 
mantrajñair mantribhiś caiva vinītaḥ praviśet sabhām  Mn 
tatrāsīnaḥ sthito vāpi pāṇim udyamya dakṣiṇam 
vinītaveṣābharaṇaḥ paśyet kāryāṇi kāryiṇām  Mn 
pratyahaṃ deśadṛṣṭaiś ca śāstradṛṣṭaiś ca hetubhiḥ 
aṣṭādaśasu mārgeṣu nibaddhāni pṛthak pṛthak  Mn 
teṣām ādyam ṛṇādānaṃ nikṣepo 'svāmivikrayaḥ 
saṃbhūya ca samutthānaṃ dattasyānapakarma ca  Mn 
vetanasyaiva cādānaṃ saṃvidaś ca vyatikramaḥ 
krayavikrayānuśayo vivādaḥ svāmipālayoḥ  Mn 
sīmāvivādadharmaś ca pāruṣye daṇḍavācike 
steyaṃ ca sāhasaṃ caiva strīsaṃgrahaṇam eva ca  Mn 
strīpuṃdharmo vibhāgaś ca dyūtam āhvaya eva ca 
padāny aṣṭādaśaitāni vyavahārasthitāv iha  Mn 
eṣu sthāneṣu bhūyiṣṭhaṃ vivādaṃ caratāṃ nṛṇām 
dharmaṃ śāśvatam āśritya kuryāt kāryavinirṇayam  Mn 
yadā svayaṃ na kuryāt tu nṛpatiḥ kāryadarśanam 
tadā niyuñjyād vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ kāryadarśane  Mn 
so 'sya kāryāṇi saṃpaśyet sabhyair eva tribhir vṛtaḥ 
sabhām eva praviśyāgryām āsīnaḥ sthita eva vā  Mn 
yasmin deśe niṣīdanti viprā vedavidas trayaḥ 
rājñaś cādhikṛto vidvān brahmaṇas tāṃ sabhāṃ viduḥ  Mn 
dharmo viddhas tv adharmeṇa sabhāṃ yatropatiṣṭhate 
śalyaṃ cāsya na kṛntanti viddhās tatra sabhāsadaḥ  Mn 
sabhāṃ vā na praveṣṭavyaṃ vaktavyaṃ vā samañjasam 
abruvan vibruvan vāpi naro bhavati kilbiṣī  Mn 
yatra dharmo hy adharmeṇa satyaṃ yatrānṛtena ca 
hanyate prekṣamāṇānāṃ hatās tatra sabhāsadaḥ  Mn 
dharma eva hato hanti dharmo rakṣati rakṣitaḥ 
tasmād dharmo na hantavyo mā no dharmo hato 'vadhīt  Mn 
vṛṣo hi bhagavān dharmas tasya yaḥ kurute hy alam 
vṛṣalaṃ taṃ vidur devās tasmād dharmaṃ na lopayet  Mn 
eka eva suhṛd dharmo nidhāne 'py anuyāti yaḥ 
śarīreṇa samaṃ nāśaṃ sarvam anyad dhi gacchati  Mn 
pādo 'dharmasya kartāraṃ pādaḥ sākṣiṇam ṛcchati 
pādaḥ sabhāsadaḥ sarvān pādo rājānam ṛcchati  Mn 
rājā bhavaty anenās tu mucyante ca sabhāsadaḥ 
eno gacchati kartāraṃ nindārho yatra nindyate  Mn 
jātimātropajīvī vā kāmaṃ syād brāhmaṇabruvaḥ 
dharmapravaktā nṛpater na tu śūdraḥ kathaṃ cana  Mn 
yasya śūdras tu kurute rājño dharmavivecanam 
tasya sīdati tad rāṣṭraṃ paṅke gaur iva paśyataḥ  Mn 
yad rāṣṭraṃ śūdrabhūyiṣṭhaṃ nāstikākrāntam advijam 
vinaśyaty āśu tat kṛtsnaṃ durbhikṣavyādhipīḍitam  Mn 
dharmāsanam adhiṣṭhāya saṃvītāṅgaḥ samāhitaḥ 
praṇamya lokapālebhyaḥ kāryadarśanam ārabhet  Mn 
arthānarthāv ubhau buddhvā dharmādharmau ca kevalau 
varṇakrameṇa sarvāṇi paśyet kāryāṇi kāryiṇām  Mn 
bāhyair vibhāvayel liṅgair bhāvam antargataṃ nṛṇām 
svaravarṇeṅgitākāraiś cakṣuṣā ceṣṭitena ca  Mn 
ākārair iṅgitair gatyā ceṣṭayā bhāṣitena ca 
netravaktravikāraiś ca gṛhyate 'ntargataṃ manaḥ  Mn 
bāladāyādikaṃ rikthaṃ tāvad rājānupālayet 
yāvat sa syāt samāvṛtto yāvac cātītaśaiśavaḥ  Mn 
vaśāputrāsu caivaṃ syād rakṣaṇaṃ niṣkulāsu ca 
pativratāsu ca strīṣu vidhavāsv āturāsu ca  Mn 
jīvantīnāṃ tu tāsāṃ ye tad dhareyuḥ svabāndhavāḥ 
tāñ śiṣyāc cauradaṇḍena dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ  Mn 
praṇaṣṭasvāmikaṃ rikthaṃ rājā tryabdaṃ nidhāpayet 
arvāk tryabdād dharet svāmī pareṇa nṛpatir haret  Mn 
mamedam iti yo brūyāt so 'nuyojyo yathāvidhi 
saṃvādya rūpasaṃkhyādīn svāmī tad dravyam arhati  Mn 
avedayāno naṣṭasya deśaṃ kālaṃ ca tattvataḥ 
varṇaṃ rūpaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca tatsamaṃ daṇḍam arhati  Mn 
ādadītātha ṣaḍbhāgaṃ pranaṣṭādhigatān nṛpaḥ 
daśamaṃ dvādaśaṃ vāpi satāṃ dharmam anusmaran  Mn 
pranaṣṭādhigataṃ dravyaṃ tiṣṭhed yuktair adhiṣṭhitam 
yāṃs tatra caurān gṛhṇīyāt tān rājebhena ghātayet  Mn 
mamāyam iti yo brūyān nidhiṃ satyena mānavaḥ 
tasyādadīta ṣaḍbhāgaṃ rājā dvādaśam eva vā  Mn 
anṛtaṃ tu vadan daṇḍyaḥ svavittasyāṃśam aṣṭamam 
tasyaiva vā nidhānasya saṃkhyayālpīyasīṃ kalām  Mn 
vidvāṃs tu brāhmaṇo dṛṣṭvā pūrvopanihitaṃ nidhim 
aśeṣato 'py ādadīta sarvasyādhipatir hi saḥ  Mn 
yaṃ tu paśyen nidhiṃ rājā purāṇaṃ nihitaṃ kṣitau 
tasmād dvijebhyo dattvārdham ardhaṃ kośe praveśayet  Mn 
nidhīnāṃ tu purāṇānāṃ dhātūnām eva ca kṣitau 
ardhabhāg rakṣaṇād rājā bhūmer adhipatir hi saḥ  Mn 
dātavyaṃ sarvavarṇebhyo rājñā caurair hṛtaṃ dhanam 
rājā tad upayuñjānaś caurasyāpnoti kilbiṣam  Mn 
jātijānapadān dharmān śreṇīdharmāṃś ca dharmavit 
samīkṣya kuladharmāṃś ca svadharmaṃ pratipādayet  Mn 
svāni karmāṇi kurvāṇā dūre santo 'pi mānavāḥ 
priyā bhavanti lokasya sve sve karmaṇy avasthitāḥ  Mn 
notpādayet svayaṃ kāryaṃ rājā nāpy asya puruṣaḥ 
na ca prāpitam anyena grased arthaṃ kathaṃ cana  Mn 
yathā nayaty asṛkpātair mṛgasya mṛgayuḥ padam 
nayet tathānumānena dharmasya nṛpatiḥ padam  Mn 
satyam arthaṃ ca saṃpaśyed ātmānam atha sākṣiṇaḥ 
deśaṃ rūpaṃ ca kālaṃ ca vyavahāravidhau sthitaḥ  Mn 
sadbhir ācaritaṃ yat syād dhārmikaiś ca dvijātibhiḥ 
tad deśakulajātīnām aviruddhaṃ prakalpayet  Mn 
adhamarṇārthasiddhyartham uttamarṇena coditaḥ 
dāpayed dhanikasyārtham adhamarṇād vibhāvitam  Mn 
yair yair upāyair arthaṃ svaṃ prāpnuyād uttamarṇikaḥ 
tair tair upāyaiḥ saṃgṛhya dāpayed adhamarṇikam  Mn 
dharmeṇa vyavahāreṇa chalenācaritena ca 
prayuktaṃ sādhayed arthaṃ pañcamena balena ca  Mn 
yaḥ svayaṃ sādhayed artham uttamarṇo 'dhamarṇikāt 
na sa rājñābhiyoktavyaḥ svakaṃ saṃsādhayan dhanam  Mn 
arthe 'pavyayamānaṃ tu karaṇena vibhāvitam 
dāpayed dhanikasyārthaṃ daṇḍaleśaṃ ca śaktitaḥ  Mn 
apahnave 'dhamarṇasya dehīty uktasya saṃsadi 
abhiyoktā diśed deśyaṃ karaṇaṃ vānyad uddiśet  Mn 
adeśyaṃ yaś ca diśati nirdiśyāpahnute ca yaḥ 
yaś cādharottarān arthān vigītān nāvabudhyate  Mn 
apadiśyāpadeśyaṃ ca punar yas tv apadhāvati 
samyak praṇihitaṃ cārthaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ san nābhinandati  Mn 
asaṃbhāṣye sākṣibhiś ca deśe saṃbhāṣate mithaḥ 
nirucyamānaṃ praśnaṃ ca necched yaś cāpi niṣpatet  Mn 
brūhīty uktaś ca na brūyād uktaṃ ca na vibhāvayet 
na ca pūrvāparaṃ vidyāt tasmād arthāt sa hīyate  Mn 
sākṣiṇaḥ santi mety uktvā diśety ukto diśen na yaḥ 
dharmasthaḥ kāraṇair etair hīnaṃ tam api nirdiśet  Mn 
abhiyoktā na ced brūyād badhyo daṇḍyaś ca dharmataḥ 
na cet tripakṣāt prabrūyād dharmaṃ prati parājitaḥ  Mn 
yo yāvan nihnuvītārthaṃ mithyā yāvati vā vadet 
tau nṛpeṇa hy adharmajñau dāpyo taddviguṇaṃ damam  Mn 
pṛṣṭo 'pavyayamānas tu kṛtāvastho dhanaiṣiṇā 
tryavaraiḥ sākṣibhir bhāvyo nṛpabrāhmaṇasaṃnidhau  Mn 
yādṛśā dhanibhiḥ kāryā vyavahāreṣu sākṣiṇaḥ 
tādṛśān saṃpravakṣyāmi yathā vācyam ṛtaṃ ca taiḥ  Mn 
gṛhiṇaḥ putriṇo maulāḥ kṣatraviśśūdrayonayaḥ 
arthyuktāḥ sākṣyam arhanti na ye ke cid anāpadi  Mn 
āptāḥ sarveṣu varṇeṣu kāryāḥ kāryeṣu sākṣiṇaḥ 
sarvadharmavido 'lubdhā viparītāṃs tu varjayet  Mn 
nārthasaṃbandhino nāptā na sahāyā na vairiṇaḥ 
na dṛṣṭadoṣāḥ kartavyā na vyādhyārtā na dūṣitāḥ  Mn 
na sākṣī nṛpatiḥ kāryo na kārukakuśīlavau 
na śrotriyo na liṅgastho na saṅgebhyo vinirgataḥ  Mn 
nādhyadhīno na vaktavyo na dasyur na vikarmakṛt 
na vṛddho na śiśur naiko nāntyo na vikalendriyaḥ  Mn 
nārto na matto nonmatto na kṣuttṛṣṇopapīḍitaḥ 
na śramārto na kāmārto na kruddho nāpi taskaraḥ  Mn 
strīṇāṃ sākṣyaṃ striyaḥ kuryur dvijānāṃ sadṛśā dvijāḥ 
śūdrāś ca santaḥ śūdrāṇām antyānām antyayonayaḥ  Mn 
anubhāvī tu yaḥ kaś cit kuryāt sākṣyaṃ vivādinām 
antarveśmany araṇye vā śarīrasyāpi cātyaye  Mn 
striyāpy asaṃbhāve kāryaṃ bālena sthavireṇa vā 
śiṣyeṇa bandhunā vāpi dāsena bhṛtakena vā  Mn 
bālavṛddhāturāṇāṃ ca sākṣyeṣu vadatāṃ mṛṣā 
jānīyād asthirāṃ vācam utsiktamanasāṃ tathā  Mn 
sāhaseṣu ca sarveṣu steyasaṃgrahaṇeṣu ca 
vāgdaṇḍayoś ca pāruṣye na parīkṣeta sākṣiṇaḥ  Mn 
bahutvaṃ parigṛhṇīyāt sākṣidvaidhe narādhipaḥ 
sameṣu tu guṇotkṛṣṭān guṇidvaidhe dvijottamān  Mn 
samakṣadarśanāt sākṣyaṃ śravaṇāc caiva sidhyati 
tatra satyaṃ bruvan sākṣī dharmārthābhyāṃ na hīyate  Mn 
sākṣī dṛṣṭaśrutād anyad vibruvann āryasaṃsadi 
avāṅ narakam abhyeti pretya svargāc ca hīyate  Mn 
yatrānibaddho 'pīkṣeta śṛṇuyād vāpi kiṃ cana 
pṛṣṭas tatrāpi tad brūyād yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam  Mn 
eko 'lubdhas tu sākṣī syād bahvyaḥ śucyo 'pi na striyaḥ 
strībuddher asthiratvāt tu doṣaiś cānye 'pi ye vṛtāḥ  Mn 
svabhāvenaiva yad brūyus tad grāhyaṃ vyāvahārikam 
ato yad anyad vibrūyur dharmārthaṃ tad apārthakam  Mn 
sabhāntaḥ sākṣiṇaḥ prāptān arthipratyarthisaṃnidhau 
prāḍvivāko 'nuyuñjīta vidhinānena sāntvayan  Mn 
yad dvayor anayor vettha kārye 'smiṃś ceṣṭitaṃ mithaḥ 
tad brūta sarvaṃ satyena yuṣmākaṃ hy atra sākṣitā  Mn 
satyaṃ sākṣye bruvan sākṣī lokān āpnoti puṣkalān 
iha cānuttamāṃ kīrtiṃ vāg eṣā brahmapūjitā  Mn 
sākṣye 'nṛtaṃ vadan pāśair badhyate vāruṇair bhṛśam 
vivaśaḥ śatam ājātīs tasmāt sākṣyaṃ vaded ṛtam  Mn 
satyena pūyate sākṣī dharmaḥ satyena vardhate 
tasmāt satyaṃ hi vaktavyaṃ sarvavarṇeṣu sākṣibhiḥ  Mn 
ātmaiva hy ātmanaḥ sākṣī gatir ātmā tathātmanaḥ 
māvamaṃsthāḥ svam ātmānaṃ nṛṇāṃ sākṣiṇam uttamam  Mn 
manyante vai pāpakṛto na kaś cit paśyatīti naḥ 
tāṃs tu devāḥ prapaśyanti svasyaivāntarapūruṣaḥ  Mn 
dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ candrārkāgniyamānilāḥ 
rātriḥ saṃdhye ca dharmaś ca vṛttajñāḥ sarvadehinām  Mn 
devabrāhmaṇasāṃnidhye sākṣyaṃ pṛcched ṛtaṃ dvijān 
udaṅmukhān prāṅmukhān vā pūrvāhṇe vai śuciḥ śucīn  Mn 
brūhīti brāhmaṇaṃ pṛcchet satyaṃ brūhīti pārthivam 
gobījakāñcanair vaiśyaṃ śūdraṃ sarvais tu pātakaiḥ  Mn 
brahmaghno ye smṛtā lokā ye ca strībālaghātinaḥ 
mitradruhaḥ kṛtaghnasya te te syur bruvato mṛṣā  Mn 
janmaprabhṛti yat kiṃ cit puṇyaṃ bhadra tvayā kṛtam 
tat te sarvaṃ śuno gacched yadi brūyās tvam anyathā  Mn 
eko 'ham asmīty ātmānaṃ yas tvaṃ kalyāṇa manyase 
nityaṃ sthitas te hṛdy eṣa puṇyapāpekṣitā muniḥ  Mn 
yamo vaivasvato devo yas tavaiṣa hṛdi sthitaḥ 
tena ced avivādas te mā gaṅgāṃ mā kurūn gamaḥ  Mn 
nagno muṇḍaḥ kapālena ca bhikṣārthī kṣutpipāsitaḥ 
andhaḥ śatrukulaṃ gacched yaḥ sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet  Mn 
avākśirās tamasy andhe kilbiṣī narakaṃ vrajet 
yaḥ praśnaṃ vitathaṃ brūyāt pṛṣṭaḥ san dharmaniścaye  Mn 
andho matsyān ivāśnāti sa naraḥ kaṇṭakaiḥ saha 
yo bhāṣate 'rthavaikalyam apratyakṣaṃ sabhāṃ gataḥ  Mn 
yasya vidvān hi vadataḥ kṣetrajño nābhiśaṅkate 
tasmān na devāḥ śreyāṃsaṃ loke 'nyaṃ puruṣaṃ viduḥ  Mn 
yāvato bāndhavān yasmin hanti sākṣye 'nṛtaṃ vadan 
tāvataḥ saṃkhyayā tasmin śṛṇu saumyānupūrvaśaḥ  Mn 
pañca paśvanṛte hanti daśa hanti gavānṛte 
śatam aśvānṛte hanti sahasraṃ puruṣānṛte  Mn 
hanti jātān ajātāṃś ca hiraṇyārthe 'nṛtaṃ vadan 
sarvaṃ bhūmyanṛte hanti mā sma bhūmyanṛtaṃ vadīḥ  Mn 
apsu bhūmivad ity āhuḥ strīṇāṃ bhoge ca maithune 
abjeṣu caiva ratneṣu sarveṣv aśmamayeṣu ca  Mn 
etān doṣān avekṣya tvaṃ sarvān anṛtabhāṣaṇe 
yathāśrutaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ sarvam evāñjasā vada  Mn 
gorakṣakān vāṇijikāṃs tathā kārukuśīlavān 
preṣyān vārdhuṣikāṃś caiva viprān śūdravad ācaret  Mn 
tad vadan dharmato 'rtheṣu jānann apy anythā naraḥ 
na svargāc cyavate lokād daivīṃ vācaṃ vadanti tām  Mn 
śūdraviṭkṣatraviprāṇāṃ yatra rtoktau bhaved vadhaḥ 
tatra vaktavyam anṛtaṃ tad dhi satyād viśiṣyate  Mn 
vāggaivatyaiś ca carubhir yajeraṃs te sarasvatīm 
anṛtasyainasas tasya kurvāṇā niṣkṛtiṃ parām  Mn 
kūṣmāṇḍair vāpi juhuyād ghṛtam agnau yathāvidhi 
ud ity ṛcā vā vāruṇyā tṛcenābdaivatena vā  Mn 
tripakṣād abruvan sākṣyam ṛṇādiṣu naro 'gadaḥ 
tadṛṇaṃ prāpnuyāt sarvaṃ daśabandhaṃ ca sarvataḥ  Mn 
yasya dṛśyeta saptāhād uktavākyasya sākṣiṇaḥ 
rogo 'gnir jñātimaraṇam ṛṇaṃ dāpyo damaṃ ca saḥ  Mn 
asākṣikeṣu tv artheṣu mitho vivādamānayoḥ 
avindaṃs tattvataḥ satyaṃ śapathenāpi lambhayet  Mn 
maharṣibhiś ca devaiś ca kāryārthaṃ śapathāḥ kṛtāḥ 
vasiṣṭhaś cāpi śapathaṃ śepe paijavane nṛpe  Mn 
na vṛthā śapathaṃ kuryāt svalpe 'py arthe naro budhaḥ 
vṛthā hi śapathaṃ kurvan pretya ceha ca naśyati  Mn 
kāminīṣu vivāheṣu gavāṃ bhakṣye tathendhane 
brāhmaṇābhyupapattau ca śapathe nāsti pātakam  Mn 
satyena śāpayed vipraṃ kṣatriyaṃ vāhanāyudhaiḥ 
gobījakāñcanair vaiśyaṃ śūdraṃ sarvais tu pātakaiḥ  Mn 
agniṃ vāhārayed enam apsu cainaṃ nimajjayet 
putradārasya vāpy enaṃ śirāṃsi sparśayet pṛthak  Mn 
yam iddho na dahaty agnir āpo nonmajjayanti ca 
na cārtim ṛcchati kṣipraṃ sa jñeyaḥ śapathe śuciḥ  Mn 
vatsasya hy abhiśastasya purā bhrātrā yavīyasā 
nāgnir dadāha romāpi satyena jagataḥ spaśaḥ  Mn 
yasmin yasmin vivāde tu kauṭasākṣyaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavet 
tat tat kāryaṃ nivarteta kṛtaṃ cāpy akṛtaṃ bhavet  Mn 
lobhān mohād bhayān maitrāt kāmāt krodhāt tathaiva ca 
ajñānād bālabhāvāc ca sākṣyaṃ vitatham ucyate  Mn 
eṣām anyatame sthāne yaḥ sākṣyam anṛtaṃ vadet 
tasya daṇḍaviśeṣāṃs tu pravakṣyāmy anupūrvaśaḥ  Mn 
lobhāt sahasraṃ daṇḍyas tu mohāt pūrvaṃ tu sāhasam 
bhayād dvau madhyamau daṇḍau maitrāt pūrvaṃ caturguṇam  Mn 
kāmād daśaguṇaṃ pūrvaṃ krodhāt tu triguṇaṃ param 
ajñānād dve śate pūrṇe bāliśyāc chatam eva tu  Mn 
etān āhuḥ kauṭasākṣye proktān daṇḍān manīṣibhiḥ 
dharmasyāvyabhicārārtham adharmaniyamāya ca  Mn 
kauṭasākṣyaṃ tu kurvāṇāṃs trīn varṇān dhārmiko nṛpaḥ 
pravāsayed daṇḍayitvā brāhmaṇaṃ tu vivāsayet  Mn 
daśa sthānāni daṇḍasya manuḥ svayaṃbhuvo 'bravīt 
triṣu varṇeṣu yāni syur akṣato brāhmaṇo vrajet  Mn 
upastham udaraṃ jihvā hastau pādau ca pañcamam 
cakṣur nāsā ca karṇau ca dhanaṃ dehas tathaiva ca  Mn 
anubandhaṃ parijñāya deśakālau ca tattvataḥ 
sārāparādho cālokya daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu pātayet  Mn 
adharmadaṇḍanaṃ loke yaśoghnaṃ kīrtināśanam 
asvargyaṃ ca paratrāpi tasmāt tat parivarjayet  Mn 
adaṇḍyān daṇḍayan rājā daṇḍyāṃś caivāpy adaṇḍayan 
ayaśo mahad āpnoti narakaṃ caiva gacchati  Mn 
vāgdaṇḍaṃ prathamaṃ kuryād dhigdaṇḍaṃ tadanantaram 
tṛtīyaṃ dhanadaṇḍaṃ tu vadhadaṇḍam ataḥ param  Mn 
vadhenāpi yadā tv etān nigrahītuṃ na śaknuyāt 
tadaiṣu sarvam apy etat prayuñjīta catuṣṭayam  Mn 
lokasaṃvyavahārārthaṃ yāḥ saṃjñāḥ prathitā bhuvi 
tāmrarūpyasuvarṇānāṃ tāḥ pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ  Mn 
jālāntaragate bhānau yat sūkṣmaṃ dṛśyate rajaḥ 
prathamaṃ tat pramāṇānāṃ trasareṇuṃ pracakṣate  Mn 
trasareṇavo 'ṣṭau vijñeyā likṣaikā parimāṇataḥ 
tā rājasarṣapas tisras te trayo gaurasarṣapaḥ  Mn 
sarṣapāḥ ṣaḍ yavo madhyas triyavaṃ tv ekakṛṣṇalam 
pañcakṛṣṇalako māṣas te suvarṇas tu ṣoḍaśa  Mn 
palaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ palāni dharaṇaṃ daśa 
dve kṛṣṇale samadhṛte vijñeyo raupyamāṣakaḥ  Mn 
te ṣoḍaśa syād dharaṇaṃ purāṇaś caiva rājataḥ 
kārṣāpaṇas tu vijñeyas tāmrikaḥ kārṣikaḥ paṇaḥ  Mn 
dharaṇāni daśa jñeyaḥ śatamānas tu rājataḥ 
catuḥsauvarṇiko niṣko vijñeyas tu pramāṇataḥ  Mn 
paṇānāṃ dve śate sārdhe prathamaḥ sāhasaḥ smṛtaḥ 
madhyamaḥ pañca vijñeyaḥ sahasraṃ tv eva cottamaḥ  Mn 
ṛṇe deye pratijñāte pañcakaṃ śatam arhati 
apahnave taddviguṇaṃ tan manor anuśāsanam  Mn 
vasiṣṭhavihitāṃ vṛddhiṃ sṛjed vittavivardhinīm 
aśītibhāgaṃ gṛhṇīyān māsād vārdhuṣikaḥ śate  Mn 
dvikaṃ śataṃ vā gṛhṇīyāt satāṃ dharmam anusmaran 
dvikaṃ śataṃ hi gṛhṇāno na bhavaty arthakilbiṣī  Mn 
dvikaṃ trikaṃ catuṣkaṃ ca pañcakaṃ ca śataṃ samam 
māsasya vṛddhiṃ gṛhṇīyād varṇānām anupūrvaśaḥ  Mn 
na tv evādhau sopakāre kausīdīṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt 
na cādheḥ kālasaṃrodhān nisargo 'sti na vikrayaḥ  Mn 
na bhoktavyo balād ādhir bhuñjāno vṛddhim utsṛjet 
mūlyena toṣayec cainam ādhisteno 'nyathā bhavet  Mn 
ādhiś copanidhiś cobhau na kālātyayam arhataḥ 
avahāryau bhavetāṃ tau dīrghakālam avasthitau  Mn 
saṃprītyā bhujyamānāni na naśyanti kadā cana 
dhenur uṣṭro vahann aśvo yaś ca damyaḥ prayujyate  Mn 
yat kiṃ cid daśavarṣāṇi saṃnidhau prekṣate dhanī 
bhujyamānaṃ parais tūṣṇīṃ na sa tal labdhum arhati  Mn 
ajaḍaś ced apogaṇḍo viṣaye cāsya bhujyate 
bhagnaṃ tad vyavahāreṇa bhoktā tad dravyam arhati  Mn 
ādhiḥ sīmā bāladhanaṃ nikṣepopanidhiḥ striyaḥ 
rājasvaṃ śrotriyasvaṃ ca na bhogena praṇaśyati  Mn 
yaḥ svāminānanujñātam ādhiṃ bhūṅkte 'vicakṣaṇaḥ 
tenārdhavṛddhir moktavyā tasya bhogasya niṣkṛtiḥ  Mn 
kusīdavṛddhir dvaiguṇyaṃ nātyeti sakṛd āhṛtā 
dhānye sade lave vāhye nātikrāmati pañcatām  Mn 
kṛtānusārād adhikā vyatiriktā na sidhyati 
kusīdapatham āhus taṃ pañcakaṃ śatam arhati  Mn 
nātisāṃvatsarīṃ vṛddhiṃ na cādṛṣṭāṃ punar haret 
cakravṛddhiḥ kālavṛddhiḥ kāritā kāyikā ca yā  Mn 
ṛṇaṃ dātum aśakto yaḥ kartum icchet punaḥ kriyām 
sa dattvā nirjitāṃ vṛddhiṃ karaṇaṃ parivartayet  Mn 
adarśayitvā tatraiva hiraṇyaṃ parivartayet 
yāvatī saṃbhaved vṛddhis tāvatīṃ dātum arhati  Mn 
cakravṛddhiṃ samārūḍho deśakālavyavasthitaḥ 
atikrāman deśakālau na tatphalam avāpnuyāt  Mn 
samudrayānakuśalā deśakālārthadarśinaḥ 
sthāpayanti tu yāṃ vṛddhiṃ sā tatrādhigamaṃ prati  Mn 
yo yasya pratibhūs tiṣṭhed darśanāyeha mānavaḥ 
adarśayan sa taṃ tasya prayacchet svadhanād ṛṇam  Mn 
prātibhāvyaṃ vṛthādānam ākṣikaṃ saurikāṃ ca yat 
daṇḍaśulkāvaśeṣaṃ ca na putro dātum arhati  Mn 
darśanaprātibhāvye tu vidhiḥ syāt pūrvacoditaḥ 
dānapratibhuvi prete dāyādān api dāpayet  Mn 
adātari punar dātā vijñātaprakṛtāv ṛṇam 
paścāt pratibhuvi prete parīpset kena hetunā  Mn 
nirādiṣṭadhanaś cet tu pratibhūḥ syād alaṃdhanaḥ 
svadhanād eva tad dadyān nirādiṣṭa iti sthitiḥ  Mn 
mattonmattārtādhyadhīnair bālena sthavireṇa vā 
asaṃbaddhakṛtaś caiva vyāvahāro na sidhyati  Mn 
satyā na bhāṣā bhavati yady api syāt pratiṣṭhitā 
bahiś ced bhāṣyate dharmān niyatād vyavahārikāt  Mn 
yogādhamanavikrītaṃ yogadānapratigraham 
yatra vāpy upadhiṃ paśyet tat sarvaṃ vinivartayet  Mn 
grahītā yadi naṣṭaḥ syāt kuṭumbārthe kṛto vyayaḥ 
dātavyaṃ bāndhavais tat syāt pravibhaktair api svataḥ  Mn 
kuṭumbārthe 'dhyadhīno 'pi vyavahāraṃ yam ācaret 
svadeśe vā videśe vā taṃ jyāyān na vicālayet  Mn 
balād dattaṃ balād bhuktaṃ balād yac cāpi lekhitam 
sarvān balakṛtān arthān akṛtān manur abravīt  Mn 
trayaḥ parārthe kliśyanti sākṣiṇaḥ pratibhūḥ kulam 
catvāras tūpacīyante vipra āḍhyo vaṇiṅ nṛpaḥ  Mn 
anādeyaṃ nādadīta parikṣīṇo 'pi pārthivaḥ 
na cādeyaṃ samṛddho 'pi sūkṣmam apy artham utsṛjet  Mn 
anādeyasya cādānād ādeyasya ca varjanāt 
daurbalyaṃ khyāpyate rājñaḥ sa pretyeha ca naśyati  Mn 
svādānād varṇasaṃsargāt tv abalānāṃ ca rakṣaṇāt 
balaṃ saṃjāyate rājñaḥ sa pretyeha ca vardhate  Mn 
tasmād yama iva svāmī svayaṃ hitvā priyāpriye 
varteta yāmyayā vṛttyā jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ  Mn 
yas tv adharmeṇa kāryāṇi mohāt kuryān narādhipaḥ 
acirāt taṃ durātmānaṃ vaśe kurvanti śatravaḥ  Mn 
kāmakrodhau tu saṃyamya yo 'rthān dharmeṇa paśyati 
prajās tam anuvartante samudram iva sindhavaḥ  Mn 
yaḥ sādhayantaṃ chandena vedayed dhanikaṃ nṛpe 
sa rājñā tac caturbhāgaṃ dāpyas tasya ca tad dhanam  Mn 
karmaṇāpi samaṃ kuryād dhanikāyādhamarṇikaḥ 
samo 'vakṛṣṭajātis tu dadyāc chreyāṃs tu tac chanaiḥ  Mn 
anena vidhinā rājā mitho vivadatāṃ nṛṇām 
sākṣipratyayasiddhāni kāryāṇi samatāṃ nayet  Mn 
kulaje vṛttasaṃpanne dharmajñe satyavādini 
mahāpakṣe dhaniny ārye nikṣepaṃ nikṣiped budhaḥ  Mn 
yo yathā nikṣiped dhaste yam arthaṃ yasya mānavaḥ 
sa tathaiva grahītavyo yathā dāyas tathā grahaḥ  Mn 
yo nikṣepaṃ yācyamāno nikṣeptur na prayacchati 
sa yācyaḥ prāḍvivākena tan nikṣeptur asaṃnidhau  Mn 
sākṣyabhāve praṇidhibhir vayorūpasamanvitaiḥ 
apadeśaiś ca saṃnyasya hiraṇyaṃ tasya tattvataḥ  Mn 
sa yadi pratipadyeta yathānyastaṃ yathākṛtam 
na tatra vidyate kiṃ cid yat parair abhiyujyate  Mn 
teṣāṃ na dadyād yadi tu tad dhiraṇyaṃ yathāvidhi 
ubhau nigṛhya dāpyaḥ syād iti dharmasya dhāraṇā  Mn 
nikṣepopanidhī nityaṃ na deyau pratyanantare 
naśyato vinipāte tāv anipāte tv anāśinau  Mn 
svayam eva tu yau dadyān mṛtasya pratyanantare 
na sa rājñābhiyoktavyo na nikṣeptuś ca bandhubhiḥ  Mn 
acchalenaiva cānvicchet tam arthaṃ prītipūrvakam 
vicārya tasya vā vṛttaṃ sāmnaiva parisādhayet  Mn 
nikṣepeṣv eṣu sarveṣu vidhiḥ syāt parisādhane 
samudre nāpnuyāt kiṃ cid yadi tasmān na saṃharet  Mn 
caurair hṛtaṃ jalenoḍham agninā dagdham eva vā 
na dadyād yadi tasmāt sa na saṃharati kiṃ cana  Mn 
nikṣepasyāpahartāram anikṣeptāram eva ca 
sarvair upāyair anvicchec chapathaiś caiva vaidikaiḥ  Mn 
yo nikṣepaṃ nārpayati yaś cānikṣipya yācate 
tāv ubhau cauravac chāsyau dāpyau vā tatsamaṃ damam  Mn 
nikṣepasyāpahartāraṃ tatsamaṃ dāpayed damam 
tathopanidhihartāram aviśeṣeṇa pārthivaḥ  Mn 
upadhābhiś ca yaḥ kaś cit paradravyaṃ haren naraḥ 
sasahāyaḥ sa hantavyaḥ prakāśaṃ vividhair vadhaiḥ  Mn 
nikṣepo yaḥ kṛto yena yāvāṃś ca kulasaṃnidhau 
tāvān eva sa vijñeyo vibruvan daṇḍam arhati  Mn 
mitho dāyaḥ kṛto yena gṛhīto mitha eva vā 
mitha eva pradātavyo yathā dāyas tathā grahaḥ  Mn 
nikṣiptasya dhanasyaivaṃ prītyopanihitasya ca 
rājā vinirṇayaṃ kuryād akṣiṇvan nyāsadhāriṇam  Mn 
vikrīṇīte parasya svaṃ yo 'svāmī svāmyasammataḥ 
na taṃ nayeta sākṣyaṃ tu stenam astenamāninam  Mn 
avahāryo bhavec caiva sānvayaḥ ṣaṭśataṃ damam 
niranvayo 'napasaraḥ prāptaḥ syāc caurakilbiṣam  Mn 
asvāminā kṛto yas tu dāyo vikraya eva vā 
akṛtaḥ sa tu vijñeyo vyavahāre yathā sthitiḥ  Mn 
saṃbhogo dṛśyate yatra na dṛśyetāgamaḥ kva cit 
āgamaḥ kāraṇaṃ tatra na saṃbhoga iti sthitiḥ  Mn 
vikrayād yo dhanaṃ kiṃ cid gṛhṇīyat kulasaṃnidhau 
krayeṇa sa viśuddhaṃ hi nyāyato labhate dhanam  Mn 
atha mūlam anāhāryaṃ prakāśakrayaśodhitaḥ 
adaṇḍyo mucyate rājñā nāṣṭiko labhate dhanam  Mn 
nānyad anyena saṃsṛṣṭa rūpaṃ vikrayam arhati 
na cāsāraṃ na ca nyūnaṃ na dūreṇa tirohitam  Mn 
anyāṃ ced darśayitvānyā voḍhuḥ kanyā pradīyate 
ubhe ta ekaśulkena vahed ity abravīn manuḥ  Mn 
nonmattāyā na kuṣṭhinyā na ca yā spṛṣṭamaithunā 
pūrvaṃ doṣān abhikhyāpya pradātā daṇḍam arhati  Mn 
ṛtvig yadi vṛto yajñe svakarma parihāpayet 
tasya karmānurūpeṇa deyo 'ṃśaḥ sahakartṛbhiḥ  Mn 
dakṣiṇāsu ca dattāsu svakarma parihāpayan 
kṛtsnam eva labhetāṃśam anyenaiva ca kārayet  Mn 
yasmin karmaṇi yās tu syur uktāḥ pratyaṅgadakṣiṇāḥ 
sa eva tā ādidīta bhajeran sarva eva vā  Mn 
rathaṃ haret cādhvaryur brahmādhāne ca vājinam 
hotā vāpi hared aśvam udgātā cāpy anaḥ kraye  Mn 
sarveṣām ardhino mukhyās tadardhenārdhino 'pare 
tṛtīyinas tṛtīyāṃśāś caturthāṃśāś ca pādinaḥ  Mn 
saṃbhūya svāni karmāṇi kurvadbhir iha mānavaiḥ 
anena vidhiyogena kartavyāṃśaprakalpanā  Mn 
dharmārthaṃ yena dattaṃ syāt kasmai cid yācate dhanam 
paścāc ca na tathā tat syān na deyaṃ tasya tad bhavet  Mn 
yadi saṃsādhayet tat tu darpāl lobhena vā punaḥ 
rājñā dāpyaḥ suvarṇaṃ syāt tasya steyasya niṣkṛtiḥ  Mn 
dattasyaiṣoditā dharmyā yathāvad anapakriyā 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi vetanasyānapakriyām  Mn 
bhṛto nārto na kuryād yo darpāt karma yathoditam 
sa daṇḍyaḥ kṛṣṇalāny aṣṭau na deyaṃ cāsya vetanam  Mn 
ārtas tu kuryāt svasthaḥ san yathābhāṣitam āditaḥ 
sa dīrghasyāpi kālasya tal labhetaiva vetanam  Mn 
yathoktam ārtaḥ sustho vā yas tat karma na kārayet 
na tasya vetanaṃ deyam alponasyāpi karmaṇaḥ  Mn 
eṣa dharmo 'khilenokto vetanādānakarmaṇaḥ 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi dharmaṃ samayabhedinām  Mn 
yo grāmadeśasaṃghānāṃ kṛtvā satyena saṃvidam 
visaṃvaden naro lobhāt taṃ rāṣṭrād vipravāsayet  Mn 
nigṛhya dāpayec cainaṃ samayavyabhicāriṇam 
catuḥsuvarṇān ṣaṇniṣkāṃś chatamānaṃ ca rājakam  Mn 
etad daṇḍavidhiṃ kuryād dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ 
grāmajātisamūheṣu samayavyabhicāriṇām  Mn 
krītvā vikrīya vā kiṃ cid yasyehānuśayo bhavet 
so 'ntar daśāhāt tad dravyaṃ dadyāc caivādadīta vā  Mn 
pareṇa tu daśāhasya na dadyān nāpi dāpayet 
ādadāno dadat caiva rājñā daṇḍyau śatāni ṣaṭ  Mn 
yas tu doṣavatīṃ kanyām anākhyāya prayacchati 
tasya kuryān nṛpo daṇḍaṃ svayaṃ ṣaṇṇavatiṃ paṇān  Mn 
akanyeti tu yaḥ kanyāṃ brūyād dveṣeṇa mānavaḥ 
sa śataṃ prāpnuyād daṇḍaṃ tasyā doṣam adarśayan  Mn 
pāṇigrahaṇikā mantrāḥ kanyāsv eva pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
nākanyāsu kva cin nṝṇāṃ luptadharmakriyā hi tāḥ  Mn 
pāṇigrahaṇikā mantrā niyataṃ dāralakṣaṇam 
teṣāṃ niṣṭhā tu vijñeyā vidvadbhiḥ saptame pade  Mn 
yasmin yasmin kṛte kārye yasyehānuśayo bhavet 
tam anena vidhānena dharmye pathi niveśayet  Mn 
paśuṣu svāmināṃ caiva pālānāṃ ca vyatikrame 
vivādaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvad dharmatattvataḥ  Mn 
divā vaktavyatā pāle rātrau svāmini tadgṛhe 
yogakṣeme 'nyathā cet tu pālo vaktavyatām iyāt  Mn 
gopaḥ kṣīrabhṛto yas tu sa duhyād daśato varām 
gosvāmyanumate bhṛtyaḥ sā syāt pāle 'bhṛte bhṛtiḥ  Mn 
naṣṭaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ kṛmibhiḥ śvahataṃ viṣame mṛtam 
hīnaṃ puruṣakāreṇa pradadyāt pāla eva tu  Mn 
vighuṣya tu hṛtaṃ caurair na pālo dātum arhati 
yadi deśe ca kāle ca svāminaḥ svasya śaṃsati  Mn 
karṇau carma ca vālāṃś ca bastiṃ snāyuṃ ca rocanām 
paśuṣu svāmināṃ dadyān mṛteṣv aṅkāni darśayet  Mn 
ajāvike tu saṃruddhe vṛkaiḥ pāle tv anāyati 
yāṃ prasahya vṛko hanyāt pāle tat kilbiṣaṃ bhavet  Mn 
tāsāṃ ced avaruddhānāṃ carantīnāṃ mitho vane 
yām utplutya vṛko hanyān na pālas tatra kilbiṣī  Mn 
dhanuḥśataṃ parīhāro grāmasya syāt samantataḥ 
śamyāpātās trayo vāpi triguṇo nagarasya tu  Mn 
tatrāparivṛtaṃ dhānyaṃ vihiṃsyuḥ paśavo yadi 
na tatra praṇayed daṇḍaṃ nṛpatiḥ paśurakṣiṇām  Mn 
vṛtiṃ tatra prakurvīta yām uṣṭro na vilokayet 
chidraṃ ca vārayet sarvaṃ śvasūkaramukhānugam  Mn 
pathi kṣetre parivṛte grāmāntīye 'tha vā punaḥ 
sapālaḥ śatadaṇḍārho vipālān vārayet paśūn  Mn 
kṣetreṣv anyeṣu tu paśuḥ sapādaṃ paṇam arhati 
sarvatra tu sado deyaḥ kṣetrikasyeti dhāraṇā  Mn 
anirdaśāhāṃ gāṃ sūtāṃ vṛṣān devapaśūṃs tathā 
sapālān vā vipālān vā na daṇḍyān manur abravīt  Mn 
kṣetriyasyātyaye daṇḍo bhāgād daśaguṇo bhavet 
tato 'rdhadaṇḍo bhṛtyānām ajñānāt kṣetrikasya tu  Mn 
etad vidhānam ātiṣṭhed dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ 
svāmināṃ ca paśūnāṃ ca pālānāṃ ca vyatikrame  Mn 
sīmāṃ prati samutpanne vivāde grāmayor dvayoḥ 
jyeṣṭhe māsi nayet sīmāṃ suprakāśeṣu setuṣu  Mn 
sīṃāvṛkṣāṃś ca kurvīta nyagrodhāśvatthakiṃśukān 
śālmalīn sālatālāṃś ca kṣīriṇaś caiva pādapān  Mn 
gulmān veṇūṃś ca vividhān śamīvallīsthalāni ca 
śarān kubjakagulmāṃś ca tathā sīmā na naśyati  Mn 
taḍāgāny udapānāni vāpyaḥ prasravaṇāni ca  MnaM 
sīmāsaṃdhiṣu kāryāṇi devatāyatanāni ca  MnMc 
upachannāni cānyāni sīmāliṅgāni kārayet 
sīmājñāne nṛṇāṃ vīkṣya nityaṃ loke viparyayam  Mn 
aśmano 'sthīni govālāṃs tuṣān bhasma kapālikāḥ 
karīṣam iṣṭakāṅgārāṃś śarkarā vālukās tathā  MnM 
yāni caivaṃprakārāṇi kālād bhūmir na bhakṣayet 
tāni saṃdhiṣu sīmāyām aprakāśāni kārayet  Mn 
etair liṅgair nayet sīmāṃ rājā vivadamānayoḥ 
pūrvabhuktyā ca satatam udakasyāgamena ca  Mn 
yadi sṃśaya eva syāl liṅgānām api darśane 
sākṣipratyaya eva syāt sīmāvādavinirṇayaḥ  Mn 
grāmīyakakulānāṃ ca samakṣaṃ sīmni sākṣiṇaḥ 
praṣṭavyāḥ sīmaliṅgāni tayoś caiva vivādinoḥ  Mn 
te pṛṣṭās tu yathā brūyuḥ samastāḥ sīmni niścayam 
nibadhnīyāt tathā sīmāṃ sarvāṃs tāṃś caiva nāmataḥ  Mn 
śirobhis te gṛhītvorvīṃ sragviṇo raktavāsasaḥ 
sukṛtaiḥ śāpithāḥ svaiḥ svair nayeyus te samañjasam  Mn 
yathoktena nayantas te pūyante satyasākṣiṇaḥ 
viparītaṃ nayantas tu dāpyāḥ syur dviśataṃ damam  Mn 
sākṣyabhāve tu catvāro grāmāḥ sāmantavāsinaḥ 
sīmāvinirṇayaṃ kuryuḥ prayatā rājasaṃnidhau  Mn 
sāmantānām abhāve tu maulānāṃ sīmni sākṣiṇām 
imān apy anuyuñjīta puruṣān vanagocarān  Mn 
vyādhāñ śākunikān gopān kaivartān mūlakhānakān 
vyālagrāhān uñchavṛttīn anyāṃś ca vanacāriṇaḥ  Mn 
te pṛṣṭās tu yathā brūyuḥ sīmāsaṃdhiṣu lakṣaṇam 
tat tathā sthāpayed rājā dharmeṇa grāmayor dvayoḥ  Mn 
kṣetrakūpataḍāgānām ārāmasya gṛhasya ca 
sāmantapratyayo jñeyaḥ sīmāsetuvinirṇayaḥ  Mn 
sāmantāś cen mṛṣā brūyuḥ setau vivādatāṃ nṛṇām 
sarve pṛthak pṛthag daṇḍyā rājñā madhyamasāhasam  Mn 
gṛhaṃ taḍāgam ārāmaṃ kṣetraṃ vā bhīṣayā haran 
śatāni pañca daṇḍyaḥ syād ajñānād dviśato damaḥ  Mn 
sīmāyām aviṣahyāyāṃ svayaṃ rājaiva dharmavit 
pradiśed bhūmim ekeṣām upakārād iti sthitiḥ  Mn 
eṣo 'khilenābhihito dharmaḥ sīmāvinirṇaye 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi vākpāruṣyavinirṇayam  Mn 
śataṃ brāhmaṇam ākruśya kṣatriyo daṇḍam arhati 
vaiśyo 'py ardhaśataṃ dve vā śūdras tu vadham arhati  Mn 
pañcāśad brāhmaṇo daṇḍyaḥ kṣatriyasyābhiśaṃsane 
vaiśye syād ardhapañcāśac chūdre dvādaśako damaḥ  Mn 
samavarṇe dvijātīnāṃ dvādaśaiva vyatikrame 
vādeṣv avacanīyeṣu tad eva dviguṇaṃ bhavet  Mn 
ekajātir dvijātīṃs tu vācā dāruṇayā kṣipan 
jihvāyāḥ prāpnuyāc chedaṃ jaghanyaprabhavo hi saḥ  Mn 
nāmajātigrahaṃ tv eṣām abhidroheṇa kurvataḥ 
nikṣepyo 'yomayaḥ śaṅkur jvalann āsye daśāṅgulaḥ  Mn 
dharmopadeśaṃ darpeṇa viprāṇām asya kurvataḥ 
taptam āsecayet tailaṃ vaktre śrotre ca pārthivaḥ  Mn 
śrutaṃ deśaṃ ca jātiṃ ca karma śarīram eva ca 
vitathena bruvan darpād dāpyaḥ syād dviśataṃ damam  Mn 
kāṇaṃ vāpy atha vā khañjam anyaṃ vāpi tathāvidham 
tathyenāpi bruvan dāpyo daṇḍaṃ kārṣāpaṇāvaram  Mn 
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ jāyāṃ bhrātaraṃ tanayaṃ gurum 
ākṣārayañ śataṃ dāpyaḥ panthānaṃ cādadad guroḥ  Mn 
brāhmaṇakṣatriyābhyāṃ tu daṇḍaḥ kāryo vijānatā 
brāhmaṇe sāhasaḥ pūrvaḥ kṣatriye tv eva madhyamaḥ  Mn 
viṭśūdrayor evam eva svajātiṃ prati tattvataḥ 
chedavarjaṃ praṇayanaṃ daṇḍasyeti viniścayaḥ  Mn 
eṣa daṇḍavidhiḥ prokto vākpāruṣyasya tattvataḥ 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi daṇḍapāruṣyanirṇayam  Mn 
yena kena cid aṅgena hiṃsyāc cec chreṣṭham antyajaḥ 
chettavyaṃ tad tad evāsya tan manor anuśāsanam  Mn 
pāṇim udyamya daṇḍaṃ vā pāṇicchedanam arhati 
pādena praharan kopāt pādacchedanam arhati  Mn 
sahāsanam abhiprepsur utkṛṣṭasyāpakṛṣṭajaḥ 
kaṭyāṃ kṛtāṅko nirvāsyaḥ sphicaṃ vāsyāvakartayet  Mn 
avaniṣṭhīvato darpād dvāv oṣṭhau chedayen nṛpaḥ 
avamūtrayato meḍhram avaśardhayato gudam  Mn 
keśeṣu gṛhṇato hastau chedayed avicārayan 
pādayor dāḍhikāyāṃ ca grīvāyāṃ vṛṣaṇeṣu ca  Mn 
tvagbhedakaḥ śataṃ daṇḍyo lohitasya ca darśakaḥ 
māṃsabhettā tu ṣaṇniṣkān pravāsyas tv asthibhedakaḥ  Mn 
vanaspatīnāṃ sarveṣām upabhogo yathā yathā 
yathā tathā damaḥ kāryo hiṃsāyām iti dhāraṇā  Mn 
manuṣyāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ ca duḥkhāya prahṛte sati 
yathā yathā mahad duḥkhaṃ daṇḍaṃ kuryāt tathā tathā  Mn 
aṅgāvapīḍanāyāṃ ca vraṇaśonitayos tathā 
samutthānavyayaṃ dāpyaḥ sarvadaṇḍam athāpi vā  Mn 
dravyāṇi hiṃsyād yo yasya jñānato 'jñānato 'pi vā 
sa tasyotpādayet tuṣṭiṃ rājñe dadyāc ca tatsamam  Mn 
carmacārmikabhāṇḍeṣu kāṣṭhaloṣṭamayeṣu 
mūlyāt pañcaguṇo daṇḍaḥ puṣpamūlaphaleṣu ca  Mn 
yānasya caiva yātuś ca yānasvāmina eva ca 
daśātivartanāny āhuḥ śeṣe daṇḍo vidhīyate  Mn 
chinnanāsye bhagnayuge tiryakpratimukhāgate 
akṣabhaṅge ca yānasya cakrabhaṅge tathaiva ca  Mn 
chedane caiva yantrāṇāṃ yoktraraśmyos tathaiva ca 
ākrande cāpy apaihīti na daṇḍaṃ manur abravīt  Mn 
yatrāpavartate yugyaṃ vaiguṇyāt prājakasya tu 
tatra svāmī bhaved daṇḍyo hiṃsāyāṃ dviśataṃ damam  Mn 
prājakaś ced bhaved āptaḥ prājako daṇḍam arhati 
yugyasthāḥ prājake 'nāpte sarve daṇḍyāḥ śataṃ śatam  Mn 
sa cet tu pathi saṃruddhaḥ paśubhir vā rathena vā 
pramāpayet prāṇabhṛtas tatra daṇḍo 'vicāritaḥ  Mn 
manuṣyamāraṇe kṣipraṃ cauravat kilbiṣaṃ bhavet 
prāṇabhṛtsu mahatsv ardhaṃ gogajoṣṭrahayādiṣu  Mn 
kṣudrakāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ tu hiṃsāyāṃ dviśato damaḥ 
pañcāśat tu bhaved daṇḍaḥ śubheṣu mṛgapakṣiṣu  Mn 
gardhabhājāvikānāṃ tu daṇḍaḥ syāt pañcamāṣikaḥ 
māṣikas tu bhaved daṇḍaḥ śvasūkaranipātane  Mn 
bhāryā putraś ca dāsaś ca preṣyo bhrātrā ca sodaraḥ 
prāptāparādhās tāḍyāḥ syū rajjvā veṇudalena vā  Mn 
pṛṣṭhatas tu śarīrasya nottamāṅge kathaṃ cana 
ato 'nyathā tu praharan prāptaḥ syāc caurakilbiṣam  Mn 
eṣo 'khilenābhihito daṇḍapāruṣyanirṇayaḥ 
stenasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ daṇḍavinirṇaye  Mn 
paramaṃ yatnam ātiṣṭhet stenānāṃ nigrahe nṛpaḥ 
stenānāṃ nigrahād asya yaśo rāṣṭraṃ ca vardhate  Mn 
abhayasya hi yo dātā sa pūjyaḥ satataṃ nṛpaḥ 
sattraṃ hi vardhate tasya sadaivābhayadakṣiṇam  Mn 
sarvato dharmaṣaḍbhāgo rājño bhavati rakṣataḥ 
adharmād api ṣaḍbhāgo bhavaty asya hy arakṣataḥ  Mn
