yad adhīte yad yajate yad dadāti yad arcati 
tasya ṣaḍbhāgabhāg rājā samyag bhavati rakṣaṇāt  Mn 
rakṣan dharmeṇa bhūtāni rājā vadhyāṃś ca ghātayan 
yajate 'har ahar yajñaiḥ sahasraśatadakṣiṇaiḥ  Mn 
yo 'rakṣan balim ādatte karaṃ śulkaṃ ca pārthivaḥ 
pratibhāgaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ ca sa sadyo narakaṃ vrajet  Mn 
arakṣitāraṃ rājānaṃ baliṣaḍbhāgahāriṇam 
tam āhuḥ sarvalokasya samagramalahārakam  Mn 
anapekṣitamaryādaṃ nāstikaṃ vipraluṃpakam 
arakṣitāram attāraṃ nṛpaṃ vidyād adhogatim  Mn 
adhārmikaṃ tribhir nyāyair nigṛhṇīyāt prayatnataḥ 
nirodhanena bandhena vividhena vadhena ca  Mn 
nigraheṇa hi pāpānāṃ sādhūnāṃ saṃgraheṇa ca 
dvijātaya ivejyābhiḥ pūyante satataṃ nṛpāḥ  Mn 
kṣantavyaṃ prabhuṇā nityaṃ kṣipatāṃ kāryiṇāṃ nṛṇām 
bālavṛddhāturāṇāṃ ca kurvatā hitam ātmanaḥ  Mn 
yaḥ kṣipto marṣayaty ārtais tena svarge mahīyate 
yas tv aiśvaryān na kṣamate narakaṃ tena gacchati  Mn 
rājā stenena gantavyo muktakeśena dhāvatā 
ācakṣāṇena tat steyam evaṃkarmāsmi śādhi mām  Mn 
skandhenādāya musalaṃ laguḍaṃ vāpi khādiram 
śaktiṃ cobhayatas tīkṣṇām āyasaṃ daṇḍam eva vā  Mn 
śāsanād vā vimokṣād vā stenaḥ steyād vimucyate 
aśāsitvā tu taṃ rājā stenasyāpnoti kilbiṣam  Mn 
annāde bhrūṇahā mārṣṭi patyau bhāryāpacāriṇī 
gurau śiṣyaś ca yājyaś ca steno rājani kilbiṣam  Mn 
rājabhiḥ kṛtadaṇḍās tu kṛtvā pāpāni mānavāḥ 
nirmalāḥ svargam āyānti santaḥ sukṛtino yathā  Mn 
yas tu rajjuṃ ghaṭaṃ kūpād dhared bhindyāc ca yaḥ prapām 
sa daṇḍaṃ prāpnuyān māṣaṃ tac ca tasmin samāharet  Mn 
dhānyaṃ daśabhyaḥ kumbhebhyo harato 'bhyadhikaṃ vadhaḥ 
śeṣe 'py ekādaśaguṇaṃ dāpyas tasya ca tad dhanam  Mn 
tathā dharimameyānāṃ śatād abhyadhike vadhaḥ 
suvarṇarajatādīnām uttamānāṃ ca vāsasām  Mn 
pañcāśatas tv abhyadhike hastacchedanam iṣyate 
śeṣe tv ekādaśaguṇaṃ mūlyād daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet  Mn 
puruṣāṇāṃ kulīnānāṃ nārīṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ 
mukhyānāṃ caiva ratnānāṃ haraṇe vadham arhati  Mn 
mahāpaśūnāṃ haraṇe śastrāṇām auṣadhasya ca 
kālam āsādya kāryaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ rājā prakalpayet  Mn 
goṣu brāhmaṇasaṃsthāsu churikāyāś ca bhedane 
paśūnāṃ haraṇe caiva sadyaḥ kāryo 'rdhapādikaḥ  Mn 
sūtrakārpāsakiṇvānāṃ gomayasya guḍasya ca 
dadhnaḥ kṣīrasya takrasya pānīyasya tṛṇasya ca  Mn 
veṇuvaidalabhāṇḍānāṃ lavaṇānāṃ tathaiva ca 
mṛṇmayānāṃ ca haraṇe mṛdo bhasmana eva ca  Mn 
matsyānāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ caiva tailasya ca ghṛtasya ca 
māṃsasya madhunaś caiva yac cānyat paśusaṃbhavam  Mn 
anyeṣāṃ caivamādīnāṃ madyānām odanasya ca 
pakvānnānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ tanmulyād dviguṇo damaḥ  Mn 
puṣpeṣu harite dhānye gulmavallīnageṣu ca 
anyeṣv aparipūteṣu daṇḍaḥ syāt pañcakṛṣṇalaḥ  Mn 
paripūteṣu dhānyeṣu śākamūlaphaleṣu ca 
niranvaye śataṃ daṇḍaḥ sānvaye 'rdhaśataṃ damaḥ  Mn 
syāt sāhasaṃ tv anvayavat prasabhaṃ karma yat kṛtam 
niranvayaṃ bhavet steyaṃ hṛtvāpavyayate ca yat  Mn 
yas tv etāny upakḷptāni dravyāṇi stenayen naraḥ 
tam ādyaṃ daṇḍayed rājā yaś cāgniṃ corayed gṛhāt  Mn 
yena yena yathāṅgena steno nṛṣu viceṣṭate 
tat tad eva haret tasya pratyādeśāya pārthivaḥ  Mn 
pitācāryaḥ suhṛn mātā bhāryā putraḥ purohitaḥ 
nādaṇḍyo nāma rājño 'sti yaḥ svadharme na tiṣṭhati  Mn 
kārṣāpaṇaṃ bhaved daṇḍyo yatrānyaḥ prākṛto janaḥ 
tatra rājā bhaved daṇḍyaḥ sahasram iti dhāraṇā  Mn 
aṣṭāpādyaṃ tu śūdrasya steye bhavati kilbiṣam 
ṣoḍaśaiva tu vaiśyasya dvātriṃśat kṣatriyasya ca  Mn 
brāhmaṇasya catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ pūrṇaṃ vāpi śataṃ bhavet 
dviguṇā vā catuḥṣaṣṭis taddoṣaguṇavid dhi saḥ  Mn 
vānaspatyaṃ mūlaphalaṃ dārv agnyarthaṃ tathaiva ca 
tṛṇaṃ ca gobhyo grāsārtham asteyaṃ manur abravīt  Mn 
yo 'dattādāyino hastāl lipseta brāhmaṇo dhanam 
yājanādhyāpanenāpi yathā stenas tathaiva saḥ  Mn 
dvijo 'dhvagaḥ kṣīṇavṛttir dvāv ikṣū dve ca mūlake 
ādadānaḥ parakṣetrān na daṇḍaṃ dātum arhati  Mn 
asaṃditānāṃ saṃdātā saṃditānāṃ ca mokṣakaḥ 
dāsāśvarathahartā ca prāptaḥ syāc corakilbiṣam  Mn 
anena vidhinā rājā kurvāṇaḥ stenanigraham 
yaśo 'smin prāpnuyāl loke pretya cānuttamaṃ sukham  Mn 
aindraṃ sthānam abhiprepsur yaśaś cākṣayam avyayam 
nopekṣeta kṣaṇam api rājā sāhasikaṃ naram  Mn 
vāgduṣṭāt taskarāc caiva daṇḍenaiva ca hiṃsataḥ 
sāhasasya naraḥ kartā vijñeyaḥ pāpakṛttamaḥ  Mn 
sāhase vartamānaṃ tu yo marṣayati pārthivaḥ 
sa vināśaṃ vrajaty āśu vidveṣaṃ cādhigacchati  Mn 
na mitrakāraṇād rājā vipulād vā dhanāgamāt 
samutsṛjet sāhasikān sarvabhūtabhayāvahān  Mn 
śastraṃ dvijātibhir grāhyaṃ dharmo yatroparudhyate 
dvijātīnāṃ ca varṇānāṃ viplave kālakārite  Mn 
ātmanaś ca paritrāṇe dakṣiṇānāṃ ca saṃgare 
strīviprābhyupapattau ca ghnan dharmeṇa na duṣyati  Mn 
guruṃ vā bālavṛddhau vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā bahuśrutam 
ātatāyinam āyāntaṃ hanyād evāvicārayan  Mn 
nātatāyivadhe doṣo hantur bhavati kaś cana 
prakāśaṃ vāprakāśaṃ vā manyus taṃ manyum ṛcchati  Mn 
paradārābhimarśeṣu pravṛttān nṝn mahīpatiḥ 
udvejanakarair daṇḍaiś chinnayitvā pravāsayet  Mn 
tatsamuttho hi lokasya jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ 
yena mūlaharo 'dharmaḥ sarvanāśāya kalpate  Mn 
parasya patnyā puruṣaḥ saṃbhāṣāṃ yojayan rahaḥ 
pūrvam ākṣārito doṣaiḥ prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam  Mn 
yas tv anākṣāritaḥ pūrvam abhibhāṣate kāraṇāt 
na doṣaṃ prāpnuyāt kiṃ cin na hi tasya vyatikramaḥ  Mn 
parastriyaṃ yo 'bhivadet tīrthe 'raṇye vane 'pi vā 
nadīnāṃ vāpi saṃbhede sa saṃgrahaṇam āpnuyāt  Mn 
upacārakriyā keliḥ sparśo bhūṣaṇavāsasām 
saha khaṭvāsanaṃ caiva sarvaṃ saṃgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam  Mn 
striyaṃ spṛśed adeśe yaḥ spṛṣṭo vā marṣayet tayā 
parasparasyānumate sarvaṃ saṃgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam  Mn 
abrāhmaṇaḥ saṃgrahaṇe prāṇāntaṃ daṇḍam arhati 
caturṇām api varṇānāṃ dārā rakṣyatamāḥ sadā  Mn 
bhikṣukā bandinaś caiva dīkṣitāḥ kāravas tathā 
saṃbhāṣanaṃ saha strībhiḥ kuryur aprativāritāḥ  Mn 
na saṃbhāṣāṃ parastrībhiḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ samācaret 
niṣiddho bhāṣamāṇas tu suvarṇaṃ daṇḍam arhati  Mn 
naiṣa cāraṇadāreṣu vidhir nātmopajīviṣu 
sajjayanti hi te nārīr nigūḍhāś cārayanti ca  Mn 
kiṃ cid eva tu dāpyaḥ syāt saṃbhāṣāṃ tābhir ācaran 
praiṣyāsu caikabhaktāsu rahaḥ pravrajitāsu ca  Mn 
yo 'kāmāṃ dūṣayet kanyāṃ sa sadyo vadham arhati 
sakāmāṃ dūṣayaṃs tulyo na vadhaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥ  Mn 
kanyāṃ bhajantīm utkṛṣṭaṃ na kiṃ cid api dāpayet 
jaghanyaṃ sevamānāṃ tu saṃyatāṃ vāsayed gṛhe  Mn 
uttamāṃ sevamānas tu jaghanyo vadham arhati 
śulkaṃ dadyāt sevamānaḥ samām icchet pitā yadi  Mn 
abhiṣahya tu yaḥ kanyāṃ kuryād darpeṇa mānavaḥ 
tasyāśu kartye aṅgulyau daṇḍaṃ cārhati ṣaṭśatam  Mn 
sakāmāṃ dūṣayaṃs tulyo nāṅgulicchedam āpnuyāt 
dviśataṃ tu damaṃ dāpyaḥ prasaṅgavinivṛttaye  Mn 
kanyaiva kanyāṃ yā kuryāt tasyāḥ syād dviśato damaḥ 
śulkaṃ ca dviguṇaṃ dadyāc chiphāś caivāpnuyād daśa  Mn 
yā tu kanyāṃ prakuryāt strī sā sadyo mauṇḍyam arhati 
aṅgulyor eva vā chedaṃ khareṇodvahanaṃ tathā  Mn 
bhartāraṃ laṅghayed yā tu strī jñātiguṇadarpitā 
tāṃ śvabhiḥ khādayed rājā saṃsthāne bahusaṃsthite  Mn 
pumāṃsaṃ dāhayet pāpaṃ śayane tapta āyase 
abhyādadhyuś ca kāṣṭhāni tatra dahyeta pāpakṛt  Mn 
saṃvatsarābhiśastasya duṣṭasya dviguṇo damaḥ 
vrātyayā saha saṃvāse cāṇḍālyā tāvad eva tu  Mn 
śūdro guptam aguptaṃ vā dvaijātaṃ varṇam āvasan 
aguptam aṅgasarvasvair guptaṃ sarveṇa hīyate  Mn 
vaiśyaḥ sarvasvadaṇḍaḥ syāt saṃvatsaranirodhataḥ 
sahasraṃ kṣatriyo daṇḍyo mauṇḍyaṃ mūtreṇa cārhati  Mn 
brāhmaṇīṃ yady aguptāṃ tu gacchetāṃ vaiśyapārthivau 
vaiśyaṃ pañcaśataṃ kuryāt kṣatriyaṃ tu sahasriṇam  Mn 
ubhāv api tu tāv eva brāhmaṇyā guptayā saha 
viplutau śūdravad daṇḍyau dagdhavyau vā kaṭāgninā  Mn 
sahasraṃ brāhmaṇo daṇḍyo guptāṃ viprāṃ balād vrajan 
śatāni pañca daṇḍyaḥ syād icchantyā saha saṃgataḥ  Mn 
mauṇḍyaṃ prāṇāntikaṃ daṇḍo brāhmaṇasya vidhīyate 
itareṣāṃ tu varṇānāṃ daṇḍaḥ prāṇāntiko bhavet  Mn 
na jātu brāhmaṇaṃ hanyāt sarvapāpeṣv api sthitam 
rāṣṭrād enaṃ bahiḥ kuryāt samagradhanam akṣatam  Mn 
na brāhmaṇavadhād bhūyān adharmo vidyate bhuvi 
tasmād asya vadhaṃ rājā manasāpi na cintayet  Mn 
vaiśyaś cet kṣatriyāṃ guptāṃ vaiśyāṃ vā kṣatriyo vrajet 
yo brāhmaṇyām aguptāyāṃ tāv ubhau daṇḍam arhataḥ  Mn 
sahasraṃ brāhmaṇo daṇḍaṃ dāpyo gupte tu te vrajan 
śūdrāyāṃ kṣatriyaviśoḥ sāhasro vai bhaved damaḥ  Mn 
kṣatriyāyām aguptāyāṃ vaiśye pañcaśataṃ damaḥ 
mūtreṇa mauṇḍyam icchet tu kṣatriyo daṇḍam eva vā  Mn 
agupte kṣatriyāvaiśye śūdrāṃ vā brāhmaṇo vrajan 
śatāni pañca daṇḍyaḥ syāt sahasraṃ tv antyajastriyam  Mn 
yasya stenaḥ pure nāsti nānyastrīgo na duṣṭavāk 
na sāhasikadaṇḍaghno sa rājā śakralokabhāk  Mn 
eteṣāṃ nigraho rājñaḥ pañcānāṃ viṣaye svake 
sāṃrājyakṛt sajātyeṣu loke caiva yaśaskaraḥ  Mn 
ṛtvijaṃ yas tyajed yājyo yājyaṃ ca rtvik tyajed yadi 
śaktaṃ karmaṇy aduṣṭaṃ ca tayor daṇḍaḥ śataṃ śatam  Mn 
na mātā na pitā na strī na putras tyāgam arhati 
tyajann apatitān etān rājñā daṇḍyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ  Mn 
āśrameṣu dvijātīnāṃ kārye vivadatāṃ mithaḥ 
na vibrūyān nṛpo dharmaṃ cikīrṣan hitam ātmanaḥ  Mn 
yathārham etān abhyarcya brāhmaṇaiḥ saha pārthivaḥ 
sāntvena praśamayyādau svadharmaṃ pratipādayet  Mn 
prativeśyānuveśyau ca kalyāṇe viṃśatidvije 
arhāv abhojayan vipro daṇḍam arhati māṣakam  Mn 
śrotriyaḥ śrotriyaṃ sādhuṃ bhūtikṛtyeṣv abhojayan 
tadannaṃ dviguṇaṃ dāpyo hiraṇyaṃ caiva māṣakam  Mn 
andho jaḍaḥ pīṭhasarpī saptatyā sthaviraś ca yaḥ 
śrotriyeṣūpakurvaṃś ca na dāpyāḥ kena cit karam  Mn 
śrotriyaṃ vyādhitārtau ca bālavṛddhāv akiṃcanam 
mahākulīnam āryaṃ ca rājā saṃpūjayet sadā  Mn 
śālmalīphalake ślakṣṇe nenijyān nejakaḥ śanaiḥ 
na ca vāsāṃsi vāsobhir nirharen na ca vāsayet  Mn 
tantuvāyo daśapalaṃ dadyād ekapalādhikam 
ato 'nyathā vartamāno dāpyo dvādaśakaṃ damam  Mn 
śulkasthāneṣu kuśalāḥ sarvapaṇyavicakṣaṇāḥ 
kuryur arghaṃ yathāpaṇyaṃ tato viṃśaṃ nṛpo haret  Mn 
rājñaḥ prakhyātabhāṇḍāni pratiṣiddhāni yāni ca 
tāṇi nirharato lobhāt sarvahāraṃ haren nṛpaḥ  Mn 
śulkasthānaṃ pariharann akāle krayavikrayī 
mithyāvādī ca saṃkhyāne dāpyo 'ṣṭaguṇam atyayam  Mn 
āgamaṃ nirgamaṃ sthānaṃ tathā vṛddhikṣayāv ubhau 
vicārya sarvapaṇyānāṃ kārayet krayavikrayau  Mn 
pañcarātre pañcarātre pakṣe pakṣe 'tha vā gate 
kurvīta caiṣāṃ pratyakṣam arghasaṃsthāpanaṃ nṛpaḥ  Mn 
tulāmānaṃ pratīmānaṃ sarvaṃ ca syāt sulakṣitam 
ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsu ca māseṣu punar eva parīkṣayet  Mn 
paṇaṃ yānaṃ tare dāpyaṃ pauruṣo 'rdhapaṇaṃ tare 
pādaṃ paśuś ca yoṣic ca pādārdhaṃ riktakaḥ pumān  Mn 
bhāṇḍapūrṇāni yānāni tāryaṃ dāpyāni sārataḥ 
riktabhāṇḍāni yat kiṃ cit pumāṃsaś cāparicchadāḥ  Mn 
dīrghādhvani yathādeśaṃ yathākālaṃ taro bhavet 
nadītīreṣu tad vidyāt samudre nāsti lakṣaṇam  Mn 
garbhiṇī tu dvimāsādis tathā pravrajito muniḥ 
brāhmaṇā liṅginaś caiva na dāpyās tārikaṃ tare  Mn 
yan nāvi kiṃ cid dāśānāṃ viśīryetāparādhataḥ 
tad dāśair eva dātavyaṃ samāgamya svato 'ṃśataḥ  Mn 
eṣa nauyāyinām ukto vyavahārasya nirṇayaḥ 
dāśāparādhatas toye daivike nāsti nigrahaḥ  Mn 
vāṇijyaṃ kārayed vaiśyaṃ kusīdaṃ kṛṣim eva ca 
paśūnāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ caiva dāsyaṃ śūdraṃ dvijanmanām  Mn 
kṣatriyaṃ caiva vaiśyaṃ ca brāhmaṇo vṛttikarśitau 
bibhṛyād ānṛśaṃsyena svāni karmāṇi kārayet  Mn 
dāsyaṃ tu kārayaṃl lobhād brāhmaṇaḥ saṃskṛtān dvijān 
anicchataḥ prābhavatyād rājñā daṇḍyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ  Mn 
śūdraṃ tu kārayed dāsyaṃ krītam akrītam eva vā 
dāsyāyaiva hi sṛṣṭo 'sau brāhmaṇasya svayaṃbhuvā  Mn 
na svāminā nisṛṣṭo 'pi śūdro dāsyād vimucyate 
nisargajaṃ hi tat tasya kas tasmāt tad apohati  Mn 
dhvajāhṛto bhaktadāso gṛhajaḥ krītadattrimau 
paitriko daṇḍadāsaś ca saptaite dāsayonayaḥ  Mn 
bhāryā putraś ca dāsaś ca traya evādhanāḥ smṛtāḥ 
yat te samadhigacchanti yasya te tasya tad dhanam  Mn 
visrabdhaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ śūdrād dravyopādānam ācaret 
na hi tasyāsti kiṃ cit svaṃ bhartṛhāryadhano hi saḥ  Mn 
vaiśyaśūdrau prayatnena svāni karmāṇi kārayet 
tau hi cyutau svakarmabhyaḥ kṣobhayetām idaṃ jagat  Mn 
ahany ahany avekṣeta karmāntān vāhanāni ca 
āyavyayau ca niyatāv ākarān kośam eva ca  Mn 
evaṃ sarvān imān rājā vyavahārān samāpayan 
vyapohya kilbiṣaṃ sarvaṃ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim  Mn 
puruṣasya striyāś caiva dharme vartmani tiṣṭhatoḥ 
saṃyoge viprayoge ca dharmān vakṣyāmi śāśvatān  Mn 
asvatantrāḥ striyaḥ kāryāḥ puruṣaiḥ svair divāniśam 
viṣayeṣu ca sajjantyaḥ saṃsthāpyā ātmano vaśe  Mn 
pitā rakṣati kaumāre bhartā rakṣati yauvane 
rakṣanti sthavire putrā na strī svātantryam arhati  Mn 
kāle 'dātā pitā vācyo vācyaś cānupayan patiḥ 
mṛte bhartari putras tu vācyo mātur arakṣitā  Mn 
sūkṣmebhyo 'pi prasaṅgebhyaḥ striyo rakṣyā viśeṣataḥ 
dvayor hi kulayoḥ śokam āvaheyur arakṣitāḥ  Mn 
imaṃ hi sarvavarṇānāṃ paśyanto dharmam uttamam 
yatante rakṣituṃ bhāryāṃ bhartāro durbalā api  Mn 
svāṃ prasūtiṃ caritraṃ ca kulam ātmānam eva ca 
svaṃ ca dharmaṃ prayatnena jāyāṃ rakṣan hi rakṣati  Mn 
patir bhāryāṃ saṃpraviśya garbho bhūtveha jāyate 
jāyāyās tad dhi jāyātvaṃ yad asyāṃ jāyate punaḥ  Mn 
yādṛśaṃ bhajate hi strī sutaṃ sūte tathāvidham 
tasmāt prajāviśuddhyarthaṃ striyaṃ rakṣet prayatnataḥ  Mn 
na kaś cid yoṣitaḥ śaktaḥ prasahya parirakṣitum 
etair upāyayogais tu śakyās tāḥ parirakṣitum  Mn 
arthasya saṃgrahe caināṃ vyaye caiva niyojayet 
śauce dharme 'nnapaktyāṃ ca pāriṇāhyasya vekṣaṇe  Mn 
arakṣitā gṛhe ruddhāḥ puruṣair āptakāribhiḥ 
ātmānam ātmanā yās tu rakṣeyus tāḥ surakṣitāḥ  Mn 
pānaṃ durjanasaṃsargaḥ patyā ca viraho 'ṭanam 
svapno 'nyagehavāsaś ca nārīsaṃdūṣaṇāni ṣaṭ  Mn 
naitā rūpaṃ parīkṣante nāsāṃ vayasi saṃsthitiḥ 
surūpaṃ vā virūpaṃ vā pumān ity eva bhuñjate  Mn 
pauṃścalyāc calacittāc ca naisnehyāc ca svabhāvataḥ 
rakṣitā yatnato 'pīha bhartṛṣv etā vikurvate  Mn 
evaṃ svabhāvaṃ jñātvāsāṃ prajāpatinisargajam 
paramaṃ yatnam ātiṣṭhet puruṣo rakṣaṇaṃ prati  Mn 
śayyāsanam alaṅkāraṃ kāmaṃ krodham anārjavam Manāryatām 
drohabhāvaṃ kucaryāṃ ca strībhyo manur akalpayat  Mn 
nāsti strīṇāṃ kriyā mantrair iti dharme vyavasthitiḥ 
nirindriyā hy amantrāś ca strībhyo 'nṛtam iti sthitiḥ  Mn 
tathā ca śrutayo bahvyo nigītā nigameṣv api 
svālakṣaṇyaparīkṣārthaṃ tāsāṃ śṛṇuta niṣkṛtīḥ  Mn 
yan me mātā pralulubhe vicaranty apativratā 
tan me retaḥ pitā vṛṅktām ity asyaitan nidarśanam  Mn 
dhyāyaty aniṣṭaṃ yat kiṃ cit pāṇigrāhasya cetasā 
tasyaiṣa vyabhicārasya nihnavaḥ samyag ucyate  Mn 
yādṛgguṇena bhartrā strī saṃyujyeta yathāvidhi 
tādṛgguṇā sā bhavati samudreṇeva nimnagā  Mn 
akṣamālā vasiṣṭhena saṃyuktādhamayonijā 
śāraṅgī mandapālena jagāmābhyarhaṇīyatām  Mn 
etāś cānyāś ca loke 'sminn apakṛṣṭaprasūtayaḥ 
utkarṣaṃ yoṣitaḥ prāptāḥ svaiḥ svair bhartṛguṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ  Mn 
eṣoditā lokayātrā nityaṃ strīpuṃsayoḥ śubhā 
pretyeha ca sukhodarkān prajādharmān nibodhata  Mn 
prajanārthaṃ mahābhāgāḥ pūjārhā gṛhadīptayaḥ 
striyaḥ śriyaś ca geheṣu na viśeṣo 'sti kaś cana  Mn 
utpādanam apatyasya jātasya paripālanam 
pratyahaṃ lokayātrāyāḥ pratyakṣaṃ strī nibandhanam  Mn 
apatyaṃ dharmakāryāṇi śuśrūṣā ratir uttamā 
dārādhīnas tathā svargaḥ pitṝṇām ātmanaś ca ha  Mn 
patiṃ yā nābhicarati manovāgdehasaṃyatā 
sā bhartṛlokān āpnoti sadbhiḥ sādhvīti cocyate  Mn 
vyabhicārāt tu bhartuḥ strī loke prāpnoti nindyatām 
sṛgālayoniṃ cāpnoti pāparogaiś ca pīḍyate  Mn 
putraṃ pratyuditaṃ sadbhiḥ pūrvajaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ 
viśvajanyam imaṃ puṇyam upanyāsaṃ nibodhata  Mn 
bhartari putraṃ vijānanti śrutidvaidhaṃ tu kartari 
āhur utpādakaṃ ke cid apare kṣetriṇaṃ viduḥ  Mn 
kṣetrabhūtā smṛtā nārī bījabhūtaḥ smṛtaḥ pumān 
kṣetrabījasamāyogāt saṃbhavaḥ sarvadehinām  Mn 
viśiṣṭaṃ kutra cid bījaṃ strīyonis tv eva kutra cit 
ubhayaṃ tu samaṃ yatra sā prasūtiḥ praśasyate  Mn 
bījasya caiva yonyāś ca bījam utkṛṣṭam ucyate 
sarvabhūtaprasūtir hi bījalakṣaṇalakṣitā  Mn 
yādṛśaṃ tūpyate bījaṃ kṣetre kālopapādite 
tādṛg rohati tat tasmin bījaṃ svair vyañjitaṃ guṇaiḥ  Mn 
iyaṃ bhūmir hi bhūtānāṃ śāśvatī yonir ucyate 
na ca yoniguṇān kāṃś cid bījaṃ puṣyati puṣṭiṣu  Mn 
bhūmāv apy ekakedāre kāloptāni kṛṣīvalaiḥ 
nānārūpāṇi jāyante bījānīha svabhāvataḥ  Mn 
vrīhayaḥ śālayo mudgās tilā māṣās tathā yavāḥ 
yathābījaṃ prarohanti laśunānīkṣavas tathā  Mn 
anyad uptaṃ jātam anyad ity etan nopapadyate 
upyate yad dhi yad bījaṃ tat tad eva prarohati  Mn 
tat prājñena vinītena jñānavijñānavedinā 
āyuṣkāmena vaptavyaṃ na jātu parayoṣiti  Mn 
atra gāthā vāyugītāḥ kīrtayanti purāvidaḥ 
yathā bījaṃ na vaptavyaṃ puṃsā paraparigrahe  Mn 
naśyatīṣur yathā viddhaḥ khe viddham anuvidhyataḥ 
tathā naśyati vai kṣipraṃ bījaṃ paraparigrahe  Mn 
pṛthor apīmāṃ pṛthivīṃ bhāryāṃ pūrvavido viduḥ 
sthāṇucchedasya kedāram āhuḥ śālyavato mṛgam  Mn 
etāvān eva puruṣo yaj jāyātmā prajeti ha 
viprāḥ prāhus tathā caitad yo bhartā sā smṛtāṅganā  Mn 
na niṣkrayavisargābhyāṃ bhartur bhāryā vimucyate 
evaṃ dharmaṃ vijānīmaḥ prāk prajāpatinirmitam  Mn 
sakṛd aṃśo nipatati sakṛt kanyā pradīyate 
sakṛd āha dadānīti trīṇy etāni satāṃ sakṛt  Mn 
yathā go'śvoṣṭradāsīṣu mahiṣy ajāvikāsu ca 
notpādakaḥ prajābhāgī tathaivānyāṅganāsv api  Mn 
ye 'kṣetriṇo bījavantaḥ parakṣetrapravāpiṇaḥ 
te vai sasyasya jātasya na labhante phalaṃ kva cit  Mn 
yad anyagoṣu vṛṣabho vatsānāṃ janayec chatam 
gominām eva te vatsā moghaṃ skanditam ārṣabham  Mn 
tathaivākṣetriṇo bījaṃ parakṣetrapravāpiṇaḥ 
kurvanti kṣetriṇām arthaṃ na bījī labhate phalam  Mn 
phalaṃ tv anabhisaṃdhāya kṣetriṇāṃ bījināṃ tathā 
pratyakṣaṃ kṣetriṇām artho bījād yonir galīyasī  Mn 
kriyābhyupagamāt tv etad bījārthaṃ yat pradīyate 
tasyeha bhāginau dṛṣṭau bījī kṣetrika eva ca  Mn 
oghavātāhṛtaṃ bījaṃ yasya kṣetre prarohati 
kṣetrikasyaiva tad bījaṃ na vaptā labhate phalam  Mn 
eṣa dharmo gavāśvasya dāsyuṣṭrājāvikasya ca 
vihaṃgamahiṣīṇāṃ ca vijñeyaḥ prasavaṃ prati  Mn 
etad vaḥ sāraphalgutvaṃ bījayonyoḥ prakīrtitam 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi yoṣitāṃ dharmam āpadi  Mn 
bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya bhāryā yā gurupatny anujasya sā 
yavīyasas tu yā bhāryā snuṣā jyeṣṭhasya sā smṛtā  Mn 
jyeṣṭho yavīyaso bhāryāṃ yavīyān vāgrajastriyam 
patitau bhavato gatvā niyuktāv apy anāpadi  Mn 
devarād vā sapiṇḍād vā striyā samyaṅ niyuktayā 
prajepsitāādhigantavyā saṃtānasya parikṣaye  Mn 
vidhavāyāṃ niyuktas tu ghṛtākto vāgyato niśi 
ekam utpādayet putraṃ na dvitīyaṃ kathaṃ cana  Mn 
dvitīyam eke prajanaṃ manyante strīṣu tadvidaḥ 
anirvṛtaṃ niyogārthaṃ paśyanto dharmatas tayoḥ  Mn 
vidhavāyāṃ niyogārthe nirvṛtte tu yathāvidhi 
guruvac ca snuṣāvac ca varteyātāṃ parasparam  Mn 
niyuktau yau vidhiṃ hitvā varteyātāṃ tu kāmataḥ 
tāv ubhau patitau syātāṃ snuṣāgagurutalpagau  Mn 
nānyasmin vidhavā nārī niyoktavyā dvijātibhiḥ 
anyasmin hi niyuñjānā dharmaṃ hanyuḥ sanātanam  Mn 
nodvāhikeṣu mantreṣu niyogaḥ kīrtyate kva cit 
na vivāhavidhāv uktaṃ vidhavāvedanaṃ punaḥ  Mn 
ayaṃ dvijair hi vidvadbhiḥ paśudharmo vigarhitaḥ 
manuṣyāṇām api prokto vene rājyaṃ praśāsati  Mn 
sa mahīm akhilāṃ bhuñjan rājarṣipravaraḥ purā 
varṇānāṃ saṃkaraṃ cakre kāmopahatacetanaḥ  Mn 
tataḥ prabhṛti yo mohāt pramītapatikāṃ striyam 
niyojayaty apatyārthaṃ taṃ vigarhanti sādhavaḥ  Mn 
yasyā mriyeta kanyāyā vācā satye kṛte patiḥ 
tām anena vidhānena nijo vindeta devaraḥ  Mn 
yathāvidhy adhigamyaināṃ śuklavastrāṃ śucivratām 
mitho bhajetā prasavāt sakṛtsakṛd ṛtāvṛtau  Mn 
na dattvā kasya cit kanyāṃ punar dadyād vicakṣaṇaḥ 
dattvā punaḥ prayacchan hi prāpnoti puruṣānṛtam  Mn 
vidhivat pratigṛhyāpi tyajet kanyāṃ vigarhitām 
vyādhitāṃ vipraduṣṭāṃ vā chadmanā copapāditām  Mn 
yas tu doṣavatīṃ kanyām anākhyāyopapādayet 
tasya tad vitathaṃ kuryāt kanyādātur durātmanaḥ  Mn 
vidhāya vṛttiṃ bhāryāyāḥ pravaset kāryavān naraḥ 
avṛttikarśitā hi strī praduṣyet sthitimaty api  Mn 
vidhāya proṣite vṛttiṃ jīven niyamam āsthitā 
proṣite tv avidhāyaiva jīvec chilpair agarhitaiḥ  Mn 
proṣito dharmakāryārthaṃ pratīkṣyo 'ṣṭau naraḥ samāḥ 
vidyārthaṃ ṣaḍ yaśo'rthaṃ vā kāmārthaṃ trīṃs tu vatsarān  Mn 
saṃvatsaraṃ pratīkṣeta dviṣantīṃ yoṣitaṃ patiḥ 
ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsarāt tv enāṃ dāyaṃ hṛtvā na saṃvaset  Mn 
atikrāmet pramattaṃ yā mattaṃ rogārtam eva vā 
sā trīn māsān parityājyā vibhūṣaṇaparicchadā  Mn 
unmattaṃ patitaṃ klībam abījaṃ pāparogiṇam 
na tyāgo 'sti dviṣantyāś ca na ca dāyāpavartanam  Mn 
madyapāsādhuvṛttā ca pratikūlā ca yā bhavet 
vyādhitā vādhivettavyā hiṃsrārthaghnī ca sarvadā  Mn 
vandhyāṣṭame 'dhivedyā'abde daśame tu mṛtaprajā 
ekādaśe strījananī sadyas tv apriyavādinī  Mn 
yā rogiṇī syāt tu hitā saṃpannā caiva śīlataḥ 
sānujñāpyādhivettavyā nāvamānyā ca karhi cit  Mn 
adhivinnā tu yā nārī nirgacched ruṣitā gṛhāt 
sā sadyaḥ saṃniroddhavyā tyājyā vā kulasaṃnidhau  Mn 
pratiṣiddhāpi ced yā tu madyam abhyudayeṣv api 
prekṣāsamājaṃ gacched vā sā daṇḍyā kṛṣṇalāni ṣaṭ  Mn 
yadi svāś cāparāś caiva vinderan yoṣito dvijāḥ 
tāsāṃ varṇakrameṇa syāj jyeṣṭhyaṃ pūjā ca veśma ca  Mn 
bhartuḥ śarīraśuśrūṣāṃ dharmakāryaṃ ca naityakam 
svā caiva kuryāt sarveṣāṃ nāsvajātiḥ kathaṃ cana  Mn 
yas tu tat kārayen mohāt sajātyā sthitayānyayā 
yathā brāhmaṇacāṇḍālaḥ pūrvadṛṣṭas tathaiva saḥ  Mn 
utkṛṣṭāyābhirūpāya varāya sadṛśāya ca 
aprāptām api tāṃ tasmai kanyāṃ dadyād yathāvidhi  Mn 
kāmam ā maraṇāt tiṣṭhed gṛhe kanyā rtumaty api 
na caivaināṃ prayaccet tu guṇahīnāya karhi cit  Mn 
trīṇi varṣāṇy udīkṣeta kumāry ṛtumatī satī 
ūrdhvaṃ tu kālād etasmād vindeta sadṛśaṃ patim  Mn 
adīyamānā bhartāram adhigacched yadi svayam 
nainaḥ kiṃ cid avāpnoti na ca yaṃ sādhigacchati  Mn 
alaṅkāraṃ nādadīta pitryaṃ kanyā svayaṃvarā 
mātṛkaṃ bhrātṛdattaṃ vā stenā syād yadi taṃ haret  Mn 
pitre na dadyāc chulkaṃ tu kanyām ṛtumatīṃ haran 
sa ca svāmyād atikrāmed ṛtūnāṃ pratirodhanāt  Mn 
triṃśadvarṣo vahet kanyāṃ hṛdyāṃ dvādaśavārṣikīm 
tryaṣṭavarṣo 'ṣṭavarṣāṃ vā dharme sīdati satvaraḥ  Mn 
devadattāṃ patir bhāryāṃ vindate necchayātmanaḥ 
tāṃ sādhvīṃ bibhṛyān nityaṃ devānāṃ priyam ācaran  Mn 
prajanārthaṃ striyaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ saṃtānārthaṃ ca mānavaḥ 
tasmāt sādhāraṇo dharmaḥ śrutau patnyā sahoditaḥ  Mn 
kanyāyāṃ dattaśulkāyāṃ mriyeta yadi śulkadaḥ 
devarāya pradātavyā yadi kanyānumanyate  Mn 
ādadīta na śūdro 'pi śulkaṃ duhitaraṃ dadan 
śulkaṃ hi gṛhṇan kurute channaṃ duhitṛvikrayam  Mn 
etat tu na pare cakrur nāpare jātu sādhavaḥ 
yad anyasya pratijñāya punar anyasya dīyate  Mn 
nānuśuśruma jātv etat pūrveṣv api hi janmasu 
śulkasaṃjñena mūlyena channaṃ duhitṛvikrayam  Mn 
anyonyasyāvyabhicāro bhaved āmaraṇāntikaḥ 
eṣa dharmaḥ samāsena jñeyaḥ strīpuṃsayoḥ paraḥ  Mn 
tathā nityaṃ yateyātāṃ strīpuṃsau tu kṛtakriyau 
yathā nābhicaretāṃ tau viyuktāv itaretaram  Mn 
eṣa strīpuṃsayor ukto dharmo vo ratisaṃhitaḥ 
āpady apatyaprāptiś ca dāyadharmaṃ nibodhata  Mn 
ūrdhvaṃ pituś ca mātuś ca sametya bhrātaraḥ samam 
bhajeran paitṛkaṃ riktham anīśās te hi jīvatoḥ  Mn 
jyeṣṭha eva tu gṛhṇīyāt pitryaṃ dhanam aśeṣataḥ 
śeṣās tam upajīveyur yathaiva pitaraṃ tathā  Mn 
jyeṣṭhena jātamātreṇa putrī bhavati mānavaḥ 
pitṝṇām anṛṇaś caiva sa tasmāt sarvam arhati  Mn 
yasminn ṛṇaṃ saṃnayati yena cānantyam aśnute 
sa eva dharmajaḥ putraḥ kāmajān itarān viduḥ  Mn 
piteva pālayet pūtrān jyeṣṭho bhrātṝṇ yavīyasaḥ 
putravac cāpi varteran jyeṣṭhe bhrātari dharmataḥ  Mn 
jyeṣṭhaḥ kulaṃ vardhayati vināśayati vā punaḥ 
jyeṣṭhaḥ pūjyatamo loke jyeṣṭhaḥ sadbhir agarhitaḥ  Mn 
yo jyeṣṭho jyeṣṭhavṛttiḥ syān māteva sa piteva saḥ 
ajyeṣṭhavṛttir yas tu syāt sa saṃpūjyas tu bandhuvat  Mn 
evaṃ saha vaseyur vā pṛthag vā dharmakāmyayā 
pṛthag vivardhate dharmas tasmād dharmyā pṛthakkriyā  Mn 
jyeṣṭhasya viṃśa uddhāraḥ sarvadravyāc ca yad varam 
tato 'rdhaṃ madhyamasya syāt turīyaṃ tu yavīyasaḥ  Mn 
jyeṣṭhaś caiva kaniṣṭhaś ca saṃharetāṃ yathoditam 
ye 'nye jyeṣṭhakaniṣṭhābhyāṃ teṣāṃ syān madhyamaṃ dhanam  Mn 
sarveṣāṃ dhanajātānām ādadītāgryam agrajaḥ 
yac ca sātiśayaṃ kiṃ cid daśataś cāpnuyād varam  Mn 
uddhāro na daśasv asti saṃpannānāṃ svakarmasu 
yat kiṃ cid eva deyaṃ tu jyāyase mānavardhanam  Mn 
evaṃ samuddhṛtoddhāre samān aṃśān prakalpayet 
uddhāre 'nuddhṛte tv eṣām iyaṃ syād aṃśakalpanā  Mn 
ekādhikaṃ harej jyeṣṭhaḥ putro 'dhyardhaṃ tato 'nujaḥ 
aṃśam aṃśaṃ yavīyāṃsa iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ  Mn 
svebhyo 'ṃśebhyas tu kanyābhyaḥ pradadyur bhrātaraḥ pṛthak 
svāt svād aṃśāc caturbhāgaṃ patitāḥ syur aditsavaḥ  Mn 
ajāvikaṃ saikaśaphaṃ na jātu viṣamaṃ bhajet 
ajāvikaṃ tu viṣamaṃ jyeṣṭhasyaiva vidhīyate  Mn 
yavīyāñ jyeṣṭhabhāryāyāṃ putram utpādayed yadi 
samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syād iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ  Mn 
upasarjanaṃ pradhānasya dharmato nopapadyate 
pitā pradhānaṃ prajane tasmād dharmeṇa taṃ bhajet  Mn 
putraḥ kaniṣṭho jyeṣṭhāyāṃ kaniṣṭhāyāṃ ca pūrvajaḥ 
kathaṃ tatra vibhāgaḥ syād iti cet saṃśayo bhavet  Mn 
ekaṃ vṛṣabham uddhāraṃ saṃhareta sa pūrvajaḥ 
tato 'pare jyeṣṭhavṛṣās tadūnānāṃ svamātṛtaḥ  Mn 
jyeṣṭhas tu jāto jyeṣṭhāyāṃ hared vṛṣabhaṣoḍaśāḥ 
tataḥ svamātṛtaḥ śeṣā bhajerann iti dhāraṇā  Mn 
sadṛśastrīṣu jātānāṃ putrāṇām aviśeṣataḥ 
na mātṛto jyaiṣṭhyam asti janmato jyaiṣṭhyam ucyate  Mn 
janmajyeṣṭhena cāhvānaṃ subrahmaṇyāsv api smṛtam 
yamayoś caiva garbheṣu janmato jyeṣṭhatā smṛtā  Mn 
aputro 'nena vidhinā sutāṃ kurvīta putrikām 
yad apatyaṃ bhaved asyāṃ tan mama syāt svadhākaram  Mn 
anena tu vidhānena purā cakre 'tha putrikāḥ 
vivṛddhyarthaṃ svavaṃśasya svayaṃ dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ  Mn 
dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa 
somāya rājñe satkṛtya prītātmā saptaviṃśatim  Mn 
yathaivātmā tathā putraḥ putreṇa duhitā samā 
tasyām ātmani tiṣṭhantyāṃ katham anyo dhanaṃ haret  Mn 
mātus tu yautakaṃ yat syāt kumārībhāga eva saḥ 
dauhitra eva ca hared aputrasyākhilaṃ dhanam  Mn 
dauhitro hy akhilaṃ riktham aputrasya pitur haret 
sa eva dadyād dvau piṇḍau pitre mātāmahāya ca  Mn 
pautradauhitrayor loke na viśeṣo 'sti dharmataḥ 
tayor hi mātāpitarau saṃbhūtau tasya dehataḥ  Mn 
putrikāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ tu yadi putro 'nujāyate 
samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāj jyeṣṭhatā nāsti hi striyāḥ  Mn 
aputrāyāṃ mṛtāyāṃ tu putrikāyāṃ kathaṃ cana 
dhanaṃ tat putrikābhartā haretaivāvicārayan  Mn 
akṛtā vā kṛtā vāpi yaṃ vindet sadṛśāt sutam 
pautrī mātāmahas tena dadyāt piṇḍaṃ hared dhanam  Mn 
putreṇa lokāñ jayati pautreṇānantyam aśnute 
atha putrasya pautreṇa bradhnasyāpnoti viṣṭapam  Mn 
puṃnāmno narakād yasmāt trāyate pitaraṃ sutaḥ 
tasmāt putra iti proktaḥ svayam eva svayaṃbhuvā  Mn 
pautradauhitrayor loke viśeṣo nopapadyate 
dauhitro 'pi hy amutrainaṃ saṃtārayati pautravat  Mn 
mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nirvapet putrikāsutaḥ 
dvitīyaṃ tu pitus tasyās tṛtīyaṃ tatpituḥ pituḥ  Mn 
upapanno guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ putro yasya tu dattrimaḥ 
sa haretaiva tadrikthaṃ saṃprāpto 'py anyagotrataḥ  Mn 
gotrarikthe janayitur na hared dattrimaḥ kva cit 
gotrarikthānugaḥ piṇḍo vyapaiti dadataḥ svadhā  Mn 
aniyuktāsutaś caiva putriṇyāptaś ca devarāt 
ubhau tau nārhato bhāgaṃ jārajātakakāmajau  Mn 
niyuktāyām api pumān nāryāṃ jāto 'vidhānataḥ 
naivārhaḥ paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ patitotpādito hi saḥ  Mn 
haret tatra niyuktāyāṃ jātaḥ putro yathāurasaḥ 
kṣetrikasya tu tad bījaṃ dharmataḥ prasavaś ca saḥ  Mn 
dhanaṃ yo bibhṛyād bhrātur mṛtasya striyam eva ca 
so 'patyaṃ bhrātur utpādya dadyāt tasyaiva taddhanam  Mn 
yā niyuktānyataḥ putraṃ devarād vāpy avāpnuyāt 
taṃ kāmajam arikthīyaṃ vṛthotpannaṃ pracakṣate  Mn 
etad vidhānaṃ vijñeyaṃ vibhāgasyaikayoniṣu 
bahvīṣu caikajātānāṃ nānāstrīṣu nibodhata  Mn 
brāhmaṇasyānupūrvyeṇa catasras tu yadi striyaḥ 
tāsāṃ putreṣu jāteṣu vibhāge 'yaṃ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
kīnāśo govṛṣo yānam alaṅkāraś ca veśma ca 
viprasyāuddhārikaṃ deyam ekāṃśaś ca pradhānataḥ  Mn 
tryaṃśaṃ dāyād dhared vipro dvāv aṃśau kṣatriyāsutaḥ 
vaiśyājaḥ sārdham evāṃśam aṃśaṃ śūdrāsuto haret  Mn 
sarvaṃ vā rikthajātaṃ tad daśadhā parikalpya ca 
dharmyaṃ vibhāgaṃ kurvīta vidhinānena dharmavit  Mn 
caturo 'ṃśān hared vipras trīn aṃśān kṣatriyāsutaḥ 
vaiśyāputro hared dvyaṃśaṃ aṃśaṃ śūdrāsuto haret  Mn 
yady api syāt tu satputro 'py asatputro 'pi vā bhavet 
nādhikaṃ daśamād dadyāc chūdrāputrāya dharmataḥ  Mn 
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śūdrāputro na rikthabhāk 
yad evāsya pitā dadyāt tad evāsya dhanaṃ bhavet  Mn 
samavarṇāsu vā jātāḥ sarve putrā dvijanmanām 
uddhāraṃ jyāyase dattvā bhajerann itare samam  Mn 
śūdrasya tu savarṇaiva nānyā bhāryā vidhīyate 
tasyāṃ jātāḥ samāṃśāḥ syur yadi putraśataṃ bhavet  Mn 
putrān dvādaśa yān āha nṝṇāṃ svāyaṃbhuvo manuḥ 
teṣāṃ ṣaḍ bandhudāyādāḥ ṣaḍ adāyādabāndhavāḥ  Mn 
aurasaḥ kṣetrajaś caiva dattaḥ kṛtrima eva ca 
gūḍhotpanno 'paviddhaś ca dāyādā bāndhavāś ca ṣaṭ  Mn 
kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca krītaḥ paunarbhavas tathā 
svayaṃdattaś ca śaudraś ca ṣaḍ adāyādabāndhavāḥ  Mn 
yādṛśaṃ phalam āpnoti kuplavaiḥ saṃtarañ jalam 
tādṛśaṃ phalam āpnoti kuputraiḥ saṃtaraṃs tamaḥ  Mn 
yady ekarikthinau syātām aurasakṣetrajau sutau 
yasya yat paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ sa tad gṛhṇīta netaraḥ  Mn 
eka evāurasaḥ putraḥ pitryasya vasunaḥ prabhuḥ 
śeṣāṇām ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ pradadyāt tu prajīvanam  Mn 
ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu kṣetrajasyāṃśaṃ pradadyāt paitṛkād dhanāt 
auraso vibhajan dāyaṃ pitryaṃ pañcamam eva vā  Mn 
aurasakṣetrajau putrau pitṛrikthasya bhāginau 
daśāpare tu kramaśo gotrarikthāṃśabhāginaḥ  Mn 
svakṣetre saṃskṛtāyāṃ tu svayam utpādayed dhi yam 
tam aurasaṃ vijānīyāt putraṃ prāthamakalpikam  Mn 
yas talpajaḥ pramītasya klībasya vyādhitasya vā 
svadharmeṇa niyuktāyāṃ sa putraḥ kṣetrajaḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
mātā pitā vā dadyātāṃ yam adbhiḥ putram āpadi 
sadṛśaṃ prītisaṃyuktaṃ sa jñeyo dattrimaḥ sutaḥ  Mn 
sadṛśaṃ tu prakuryād yaṃ guṇadoṣavicakṣaṇam 
putraṃ putraguṇair yuktaṃ sa vijñeyaś ca kṛtrimaḥ  Mn 
utpadyate gṛhe yas tu na ca jñāyeta kasya saḥ 
sa gṛhe gūḍha utpannas tasya syād yasya talpajaḥ  Mn 
mātāpitṛbhyām utsṛṣṭaṃ tayor anyatareṇa vā 
yaṃ putraṃ parigṛhṇīyād apaviddhaḥ sa ucyate  Mn 
pitṛveśmani kanyā tu yaṃ putraṃ janayed rahaḥ 
taṃ kānīnaṃ vaden nāmnā voḍhuḥ kanyāsamudbhavam  Mn 
yā garbhiṇī saṃskriyate jñātājñātāpi vā satī 
voḍhuḥ sa garbho bhavati sahoḍha iti cocyate  Mn 
krīṇīyād yas tv apatyārthaṃ mātāpitror yam antikāt 
sa krītakaḥ sutas tasya sadṛśo 'sadṛśo 'pi vā  Mn 
yā patyā vā parityaktā vidhavā vā svayecchayā 
utpādayet punar bhūtvā sa paunarbhava ucyate  Mn 
sā ced akṣatayoniḥ syād gatapratyāgatāpi vā 
paunarbhavena bhartrā sā punaḥ saṃskāram arhati  Mn 
mātāpitṛvihīno yas tyakto vā syād akāraṇāt 
ātmānam arpayed yasmai svayaṃdattas tu sa smṛtaḥ  Mn 
yaṃ brāhmaṇas tu śūdrāyāṃ kāmād utpādayet sutam 
sa pārayann eva śavas tasmāt pāraśavaḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
dāsyāṃ vā dāsadāsyāṃ vā yaḥ śūdrasya suto bhavet 
so 'nujñāto hared aṃśam iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ  Mn 
kṣetrajādīn sutān etān ekādaśa yathoditān 
putrapratinidhīn āhuḥ kriyālopān manīṣiṇaḥ  Mn 
ya ete 'bhihitāḥ putrāḥ prasaṅgād anyabījajāḥ 
yasya te bījato jātās tasya te netarasya tu  Mn 
bhrātṝṇām ekajātānām ekaś cet putravān bhavet 
sarvāṃs tāṃs tena putreṇa putriṇo manur abravīt  Mn 
sarvāsām ekapatnīnām ekā cet putriṇī bhavet 
sarvās tās tena putreṇa prāha putravatīr manuḥ  Mn 
śreyasaḥ śreyaso 'lābhe pāpīyān riktham arhati 
bahavaś cet tu sadṛśāḥ sarve rikthasya bhāginaḥ  Mn 
na bhrātaro na pitaraḥ putrā rikthaharāḥ pituḥ 
pitā hared aputrasya rikthaṃ bhrātara eva ca  Mn 
trayāṇām udakaṃ kāryaṃ triṣu piṇḍaḥ pravartate 
caturthaḥ saṃpradātaiṣāṃ pañcamo nopapadyate  Mn 
anantaraḥ sapiṇḍād yas tasya tasya dhanaṃ bhavet 
ata ūrdhvaṃ sakulyaḥ syād ācāryaḥ śiṣya eva vā  Mn 
sarveṣām apy abhāve tu brāhmaṇā rikthabhāginaḥ 
traividyāḥ śucayo dāntās tathā dharmo na hīyate  Mn 
ahāryaṃ brāhmaṇadravyaṃ rājñā nityam iti sthitiḥ 
itareṣāṃ tu varṇānāṃ sarvābhāve haren nṛpaḥ  Mn 
saṃsthitasyānapatyasya sagotrāt putram āharet 
tatra yad rikthajātaṃ syāt tat tasmin pratipādayet  Mn 
dvau tu yau vivadeyātāṃ dvābhyāṃ jātau striyā dhane 
tayor yad yasya pitryaṃ syāt tat sa gṛhṇīta netaraḥ  Mn 
jananyāṃ saṃsthitāyāṃ tu samaṃ sarve sahodarāḥ 
bhajeran mātṛkaṃ rikthaṃ bhaginyaś ca sanābhayaḥ  Mn 
yās tāsāṃ syur duhitaras tāsām api yathārhataḥ 
mātāmahyā dhanāt kiṃ cit pradeyaṃ prītipūrvakam  Mn 
adhyagnyadhyāvāhanikaṃ dattaṃ ca prītikarmaṇi 
bhrātṛmātṛpitṛprāptaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ strīdhanaṃ smṛtam  Mn 
anvādheyaṃ ca yad dattaṃ patyā prītena caiva yat 
patyau jīvati vṛttāyāḥ prajāyās tad dhanaṃ bhavet  Mn 
brāhmadaivārṣagāndharva prājāpatyeṣu yad vasu 
aprajāyām atītāyāṃ bhartur eva tad iṣyate  Mn 
yat tv asyāḥ syād dhanaṃ dattaṃ vivāheṣv āsurādiṣu 
aprajāyām atītāyāṃ mātāpitros tad iṣyate  Mn 
striyāṃ tu yad bhaved vittaṃ pitrā dattaṃ kathaṃ cana 
brāhmaṇī tad dharet kanyā tadapatyasya vā bhavet  Mn 
na nirhāraṃ striyaḥ kuryuḥ kuṭumbād bahumadhyagāt 
svakād api ca vittād dhi svasya bhartur anājñayā  Mn 
patyau jīvati yaḥ strībhir alaṅkāro dhṛto bhavet 
na taṃ bhajeran dāyādā bhajamānāḥ patanti te  Mn 
anaṃśau klībapatitau jātyandhabadhirau tathā 
unmattajaḍamūkāś ca ye ca ke cin nirindriyāḥ  Mn 
sarveṣām api tu nyāyyaṃ dātuṃ śaktyā manīṣiṇā 
grāsācchādanam atyantaṃ patito hy adadad bhavet  Mn 
yady arthitā tu dāraiḥ syāt klībādīnāṃ kathaṃ cana 
teṣām utpannatantūnām apatyaṃ dāyam arhati  Mn 
yat kiṃ cit pitari prete dhanaṃ jyeṣṭho 'dhigacchati 
bhāgo yavīyasāṃ tatra yadi vidyānupālinaḥ  Mn 
avidyānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ īhātaś ced dhanaṃ bhavet 
samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syād apitrya iti dhāraṇā  Mn 
vidyādhanaṃ tu yady asya tat tasyaiva dhanaṃ bhavet 
maitryam audvāhikaṃ caiva mādhuparkikam eva ca  Mn 
bhrātṝṇāṃ yas tu neheta dhanaṃ śaktaḥ svakarmaṇā 
sa nirbhājyaḥ svakād aṃśāt kiṃ cid dattvopajīvanam  Mn 
anupaghnan pitṛdravyaṃ śrameṇa yad upārjitam 
svayam īhitalabdhaṃ tan nākāmo dātum arhati  Mn 
paitṛkaṃ tu pitā dravyam anavāptaṃ yad āpnuyāt 
na tat putrair bhajet sārdham akāmaḥ svayam arjitam  Mn 
vibhaktāḥ saha jīvanto vibhajeran punar yadi 
samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāj jyaiṣṭhyaṃ tatra na vidyate  Mn 
yeṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ kaniṣṭho vā hīyetāṃśapradānataḥ 
mriyetānyataro vāpi tasya bhāgo na lupyate  Mn 
sodaryā vibhajeraṃs taṃ sametya sahitāḥ samam 
bhrātaro ye ca saṃsṛṣṭā bhāginyaś ca sanābhayaḥ  Mn 
yo jyeṣṭho vinikurvīta lobhād bhrātṝn yavīyasaḥ 
so 'jyeṣṭhaḥ syād abhāgaś ca niyantavyaś ca rājabhiḥ  Mn 
sarva eva vikarmasthā nārhanti bhrātaro dhanam 
na cādattvā kaniṣṭhebhyo jyeṣṭhaḥ kurvīta yautakam  Mn 
bhrātṝṇām avibhaktānāṃ yady utthānaṃ bhavet saha 
na putrabhāgaṃ viṣamaṃ pitā dadyāt kathaṃ cana  Mn 
ūrdhvaṃ vibhāgāj jātas tu pitryam eva hared dhanam 
saṃsṛṣṭās tena vā ye syur vibhajeta sa taiḥ saha  Mn 
anapatyasya putrasya mātā dāyam avāpnuyāt 
mātary api ca vṛttāyāṃ pitur mātā hared dhanam  Mn 
ṛṇe dhane ca sarvasmin pravibhakte yathāvidhi 
paścād dṛśyeta yat kiṃ cit tat sarvaṃ samatāṃ nayet  Mn 
vastraṃ patram alaṅkāraṃ kṛtānnam udakaṃ striyaḥ 
yogakṣemaṃ pracāraṃ ca na vibhājyaṃ pracakṣate  Mn 
ayam ukto vibhāgo vaḥ putrāṇāṃ ca kriyāvidhiḥ 
kramaśaḥ kṣetrajādīnāṃ dyūtadharmaṃ nibodhata  Mn 
dyūtaṃ samāhvayaṃ caiva rājā rāṣṭrān nivārayet 
rājāntakaraṇāv etau dvau doṣau pṛthivīkṣitām  Mn 
prakāśam etat tāskaryaṃ yad devanasamāhvayau 
tayor nityaṃ pratīghāte nṛpatir yatnavān bhavet  Mn 
aprāṇibhir yat kriyate tal loke dyūtam ucyate 
prāṇibhiḥ kriyate yas tu sa vijñeyaḥ samāhvayaḥ  Mn 
dyūtaṃ samāhvayaṃ caiva yaḥ kuryāt kārayeta vā 
tān sarvān ghātayed rājā śūdrāṃś ca dvijaliṅginaḥ  Mn 
kitavān kuśīlavān krūrān pāṣaṇḍasthāṃś ca mānavān 
vikarmasthān śauṇḍikāṃś ca kṣipraṃ nirvāsayet purāt  Mn 
ete rāṣṭre vartamānā rājñaḥ prachannataskarāḥ 
vikarmakriyayā nityaṃ bādhante bhadrikāḥ prajāḥ  Mn 
dyūtam etat purā kalpe dṛṣṭaṃ vairakaraṃ mahat 
tasmād dyūtaṃ na seveta hāsyārtham api buddhimān  Mn 
pracchannaṃ vā prakāśaṃ vā tan niṣeveta yo naraḥ 
tasya daṇḍavikalpaḥ syād yatheṣṭaṃ nṛpates tathā  Mn 
kṣatraviṭśūdrayonis tu daṇḍaṃ dātum aśaknuvan 
ānṛṇyaṃ karmaṇā gacched vipro dadyāc chanaiḥ śanaiḥ  Mn 
strībālonmattavṛddhānāṃ daridrāṇāṃ ca rogiṇām 
śiphāvidalarajjvādyair vidadhyān nṛpatir damam  Mn 
ye niyuktās tu kāryeṣu hanyuḥ kāryāṇi kāryiṇām 
dhanoṣmaṇā pacyamānās tān niḥsvān kārayen nṛpaḥ  Mn 
kūṭaśāsanakartṝṃś ca prakṛtīnāṃ ca dūṣakān 
strībālabrāhmaṇaghnāṃś ca hanyād dviṭsevinas tathā  Mn 
tīritaṃ cānuśiṣṭaṃ ca yatra kva cana yad bhavet 
kṛtaṃ tad dharmato vidyān na tad bhūyo nivartayet  Mn 
amātyāḥ prāḍvivāko vā yat kuryuḥ kāryam anyathā 
tat svayaṃ nṛpatiḥ kuryāt tān sahasraṃ ca daṇḍayet  Mn 
brahmahā ca surāpaś ca steyī ca gurutalpagaḥ 
ete sarve pṛthag jñeyā mahāpātakino narāḥ  Mn 
caturṇām api caiteṣāṃ prāyaścittam akurvatām 
śārīraṃ dhanasaṃyuktaṃ daṇḍaṃ dharmyaṃ prakalpayet  Mn 
gurutalpe bhagaḥ kāryaḥ surāpāne surādhvajaḥ 
steye ca śvapadaṃ kāryaṃ brahmahaṇy aśirāḥ pumān  Mn 
asaṃbhojyā hy asaṃyājyā asaṃpāṭhyā 'vivāhinaḥ 
careyuḥ pṛthivīṃ dīnāḥ sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ  Mn 
jñātisaṃbandhibhis tv ete tyaktavyāḥ kṛtalakṣaṇāḥ 
nirdayā nirnamaskārās tan manor anuśāsanam  Mn 
prāyaścittaṃ tu kurvāṇāḥ sarvavarṇā yathoditam 
nāṅkyā rājñā lalāṭe syur dāpyās tūttamasāhasam  Mn 
āgaḥsu brāhmaṇasyaiva kāryo madhyamasāhasaḥ 
vivāsyo vā bhaved rāṣṭrāt sadravyaḥ saparicchadaḥ  Mn 
itare kṛtavantas tu pāpāny etāny akāmataḥ 
sarvasvahāram arhanti kāmatas tu pravāsanam  Mn 
nādadīta nṛpaḥ sādhur mahāpātakino dhanam 
ādadānas tu tal lobhāt tena doṣeṇa lipyate  Mn 
apsu praveśya taṃ daṇḍaṃ varuṇāyopapādayet 
śrutavṛttopapanne vā brāhmaṇe pratipādayet  Mn 
īśo daṇḍasya varuṇo rājñāṃ daṇḍadharo hi saḥ 
īśaḥ sarvasya jagato brāhmaṇo vedapāragaḥ  Mn 
yatra varjayate rājā pāpakṛdbhyo dhanāgamam 
tatra kālena jāyante mānavā dīrghajīvinaḥ  Mn 
niṣpadyante ca sasyāni yathoptāni viśāṃ pṛthak 
bālāś ca na pramīyante vikṛtaṃ ca na jāyate  Mn 
brāhmaṇān bādhamānaṃ tu kāmād avaravarṇajam 
hanyāc citrair vadhopāyair udvejanakarair nṛpaḥ  Mn 
yāvān avadhyasya vadhe tāvān vadhyasya mokṣaṇe 
adharmo nṛpater dṛṣṭo dharmas tu viniyacchataḥ  Mn 
udito 'yaṃ vistaraśo mitho vivādamānayoḥ 
aṣṭādaśasu mārgeṣu vyavahārasya nirṇayaḥ  Mn 
evaṃ dharmyāṇi kāryāṇi samyak kurvan mahīpatiḥ 
deśān alabdhāṃl lipseta labdhāṃś ca paripālayet  Mn 
samyaṅ niviṣṭadeśas tu kṛtadurgaś ca śāstrataḥ 
kaṇṭakoddharaṇe nityam ātiṣṭhed yatnam uttamam  Mn 
rakṣanād āryavṛttānāṃ kaṇṭakānāṃ ca śodhanāt 
narendrās tridivaṃ yānti prajāpālanatatparāḥ  Mn 
aśāsaṃs taskarān yas tu baliṃ gṛhṇāti pārthivaḥ 
tasya prakṣubhyate rāṣṭraṃ svargāc ca parihīyate  Mn 
nirbhayaṃ tu bhaved yasya rāṣṭraṃ bāhubalāśritam 
tasya tad vardhate nityaṃ sicyamāna iva drumaḥ  Mn 
dvividhāṃs taskarān vidyāt paradravyāpahārakān 
prakāśāṃś cāprakāśāṃś ca cāracakṣur mahīpatiḥ  Mn 
prakāśavañcakās teṣāṃ nānāpaṇyopajīvinaḥ 
pracchannavañcakās tv ete ye stenāṭavikādayaḥ  Mn 
utkocakāś cāupadhikā vañcakāḥ kitavās tathā 
maṅgalādeśavṛttāś ca bhadrāś cekṣaṇikaiḥ saha  Mn 
asamyakkāriṇaś caiva mahāmātrāś cikitsakāḥ 
śilpopacārayuktāś ca nipuṇāḥ paṇyayoṣitaḥ  Mn 
evamādīn vijānīyāt prakāśāṃl lokakaṇṭakān 
nigūḍhacāriṇaś cānyān anāryān āryaliṅginaḥ  Mn 
tān viditvā sucaritair gūḍhais tatkarmakāribhiḥ 
cāraiś cānekasaṃsthānaiḥ protsādya vaśam ānayet  Mn 
teṣāṃ doṣān abhikhyāpya sve sve karmaṇi tattvataḥ 
kurvīta śāsanaṃ rājā samyak sārāparādhataḥ  Mn 
na hi daṇḍād ṛte śakyaḥ kartuṃ pāpavinigrahaḥ 
stenānāṃ pāpabuddhīnāṃ nibhṛtaṃ caratāṃ kṣitau  Mn 
sabhāprapāpūpaśālā veśamadyānnavikrayāḥ 
catuṣpathāṃś caityavṛkṣāḥ samājāḥ prekṣaṇāni ca  Mn 
jīrṇodyānāny araṇyāni kārukāveśanāni ca 
śūnyāni cāpy agārāṇi vanāny upavanāni ca  Mn 
evaṃvidhān nṛpo deśān gulmaiḥ sthāvarajaṅgamaiḥ 
taskarapratiṣedhārthaṃ cāraiś cāpy anucārayet  Mn 
tatsahāyair anugatair nānākarmapravedibhiḥ 
vidyād utsādayec caiva nipuṇaiḥ pūrvataskaraiḥ  Mn 
bhakṣyabhojyopadeśaiś ca brāhmaṇānāṃ ca darśanaiḥ 
śauryakarmāpadeśaiś ca kuryus teṣāṃ samāgamam  Mn 
ye tatra nopasarpeyur mūlapraṇihitāś ca ye 
tān prasahya nṛpo hanyāt samitrajñātibāndhavān  Mn 
na hoḍhena vinā cauraṃ ghātayed dhārmiko nṛpaḥ 
sahoḍhaṃ sopakaraṇaṃ ghātayed avicārayan  Mn 
grāmeṣv api ca ye ke cic caurāṇāṃ bhaktadāyakāḥ 
bhāṇḍāvakāśadāś caiva sarvāṃs tān api ghātayet  Mn 
rāṣṭreṣu rakṣādhikṛtān sāmantāṃś caiva coditān 
abhyāghāteṣu madhyasthāñ śiṣyāc caurān iva drutam  Mn 
yaś cāpi dharmasamayāt pracyuto dharmajīvanaḥ 
daṇḍenaiva tam apy oṣet svakād dharmād dhi vicyutam  Mn 
grāmaghāte hitābhaṅge pathi moṣābhidarśane 
śaktito nābhidhāvanto nirvāsyāḥ saparicchadāḥ  Mn 
rājñaḥ kośāpahartṝṃś ca pratikūleṣu ca sthitān 
ghātayed vividhair daṇḍair arīṇāṃ copajāpakān  Mn 
saṃdhiṃ chittvā tu ye cauryaṃ rātrau kurvanti taskarāḥ 
teṣāṃ chittvā nṛpo hastau tīkṣṇe śūle niveśayet  Mn 
aṅgulīr granthibhedasya chedayet prathame grahe 
dvitīye hastacaraṇau tṛtīye vadham arhati  Mn 
agnidān bhaktadāṃś caiva tathā śastrāvakāśadān 
saṃnidhātṝṃś ca moṣasya hanyāc cauram iveśvaraḥ  Mn 
taḍāgabhedakaṃ hanyād apsu śuddhavadhena vā 
yad vāpi pratisaṃskuryād dāpyas tūttamasāhasam  Mn 
koṣṭhāgārāyudhāgāra devatāgārabhedakān 
hastyaśvarathahartṝṃś ca hanyād evāvicārayan  Mn 
yas tu pūrvaniviṣṭasya taḍāgasyodakaṃ haret 
āgamaṃ vāpy apāṃ bhindyāt sa dāpyaḥ pūrvasāhasam  Mn 
samutsṛjed rājamārge yas tv amedhyam anāpadi 
sa dvau kārṣāpaṇau dadyād amedhyaṃ cāśu śodhayet  Mn 
āpadgato 'tha vā vṛddhā garbhiṇī bāla eva vā 
paribhāṣaṇam arhanti tac ca śodhyam iti sthitiḥ  Mn 
cikitsakānāṃ sarveṣāṃ mithyāpracaratāṃ damaḥ 
amānuṣeṣu prathamo mānuṣeṣu tu madhyamaḥ  Mn 
saṃkramadhvajayaṣṭīnāṃ pratimānāṃ ca bhedakaḥ 
pratikuryāc ca tat sarvaṃ pañca dadyāc chatāni ca  Mn 
adūṣitānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ dūṣaṇe bhedane tathā 
maṇīnām apavedhe ca daṇḍaḥ prathamasāhasaḥ  Mn 
samair hi viṣamaṃ yas tu cared vai mūlyato 'pi vā 
samāpnuyād damaṃ pūrvaṃ naro madhyamam eva vā  Mn 
bandhanāni ca sarvāṇi rājā mārge niveśayet 
duḥkhitā yatra dṛśyeran vikṛtāḥ pāpakāriṇah  Mn 
prākārasya ca bhettāraṃ parikhāṇāṃ ca pūrakam 
dvārāṇāṃ caiva bhaṅktāraṃ kṣipram eva pravāsayet  Mn 
abhicāreṣu sarveṣu kartavyo dviśato damaḥ 
mūlakarmaṇi cānāpteḥ kṛtyāsu vividhāsu ca  Mn 
abījavikrayī caiva bījotkṛṣṭā tathaiva ca 
maryādābhedakaś caiva vikṛtaṃ prāpnuyād vadham  Mn 
sarvakaṇṭakapāpiṣṭhaṃ hemakāraṃ tu pārthivaḥ 
pravartamānam anyāye chedayel lavaśaḥ kṣuraiḥ  Mn 
sītādravyāpaharaṇe śastrāṇām auṣadhasya ca 
kālam āsādya kāryaṃ ca rājā daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet  Mn 
svāmyamātyau puraṃ rāṣṭraṃ kośadaṇḍau suhṛt tathā 
sapta prakṛtayo hy etāḥ saptāṅgaṃ rājyam ucyate  Mn 
saptānāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ tu rājyasyāsāṃ yathākramam 
pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ gurutaraṃ jānīyād vyasanaṃ mahat  Mn 
saptāṅgasyeha rājyasya viṣṭabdhasya tridaṇḍavat 
anyonyaguṇavaiśeṣyān na kiṃ cid atiricyate  Mn 
teṣu teṣu tu kṛtyeṣu tat tad aṅgaṃ viśiṣyate 
yena yat sādhyate kāryaṃ tat tasmiñ śreṣṭham ucyate  Mn 
cāreṇotsāhayogena kriyayaiva ca karmaṇām 
svaśaktiṃ paraśaktiṃ ca nityaṃ vidyān mahīpatiḥ  Mn 
pīḍanāni ca sarvāṇi vyasanāni tathaiva ca 
ārabheta tataḥ kāryaṃ saṃcintya gurulāghavam  Mn 
ārabhetaiva karmāṇi śrāntaḥ śrāntaḥ punaḥ punaḥ 
karmāṇy ārabhamāṇaṃ hi puruṣaṃ śrīr niṣevate  Mn 
kṛtaṃ tretāyugaṃ caiva dvāparaṃ kalir eva ca 
rājño vṛttāni sarvāṇi rājā hi yugam ucyate  Mn 
kaliḥ prasupto bhavati sa jāgrad dvāparaṃ yugam 
karmasv abhyudyatas tretā vicaraṃs tu kṛtaṃ yugam  Mn 
indrasyārkasya vāyoś ca yamasya varuṇasya ca 
candrasyāgneḥ pṛthivyāś ca tejovṛttaṃ nṛpaś caret  Mn 
vārṣikāṃś caturo māsān yathendro 'bhipravarṣati 
tathābhivarṣet svaṃ rāṣṭraṃ kāmair indravrataṃ caran  Mn 
aṣṭau māsān yathādityas toyaṃ harati raśmibhiḥ 
tathā haret karaṃ rāṣṭrān nityam arkavrataṃ hi tat  Mn 
praviśya sarvabhūtāni yathā carati mārutaḥ 
tathā cāraiḥ praveṣṭavyaṃ vratam etad dhi mārutam  Mn 
yathā yamaḥ priyadveṣyau prāpte kāle niyacchati 
tathā rājñā niyantavyāḥ prajās tad dhi yamavratam  Mn 
varuṇena yathā pāśair baddha evābhidṛśyate 
tathā pāpān nigṛhṇīyād vratam etad dhi vāruṇam  Mn 
paripūrṇaṃ yathā candraṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛṣyanti mānavāḥ 
tathā prakṛtayo yasmin sa cāndravratiko nṛpaḥ  Mn 
pratāpayuktas tejasvī nityaṃ syāt pāpakarmasu 
duṣṭasāmantahiṃsraś ca tad āgneyaṃ vrataṃ smṛtam  Mn 
yathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni dharā dhārayate samam 
tathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni bibhrataḥ pārthivaṃ vratam  Mn 
etair upāyair anyaiś ca yukto nityam atandritaḥ 
stenān rājā nigṛhṇīyāt svarāṣṭre para eva ca  Mn 
parām apy āpadaṃ prāpto brāhmaṇān na prakopayet 
te hy enaṃ kupitā hanyuḥ sadyaḥ sabalavāhanam  Mn 
yaiḥ kṛtaḥ sarvabhakṣyo 'gnir apeyaś ca mahodadhiḥ 
kṣayī cāpyāyitaḥ somaḥ ko na naśyet prakopya tān  Mn 
lokān anyān sṛjeyur ye lokapālāṃś ca kopitāḥ 
devān kuryur adevāṃś ca kaḥ kṣiṇvaṃs tān samṛdhnuyāt  Mn 
yān upāśritya tiṣṭhanti lokā devāś ca sarvadā 
brahma caiva dhanaṃ yeṣāṃ ko hiṃsyāt tāñ jijīviṣuḥ  Mn 
avidvāṃś caiva vidvāṃś ca brāhmaṇo daivataṃ mahat 
praṇītaś cāpraṇītaś ca yathāgnir daivataṃ mahat  Mn 
śmaśāneṣv api tejasvī pāvako naiva duṣyati 
hūyamānaś ca yajñeṣu bhūya evābhivardhate  Mn 
evaṃ yady apy aniṣṭeṣu vartante sarvakarmasu 
sarvathā brāhmaṇāḥ pūjyāḥ paramaṃ daivataṃ hi tat  Mn 
kṣatrasyātipravṛddhasya brāhmaṇān prati sarvaśaḥ 
brahmaiva saṃniyantṛ syāt kṣatraṃ hi brahmasaṃbhavam  Mn 
adbhyo 'gnir brahmataḥ kṣatram aśmano loham utthitam 
teṣāṃ sarvatragaṃ tejaḥ svāsu yoniṣu śāmyati  Mn 
nābrahma kṣatram ṛdhnoti nākṣatraṃ brahma vardhate 
brahma kṣatraṃ ca saṃpṛktam iha cāmutra vardhate  Mn 
dattvā dhanaṃ tu viprebhyaḥ sarvadaṇḍasamutthitam 
putre rājyaṃ samāsṛjya kurvīta prāyaṇaṃ raṇe  Mn 
evaṃ caran sadā yukto rājadharmeṣu pārthivaḥ 
hiteṣu caiva lokasya sarvān bhṛtyān niyojayet  Mn 
eṣo 'khilaḥ karmavidhir ukto rājñaḥ sanātanaḥ 
imaṃ karmavidhiṃ vidyāt kramaśo vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ  Mn 
vaiśyas tu kṛtasaṃskāraḥ kṛtvā dāraparigraham 
vārtāyāṃ nityayuktaḥ syāt paśūnāṃ caiva rakṣaṇe  Mn 
prajāpatir hi vaiśyāya sṛṣṭvā paridade paśūn 
brāhmaṇāya ca rājñe ca sarvāḥ paridade prajāḥ  Mn 
na ca vaiśyasya kāmaḥ syān na rakṣeyaṃ paśūn iti 
vaiśye cecchati nānyena rakṣitavyāḥ kathaṃ cana  Mn 
maṇimuktāpravālānāṃ lohānāṃ tāntavasya ca 
gandhānāṃ ca rasānāṃ ca vidyād arghabalābalam  Mn 
bījānām uptivic ca syāt kṣetradoṣaguṇasya ca 
mānayogaṃ ca jānīyāt tulāyogāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ  Mn 
sārāsāraṃ ca bhāṇḍānāṃ deśānāṃ ca guṇāguṇān 
lābhālābhaṃ ca paṇyānāṃ paśūnāṃ parivardhanam  Mn 
bhṛtyānāṃ ca bhṛtiṃ vidyād bhāṣāś ca vividhā nṛṇāṃ 
dravyāṇāṃ sthānayogāṃś ca krayavikrayam eva ca  Mn 
dharmeṇa ca dravyavṛddhāv ātiṣṭhed yatnam uttamam 
dadyāc ca sarvabhūtānām annam eva prayatnataḥ  Mn 
viprāṇāṃ vedaviduṣāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ yaśasvinām 
śuśrūṣaiva tu śūdrasya dharmo naiśreyasaḥ paraḥ  Mn 
śucir utkṛṣṭaśuśrūṣur mṛduvāg anahaṃkṛtaḥ 
brāhmaṇādyāśrayo nityam utkṛṣṭāṃ jātim aśnute  Mn 
eṣo 'nāpadi varṇānām uktaḥ karmavidhiḥ śubhaḥ 
āpady api hi yas teṣāṃ kramaśas tan nibodhata  Mn 
adhīyīraṃs trayo varṇāḥ svakarmasthā dvijātayaḥ 
prabrūyād brāhmaṇas tv eṣāṃ netarāv iti niścayaḥ  Mn 
sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇo vidyād vṛttyupāyān yathāvidhi 
prabrūyād itarebhyaś ca svayaṃ caiva tathā bhavet  Mn 
vaiśeṣyāt prakṛtiśraiṣṭhyān niyamasya ca dhāraṇāt 
saṃskārasya viśeṣāc ca varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ prabhuḥ  Mn 
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyas trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ 
caturtha ekajātis tu śūdro nāsti tu pañcamaḥ  Mn 
sarvavarṇeṣu tulyāsu patnīṣv akṣatayoniṣu 
ānulomyena saṃbhūtā jātyā jñeyās ta eva te  Mn 
strīṣv anantarajātāsu dvijair utpāditān sutān 
sadṛśān eva tān āhur mātṛdoṣavigarhitān  Mn 
anantarāsu jātānāṃ vidhir eṣa sanātanaḥ 
dvyekāntarāsu jātānāṃ dharmyaṃ vidyād imaṃ vidhim  Mn 
brāhmaṇād vaiśyakanyāyām ambaṣṭho nāma jāyate 
niṣādaḥ śūdrakanyāyāṃ yaḥ pāraśava ucyate  Mn 
kṣatriyāc chūdrakanyāyāṃ krūrācāravihāravān 
kṣatraśūdravapur jantur ugro nāma prajāyate  Mn 
viprasya triṣu varṇeṣu nṛpater varṇayor dvayoḥ 
vaiśyasya varṇe caikasmin ṣaḍ ete 'pasadāḥ smṛtāḥ  Mn 
kṣatriyād viprakanyāyāṃ sūto bhavati jātitaḥ 
vaiśyān māgadhavaidehau rājaviprāṅganāsutau  Mn 
śūdrād āyogavaḥ kṣattā caṇḍālaś cādhamo nṛṇām 
vaiśyarājanyaviprāsu jāyante varṇasaṃkarāḥ  Mn 
ekāntare tv ānulomyād ambaṣṭhograu yathā smṛtau 
kṣattṛvaidehakau tadvat prātilomye 'pi janmani  Mn 
putrā ye 'nantarastrījāḥ krameṇoktā dvijanmanām 
tān anantaranāmnas tu mātṛdoṣāt pracakṣate  Mn 
brāhmaṇād ugrakanyāyām āvṛto nāma jāyate 
ābhīro 'mbaṣṭhakanyāyām āyogavyāṃ tu dhigvaṇaḥ  Mn 
āyogavaś ca kṣattā ca caṇḍālaś cādhamo nṛṇām 
prātilomyena jāyante śūdrād apasadās trayaḥ  Mn 
vaiśyān māgadhavaidehau kṣatriyāt sūta eva tu 
pratīpam ete jāyante pare 'py apasadās trayaḥ  Mn 
jāto niṣādāc chūdrāyāṃ jātyā bhavati pukkasaḥ 
śūdrāj jāto niṣādyāṃ tu sa vai kukkuṭakaḥ smṛtaḥ  Mn 
kṣattur jātas tathogrāyāṃ śvapāka iti kīrtyate 
vaidehakena tv ambaṣṭhyām utpanno veṇa ucyate  Mn 
dvijātayaḥ savarṇāsu janayanty avratāṃs tu yān 
tān sāvitrīparibhraṣṭān vrātyān iti vinirdiśet  Mn 
vrātyāt tu jāyate viprāt pāpātmā bhūrjakaṇṭakaḥ 
āvantyavāṭadhānau ca puṣpadhaḥ śaikha eva ca  Mn 
jhallo mallaś ca rājanyād vrātyān nicchivir eva ca 
naṭaś ca karaṇaś caiva khaso draviḍa eva ca  Mn 
vaiśyāt tu jāyate vrātyāt sudhanvācārya eva ca 
kāruṣaś ca vijanmā ca maitraḥ sātvata eva ca  Mn 
vyabhicāreṇa varṇānām avedyāvedanena ca 
svakarmaṇāṃ ca tyāgena jāyante varṇasaṃkarāḥ  Mn 
saṃkīrṇayonayo ye tu pratilomānulomajāḥ 
anyonyavyatiṣaktāś ca tān pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ  Mn 
sūto vaidehakaś caiva caṇḍālaś ca narādhamaḥ 
māgadhaḥ tathāyogava eva ca kṣatrajātiś ca  Mn 
ete ṣaṭ sadṛśān varṇāñ janayanti svayoniṣu 
mātṛjātyāṃ prasūyante pravārāsu ca yoniṣu  Mn 
yathā trayāṇāṃ varṇānāṃ dvayor ātmāsya jāyate 
ānantaryāt svayonyāṃ tu tathā bāhyeṣv api kramāt  Mn 
te cāpi bāhyān subahūṃs tato 'py adhikadūṣitān 
parasparasya dāreṣu janayanti vigarhitān  Mn 
yathaiva śūdro brāhmaṇyāṃ bāhyaṃ jantuṃ prasūyate 
tathā bāhyataraṃ bāhyaś cāturvarṇye prasūyate  Mn 
pratikūlaṃ vartamānā bāhyā bāhyatarān punaḥ 
hīnā hīnān prasūyante varṇān pañcadaśaiva tu  Mn 
prasādhanopacārajñam adāsaṃ dāsajīvanam 
sairindhraṃ vāgurāvṛttiṃ sūte dasyur ayogave  Mn 
maitreyakaṃ tu vaideho mādhūkaṃ saṃprasūyate 
nṝn praśaṃsaty ajasraṃ yo ghaṇṭātāḍo 'ruṇodaye  Mn 
niṣādo mārgavaṃ sūte dāsaṃ naukarmajīvinam 
kaivartam iti yaṃ prāhur āryāvartanivāsinaḥ  Mn 
mṛtavastrabhṛtsv nārīṣu garhitānnāśanāsu ca 
bhavanty āyogavīṣv ete jātihīnāḥ pṛthak trayaḥ  Mn 
kārāvaro niṣādāt tu carmakāraḥ prasūyate 
vaidehikād andhramedau bahirgrāmapratiśrayau  Mn 
caṇḍālāt pāṇḍusopākas tvaksāravyavahāravān 
āhiṇḍiko niṣādena vaidehyām eva jāyate  Mn 
caṇḍālena tu sopāko mūlavyasanavṛttimān 
pukkasyāṃ jāyate pāpaḥ sadā sajjanagarhitaḥ  Mn 
niṣādastrī tu caṇḍālāt putram antyāvasāyinam 
śmaśānagocaraṃ sūte bāhyānām api garhitam  Mn 
saṃkare jātayas tv etāḥ pitṛmātṛpradarśitāḥ 
prachannā vā prakāśā vā veditavyāḥ svakarmabhiḥ  Mn 
svajātijānantarajāḥ ṣaṭ sutā dvijadharmiṇaḥ 
śūdrāṇāṃ tu sadharmāṇaḥ sarve 'padhvaṃsajāḥ smṛtāḥ  Mn 
tapobījaprabhāvais tu te gacchanti yuge yuge 
utkarṣaṃ cāpakarṣaṃ ca manuṣyeṣv iha janmataḥ  Mn 
śanakais tu kriyālopād imāḥ kṣatriyajātayaḥ 
vṛṣalatvaṃ gatā loke brāhmaṇādarśanena ca  Mn 
pauṇḍrakāś cauḍradraviḍāḥ kāmbojā yavanāḥ śakāḥ 
pāradāpahlavāś cīnāḥ kirātā daradāḥ khaśāḥ  Mn 
mukhabāhūrupajjānāṃ yā loke jātayo bahiḥ 
mlecchavācaś cāryavācaḥ sarve te dasyavaḥ smṛtāḥ  Mn 
ye dvijānām apasadā ye cāpadhvaṃsajāḥ smṛtāḥ 
te ninditair vartayeyur dvijānām eva karmabhiḥ  Mn 
sūtānām aśvasārathyam ambaṣṭhānāṃ cikitsanam 
vaidehakānāṃ strīkāryaṃ māgadhānāṃ vaṇikpathaḥ  Mn 
matsyaghāto niṣādānāṃ tvaṣṭis tv āyogavasya ca 
medāndhracuñcumadgūnām āraṇyapaśuhiṃsanam  Mn 
kṣattrugrapukkasānāṃ tu bilaukovadhabandhanam 
dhigvaṇānāṃ carmakāryaṃ veṇānāṃ bhāṇḍavādanam  Mn 
caityadrumaśmaśāneṣu śaileṣūpavaneṣu ca 
vaseyur ete vijñātā vartayantaḥ svakarmabhiḥ  Mn 
caṇḍālaśvapacānāṃ tu bahir grāmāt pratiśrayaḥ 
apapātrāś ca kartavyā dhanam eṣāṃ śvagardabham  Mn 
vāsāṃsi mṛtacailāni bhinnabhāṇḍeṣu bhojanam 
kārṣṇāyasam alaṅkāraḥ parivrajyā ca nityaśaḥ  Mn 
na taiḥ samayam anvicchet puruṣo dharmam ācaran 
vyavahāro mithas teṣāṃ vivāhaḥ sadṛśaiḥ saha  Mn 
annam eṣāṃ parādhīnaṃ deyaṃ syād bhinnabhājane 
rātrau na vicareyus te grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca  Mn 
divā careyuḥ kāryārthaṃ cihnitā rājaśāsanaiḥ 
abāndhavaṃ śavaṃ caiva nirhareyur iti sthitiḥ  Mn 
vadhyāṃś ca hanyuḥ satataṃ yathāśāstraṃ nṛpājñayā 
vadhyavāsāṃsi gṛhṇīyuḥ śayyāś cābharaṇāni ca  Mn 
varṇāpetam avijñātaṃ naraṃ kaluṣayonijam 
āryarūpam ivānāryaṃ karmabhiḥ svair vibhāvayet  Mn 
anāryatā niṣṭhuratā krūratā niṣkriyātmatā 
puruṣaṃ vyañjayantīha loke kaluṣayonijam  Mn 
pitryaṃ vā bhajate śīlaṃ mātur vobhayam eva vā 
na kathaṃ cana duryoniḥ prakṛtiṃ svāṃ niyacchati  Mn 
kule mukhye 'pi jātasya yasya syād yonisaṃkaraḥ 
saṃśrayaty eva tacchīlaṃ naro 'lpam api vā bahu  Mn 
yatra tv ete paridhvaṃsāj jāyante varṇadūṣakāḥ 
rāṣṭrikaiḥ saha tad rāṣṭraṃ kṣipram eva vinaśyati  Mn 
brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe vā dehatyāgo 'nupaskṛtaḥ 
strībālābhyupapattau ca bāhyānāṃ siddhikāraṇam  Mn 
ahiṃsā satyam asteyaṃ śaucam indriyanigrahaḥ 
etaṃ sāmāsikaṃ dharmaṃ cāturvarṇye 'bravīn manuḥ  Mn 
śūdrāyāṃ brāhmaṇāj jātaḥ śreyasā cet prajāyate 
aśreyān śreyasīṃ jātiṃ gacchaty ā saptamād yugāt  Mn 
śūdro brāhmaṇatām eti brāhmaṇaś caiti śūdratām 
kṣatriyāj jātam evaṃ tu vidyād vaiśyāt tathaiva ca  Mn 
anāryāyāṃ samutpanno brāhmaṇāt tu yadṛcchayā 
brāhmaṇyām apy anāryāt tu śreyastvaṃ kveti ced bhavet  Mn 
jāto nāryām anāryāyām āryād āryo bhaved guṇaiḥ 
jāto 'py anāryād āryāyām anārya iti niścayaḥ  Mn 
tāv ubhāv apy asaṃskāryāv iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ 
vaiguṇyāj janmanaḥ pūrva uttaraḥ pratilomataḥ  Mn 
subījaṃ caiva sukṣetre jātaṃ saṃpadyate yathā 
tathāryāj jāta āryāyāṃ sarvaṃ saṃskāram arhati  Mn 
bījam eke praśaṃsanti kṣetram anye manīṣiṇaḥ 
bījakṣetre tathaivānye tatreyaṃ tu vyavasthitiḥ  Mn 
akṣetre bījam utsṛṣṭam antaraiva vinaśyati 
abījakam api kṣetraṃ kevalaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ bhavet  Mn 
yasmād bījaprabhāveṇa tiryagjā ṛṣayo 'bhavan 
pūjitāś ca praśastāś ca tasmād bījaṃ praśasyate  Mn 
anāryam āryakarmāṇam āryaṃ cānāryakarmiṇam 
saṃpradhāryābravīd dhātā na samau nāsamāv iti  Mn 
brāhmaṇā brahmayonisthā ye svakarmaṇy avasthitāḥ 
te samyag upajīveyuḥ ṣaṭ karmāṇi yathākramam  Mn 
adhyāpanam adhyayanaṃ yajanaṃ yājanaṃ tathā 
dānaṃ pratigrahaś caiva ṣaṭ karmāṇy agrajanmanaḥ  Mn 
ṣaṇṇāṃ tu karmaṇām asya trīṇi karmāṇi jīvikā 
yājanādhyāpane caiva viśuddhāc ca pratigrahaḥ  Mn 
trayo dharmā nivartante brāhmaṇāt kṣatriyaṃ prati 
adhyāpanaṃ yājanaṃ ca tṛtīyaś ca pratigrahaḥ  Mn 
vaiśyaṃ prati tathaivaite nivarterann iti sthitiḥ 
na tau prati hi tān dharmān manur āha prajāpatiḥ  Mn 
śastrāstrabhṛttvaṃ kṣatrasya vaṇikpaśukṛṣir viṣaḥ 
ājīvanārthaṃ dharmas tu dānam adhyayanaṃ yajiḥ  Mn 
vedābhyāso brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyasya ca rakṣaṇam 
vārtākarmaiva vaiśyasya viśiṣṭāni svakarmasu  Mn 
ajīvaṃs tu yathoktena brāhmaṇaḥ svena karmaṇā 
jīvet kṣatriyadharmeṇa sa hy asya praty anantaraḥ  Mn 
ubhābhyām apy ajīvaṃs tu kathaṃ syād iti ced bhavet 
kṛṣigorakṣam āsthāya jīved vaiśyasya jīvikām  Mn 
vaiśyavṛttyāpi jīvaṃs tu brāhmaṇaḥ ksatriyo 'pi vā 
hiṃsāprāyāṃ parādhīnāṃ kṛṣiṃ yatnena varjayet  Mn 
kṛṣiṃ sādhv iti manyante sā vṛttiḥ sadvigarhitāḥ 
bhūmiṃ bhūmiśayāṃś caiva hanti kāṣṭham ayomukham  Mn 
idaṃ tu vṛttivaikalyāt tyajato dharmanaipuṇaṃ 
viṭpaṇyam uddhṛtoddhāraṃ vikreyaṃ vittavardhanam  Mn 
sarvān rasān apoheta kṛtānnaṃ ca tilaiḥ saha 
aśmano lavaṇaṃ caiva paśavo ye ca mānuṣāḥ  Mn 
sarvaṃ ca tāntavaṃ raktaṃ śāṇakṣaumāvikāni ca 
api cet syur araktāni phalamūle tathauṣadhīḥ  Mn 
apaḥ śastraṃ viṣaṃ māṃsaṃ somaṃ gandhāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ 
kṣīraṃ kṣaudraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ madhu guḍaṃ kuśān  Mn 
āraṇyāṃś ca paśūn sarvān daṃṣṭriṇaś ca vayāṃsi ca 
madyaṃ nīliṃ ca lākṣāṃ ca sarvāṃś caikaśaphāṃs tathā  Mn 
kāmam utpādya kṛṣyāṃ tu svayam eva kṛṣīvalaḥ 
vikrīṇīta tilāñ śūdrān dharmārtham acirasthitān  Mn 
bhojanābhyañjanād dānād yad anyat kurute tilaiḥ 
kṛmibhūtaḥ śvaviṣṭhāyāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha majjati  Mn 
sadyaḥ patati māṃsena lākṣayā lavaṇena ca 
tryaheṇa śūdro bhavati brāhmaṇaḥ kṣīravikrayāt  Mn 
itareṣāṃ tu paṇyānāṃ vikrayād iha kāmataḥ 
brāhmaṇaḥ saptarātreṇa vaiśyabhāvaṃ niyacchati  Mn 
rasā rasair nimātavyā na tv eva lavaṇaṃ rasaiḥ 
kṛtānnaṃ ca kṛtānnena tilā dhānyena tatsamāḥ  Mn 
jīved etena rājanyaḥ sarveṇāpy anayaṃ gataḥ 
na tv eva jyāyaṃsīṃ vṛttim abhimanyeta karhi cit  Mn 
yo lobhād adhamo jātyā jīved utkṛṣṭakarmabhiḥ 
taṃ rājā nirdhanaṃ kṛtvā kṣipram eva pravāsayet  Mn 
varaṃ svadharmo viguṇo na pārakyaḥ svanuṣṭhitaḥ 
paradharmeṇa jīvan hi sadyaḥ patati jātitaḥ  Mn 
vaiśyo 'jīvan svadharmeṇa śūdravṛttyāpi vartayet 
anācarann akāryāṇi nivarteta ca śaktimān  Mn 
aśaknuvaṃs tu śuśrūṣāṃ śūdraḥ kartuṃ dvijanmanām 
putradārātyayaṃ prāpto jīvet kārukakarmabhiḥ  Mn 
yaiḥ karmabhiḥ pracaritaiḥ śuśrūṣyante dvijātayaḥ 
tāni kārukakarmāṇi śilpāni vividhāni ca  Mn 
vaiśyavṛttim anātiṣṭhan brāhmaṇaḥ sve pathi sthitaḥ 
avṛttikarṣitaḥ sīdann imaṃ dharmaṃ samācaret  Mn 
sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyād brāhmaṇas tv anayaṃ gataḥ 
pavitraṃ duṣyatīty etad dharmato nopapadyate  Mn 
nādhyāpanād yājanād vā garhitād vā pratigrahāt 
doṣo bhavati viprāṇāṃ jvalanāmbusamā hi te  Mn 
jīvitātyayam āpanno yo 'nnam atti tatas tataḥ 
ākāśam iva paṅkena na sa pāpena lipyate  Mn 
ajīgartaḥ sutaṃ hantum upāsarpad bubhukṣitaḥ 
na cālipyata pāpena kṣutpratīkāram ācaran  Mn 
śvamāṃsam icchan ārto 'ttuṃ dharmādharmavicakṣaṇaḥ 
prāṇānāṃ parirakṣārthaṃ vāmadevo na liptavān  Mn 
bharadvājaḥ kṣudhārtas tu saputro vijane vane 
bahvīr gāḥ pratijagrāha vṛdhos takṣṇo mahātapāḥ  Mn 
kṣudhārtaś cāttum abhyāgād viśvāmitraḥ śvajāghanīm 
caṇḍālahastād ādāya dharmādharmavicakṣaṇaḥ  Mn 
pratigrahād yājanād vā tathaivādhyāpanād api 
pratigrahaḥ pratyavaraḥ pretya viprasya garhitaḥ  Mn 
yājanādhyāpane nityaṃ kriyete saṃskṛtātmanām 
pratigrahas tu kriyate śūdrād apy antyajanmanaḥ  Mn 
japahomair apaity eno yājanādhyāpanaiḥ kṛtam 
pratigrahanimittaṃ tu tyāgena tapasaiva ca  Mn 
śiloñcham apy ādadīta vipro 'jīvan yatas tataḥ 
pratigrahāc chilaḥ śreyāṃs tato 'py uñchaḥ praśasyate  Mn 
sīdadbhiḥ kupyam icchadbhir dhane vā pṛthivīpatiḥ 
yācyaḥ syāt snātakair viprair aditsaṃs tyāgam arhati  Mn 
akṛtaṃ ca kṛtāt kṣetrād gaur ajāvikam eva ca 
hiraṇyaṃ dhānyam annaṃ ca pūrvaṃ pūrvam adoṣavat  Mn 
sapta vittāgamā dharmyā dāyo lābhaḥ krayo jayaḥ 
prayogaḥ karmayogaś ca satpratigraha eva ca  Mn 
vidyā śilpaṃ bhṛtiḥ sevā gorakṣyaṃ vipaṇiḥ kṛṣiḥ 
dhṛtir bhaikṣaṃ kusīdaṃ ca daśa jīvanahetavaḥ  Mn 
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi vṛddhiṃ naiva prayojayet 
kāmaṃ tu khalu dharmārthaṃ dadyāt pāpīyase 'lpikām  Mn 
caturtham ādadāno 'pi kṣatriyo bhāgam āpadi 
prajā rakṣan paraṃ śaktyā kilbiṣāt pratimucyate  Mn 
svadharmo vijayas tasya nāhave syāt parāṅmukhaḥ 
śastreṇa vaiśyān rakṣitvā dharmyam āhārayed balim  Mn 
dhānye 'ṣṭamaṃ viśāṃ śulkaṃ viṃśaṃ kārṣāpaṇāvaram 
karmopakaraṇāḥ śūdrāḥ kāravaḥ śilpinas tathā  Mn 
śūdras tu vṛttim ākāṅkṣan kṣatram ārādhayed yadi 
dhaninaṃ vāpy upārādhya vaiśyaṃ śūdro jijīviṣet  Mn 
svargārtham ubhayārthaṃ vā viprān ārādhayet tu saḥ 
jātabrāhmaṇaśabdasya sā hy asya kṛtakṛtyatā  Mn 
viprasevaiva śūdrasya viśiṣṭaṃ karma kīrtyate 
yad ato 'nyad dhi kurute tad bhavaty asya niṣphalam  Mn 
prakalpyā tasya tair vṛttiḥ svakuṭumbād yathārhataḥ 
śaktiṃ cāvekṣya dākṣyaṃ ca bhṛtyānāṃ ca parigraham  Mn 
ucchiṣṭam annaṃ dātavyaṃ jīrṇāni vasanāni ca 
pulākāś caiva dhānyānāṃ jīrṇāś caiva paricchadāḥ  Mn 
na śūdre pātakaṃ kiṃ cin na ca saṃskāram arhati 
nāsyādhikāro dharme 'sti na dharmāt pratiṣedhanam  Mn 
dharmepsavas tu dharmajñāḥ satāṃ vṛttam anuṣṭhitāḥ 
mantravarjyaṃ na duṣyanti praśaṃsāṃ prāpnuvanti ca  Mn 
yathā yathā hi sadvṛttam ātiṣṭhaty anasūyakaḥ 
tathā tathemaṃ cāmuṃ ca lokaṃ prāpnoty aninditaḥ  Mn 
śaktenāpi hi śūdreṇa na kāryo dhanasaṃcayaḥ 
śūdro hi dhanam āsādya brāhmaṇān eva bādhate  Mn 
ete caturṇāṃ varṇānām āpaddharmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ 
yān samyag anutiṣṭhanto vrajanti paramaṃ gatim  Mn 
eṣa dharmavidhiḥ kṛtsnaś cāturvarṇyasya kīrtitaḥ 
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi prāyaścittavidhiṃ śubham  Mn 
sāntānikaṃ yakṣyamāṇam adhvagaṃ sārvavedasam 
gurvarthaṃ pitṛmātrarthaṃ svādhyāyārthy upatāpinaḥ  Mn 
na vai tān snātakān vidyād brāhmaṇān dharmabhikṣukān 
niḥsvebhyo deyam etebhyo dānaṃ vidyāviśeṣataḥ  Mn 
etebhyo hi dvijāgryebhyo deyam annaṃ sadakṣiṇam 
itarebhyo bahirvedi kṛtānnaṃ deyam ucyate  Mn 
sarvaratnāni rājā tu yathārhaṃ pratipādayet 
brāhmaṇān vedaviduṣo yajñārthaṃ caiva dakṣiṇām  Mn 
kṛtadāro 'parān dārān bhikṣitvā yo 'dhigacchati 
ratimātraṃ phalaṃ tasya dravyadātus tu saṃtatiḥ  Mn 
dhanāni tu yathāśakti vipreṣu pratipādayet 
vedavitsu vivikteṣu pretya svargaṃ samaśnute  Mn 
yasya traivārṣikaṃ bhaktaṃ paryāptaṃ bhṛtyavṛttaye 
adhikaṃ vāpi vidyeta sa somaṃ pātum arhati  MnM 
ataḥ svalpīyasi dravye yaḥ somaṃ pibati dvijaḥ 
sa pītasomapūrvo 'pi na tasyāpnoti tatphalam  MnM 
śaktaḥ parajane dātā svajane duḥkhajīvini 
madhvāpāto viṣāsvādaḥ sa dharmapratirūpakaḥ  MnM 
bhṛtyānām uparodhena yat karoty aurdhvadehikam 
tad bhavaty asukhodarkaṃ jīvataś ca mṛtasya ca  MnM 
yajñaś cet pratiruddhaḥ syād ekenāṅgena yajvanaḥ 
brāhmaṇasya viśeṣena dhārmike sati rājani  MnM 
yo vaiśyaḥ syād bahupaśur hīnakratur asomapaḥ 
kuṭumbāt tasya tad dravyam āhared yajñasiddhaye  MnM 
āharet trīṇi vā dve vā kāmaṃ śūdrasya veśmanaḥ 
na hi śūdrasya yajñeṣu kaś cid asti parigrahaḥ  MnM 
yo 'nāhitāgniḥ śatagur ayajvā ca sahasraguḥ 
tayor api kuṭumbābhyām āhared avicārayan  MnM 
ādānanityāc cādātur āhared aprayacchataḥ 
tathā yaśo 'sya prathate dharmaś caiva pravardhate  MnM 
tathāaiva saptame bhakte bhaktāni ṣaḍ anaśnatā 
aśvastanavidhānena hartavyaṃ hīnakarmaṇaḥ  MnM 
khalāt kṣetrād agārād vā yato vāpy upalabhyate 
ākhyātavyaṃ tu tat tasmai pṛcchate yadi pṛcchati  MnM 
brāhmaṇasvaṃ na hartavyaṃ kṣatriyeṇa kadā cana 
dasyuniṣkriyayos tu svam ajīvan hartum arhati  MnM 
yo 'sādhubhyo 'rtham ādāya sādhubhyaḥ saṃprayacchati 
sa kṛtvā plavam ātmānaṃ saṃtārayati tāv ubhau  MnM 
yad dhanaṃ yajñaśīlānāṃ devasvaṃ tad vidur budhāḥ 
ayajvanāṃ tu yad vittam āsurasvaṃ tad ucyate  MnM 
na tasmin dhārayed daṇḍaṃ dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ 
kṣatriyasya hi bāliśyād brāhmaṇaḥ sīdati kṣudhā  MnM 
tasya bhṛtyajanaṃ jñātvā svakuṭumbān mahīpatiḥ 
śrutaśīle ca vijñāya vṛttiṃ dharmyāṃ prakalpayet  MnM 
kalpayitvāsya vṛttiṃ ca rakṣed enaṃ samantataḥ 
rājā hi dharmaṣaḍbhāgaṃ tasmāt prāpnoti rakṣitāt  MnM 
na yajñārthaṃ dhanaṃ śūdrād vipro bhikṣeta karhi cit 
yajamāno hi bhikṣitvā caṇḍālaḥ pretya jāyate  MnM 
yājñārtham arthaṃ bhikṣitvā yo na sarvaṃ prayacchati 
sa yāti bhāsatāṃ vipraḥ kākatāṃ vā śataṃ samāḥ  MnM 
devasvaṃ brāhmaṇasvaṃ vā lobhenopahinasti yaḥ 
sa pāpātmā pare loke gṛdhrocchiṣṭena jīvati  MnM 
iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ nityaṃ nirvaped abdaparyaye 
kḷptānāṃ paśusomānāṃ niṣkṛtyartham asaṃbhave  MnM 
āpatkalpena yo dharmaṃ kurute 'nāpadi dvijaḥ 
sa nāpnoti phalaṃ tasya paratreti vicāritam  MnM 
viśvaiś ca devaiḥ sādhyaiś ca brāhmaṇaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ 
āpatsu maraṇād bhītair vidheḥ pratinidhiḥ kṛtaḥ  MnM 
prabhuḥ prathamakalpasya yo 'nukalpena vartate 
na sāṃparāyikaṃ tasya durmater vidyate phalam  MnM 
na brāhmaṇo vedayeta kiṃ cid rājani dharmavit 
svavīryeṇaiva tāñ śiṣyān mānavān apakāriṇaḥ  MnM 
svavīryād rājavīryāc ca svavīryaṃ balavattaram 
tasmāt svenaiva vīryeṇa nigṛhṇīyād arīn dvijaḥ  MnM 
śrutīr atharvāṅgirasīḥ kuryād ity avicārayan 
vākśastraṃ vai brāhmaṇasya tena hanyād arīn dvijaḥ  MnM 
kṣatriyo bāhuvīryeṇa tared āpadam ātmanaḥ 
dhanena vaiśyaśūdrau tu japahomair dvijottamaḥ  MnM 
vidhātā śāsitā vaktā maitro brāhmaṇa ucyate 
tasmai nākuśalaṃ brūyān na śuṣkāṃ giram īrayet  MnM 
na vai kanyā na yuvatir nālpavidyo na bāliśaḥ 
hotā syād agnihotrasya nārto nāsaṃskṛtas tathā  MnM 
narake hi patanty ete juhvantaḥ sa ca yasya tat 
tasmād vaitānakuśalo hotā syād vedapāragaḥ  MnM 
prājāpatyam adattvāśvam agnyādheyasya dakṣiṇām 
anāhitāgnir bhavati brāhmaṇo vibhave sati  MnM 
puṇyāny anyāni kurvīta śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ 
na tv alpadakṣiṇair yajñair yajeteha kathaṃ cana  MnM 
indriyāṇi yaśaḥ svargam āyuḥ kīrtiṃ prajāḥ paśūn 
hanty alpadakṣiṇo yajñas tasmān nālpadhano yajet  MnM 
agnihotry apavidhyāgnīn brāhmaṇaḥ kāmakārataḥ 
cāndrāyaṇaṃ caren māsaṃ vīrahatyāsamaṃ hi tat  MnM 
ye śūdrād adhigamyārtham agnihotram upāsate 
ṛtvijas te hi śūdrāṇāṃ brahmavādiṣu garhitāḥ  MnM 
teṣāṃ satatam ajñānāṃ vṛṣalāgnyupasevinām 
padā mastakam ākramya dātā durgāṇi saṃtaret  MnM 
akurvan vihitaṃ karma ninditaṃ ca samācaran 
prasaktaś cendriyārtheṣu prāyaścittīyate naraḥ  MnM 
akāmataḥ kṛte pāpe prāyaścittaṃ vidur budhāḥ 
kāmakārakṛte 'py āhur eke śrutinidarśanāt  MnM 
akāmataḥ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vedābhyāsena śudhyati 
kāmatas tu kṛtaṃ mohāt prāyaścittaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ  MnM 
prāyaścittīyatāṃ prāpya daivāt pūrvakṛtena vā 
na saṃsargaṃ vrajet sadbhiḥ prāyaścitte 'kṛte dvijaḥ  MnM 
iha duścaritaiḥ ke cit ke cit pūrvakṛtais tathā 
prāpnuvanti durātmāno narā rūpaviparyayam  MnM 
suvarṇacauraḥ kaunakhyaṃ surāpaḥ śyāvadantatām 
brahmahā kṣayarogitvaṃ dauścarmyaṃ gurutalpagaḥ  MnM 
piśunaḥ pautināsikyaṃ sūcakaḥ pūtivaktratām 
dhānyacauro 'ṅgahīnatvam ātiraikyaṃ tu miśrakaḥ  MnM 
annahartāmayāvitvaṃ maukyaṃ vāgapahārakaḥ 
vastrāpahārakaḥ śvaitryaṃ paṅgutām aśvahārakaḥ  MnM 
evaṃ karmaviśeṣeṇa jāyante sadvigarhitāḥ 
jaḍamūkāndhabadhirā vikṛtākṛtayas tathā  MnM 
caritavyam ato nityaṃ prāyaścittaṃ viśuddhaye 
nindyair hi lakṣaṇair yuktā jāyante 'niṣkṛtainasaḥ  MnM 
brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ steyaṃ gurvaṅganāgamaḥ 
mahānti pātakāny āhuḥ saṃsargaś cāpi taiḥ saha  MnM 
anṛtaṃ ca samutkarṣe rājagāmi ca paiśunam 
guroś cālīkanirbandhaḥ samāni brahmahatyayā  MnM 
brahmojjhatā vedanindā kauṭasākṣyaṃ suhṛdvadhaḥ 
garhitānādyayor jagdhiḥ surāpānasamāni ṣaṭ  MnM 
nikṣepasyāpaharaṇaṃ narāśvarajatasya ca 
bhūmivajramaṇīnāṃ ca rukmasteyasamaṃ smṛtam  MnM 
retaḥsekaḥ svayonīṣu kumārīṣv antyajāsu ca 
sakhyuḥ putrasya ca strīṣu gurutalpasamaṃ viduḥ  MnM 
govadho 'yājyasaṃyājyaṃ pāradāryātmavikrayaḥ 
gurumātṛpitṛtyāgaḥ svādhyāyāgnyoḥ sutasya ca  MnM 
parivittitānuje 'nūḍhe parivedanam eva ca 
tayor dānaṃ ca kanyāyās tayor eva ca yājanam  MnM 
kanyāyā dūṣaṇaṃ caiva vārdhuṣyaṃ vratalopanam 
taḍāgārāmadārāṇām apatyasya ca vikrayaḥ  MnM 
vrātyatā bāndhavatyāgo bhṛtyādhyāpanam eva ca 
bhṛtyā cādhyayanādānam apaṇyānāṃ ca vikrayaḥ  MnM 
sarvākāreṣv adhīkāro mahāyantrapravartanam 
hiṃsauṣadhīnāṃ stryājīvo 'bhicāro mūlakarma ca  MnM 
indhanārtham aśuṣkāṇāṃ drumāṇām avapātanam 
ātmārthaṃ ca kriyārambho ninditānnādanaṃ tathā  MnM 
anāhitāgnitā steyam ṛṇānām anapakriyā 
asacchāṣṭrādhigamanaṃ kauśīlavyasya ca kriyā  MnM 
dhānyakupyapaśusteyaṃ madyapastrīniṣevaṇam 
strīśūdraviṭkṣatravadho nāstikyaṃ copapātakam  MnM 
brāhmaṇasya rujaḥ kṛtvā ghrātir aghreyamadyayoḥ 
jaihmyaṃ ca maithunaṃ puṃsi jātibhraṃśakaraṃ smṛtam  MnM 
kharāśvoṣṭramṛgebhānām ajāvikavadhas tathā 
saṃkarīkaraṇaṃ jñeyaṃ mīnāhimahiṣasya ca  MnM 
ninditebhyo dhanādānaṃ vāṇijyaṃ śūdrasevanam 
apātrīkaraṇaṃ jñeyam asatyasya ca bhāṣaṇam  MnM 
kṛmikīṭavayohatyā madyānugatabhojanam 
phalaidhaḥkusumasteyam adhairyaṃ ca malāvaham  MnM 
etāny enāṃsi sarvāṇi yathoktāni pṛthak pṛthak 
yair yair vratair apohyante tāni samyaṅ nibodhata  MnM 
brahmahā dvādaśa samāḥ kuṭīṃ kṛtvā vane vaset 
bhaikṣāśy ātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ kṛtvā śavaśiro dhvajam  MnM 
lakṣyaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ vā syād viduṣām icchayātmanaḥ 
prāsyed ātmānam agnau vā samiddhe trir avākśirāḥ  MnM 
yajeta vāśvamedhena svarjitā gosavena vā 
abhijidviśvajidbhyāṃ vā trivṛtāgniṣṭutāpi vā  MnM 
japan vānyatamaṃ vedaṃ yojanānāṃ śataṃ vrajet 
brahmahatyāpanodāya mitabhuṅ niyatendriyaḥ  MnM 
sarvasvaṃ vedaviduṣe brāhmaṇāyopapādayet 
dhanaṃ hi jīvanāyālaṃ gṛhaṃ vā saparicchadam  MnM 
haviṣyabhug vānusaret pratisrotaḥ sarasvatīm 
japed vā niyatāhāras trir vai vedasya saṃhitām  MnM 
kṛtavāpano nivased grāmānte govraje 'pi vā 
āśrame vṛkṣamūle vā gobrāhmaṇahite rataḥ  MnM 
brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe vā sadyaḥ prāṇān parityajet 
mucyate brahmahatyāyā goptā gor brāhmaṇasya ca  MnM 
trivāraṃ pratiroddhā vā sarvasvam avajitya vā 
viprasya tannimitte vā prāṇālābhe vimucyate  MnM 
evaṃ dṛḍhavrato nityaṃ brahmacārī samāhitaḥ 
samāpte dvādaśe varṣe brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati  MnM 
śiṣṭvā vā bhūmidevānāṃ naradevasamāgame 
svam eno 'vabhṛthasnāto hayamedhe vimucyate  MnM 
dharmasya brāhmaṇo mūlam agraṃ rājanya ucyate 
tasmāt samāgame teṣām eno vikhyāpya śudhyati  MnM 
brahmaṇaḥ saṃbhavenaiva devānām api daivatam 
pramāṇaṃ caiva lokasya brahmātraiva hi kāraṇam  MnM 
teṣāṃ vedavido brūyus trayo 'py enaḥ suniṣkṛtim 
sā teṣāṃ pāvanāya syāt pavitrā viduṣāṃ hi vāk  MnM 
ato 'nyatamam āsthāya vidhiṃ vipraḥ samāhitaḥ 
brahmahatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vyapohaty ātmavattayā  MnM 
hatvā garbham avijñātam etad eva vrataṃ caret 
rājanyavaiśyau cejānāv ātreyīm eva ca striyam  MnM 
uktvā caivānṛtaṃ sākṣye pratirudhya guruṃ tathā 
apahṛtya ca niḥkṣepaṃ kṛtvā ca strīsuhṛdvadham  MnM 
iyaṃ viśuddhir uditā pramāpyākāmato dvijam 
kāmato brāhmaṇavadhe niṣkṛtir na vidhīyate  MnM 
surāṃ pītvā dvijo mohād agnivarṇāṃ surāṃ pibet 
tayā sa kāye nirdagdhe mucyate kilbiṣāt tataḥ  MnM 
gomūtram agnivarṇaṃ vā pibed udakam eva vā 
payo ghṛtaṃ vā maraṇād gośakṛdrasam eva vā  MnM 
kaṇān vā bhakṣayed abdaṃ piṇyākaṃ vā sakṛn niśi 
surāpānāpanuttyarthaṃ vālavāsā jaṭī dhvajī  MnM 
surā vai malam annānāṃ pāpmā ca malam ucyate 
tasmād brāhmaṇarājanyau vaiśyaś ca na surāṃ pibet  MnM 
gauḍī paiṣṭī ca mādhvī ca vijñeyā trividhā surā 
yathaivaikā tathā sarvā na pātavyā dvijottamaiḥ  MnM 
yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācānnaṃ madyaṃ māṃsaṃ surāsavam 
tad brāhmaṇena nāttavyaṃ devānām aśnatā haviḥ  MnM 
amedhye vā paten matto vaidikaṃ vāpy udāharet 
akāryam anyat kuryād vā brāhmaṇo madamohitaḥ  MnM 
yasya kāyagataṃ brahma madyenāplāvyate sakṛt 
tasya vyapaiti brāhmaṇyaṃ śūdratvaṃ ca sa gacchati  MnM 
eṣā vicitrābhihitā surāpānasya niṣkṛtiḥ 
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi suvarṇasteyaniṣkṛtim  MnM 
suvarṇasteyakṛd vipro rājānam abhigamya tu 
svakarma khyāpayan brūyān māṃ bhavān anuśāstv iti  MnM 
gṛhītvā musalaṃ rājā sakṛd dhanyāt tu taṃ svayam 
vadhena śudhyati steno brāhmaṇas tapasaiva tu  MnM 
tapasāpanunutsus tu suvarṇasteyajaṃ malam 
cīravāsā dvijo 'raṇye cared brahmahaṇo vratam  MnM 
etair vratair apoheta pāpaṃ steyakṛtaṃ dvijaḥ 
gurustrīgamanīyaṃ tu vratair ebhir apānudet  MnM 
gurutalpy abhibhāṣyainas tapte svapyād ayomaye 
sūrmīṃ jvalantīṃ svāśliṣyen mṛtyunā sa viśudhyati  MnM 
svayaṃ vā śiṣṇavṛṣaṇāv utkṛtyādhāya cāñjalau 
nairṛtīṃ diśam ātiṣṭhed ā nipātād ajihmagaḥ  MnM 
khaṭvāṅgī cīravāsā vā śmaśrulo vijane vane 
prājāpatyaṃ caret kṛcchram abdam ekaṃ samāhitaḥ  MnM 
cāndrāyaṇaṃ vā trīn māsān abhyasyen niyatendriyaḥ 
haviṣyeṇa yavāgvā vā gurutalpāpanuttaye  MnM 
etair vratair apoheyur mahāpātakino malam 
upapātakinas tv evam ebhir nānāvidhair vrataiḥ  MnM 
upapātakasaṃyukto goghno māsaṃ yavān pibet 
kṛtavāpo vased goṣṭhe carmaṇā tena saṃvṛtaḥ  MnM 
caturthakālam aśnīyād akṣāralavaṇaṃ mitam 
gomūtreṇācaret snānaṃ dvau māsau niyatendriyaḥ  MnM 
divānugacched gās tās tu tiṣṭhann ūrdhvaṃ rajaḥ pibet 
śuśrūṣitvā namaskṛtya rātrau vīrāsanaṃ vaset  MnM 
tiṣṭhantīṣv anutiṣṭhet tu vrajantīṣv apy anuvrajet 
āsīnāsu tathāsīno niyato vītamatsaraḥ  MnM 
āturām abhiśastāṃ vā cauravyāghrādibhir bhayaiḥ 
patitāṃ paṅkalagnaṃ vā sarvopāyair vimocayet  MnM 
uṣṇe varṣati śīte vā mārute vāti vā bhṛśam 
na kurvītātmanas trāṇaṃ gor akṛtvā tu śaktitaḥ  MnM 
ātmano yadi vānyeṣāṃ gṛhe kṣetre 'tha vā khale 
bhakṣayantīṃ na kathayet pibantaṃ caiva vatsakam  MnM 
anena vidhinā yas tu goghno gām anugacchati 
sa gohatyākṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tribhir māsair vyapohati  MnM 
vṛṣabhaikādaśā gāś ca dadyāt sucaritavrataḥ 
avidyamāne sarvasvaṃ vedavidbhyo nivedayet  MnM 
etad eva vrataṃ kuryur upapātakino dvijāḥ 
avakīrṇivarjyaṃ śuddhyarthaṃ cāndrāyaṇam athāpi vā  MnM 
avakīrṇī tu kāṇena gardabhena catuṣpathe 
pākayajñavidhānena yajeta nirṛtiṃ niśi  MnM 
hutvāgnau vidhivad dhomān antataś ca samety ṛcā 
vātendraguruvahnīnāṃ juhuyāt sarpiṣāhutīḥ  MnM 
kāmato retasaḥ sekaṃ vratasthasya dvijanmanaḥ 
atikramaṃ vratasyāhur dharmajñā brahmavādinaḥ  MnM 
mārutaṃ puruhūtaṃ ca guruṃ pāvakam eva ca 
caturo vratino 'bhyeti brāhmaṃ tejo 'vakīrṇinaḥ  MnM 
etasminn enasi prāpte vasitvā gardabhājinam 
saptāgārāṃś cared bhaikṣaṃ svakarma parikīrtayan  MnM 
tebhyo labdhena bhaikṣeṇa vartayann ekakālikam 
upaspṛśaṃs triṣavaṇaṃ tv abdena sa viśudhyati  MnM 
jātibhraṃśakaraṃ karma kṛtvānyatamam icchayā 
caret sāṃtapanaṃ kṛcchraṃ prājāpatyam anicchayā  MnM 
saṃkarāpātrakṛtyāsu māsaṃ śodhanam aindavam 
malinīkaraṇīyeṣu taptaḥ syād yāvakais tryaham  MnM 
turīyo brahmahatyāyāḥ kṣatriyasya vadhe smṛtaḥ 
vaiśye 'ṣṭamāṃśo vṛttasthe śūdre jñeyas tu ṣoḍaśaḥ  MnM 
akāmatas tu rājanyaṃ vinipātya dvijottamaḥ 
vṛṣabhaikasahasrā gā dadyāt sucaritavrataḥ  MnM 
tryabdaṃ cared vā niyato jaṭī brahmahaṇo vratam 
vasan dūratare grāmād vṛkṣamūlaniketanaḥ  MnM 
etad eva cared abdaṃ prāyaścittaṃ dvijottamaḥ 
pramāpya vaiśyaṃ vṛttasthaṃ dadyāc caikaśataṃ gavām  MnM 
etad eva vrataṃ kṛtsnaṃ ṣaṇmāsāñ śūdrahā caret 
vṛṣabhaikādaśā vāpi dadyād viprāya gāḥ sitāḥ  MnM 
mārjāranakulau hatvā cāṣaṃ maṇḍūkam eva ca 
śvagodholūkakākāṃś ca śūdrahatyāvrataṃ caret  MnM 
payaḥ pibet trirātraṃ vā yojanaṃ vādhvano vrajet 
upaspṛśet sravantyāṃ vā sūktaṃ vābdaivataṃ japet  MnM 
abhriṃ kārṣṇāyasīṃ dadyāt sarpaṃ hatvā dvijottamaḥ 
palālabhārakaṃ ṣaṇḍhe saisakaṃ caikamāṣakam  MnM 
ghṛtakumbhaṃ varāhe tu tiladroṇaṃ tu tittirau 
śuke dvihāyanaṃ vatsaṃ krauñcaṃ hatvā trihāyanam  MnM 
hatvā haṃsaṃ balākāṃ ca bakaṃ barhiṇam eva ca 
vānaraṃ śyenabhāsau ca sparśayed brāhmaṇāya gām  MnM 
vāso dadyād dhayaṃ hatvā pañca nīlān vṛṣān gajam 
ajameṣāv anaḍvāhaṃ kharaṃ hatvaikahāyanam  MnM 
kravyādāṃs tu mṛgān hatvā dhenuṃ dadyāt payasvinīm 
akravyādān vatsatarīm uṣṭraṃ hatvā tu kṛṣṇalam  MnM 
jīnakārmukabastāvīn pṛthag dadyād viśuddhaye 
caturṇām api varṇānāṃ nārīr hatvānavasthitāḥ  MnM 
dānena vadhanirṇekaṃ sarpādīnām aśaknuvan 
ekaikaśaś caret kṛcchraṃ dvijaḥ pāpāpanuttaye  MnM 
asthimatāṃ tu sattvānāṃ sahasrasya pramāpaṇe 
pūrṇe cānasy anasthnāṃ tu śūdrahatyāvrataṃ caret  MnM 
kiṃ cid eva tu viprāya dadyād asthimatāṃ vadhe 
anasthnāṃ caiva hiṃsāyāṃ prāṇāyāmena śudhyati  MnM 
phaladānāṃ tu vṛkṣāṇāṃ chedane japyam ṛkśatam 
gulmavallīlatānāṃ ca puṣpitānāṃ ca vīrudhām  MnM 
annādyajānāṃ sattvānāṃ rasajānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ 
phalapuṣpodbhavānāṃ ca ghṛtaprāśo viśodhanam  MnM 
kṛṣṭajānām oṣadhīnāṃ jātānāṃ ca svayaṃ vane 
vṛthālambhe 'nugacched gāṃ dinam ekaṃ payovrataḥ  MnM 
etair vratair apohyaṃ syād eno hiṃsāsamudbhavam 
jñānājñānakṛtaṃ kṛtsnaṃ śṛṇutānādyabhakṣaṇe  MnM 
ajñānād vāruṇīṃ pītvā saṃskāreṇaiva śudhyati 
matipūrvam anirdeśyaṃ prāṇāntikam iti sthitiḥ  MnM 
apaḥ surābhājanasthā madyabhāṇḍasthitās tathā 
pañcarātraṃ pibet pītvā śaṅkhapuṣpīśṛtaṃ payaḥ  MnM 
spṛṣṭva dattvā ca madirāṃ vidhivat pratigṛhya ca 
śūdrocchiṣṭāś ca pītvāpaḥ kuśavāri pibet tryaham  MnM 
brāhmaṇas tu surāpasya gandham āghrāya somapaḥ 
prāṇān apsu trir āyamya ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyati  MnM 
ajñānāt prāśya viṇmūtraṃ surāsaṃspṛṣṭam eva ca 
punaḥ saṃskāram arhanti trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ  MnM 
vapanaṃ mekhalā daṇḍo bhaikṣacaryā vratāni ca 
nivartante dvijātīnāṃ punaḥsaṃskārakarmaṇi  MnM 
abhojyānāṃ tu bhuktvānnaṃ strīśūdrocchiṣṭam eva ca 
jagdhvā māṃsam abhakṣyaṃ ca saptarātraṃ yavān pibet  MnM 
śuktāni ca kaṣāyāṃś ca pītvā medhyāny api dvijaḥ 
tāvad bhavaty aprayato yāvat tan na vrajaty adhaḥ  MnM 
viḍvarāhakharoṣṭrāṇāṃ gomāyoḥ kapikākayoḥ 
prāśya mūtrapurīṣāṇi dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret  MnM 
śuṣkāṇi bhuktvā māṃsāni bhaumāni kavakāni ca 
ajñātaṃ caiva sūnāstham etad eva vrataṃ caret  MnM 
kravyādasūkaroṣṭrāṇāṃ kukkuṭānāṃ ca bhakṣaṇe 
narakākakharāṇāṃ ca taptakṛcchraṃ viśodhanam  MnM 
māsikānnaṃ tu yo 'śnīyād asamāvartako dvijaḥ 
sa trīṇy ahāny upavased ekāhaṃ codake vaset  MnM 
brahmacārī tu yo 'śnīyān madhu māṃsaṃ kathaṃ cana 
sa kṛtvā prākṛtaṃ kṛcchraṃ vrataśeṣaṃ samāpayet  MnM 
biḍālakākākhūcchiṣṭaṃ jagdhvā śvanakulasya ca 
keśakīṭāvapannaṃ ca pibed brahmasuvarcalām  MnM 
abhojyam annaṃ nāttavyam ātmanaḥ śuddhim icchatā 
ajñānabhuktaṃ tūttāryaṃ śodhyaṃ vāpy āśu śodhanaiḥ  MnM 
eṣo 'nādyādanasyokto vratānāṃ vividho vidhiḥ 
steyadoṣāpahartṝṇāṃ vratānāṃ śrūyatāṃ vidhiḥ  MnM 
dhānyānnadhanacauryāṇi kṛtvā kāmād dvijottamaḥ 
svajātīyagṛhād eva kṛcchrābdena viśudhyati  MnM 
manuṣyāṇāṃ tu haraṇe strīṇāṃ kṣetragṛhasya ca 
kūpavāpījalānāṃ ca śuddhiś cāndrāyaṇaṃ smṛtam  MnM 
dravyāṇām alpasārāṇāṃ steyaṃ kṛtvānyaveśmataḥ 
caret sāṃtapanaṃ kṛcchraṃ tan niryāty ātmaśuddhaye  MnM 
bhakṣyabhojyāpaharaṇe yānaśayyāsanasya ca 
puṣpamūlaphalānāṃ ca pañcagavyaṃ viśodhanam  MnM 
tṛṇakāṣṭhadrumāṇāṃ ca śuṣkānnasya guḍasya ca 
celacarmāmiṣāṇāṃ ca trirātraṃ syād abhojanam  MnM 
maṇimuktāpravālānāṃ tāmrasya rajatasya ca 
ayaḥkāṃsyopalānāṃ ca dvādaśāhaṃ kaṇānnatā  MnM 
kārpāsakīṭajorṇānāṃ dviśaphaikaśaphasya ca 
pakṣigandhauṣadhīnāṃ ca rajjvāś caiva tryahaṃ payaḥ  MnM 
etair vratair apoheta pāpaṃ steyakṛtaṃ dvijaḥ 
agamyāgamanīyaṃ tu vratair ebhir apānudet  MnM 
gurutalpavrataṃ kuryād retaḥ siktvā svayoniṣu 
sakhyuḥ putrasya ca strīṣu kumārīṣv antyajāsu ca  MnM 
paitṛsvaseyīṃ bhaginīṃ svasrīyāṃ mātur eva ca 
mātuś ca bhrātus tanayāṃ gatvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret  MnM 
etās tisras tu bhāryārthe nopayacchet tu buddhimān 
jñātitvenānupeyās tāḥ patati hy upayann adhaḥ  MnM 
amānuṣīṣū puruṣa udakyāyām ayoniṣu 
retaḥ siktvā jale caiva kṛcchraṃ sāṃtapanaṃ caret  MnM 
maithunaṃ tu samāsevya puṃsi yoṣiti vā dvijaḥ 
goyāne 'psu divā caiva savāsāḥ snānam ācaret  MnM 
caṇḍālāntyastriyo gatvā bhuktvā ca pratigṛhya ca 
pataty ajñānato vipro jñānāt sāmyaṃ tu gacchati  MnM 
vipraduṣṭāṃ striyaṃ bhartā nirundhyād ekaveśmani 
yat puṃsaḥ paradāreṣu tac caināṃ cārayed vratam  MnM 
sā cet punaḥ praduṣyet tu sadṛśenopamantritā 
kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ caiva tad asyāḥ pāvanaṃ smṛtam  MnM 
yat karoty ekarātreṇa vṛṣalīsevanād dvijaḥ 
tad bhaikṣabhug japan nityaṃ tribhir varṣair vyapohati  MnM 
eṣā pāpakṛtām uktā caturṇām api niṣkṛtiḥ 
patitaiḥ saṃprayuktānām imāḥ śṛṇuta niṣkṛtīḥ  MnM 
saṃvatsareṇa patati patitena sahācaran 
yājanādhyāpanād yaunān na tu yānāsanāśanāt  MnM 
yo yena patitenaiṣāṃ saṃsargaṃ yāti mānavaḥ 
sa tasyaiva vrataṃ kuryāt tatsaṃsargaviśuddhaye  MnM 
patitasyodakaṃ kāryaṃ sapiṇḍair bāndhavair bahiḥ 
nindite 'hani sāyāhne jñātirtviggurusaṃnidhau  MnM 
dāsī ghaṭam apāṃ pūrṇaṃ paryasyet pretavat padā 
ahorātram upāsīrann aśaucaṃ bāndhavaiḥ saha  MnM 
nivarteraṃś ca tasmāt tu saṃbhāṣaṇasahāsane 
dāyādyasya pradānaṃ ca yātrā caiva hi laukikī  MnM 
jyeṣṭhatā ca nivarteta jyeṣṭhāvāpyaṃ ca yad dhanam 
jyeṣṭhāṃśaṃ prāpnuyāc cāsya yavīyān guṇato 'dhikaḥ  MnM 
prāyaścitte tu carite pūrṇakumbham apāṃ navam 
tenaiva sārdhaṃ prāsyeyuḥ snātvā puṇye jalāśaye  MnM 
sa tv apsu taṃ ghaṭaṃ prāsya praviśya bhavanaṃ svakam 
sarvāṇi jñātikāryāṇi yathāpūrvaṃ samācaret  MnM 
etad eva vidhiṃ kuryād yoṣitsu patitāsv api 
vastrānnapānaṃ deyaṃ tu vaseyuś ca gṛhāntike  MnM 
enasvibhir anirṇiktair nārthaṃ kiṃ cit sahācaret 
kṛtanirṇejanāṃś caiva na jugupseta karhi cit  MnM 
bālaghnāṃś ca kṛtaghnāṃś ca viśuddhān api dharmataḥ 
śaraṇāgatahantṝṃś ca strīhantṝṃś ca na saṃvaset  MnM 
yeṣāṃ dvijānāṃ sāvitrī nānūcyeta yathāvidhi 
tāṃś cārayitvā trīn kṛcchrān yathāvidhy upanāyayet  MnM 
prāyaścittaṃ cikīrṣanti vikarmasthās tu ye dvijāḥ 
brahmaṇā ca parityaktās teṣām apy etad ādiśet  MnM 
yad garhitenārjayanti karmaṇā brāhmaṇā dhanam 
tasyotsargeṇa śudhyanti japyena tapasaiva ca  MnM 
japitvā trīṇi sāvitryāḥ sahasrāṇi samāhitaḥ 
māsaṃ goṣṭhe payaḥ pītvā mucyate 'satpratigrahāt  MnM 
upavāsakṛśaṃ taṃ tu govrajāt punar āgatam 
praṇataṃ prati pṛccheyuḥ sāmyaṃ saumyecchasīti kim  MnM 
satyam uktvā tu vipreṣu vikired yavasaṃ gavām 
gobhiḥ pravartite tīrthe kuryus tasya parigraham  MnM 
vrātyānāṃ yājanaṃ kṛtvā pareṣām antyakarma ca 
abhicāram ahīnaṃ ca tribhiḥ kṛcchrair vyapohati  MnM 
śaraṇāgataṃ parityajya vedaṃ viplāvya ca dvijaḥ 
saṃvatsaraṃ yavāhāras tat pāpam apasedhati  MnM 
śvaśṛgālakharair daṣṭo grāmyaiḥ kravyādbhir eva ca 
narāśvoṣṭravarāhaiś ca prāṇāyāmena śudhyati  MnM 
ṣaṣṭhānnakālatā māsaṃ saṃhitājapa eva vā 
homāś ca sakalā nityam apāṅktyānāṃ viśodhanam  MnM 
uṣṭrayānaṃ samāruhya kharayānaṃ tu kāmataḥ 
snātvā tu vipro digvāsāḥ prāṇāyāmena śudhyati  MnM 
vinādbhir apsu vāpy ārtaḥ śārīraṃ saṃniṣevya ca 
sacailo bahir āplutya gām ālabhya viśudhyati  MnM 
vedoditānāṃ nityānāṃ karmaṇāṃ samatikrame 
snātakavratalope ca prāyaścittam abhojanam  MnM 
huṅkāraṃ brāhmaṇasyoktvā tvamkāraṃ ca garīyasaḥ 
snātvānaśnann ahaḥ śeṣam abhivādya prasādayet  MnM 
tāḍayitvā tṛṇenāpi kaṇṭhe vābadhya vāsasā 
vivāde vā vinirjitya praṇipatya prasādayet  MnM 
avagūrya tv abdaśataṃ sahasram abhihatya ca 
jighāṃsayā brāhmaṇasya narakaṃ pratipadyate  MnM 
śoṇitaṃ yāvataḥ pāṃsūn saṃgṛhṇāti mahītale 
tāvanty abdasahasrāṇi tatkartā narake vaset  MnM 
avagūrya caret kṛcchram atikṛcchraṃ nipātane 
kṛcchrātikṛcchrau kurvīta viprasyotpādya śoṇitam  MnM 
anuktaniṣkṛtīnāṃ tu pāpānām apanuttaye 
śaktiṃ cāvekṣya pāpaṃ ca prāyaścittaṃ prakalpayet  MnM 
yair abhyupāyair enāṃsi mānavo vyapakarṣati 
tān vo 'bhyupāyān vakṣyāmi devarṣipitṛsevitān  MnM 
tryahaṃ prātas tryahaṃ sāyaṃ tryaham adyād ayācitam 
tryahaṃ paraṃ ca nāśnīyāt prājāpatyaṃ caran dvijaḥ  MnM 
gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi sarpiḥ kuśodakam 
ekarātropavāsaś ca kṛcchraṃ sāṃtapanaṃ smṛtam  MnM 
ekaikaṃ grāsam aśnīyāt tryahāṇi trīṇi pūrvavat 
tryahaṃ copavased antyam atikṛcchraṃ caran dvijaḥ  MnM 
taptakṛcchraṃ caran vipro jalakṣīraghṛtānilān 
pratitryahaṃ pibed uṣṇān sakṛtsnāyī samāhitaḥ  MnM 
yatātmano 'pramattasya dvādaśāham abhojanam 
parāko nāma kṛcchro 'yaṃ sarvapāpāpanodanaḥ  MnM 
ekaikaṃ hrāsayet piṇḍaṃ kṛṣṇe śukle ca vardhayet 
upaspṛśaṃs triṣavaṇam etac cāṇdrāyaṇaṃ smṛtam  MnM 
etam eva vidhiṃ kṛtsnam ācared yavamadhyame 
śuklapakṣādiniyataś caraṃś cāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam  MnM 
aṣṭāv aṣṭau samaśnīyāt piṇḍān madhyaṃdine sthite 
niyatātmā haviṣyāśī yaticāndrāyaṇaṃ caran  MnM 
caturaḥ prātar aśnīyāt piṇḍān vipraḥ samāhitaḥ 
caturo 'stam ite sūrye śiśucāndrāyaṇaṃ smṛtam  MnM 
yathā kathaṃ cit piṇḍānāṃ tisro 'śītīḥ samāhitaḥ 
māsenāśnan haviṣyasya candrasyaiti salokatām  MnM 
etad rudrās tathādityā vasavaś cācaran vratam 
sarvākuśalamokṣāya marutaś ca maharṣibhiḥ  MnM 
mahāvyāhṛtibhir homaḥ kartavyaḥ svayam anvaham 
ahiṃsā satyam akrodham ārjavaṃ ca samācaret  MnM 
trir ahnas trir niśāyāṃ ca savāsā jalam āviśet 
strīśūdrapatitāṃś caiva nābhibhāṣeta karhi cit  MnM
