sthānāsanābhyāṃ vihared aśakto 'dhaḥ śayīta vā 
brahmacārī vratī ca syād gurudevadvijārcakaḥ  MnM 
sāvitrīṃ ca japen nityaṃ pavitrāṇi ca śaktitaḥ 
sarveṣv eva vrateṣv evaṃ prāyaścittārtham ādṛtaḥ  MnM 
etair dvijātayaḥ śodhyā vratair āviṣkṛtainasaḥ 
anāviṣkṛtapāpāṃs tu mantrair homaiś ca śodhayet  MnM 
khyāpanenānutāpena tapasādhyayanena ca 
pāpakṛn mucyate pāpāt tathā dānena cāpadi  MnM 
yathā yathā naro 'dharmaṃ svayaṃ kṛtvānubhāṣate 
tathā tathā tvacevāhis tenādharmeṇa mucyate  MnM 
yathā yathā manas tasya duṣkṛtaṃ karma garhati 
tathā tathā śarīraṃ tat tenādharmeṇa mucyate  MnM 
kṛtvā pāpaṃ hi saṃtapya tasmāt pāpāt pramucyate 
naivaṃ kuryāṃ punar iti nivṛttyā pūyate tu saḥ  MnM 
evaṃ saṃcintya manasā pretya karmaphalodayam 
manovāṅgūrtibhir nityaṃ śubhaṃ karma samācaret  MnM 
ajñānād yadi vā jñānāt kṛtvā karma vigarhitam 
tasmād vimuktim anvicchan dvitīyaṃ na samācaret  MnM 
yasmin karmaṇy asya kṛte manasaḥ syād alāghavam 
tasmiṃs tāvat tapaḥ kuryād yāvat tuṣṭikaraṃ bhavet  MnM 
tapomūlam idaṃ sarvaṃ daivamānuṣakaṃ sukham 
tapomadhyaṃ budhaiḥ proktaṃ tapo'ntaṃ vedadarśibhiḥ  MnM 
brāhmaṇasya tapo jñānaṃ tapaḥ kṣatrasya rakṣaṇam 
vaiśyasya tu tapo vārtā tapaḥ śūdrasya sevanam  MnM 
ṛṣayaḥ saṃyatātmānaḥ phalamūlānilāśanāḥ 
tapasaiva prapaśyanti trailokyaṃ sacarācaram  MnM 
auṣadhāny agado vidyā daivī ca vividhā sthitiḥ 
tapasaiva prasidhyanti tapas teṣāṃ hi sādhanam  MnM 
yad dustaraṃ yad durāpaṃ yad durgaṃ yac ca duṣkaram 
sarvaṃ tu tapasā sādhyaṃ tapo hi duratikramam  MnM 
mahāpātakinaś caiva śeṣāś cākāryakāriṇaḥ 
tapasaiva sutaptena mucyante kilbiṣāt tataḥ  MnM 
kītāś cāhipataṃgāś ca paśavaś ca vayāṃsi ca 
sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni divaṃ yānti tapobalāt  MnM 
yat kiṃ cid enaḥ kurvanti manovāṅgūrtibhir janāḥ 
tat sarvaṃ nirdahanty āśu tapasaiva tapodhanāḥ  MnM 
tapasaiva viśuddhasya brāhmaṇasya divaukasaḥ 
ijyāś ca pratigṛhṇanti kāmān saṃvardhayanti ca  MnM 
prajāpatir idaṃ śāstraṃ tapasaivāsṛjat prabhuḥ 
tathaiva vedān ṛṣayas tapasā pratipedire  MnM 
ity etat tapaso devā mahābhāgyaṃ pracakṣate 
sarvasyāsya prapaśyantas tapasaḥ puṇyam uttamam  MnM 
vedābhyāso 'nvahaṃ śaktyā mahāyajñakriyā kṣamā 
nāśayanty āśu pāpāni mahāpātakajāny api  MnM 
yathaidhas tejasā vahniḥ prāptaṃ nirdahati kṣaṇāt 
tathā jñānāgninā pāpaṃ sarvaṃ dahati vedavit  MnM 
ity etad enasām uktaṃ prāyaścittaṃ yathāvidhi 
ata ūrdhvaṃ rahasyānāṃ prāyaścittaṃ nibodhata  MnM 
savyāhṛtipraṇavakāḥ prāṇāyāmās tu ṣoḍaśa 
api bhrūṇahanaṃ māsāt punanty ahar ahaḥ kṛtāḥ  MnM 
kautsaṃ japtvāpa ity etad vasiṣṭhaṃ ca pratīty ṛcam 
māhitraṃ śuddhavatyaś ca surāpo 'pi viśudhyati  MnM 
sakṛj japtvāsyavāmīyaṃ śivasaṃkalpam eva ca 
apahṛtya suvarṇaṃ tu kṣaṇād bhavati nirmalaḥ  MnM 
haviṣpāntīyam abhyasya na tamaṃ ha itīti ca 
japitvā pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ mucyate gurutalpagaḥ  MnM 
enasāṃ sthūlasūkṣmāṇāṃ cikīrṣann apanodanam 
avety ṛcaṃ japed abdaṃ yat kiṃ cedam itīti vā  MnM 
pratigṛhyāpratigrāhyaṃ bhuktvā cānnaṃ vigarhitam 
japaṃs taratsamandīyaṃ pūyate mānavas tryahāt  MnM 
somāraudraṃ tu bahvenāḥ māsam abhyasya śudhyati 
sravantyām ācaran snānam aryamṇām iti ca tṛcam  MnM 
abdārdham indram ity etad enasvī saptakaṃ japet 
apraśastaṃ tu kṛtvāpsu māsam āsīta bhaikṣabhuk  MnM 
mantraiḥ śākalahomīyair abdaṃ hutvā ghṛtaṃ dvijaḥ 
sugurv apy apahanty eno japtvā vā nama ity ṛcam  MnM 
mahāpātakasaṃyukto 'nugacched gāḥ samāhitaḥ 
abhyasyābdaṃ pāvamānīr bhaikṣāhāro viśudhyati  MnM 
araṇye vā trir abhyasya prayato vedasaṃhitām 
mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvaiḥ parākaiḥ śodhitas tribhiḥ  MnM 
tryahaṃ tūpavased yuktas trir ahno 'bhyupayann apaḥ 
mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvais trir japitvāghamarṣaṇam  MnM 
yathāśvamedhaḥ kraturāṭ sarvapāpāpanodanaḥ 
tathāghamarṣaṇaṃ sūktaṃ sarvapāpāpanodanam  MnM 
hatvā lokān apīmāṃs trīn aśnann api yatas tataḥ 
ṛgvedaṃ dhārayan vipro nainaḥ prāpnoti kiṃ cana  MnM 
ṛksaṃhitāṃ trir abhyasya yajuṣāṃ vā samāhitaḥ 
sāmnāṃ vā sarahasyānāṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  MnM 
yathā mahāhradaṃ prāpya kṣiptaṃ loṣṭaṃ vinaśyati 
tathā duścaritaṃ sarvaṃ vede trivṛti majjati  MnM 
ṛco yajūṃṣi cānyāni sāmāni vividhāni ca 
eṣa jñeyas trivṛdvedo yo vedainaṃ sa vedavit  MnM 
ādyaṃ yat tryakṣaraṃ brahma trayī yasmin pratiṣṭhitā 
sa guhyo 'nyas trivṛdvedo yas taṃ veda sa vedavit  MnM 
cāturvarṇyasya kṛtsno 'yam ukto dharmas tvayānaghaḥ 
karmaṇāṃ phalanirvṛttiṃ śaṃsa nas tattvataḥ parām  Mn 
sa tān uvāca dharmātmā maharṣīn mānavo bhṛguḥ 
asya sarvasya śṛṇuta karmayogasya nirṇayam  Mn 
śubhāśubhaphalaṃ karma manovāgdehasaṃbhavam 
karmajā gatayo nṝṇām uttamādhamamadhyamaḥ  Mn 
tasyeha trividhasyāpi tryadhiṣṭhānasya dehinaḥ 
daśalakṣaṇayuktasya mano vidyāt pravartakam  Mn 
paradravyeṣv abhidhyānaṃ manasāniṣṭacintanam 
vitathābhiniveśaś ca trividhaṃ karma mānasam  Mn 
pāruṣyam anṛtaṃ caiva paiśunyaṃ cāpi sarvaśaḥ 
asaṃbaddhapralāpaś ca vāṅmayaṃ syāc caturvidham  Mn 
adattānām upādānaṃ hiṃsā caivāvidhānataḥ 
paradāropasevā ca śārīraṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam  Mn 
mānasaṃ manasaivāyam upabhuṅkte śubhāśubham 
vācā vācā kṛtaṃ karma kāyenaiva ca kāyikam  Mn 
śarīrajaiḥ karmadoṣair yāti sthāvaratāṃ naraḥ 
vācikaiḥ pakṣimṛgatāṃ mānasair antyajātitām  Mn 
vāgdaṇḍo 'tha manodaṇḍaḥ kāyadaṇḍas tathaiva ca 
yasyaite nihitā buddhau tridaṇḍīti sa ucyate  Mn 
tridaṇḍam etan nikṣipya sarvabhūteṣu mānavaḥ 
kāmakrodhau tu saṃyamya tataḥ siddhiṃ niyacchati  Mn 
yo 'syātmanaḥ kārayitā taṃ kṣetrajñaṃ pracakṣate 
yaḥ karoti tu karmāṇi sa bhūtātmocyate budhaiḥ  Mn 
jīvasaṃjño 'ntarātmānyaḥ sahajaḥ sarvadehinām 
yena vedayate sarvaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca janmasu  Mn 
tāv ubhau bhūtasaṃpṛktau mahān kṣetrajña eva ca 
uccāvaceṣu bhūteṣu sthitaṃ taṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhataḥ  Mn 
asaṃkhyā mūrtayas tasya niṣpatanti śarīrataḥ 
uccāvacāni bhūtāni satataṃ ceṣṭayanti yāḥ  Mn 
pañcabhya eva mātrābhyaḥ pretya duṣkṛtināṃ nṛṇām 
śarīraṃ yātanārthīyam anyad utpadyate dhruvam  Mn 
tenānubhūya tā yāmīḥ śarīreṇeha yātanāḥ 
tāsv eva bhūtamātrāsu pralīyante vibhāgaśaḥ  Mn 
so 'nubhūyāsukhodarkān doṣān viṣayasaṅgajān 
vyapetakalmaṣo 'bhyeti tāv evobhau mahaujasau  Mn 
tau dharmaṃ paśyatas tasya pāpaṃ cātandritau saha 
yābhyāṃ prāpnoti saṃpṛktaḥ pretyeha ca sukhāsukham  Mn 
yady ācarati dharmaṃ sa prāyaśo 'dharmam alpaśaḥ 
tair eva cāvṛto bhūtaiḥ svarge sukham upāśnute  Mn 
yadi tu prāyaśo 'dharmaṃ sevate dharmam alpaśaḥ 
tair bhūtaiḥ sa parityakto yāmīḥ prāpnoti yātanāḥ  Mn 
yāmīs tā yātanāḥ prāpya sa jīvo vītakalmaṣaḥ 
tāny eva pañca bhūtāni punar apyeti bhāgaśaḥ  Mn 
etā dṛṣṭvāsya jīvasya gatīḥ svenaiva cetasā 
dharmato 'dharmataś caiva dharme dadhyāt sadā manaḥ  Mn 
sattvaṃ rajas tamaś caiva trīn vidyād ātmano guṇān 
yair vyāpyemān sthito bhāvān mahān sarvān aśeṣataḥ  Mn 
yo yadaiṣāṃ guṇo dehe sākalyenātiricyate 
sa tadā tadguṇaprāyaṃ taṃ karoti śarīriṇam  Mn 
sattvaṃ jñānaṃ tamo 'jñānaṃ rāgadveṣau rajaḥ smṛtam 
etad vyāptimad eteṣāṃ sarvabhūtāśritaṃ vapuḥ  Mn 
tatra yat prītisaṃyuktaṃ kiṃ cid ātmani lakṣayet 
praśāntam iva śuddhābhaṃ sattvaṃ tad upadhārayet  Mn 
yat tu duḥkhasamāyuktam aprītikaram ātmanaḥ 
tad rajo pratīpaṃ vidyāt satataṃ hāri dehinām  Mn 
yat tu syān mohasaṃyuktam avyaktaṃ viṣayātmakam 
apratarkyam avijñeyaṃ tamas tad upadhārayet  Mn 
trayāṇām api caiteṣāṃ guṇānāṃ yaḥ phalodayaḥ 
agryo madhyo jaghanyaś ca taṃ pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ  Mn 
vedābhyāsas tapo jñānaṃ śaucam indriyanigrahaḥ 
dharmakriyātmacintā ca sāttvikaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam  Mn 
ārambharucitādhairyam asatkāryaparigrahaḥ 
viṣayopasevā cājasraṃ rājasaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam  Mn 
lobhaḥ svapno 'dhṛtiḥ krauryaṃ nāstikyaṃ bhinnavṛttitā 
yāciṣṇutā pramādaś ca tāmasaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam  Mn 
trayāṇām api caiteṣāṃ guṇānāṃ triṣu tiṣṭhatām 
idaṃ sāmāsikaṃ jñeyaṃ kramaśo guṇalakṣaṇam  Mn 
yat karma kṛtvā kurvaṃś ca kariṣyaṃś caiva lajjati 
taj jñeyaṃ viduṣā sarvaṃ tāmasaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam  Mn 
yenāsmin karmanā loke khyātim icchati puṣkalām 
na ca śocaty asaṃpattau tad vijñeyaṃ tu rājasam  Mn 
yat sarveṇecchati jñātuṃ yan na lajjati cācaran 
yena tuṣyati cātmāsya tat sattvaguṇalakṣaṇam  Mn 
tamaso lakṣaṇaṃ kāmo rajasas tv artha ucyate 
sattvasya lakṣaṇaṃ dharmaḥ śraiṣṭhyam eṣāṃ yathottaram  Mn 
yena yas tu guṇenaiṣāṃ saṃsarān pratipadyate 
tān samāsena vakṣyāmi sarvasyāsya yathākramam  Mn 
devatvaṃ sāttvikā yānti manuṣyatvaṃ ca rājasāḥ 
tiryaktvaṃ tāmasā nityam ity eṣā trividhā gatiḥ  Mn 
trividhā trividhaiṣā tu vijñeyā gauṇikī gatiḥ 
adhamā madhyamāgryā ca karmavidyāviśeṣataḥ  Mn 
sthāvarāḥ kṛmikīṭāś ca matsyāḥ sarpāḥ sakacchapāḥ 
paśavaś ca mṛgāś caiva jaghanyā tāmasī gatiḥ  Mn 
hastinaś ca turaṅgāś ca śūdrā mlecchāś ca garhitāḥ 
siṃhā vyāghrā varāhāś ca madhyamā tāmasī gatiḥ  Mn 
cāraṇāś ca suparṇāś ca puruṣāś caiva dāmbhikāḥ 
rakṣāṃsi ca piśācāś ca tāmasīṣūttamā gatiḥ  Mn 
jhallā mallā naṭāś caiva puruṣāḥ śastravṛttayaḥ 
dyūtapānaprasaktāś ca jaghanyā rājasī gatiḥ  Mn 
rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś caiva rājñāṃ caiva purohitāḥ 
vādayuddhapradhānāś ca madhyamā rājasī gatiḥ  Mn 
gandharvā guhyakā yakṣā vibudhānucarāś ca ye 
tathaivāpsarasaḥ sarvā rājasīṣūttamā gatiḥ  Mn 
tāpasā yatayo viprā ye ca vaimānikā gaṇāḥ 
nakṣatrāṇi ca daityāś ca prathamā sāttvikī gatiḥ  Mn 
yajvāna ṛṣayo devā vedā jyotīṃṣi vatsarāḥ 
pitaraś caiva sādhyāś ca dvitīyā sāttvikī gatiḥ  Mn 
brahmā viśvasṛjo dharmo mahān avyaktam eva ca 
uttamāṃ sāttvikīm etāṃ gatim āhur manīṣiṇaḥ  Mn 
eṣa sarvaḥ samuddiṣṭas triprakārasya karmaṇaḥ 
trividhas trividhaḥ kṛtsnaḥ saṃsāraḥ sārvabhautikaḥ  Mn 
indriyāṇāṃ prasaṅgena dharmasyāsevanena ca 
pāpān saṃyānti saṃsārān avidvāṃso narādhamāḥ  Mn 
yāṃ yāṃ yoniṃ tu jīvo 'yaṃ yena yeneha karmaṇā 
kramaśo yāti loke 'smiṃs tat tat sarvaṃ nibodhata  Mn 
bahūn varṣagaṇān ghorān narakān prāpya tatkṣayāt 
saṃsārān pratipadyante mahāpātakinas tv imān  Mn 
śvasūkarakharoṣṭrāṇāṃ go'jāvimṛgapakṣiṇāṃ 
caṇḍālapukkasānāṃ ca brahmahā yonim ṛcchati  Mn 
kṛmikīṭapataṅgānāṃ viḍbhujāṃ caiva pakṣiṇām 
hiṃsrāṇāṃ caiva sattvānāṃ surāpo brāhmaṇo vrajet  Mn 
lūtāhisaraṭānāṃ ca tiraścāṃ cāmbucāriṇām 
hiṃsrāṇāṃ ca piśācānāṃ steno vipraḥ sahasraśaḥ  Mn 
tṛṇagulmalatānāṃ ca kravyādāṃ daṃṣṭriṇām api 
krūrakarmakṛtāṃ caiva śataśo gurutalpagaḥ  Mn 
hiṃsrā bhavanti kravyādāḥ kṛmayo 'medhyabhakṣiṇaḥ 
parasparādinaḥ stenāḥ pretyāntyastrīniṣeviṇaḥ  Mn 
saṃyogaṃ patitair gatvā parasyaiva ca yoṣitam 
apahṛtya ca viprasvaṃ bhavati brahmarākṣasaḥ  Mn 
maṇimuktāpravālāni hṛtvā lobhena mānavaḥ 
vividhāṇi ca ratnāni jāyate hemakartṛṣu  Mn 
dhānyaṃ hṛtvā bhavaty ākhuḥ kāṃsyaṃ haṃso jalaṃ plavaḥ 
madhu daṃśaḥ payaḥ kāko rasaṃ śvā nakulo ghṛtam  Mn 
māṃsaṃ gṛdhro vapāṃ madgus tailaṃ tailapakaḥ khagaḥ 
cīrīvākas tu lavaṇaṃ balākā śakunir dadhi  Mn 
kauśeyaṃ tittirir hṛtvā kṣaumaṃ hṛtvā tu darduraḥ 
kārpāsatāntavaṃ krauñco godhā gāṃ vāggudo guḍam  Mn 
chucchundariḥ śubhān gandhān patraśākaṃ tu barhiṇaḥ 
śvāvit kṛtānnaṃ vividham akṛtānnaṃ tu śalyakaḥ  Mn 
bako bhavati hṛtvāgniṃ gṛhakārī hy upaskaram 
raktāni hṛtvā vāsāṃsi jāyate jīvajīvakaḥ  Mn 
vṛko mṛgebhaṃ vyāghro 'śvaṃ phalamūlaṃ tu markaṭaḥ 
strīm ṛkṣaḥ stokako vāri yānāny uṣṭraḥ paśūn ajaḥ  Mn 
yad vā tad vā paradravyam apahṛtya balān naraḥ 
avaśyaṃ yāti tiryaktvaṃ jagdhvā caivāhutaṃ haviḥ  Mn 
striyo 'py etena kalpena hṛtvā doṣam avāpnuyuḥ 
eteṣām eva jantūnāṃ bhāryātvam upayānti tāḥ  Mn 
svebhyaḥ svebhyas tu karmabhyaś cyutā varṇā hy anāpadi 
pāpān saṃsṛtya saṃsārān preṣyatāṃ yānti śatruṣu  Mn 
vāntāśy ulkāmukhaḥ preto vipro dharmāt svakāc cyutaḥ 
amedhyakuṇapāśī ca kṣatriyaḥ kaṭapūtanaḥ  Mn 
maitrākṣajyotikaḥ preto vaiśyo bhavati pūyabhuk 
cailāśakaś ca bhavati śūdro dharmāt svakāc cyutaḥ  Mn 
yathā yathā niṣevante viṣayān viṣayātmakāḥ 
tathā tathā kuśalatā teṣāṃ teṣūpajāyate  Mn 
te 'bhyāsāt karmaṇāṃ teṣāṃ pāpānām alpabuddhayaḥ 
saṃprāpnuvanti duḥkhāni tāsu tāsv iha yoniṣu  Mn 
tāmisrādiṣu cogreṣu narakeṣu vivartanam 
asipatravanādīni bandhanachedanāni ca  Mn 
vividhāś caiva saṃpīḍāḥ kākolūkaiś ca bhakṣaṇam 
karambhavālukātāpān kumbhīpākāṃś ca dāruṇān  Mn 
saṃbhavāṃś ca viyonīṣu duḥkhaprāyāsu nityaśaḥ 
śītātapābhighātāṃś ca vividhāni bhayāni ca  Mn 
asakṛd garbhavāseṣu vāsaṃ janma ca dāruṇam 
bandhanāni ca kāṣṭhāni parapreṣyatvam eva ca  Mn 
bandhupriyaviyogāṃś ca saṃvāsaṃ caiva durjanaiḥ 
dravyārjanaṃ ca nāśaṃ ca mitrāmitrasya cārjanam  Mn 
jarāṃ caivāpratīkārāṃ vyādhibhiś copapīḍanam 
kleśāṃś ca vividhāṃs tāṃs tān mṛtyum eva ca durjayam  Mn 
yādṛśena tu bhāvena yad yat karma niṣevate 
tādṛśena śarīreṇa tat tat phalam upāśnute  Mn 
eṣa sarvaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ karmaṇāṃ vaḥ phalodayaḥ 
naiḥśreyasakaraṃ karma viprasyedaṃ nibodhata  Mn 
vedābhyāsas tapo jñānam indriyāṇāṃ ca saṃyamaḥ 
ahiṃsā gurusevā ca niḥśreyasakaraṃ param  Mn 
sarveṣām api caiteṣāṃ śubhānām iha karmaṇām 
kiṃ cic chreyaskarataraṃ karmoktaṃ puruṣaṃ prati  Mn 
sarveṣām api caiteṣām ātmajñānaṃ paraṃ smṛtam 
tad dhy agryaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ prāpyate hy amṛtaṃ tataḥ  Mn 
ṣaṇṇām eṣāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ pretya ceha ca 
śreyaskarataraṃ jñeyaṃ sarvadā karma vaidikam  Mn 
vaidike karmayoge tu sarvāṇy etāny aśeṣataḥ 
antarbhavanti kramaśas tasmiṃs tasmin kriyāvidhau  Mn 
sukhābhyudayikaṃ caiva naiḥśreyasikam eva ca 
pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca dvividhaṃ karma vaidikam  Mn 
iha cāmutra vā kāmyaṃ pravṛttaṃ karma kīrtyate 
niṣkāmaṃ jñātapūrvaṃ tu nivṛttam upadiśyate  Mn 
pravṛttaṃ karma saṃsevyaṃ devānām eti sāmyatām 
nivṛttaṃ sevamānas tu bhūtāny atyeti pañca vai  Mn 
sarvabhūteṣu cātmānaṃ sarvabhūtāni cātmani 
samaṃ paśyann ātmayājī svārājyam adhigacchati  Mn 
yathoktāny api karmāṇi parihāya dvijottamaḥ 
ātmajñāne śame ca syād vedābhyāse ca yatnavān  Mn 
etad dhi janmasāphalyaṃ brāhmaṇasya viśeṣataḥ 
prāpyaitat kṛtakṛtyo hi dvijo bhavati nānyathā  Mn 
pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ vedaś cakṣuḥ sanātanam 
aśakyaṃ cāprameyaṃ ca vedaśāstram iti sthitiḥ  Mn 
yā vedabāhyāḥ smṛtayo yāś ca kāś ca kudṛṣṭayaḥ 
sarvās tā niṣphalāḥ pretya tamoniṣṭhā hi tāḥ smṛtāḥ  Mn 
utpadyante cyavante ca yāny ato 'nyāni kāni cit 
tāny arvākkālikatayā niṣphalāny anṛtāni ca  Mn 
cāturvarṇyaṃ trayo lokāś catvāraś cāśramāḥ pṛthak 
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca sarvaṃ vedāt prasidhyati  Mn 
śabdaḥ sparśaś ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaś ca pañcamaḥ 
vedād eva prasūyante prasūtir guṇakarmataḥ  Mn 
bibharti sarvabhūtāni vedaśāstraṃ sanātanam 
tasmād etat paraṃ manye yaj jantor asya sādhanam  Mn 
senāpatyaṃ ca rājyaṃ ca daṇḍanetṛtvam eva ca 
sarvalokādhipatyaṃ ca vedaśāstravid arhati  Mn 
yathā jātabalo vahnir dahaty ārdrān api drumān 
tathā dahati vedajñaḥ karmajaṃ doṣam ātmanaḥ  Mn 
vedaśāstrārthatattvajño yatra tatrāśrame vasan 
ihaiva loke tiṣṭhan sa brahmabhūyāya kalpate  Mn 
ajñebhyo granthinaḥ śreṣṭhā granthibhyo dhāriṇo varāḥ 
dhāribhyo jñāninaḥ śreṣṭhā jñānibhyo vyavasāyinaḥ  Mn 
tapo vidyā ca viprasya niḥśreyasakaraṃ param 
tapasā kilbiṣaṃ hanti vidyayāmṛtam aśnute  Mn 
pratyakṣaṃ cānumānaṃ ca śāstraṃ ca vividhāgamam 
trayaṃ suviditaṃ kāryaṃ dharmaśuddhim abhīpsatā  Mn 
ārṣaṃ dharmopadeśaṃ ca vedaśāstrāvirodhinā 
yas tarkeṇānusaṃdhatte sa dharmaṃ veda netaraḥ  Mn 
naiḥśreyasam idaṃ karma yathoditam aśeṣataḥ 
mānavasyāsya śāstrasya rahasyam upadiśyate  Mn 
anāmnāteṣu dharmeṣu kathaṃ syād iti ced bhavet 
yaṃ śiṣṭā brāhmaṇā brūyuḥ sa dharmaḥ syād aśaṅkitaḥ  Mn 
dharmeṇādhigato yais tu vedaḥ saparibṛṃhaṇaḥ 
te śiṣṭā brāhmaṇā jñeyāḥ śrutipratyakṣahetavaḥ  Mn 
daśāvarā vā pariṣad yaṃ dharmaṃ parikalpayet 
tryavarā vāpi vṛttasthā taṃ dharmaṃ na vicālayet  Mn 
traividyo hetukas tarkī nairukto dharmapāṭhakaḥ 
trayaś cāśramiṇaḥ pūrve pariṣat syād daśāvarā  Mn 
ṛgvedavid yajurvic ca sāmavedavid eva ca 
tryavarā pariṣaj jñeyā dharmasaṃśayanirṇaye  Mn 
eko 'pi vedavid dharmaṃ yaṃ vyavasyed dvijottamaḥ 
sa vijñeyaḥ paro dharmo nājñānām udito 'yutaiḥ  Mn 
avratānām amantrāṇāṃ jātimātropajīvinām 
sahasraśaḥ sametānāṃ pariṣattvaṃ na vidyate  Mn 
yaṃ vadanti tamobhūtā mūrkhā dharmam atadvidaḥ 
tatpāpaṃ śatadhā bhūtvā tadvaktṝn anugacchati  Mn 
etad vo 'bhihitaṃ sarvaṃ niḥśreyasakaraṃ param 
asmād apracyuto vipraḥ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim  Mn 
evaṃ sa bhagavān devo lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā 
dharmasya paramaṃ guhyaṃ mamedaṃ sarvam uktavān  Mn 
sarvam ātmani saṃpaśyet sac cāsac ca samāhitaḥ 
sarvaṃ hy ātmani saṃpaśyan nādharme kurute manaḥ  Mn 
ātmaiva devatāḥ sarvāḥ sarvam ātmany avasthitam 
ātmā hi janayaty eṣāṃ karmayogaṃ śarīriṇām  Mn 
khaṃ saṃniveśayet kheṣu ceṣṭanasparśane 'nilam 
paktidṛṣṭyoḥ paraṃ tejaḥ snehe 'po gāṃ ca mūrtiṣu  Mn 
manasīnduṃ diśaḥ śrotre krānte viṣṇuṃ bale haram 
vācy agniṃ mitram utsarge prajane ca prajāpatim  Mn 
praśāsitāraṃ sarveṣām aṇīyāṃsam aṇor api 
rukmābhaṃ svapnadhīgamyaṃ vidyāt taṃ puruṣaṃ param  Mn 
etam eke vadanty agniṃ manum anye prajāpatim 
indram eke pare prāṇam apare brahma śāśvatam  Mn 
eṣa sarvāṇi bhūtāni pañcabhir vyāpya mūrtibhiḥ 
janmavṛddhikṣayair nityaṃ saṃsārayati cakravat  Mn 
evaṃ yaḥ sarvabhūteṣu paśyaty ātmānam ātmanā 
sa sarvasamatām etya brahmābhyeti paraṃ padam  Mn 
ity etan mānavaṃ śāstraṃ bhṛguproktaṃ paṭhan dvijaḥ 
bhavaty ācāravān nityaṃ yatheṣṭāṃ prāpnuyād gatim  Mn
